/ /bla ma rin po che mkhan chen pa'i rnam thar ngo mtshar snye ma zhes bya ba sgro bkur dang bral zhing yid ches la dgod bro ba zhig bzhugs//

/ /na maHshrI gu ru buddha boddhi satwa maNDa la de wa ta dharmma pA la dha na de wa sa pa ri wA re bhyaH kun mkhyen gsung gi snying po dga' bzhi'i lam/ /legs par ston pa'i
blo gros cher gsal bas/ /gsang chen bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan 'dzin pa'i dpal/ /'dren mchog bzang por snying nas dad pas 'dud/ /blo mchog rgyal ba ma lus 'dus pa'i dngos/
/gdul bya'i khams dang bsam pa gsal mkhyen nas/ /phan bde rgya mtsho yid bzhin stsol mdzad pa/ /pha rgod sku drin dbang por gsol ba 'debs/ /nam mkha'i mthas klas sems can
rjes gzung phyir/ /rin chen dam pa'i chos kyi mdzod bzung nas/ /gang 'dul chos kyi dga' ston spel ba'i rje/ /snying nas dran no byang chub bar du skyongs/ /rab 'byams rgyud
sde'i mnga' bdag byang gling pa/ /zab gter bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan mnga' ris pa/ /

lugs gnyis phan bde'i rtsa lag gnas gsar ba/ /sku drin mnyam med gsum la skyabs su mchi/ /gang gi sku drin zer phreng phra mos kyang / /bdag lta'i mun pa stug po drung phyungs
nas/ /lhan skyes bde ba'i ge sar bzhad pa'i dpal/ /rgya bod bla ma rnams la phyag 'tshal lo/ /smin byed dbang gi rtsa ba rab brtan zhing / /byin rlabs bka' gnang yal
'dab bye bas spud/ /zab don snyan brgyud 'bras bu'i khur 'dzin pa/ /dpag bsam brgyud pa'i bla ma rnams la 'dud/ /bde chen dmigs med thugs rjes khros pa'i sku/ /'od gsal stong
nyid bdag med yum gyis 'khyud/ /rnam thar brgyad dngos lha mo'i 'khor gyis bskor/ /dgyes mdzad lhag pa'i lha des ring du skyongs/ /dpal ldan byang chub phyogs chos bdag
nyid can/ /mdzes ldan khro chags stong nyid phag mos rtsen/ /skal ldan snying la bdud rtsi'i dpal ster ba/ /bcom ldan bde mchog snying

dbus bzhugs su gsol/ /mthu stobs nyi 'od bdud dpung mun pa'i gshed/ /dngos grub 'od dkar skal bzang ku mud gnyen/ /dran pas gdung sel khrag 'thung yang phur zhes/ /nyi zla
ltar grags de yis gzigs su gsol/ /mkha' khyab chos dbyings ye shes zhi ba'i ngang / /dmigs med thugs rjes rab khros khro bo'i gar/ /snying gi mun sel rje btsun 'jam pa'i
dbyangs/ /lha mchog khyod kyis da dung ma gtong zhig /dgyes mdzad khros pa'i mkha' dbyings las 'ongs shing / /rmad byung mthu stobs zer 'phreng bye ba brgyas/ /bdud dpung
mun pa mthar byed nag po che/ /lha mchog nyin mo'i mgon pos bdag la skyongs/ /mdor na rtsa brgyud bla ma thams cad dang / /rab 'byams rgyal ba dkon mchog yi dam lha/ /mkha'
'gro chos skyong nor lha gter bdag bcas/ /skyabs gnas mchod 'os kun la phyag btsal te/ /sngon byon dam pa 'ga' yi rjes zhugs nas/ /bdag gi rtogs brjod sgro skur spangs
pa'i gtam/ /dad ldan gus pa'i zhal ngo ma chogs par/ /cung zad 'dzem pa spangs te bri bar bya/ /skyon med dal 'byaur lus bzang thob kyang phal cher mi khom dbang du song
/ /shAkya'i sras kyi rjes su zhugs kyang shAkya'i gsung la rgyab kyis phyogs/ /yongs 'dzin dam pa ji snyed bsten kyang dam pa'i byin rlabs cher ma zhugs/ /zab rgyas dam
chos dpag med thob kyang phal cher ming rkyang tsam du bas/ /de slad sa chen rdul dang rin chen bzhin/ /bdag skyon mtha' yas yon tan srid pa tsam/ /cung zad mchis na'ang
snying po ma mthong na/ /yi ge'i ngal ba 'di 'dras ci zhig bgyi/ /'on kyang tshul 'dis bstan la mi phan mod/ /rnam kun gnod par mi nus de bsams nas/ /rkun po'i nor bzhin

skyon rnams sbas nas ni/ /'bad pas yon tan gang yod 'dri bar bgyi/ /e ma hoH de la gtsang stod bo dong er chos ldan rgyal po'i rigs su skye ba blangs nas/ skyes bu dam pa mang
po dang / ches mchog tu sku drin che ba'i dbang por gyur pa chos rje sgo rum pa chen po yab sras gsum gyi sku drin las/ rgyal ba'i bstan pa rin po che la dang ba dang
/ shes pa dang / yid ches pa'i dad pa thob pa'i mthus/ ris med pa'i chos kyi rgya mtsho chen por 'jug nus pa'i dpa' bo/ rig pa 'dzin pa mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug ces bgyi
ba bdag gis/ lo brgyad lon pa na rje btsun rdo rje 'chang sgo rum pa chen po'i zhabs las rab tu byung ba nas bzung ste/ deng sang gi bar du bla ma dam pa'i sku drin las
rnyed pa'i yon tan ni cung zad tsam/ so so skye bo'i rang bzhin ngan goms kyi skyon ni mtha' yas pa zhig /nyung ngur gyur pa'i rtogs brjod dag kyang brjod pa la dgos pa
dang / ma brjod pa la skyon du 'gyur ba sogs ni ci yang med/ de lta na'ang snang ba gdong 'ded gzhir bzhag nas/ da ltar gyi shes pa la gang shar de sbas gyib med par chol
le smras gtong ba nga rang gi srol yin pa ltar/ 'ga' zhig gi ngor che long zhig smras pa 'di la dgyes pa yod na yang legs/ mi dgyes pa yod na yang legs/ gang byung kyang
legs pa sprang po'i chal gtam chen mo zhes bya ba 'di lta ste/ gang zhig bla ma dam pa bsten pa dang / /zab dgu'i gdams pa rgya mtsho thos pa dang / /las 'phro smon lam
thugs rje'i 'phro 'thud pas/ /ngo mtshar gtam gyi snang brnyan mang du snang / /ma rig mun thibs

las ngan 'ching ba dam/ /nyon mongs shugs drag gnyen po'i go cha ngan/ /dus ngan mtha' 'dir rkyen ngan mang chen pas/ /yi mug gtam gyi gleng rgyu brjod las 'das/ /rang sems
col chung grong 'dabs g.yeng ba mang / /le los dus 'das gnyid kyi dbang du song / /bar ma'i rkyen gyis rang sems kha khrid pas/ /btang snyoms 'di yin med kyang shin tu mang
/ /de la bdag dad pa dang shes rab tu ldan pas bla ma dam pa bsten pa sogs mkhas pa dga' ba bskyed thub pa'i bya ba yang re mang bgyis/ skyid chos ngan lang ma thon pa'i
bag med kyi spyod pa gzhon pa 'dod sred can kha gcig la 'gran sdo ba 'dra ba yang mang po bdog /'di yin ci yang med pa'i phyo ma ling byis pa mno mi shes pa thal rtsed
la yengs pa 'dra ba ni bsam gyis mi khyab/ de dag gi skabs su dga' ba dang skyid po byung ba la bsams na nam langs pa'i khar nyi ma shar ba lta bu/ sdug po byung ba bsams
na snying rlung ldang la khad pa mang po myong ste/ thams cad dran pa'ang mi gda'/ dran tshad bris kyang thang chad la snag shog gzan pa las/ 'di byed ci yang med pa 'dra
zhing / dam pa gzhan tsho'i rnam thar du 'das ma 'ongs thams cad legs par bris yong gin 'dug na'ang / bdag gis na ning byas pa tsho da lo mi dran pa gda' bas/ skye ba
snga ma phan ci 'dra yin/ gang 'dra byas dran pa'i nam mi gda'/ skyes bu dam pa rnams kyi gsung las/ snga ma gang byas rang gi lus la ltos/ /zhes gsungs 'dug pas/ skye ba
snga ma des mi dge ba kham chen rang ma byas tsam zhig yin pa 'dra snyam pa ni yong gin 'dug /des mtshon ma 'ongs pa'i cha'ang / bla ma yab sras kyi

thugs rje la bsams na a tho yod la re/ nga rang gi byed lugs la bltas na dmyal ba las 'os mi gda' bas/ gang 'dra 'char ram bsam pa'i the tshom me ba 'di ga ma gtogs/ da lta
gdengs khel ba zhu rgyu mi gda'/ da lta ba rang nyid skye ba blangs pa nas brtsams te/ rang lo sum cu rtsa brgyad phan gyi gnas tshul sgro ma btags/ skur pa ma btab par/
ji ltar gnas pa'i yon tan gyi cha rnams mdo tsam yi ger 'dri ba la/ skyon ci yang med/ yod na'ang yod du chug /sprang po kha 'chal 'don pa'i kha sus kyang dgag par nus pa
ma yin no/ /e ma ho/ rgyal ba kun dngos tshar chen chos kyi rjes/ /rjes su bzung nas chos kyi rgyal srid la/ /dbang sgyur sngags 'chang dbang po mkhyen brtse'i dbang /
/dpal ldan skal pa bzang po 'di na dge /bskyed rim gdengs ka'i dbang phyug gis bskrun zhing / /rdzogs rim sprin sngon gsar pa'i phreng ba las/ /bzlas brjod 'brug sgra bye
ba'i sgra dbyangs kyis/ /dngos grub nor bu'i char rgyun 'bebs la dbang / /thog med 'khor bar zo chun 'phyan pa bzhin/ /mtho dman 'byor rgud 'dus rten ji snyed blangs/ /de
dag phal cher don med don log dang / /don chung bya ba sgrub pa kho nar song / /da lam sngon gyi smon lam thugs rje'i mthus/ /skyon med rdo rje theg pa'i dal 'byor thob/
/mtshan ldan dam pa du ma'i drin gyis bskyangs/ /bsams na bde zhing skyid pa'i tshad du snang / /de yang dngos po'i gnas tshod la rang res grul btub mi btub gtso ba ma
gtogs/ rigs brgyud bzang po yin pas dga' ba'i nges pa mi gda'

zhing / mi byed dgu byed mangs pa 'di tshos ni gong ma de dag gi zhabs 'dren pa las mi 'dug na'ang / rigs rus smos pa de kun gyi srol du 'dug pas/ de'i lugs la/ bod kyi rtsa
ba'i rus chen mi'u gdung drug tu grags pa'i nang tshan/ dang po ni 'a zhwa rje zhes bya ba rgyal phran cig yin par 'dug pa las/ je zhig nas bod kyi rgyal po'i mnga' 'og
tu song zhing / rgyal po'i dpon du'ang gyur/ bod du dam pa'i chos byed pa'i bca' khrims mdzad dus kyi nang rje la gtogs pa zhig pas/ dpon 'a zhwa rje zhes rdo ring gi yi
ge rnams su'ang thebs pa'i rgyal brgyud de las rim gyis mched nas/ bstan pa phyi dar gyi dbu la/ 'a zhwa mgo bo che'i sras/ 'a zhwa ye shes g.yung drung zhes bya bas khams
su sdom pa len du byon pa'i tshe/ dpal lha sar ye shes kyi mgon po dngos dang mjal/ khyod kyi mi brgyud chos brgyud dang bcas pa'i srung ma ngas bya/ khyod khams nas zla
gcig la 'khor ba gyis zhes gnang ba thob/ bla chen po'i mkhan bu kre'o mchog bla zhes bya ba las sdom pa der bsam bya ba thob nas gtsang du byon/ rda ni 'dres rdas/ 'o
yug mda'i ra shag /rtag gi gnas po che rnams su dge 'dun gyi sde btsugs shing / de dag las gyes pa/ ldan pa bo thang/ khor re skyi sgang / nyang ro bud mdo/ khu lung lhags
phral/ 'o yug gsal la sgang sogs sde dum gyis shing 'tsho mthu che ba'i grags pa thob/ de nas rim gyis 'a zhwa lha'i blo gros kyis lha sa la zhig gsos mdzad/ lugs gnyis
kyi khrims bcas/ rdo ong bkra shis 'od 'bar du grags pa btsugs pa da lta'ang yod par gda'/ a mes jo sras phur pa 'phel gyis rngog lo chen po blo

ldan shes rab la gser srang bcu bdun phul nas rgya gar du brdzangs/ mkhas par gyur nas mchod yon mdzad par zhal bzhes pa bzhin/ rngog lo chen po bod du byon dus/ chos 'khor
thog ma yang 'dol chung du skor/ khyad par jo bo blo gros kyis slob dpon chen po padmas byin gyis brlabs shing / nag po chen po mngon du bzhugs pa'i gnas/ nyang bar rtsis
kyi lha khang zhes bya ba'i 'gram du gnas gzhi btab pas gnas gsar du grags pa der bzhugs nas lugs gnyis kyi bya ba rgyas par mdzad pas rtsis gnas gsar pa zhes yongs su
grags/ 'a zhwa nam mkha' rgyal mtshan/ nam mkha' bzang po/ shAkya seng ge sogs kyis dpal ldan sa skya pa'i zhabs 'degs mdzad/ chos kyi rgyal po 'phags pa rin po che dang
/ ti shri kun blo sogs kyis nyang gzhung tshang ma la shes su bcug pa'i 'ja' sa/ gser gyi dam kha/ shel gyi nyi shan/ dngul gyi sgor mo lung dang bcas pa'i lung lag rtags
rim par gnang ste gnas gsar stong dpon du grags/ mdor na che gnyan btsun gsum 'dzom pa rgyal po'i brgyud pa/ mthu rtsal nus par ldan pa sngags pa'i brgyud pa/ dpal rtsal
gdong ngar dang ldan pa ge sar gyi brgyud pa zhes yon tan gyi ldog pas gsum du phye ba tshang ba zhig rim bzhin byon pa las/ stong dpon kun dga' rdo rje'i sras nang so chos
kyi rgyal po'i khab tu/ dpal ldan sa skya pa'i bdag mo rdo rje phag mo'i rnam 'phrul du grags pa dpal ldan 'dzom pa phebs pa las sras lcam sring brgyad bltams pa'i bgres
pa nang so rnam rgyal dpal bzang po ba ni/ rang gi zhang po bdag chen 'jam dbyangs chen po yab sras gsum las zab chos du ma gsan

zhing / khyad par dpal rdo rje gzhon nu'i smin grol rnams zhus te rim gnyis bzlas pa dang bcas pa lhur mdzad/ rtsis kyi mchod rten nag po nas slob dpon chen po padma'i bsnyen
phur me 'bar bzhin pa gter nas spyan drangs/ dgung lo brgyad cu gya lnga bzhes nas kyang sku yang zor che zhing / dbang po dngas pa sogs grub pa'i mtshan mas phyug pa
zhig yin la/ de'i gcung nang so mgon po rin chen pa ni/ blo rtsal dang gdong ngar bsam gyis mi khyab pas/ skyes thog de la 'gran par phod pa su yang ma byung zhing / dpal
phyag na rdo rjes rjes su bzung / nag po chen po dngos su zhal gzigs pas thal mo brdabs pa tsam gyis log par lta ba rnams tshar gcod nus pa dang / bya glag sogs kyis sems
can la gnod pa byed pa gzigs pa na dgug gzhug gi phyag rgya sngags dang bcas pa mdzad pa tsam gyis sa la lhung yong ba sogs drag sngags kyi nus pa mthar phyin pa zhig byon/
gsum pa ni/ 'jam dbyangs kun dga' blo gros zhes bya ste/ bde bar gshegs pa'i gsung rab rab 'byams kyis mgur gyi bum par phyug cing / rig pa'i lta zer gzhan gyis mi bzod
pas/ mkhas pa dang rlom pa'i skye bo phal mo che'i snying 'dar bar byed pa'i spobs pa can/ gnas gsar chos mdzad ces gangs can gyi ljongs na nyi ma ltar grags pa de nyid
yin no/ /lcam che ba ni slob dpon padmas sgrol dkar gyi sprul par lung bstan zhing sde srid chen po shar pa ba'i khab tu byon/ phyogs de'i gsang sngags rnying ma pa mtha'
dag gi dpung gnyen mdzad/ rnying ma'i rgyud 'bum bzheng pa dang / paN chen 'bum phrag gsum pa spyan drangs nas bka' brgyad kyi chos 'khor bskor ba'i bdag rkyen la brten
nas deng sang gi bar du/ sngags

'chang rnams gzhan las khyad du 'phags pa'i rgyun ma nyams pa sogs bstan pa la bya ba lhag par mdzad/ gcig ni bka' brgyud bstan pa'i bdag po 'brug pa dpon rin po che'i khab
tu bzhes nas yum bdag med ma'i rnam 'phrul du grags/ lcam gsum gyis 'jig rten bya ba sgrub par dka' la 'grub kyang don med pa/ sdug la skyid por 'dzin pa'i zir long thams
cad rgyab tu bor nas sgrub pa snying por mdzad de/ de yang gcig gis ni bdag chen rdo rje 'chang chen po'i zhabs bsten nas/ gsung ngag rin po che la thugs dam snying por
mdzad de/ sku gshegs pa'i tshe/ snyel ba sogs ci yang med par/ tshes bzhi mchod pa'i nyin/ cung zad tsog pur bzhugs 'dug pa'i tshe/ thag sgra dang bcas dbu gtsug nas thod
pa sor bzhi tsam gar song med par rgya mthong phye ba ha re las pa de lta bu'i ngang nas 'da' kha mas grub mtha' snyogs pa yin la/ gnyis kyis ni/ shar ka thog chos kyi
rgyal po bzhag bla ye shes 'bum dang / mchog gi sprul sku padma gling pa mnyes par mdzad de/ chos nyid zad pa'i snang ba mthar phyin pa'i rnal 'byor dbang mo kun dga' chos
ldan dang / ne gu chos kyi sgron ma zhes grags pa gnyis byung bar gda'/ de las nang so sku mched kyi khab tu/ dpal ldan sa skya pa'i nye gnas chen po nang so lha khang
chen mo ba'i sras mo dpal 'dzom pa zhes bya ba khab tu bzhes pa las/ bdag gi yab bltam pa yin te/ de ni byis pa'i dus nyid nas rgan pa'i skye bo

thams cad zil gyis gnon par nus pa'i blo gros dang / sgam zhing brtan la mthu stobs phun tshogs pas/ yi ge dang / rtsis dang / brtag pa rnam pa brgyad la sogs pa lugs kyi bstan
bcos thams cad bde blag tu mkhyen nas/ lugs gnyis kyi spang blang phra mo tshun chod la gzhan dring mi 'jog pa'i spobs pa thob/ mtshan lhun grub nam mkha' rdo rje tshe
brtan dpal 'byor bzang po zhes grags/ bdag chen 'jam dbyangs chen po yab sras gsum/ lce ston rin po che seng ge yab sras/ paN chen bsod nams blo gros/ mkhas grub chos
kyi dbang phyug /rje btsun rdo ring pa chen po/ mkhan chen dkon mchog tshul khrims/ rje bya btang kun dga' chos ldan/ rnal 'byor dbang phyug kun dga' rgyal mtshan/ sems dpa'
chen po bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ bdag chen thams cad mkhyen pa/ ri khrod pa nyi ma grags pa/ mthu stobs dbang phyug dkar chen kun dga' grags sogs las snga phyir chos mang
du gsan/ khyad par dgung lo bcu gsum pa la rang gi a ne 'khrul zhig kun dga' chos ldan las rdzogs pa chen po sangs rgyas mnyam sbyor gyi 'khrid bskyangs pas/ nyams gong
'phel gyi snang ba mngon du gyur/ gzhan yang zhi khro dgongs pa rang grol dang / spyod yul sogs khrid du ma gsan zhing / nyams su blangs pas sgyu lus rmi lam la rang dbang
thob ste lcang lo can la sogs pa sangs rgyas kyi zhing du mar yang byon/

rang la gnod pa'i klu gdug pa can zhig 'dul ba sogs mdzad/ skabs shig tu 'bri mtshams kyi gam pa rdzong zhes bya bar phyag na rdo rje'i bsnyen pa mdzad pa na/ mar me snum med
kyang yun ring du 'bar ba dang / res 'ga' thun mtshams kyi zhal 'phros mdzad pa na mar me mnal 'gro zhing / thugs dam la bzhugs pa na sgron mkhan med par gsal gyis 'bar
ba dang / dri bzang pos nang khengs pa sogs byung zhing / khyad par snying rje byang chub kyi sems sems can la dmigs pa'i rnam pa can bcos min du 'khrungs/ klu 'bum gnya'
khri'i gdan rnams shin tu gsal bar gzigs/ mnal lam du khyod khyung 'di la zhon nas ri rab la skor ba gsum byas pa'i mthar lcang lo can du 'gro'o zhes pa'i lung bstan gsal
bar thob/ dus de nas bzung ste lhag pa'i lhar bzung ste bsnyen sgrub kho nas dus 'da' bar mdzad/ sde srid seng ge rtse pa'i nang blon thogs shig mdzad de/ lugs gnyis
kyi zir long nyin mtshan mi phyed pa lta bu dang / bde gzar du mas g.yeng ba dpag tu med pa'i skabs su yang / thugs dam gyi rim pa rnams dang nang gtor bskang gso dang bcas
pa gcig kyang 'chag ma myong / skabs shig tu ches bsnyung ba yun ring po zhig byung ba na/ rang gi khu bo chos kyi rje las/ sgrol ma sngo ljang gi rjes gnang gsan pa'i
dus/ rje btsun ma ma rgad dwangs pa'i mdog can ri bo tsam zhig dngos su gzigs/ sku nyams bsam gyis mi khyab pa byung / de nas myur du bsnyung ba las grol/ gzhan yang dpal
kye rdo rje'i dbang /

bka' gdams lha bzhi'i khrid la sogs pa snga phyir chos du ma yang gsan/ de nas bo dong er byon te/ lugs gnyis nas phyogs de bde skyid dang ldan pa mdzad/ khyad par dus gsum
sangs rgyas thams cad kyi ngo bo rje btsun rdo rje 'chang sgo rum pa'i zhal snga nas jo nang gi gdan sar bzhugs pa spyan drangs te/ zab dgu'i gdams pa du ma snga phyir gsan/
bdag nyid 'khor 'bangs longs spyod dang bcas pa bran du phul nas/ ci mdzad legs pa dang / ci gsung tshad mar 'dzin pa'i mos gus kyis/ mi mnyes pa skad cig kyang med
par mchod cing / bsnyen bkur ba dang bsti stang du mdzad pas thugs yid gcig tu 'dres/ thun mong ma yin pa'i byin rlabs kyi 'pho ba thob/ rje btsun chen po grags pa'i sku
byin rlabs kyi gzi 'od 'bar ba dran pa tsam gyis dge legs stsol nus pa 'di nyid gtsug lag khang mchod sprin dang bcas pa bzheng ba sogs rnam dkar gyi bya ba du ma mdzad/
bdag gi bla ma rdo rje 'chang chen po de zhing gzhan du 'byon par bzhed pa'i tshe/ brgyud pa 'khor bcas dkar nag gi 'brel pa dang bcas pa srid pa kun tu rjes su 'dzin par
gsol ba btab pa bzhin zhal gyis bzhes 'dug pas/ bdag cag brgyud pa rnams la 'di gcig pu'i sku drin yang bsam pa'i ra ba las 'das gda'/ gzhan yang / rgyal dbang rdo rje 'chang
mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen pa'i zhal snga nas dang / grub thob kyi 'khor los sgyur ba sangs rgyas seng ge'i zhabs spyan drangs nas/ snying por gyur pa'i gdams pa mang
du gsan/ 'jig rten gyi mdzad pa mtha' dag thu bor gyur

pa'i sras gnyis la gtad de/ rang nyid sku mtshams lo re bzhin yang zla ba lnga tsam ma chad pa dang / dus rgyun du'ang nyi ma snga phyed yan thugs dam kho na la mnyam par 'jog
/bzhugs gral dang / zhabs 'chag sogs mdzad pa'i tshe a cang / tha na gsol ja bzhes pa'i bar la'ang phyag phreng nyed cing gsang sngags kyi bzlas brjod kho na shib bur
mdzad pas/ lhag pa'i lha'i bzlas brjod dung phyur gsum lhag pa song gda' zhing / rdo rje chos skyong rnams kyi bskang gso/ bshags pa/ mdos/ tshogs kyi 'khor lo sogs kyang
sngags pa gzhan gyi sngags kyi grangs las mang ba tsam song gda' na'ang / rlom sems dang yus ye mi mdzad mod/ grub pa'i mtshan ma sgrib ma nus par mngon du mthong ba ni/
gam pa rdzong du bzhugs pa'i dus shig nam mkha' la thog ris bcas te thog 'bab par rtsom pa na sdigs mdzub kyi rtse la bslangs te phyogs gzhan ring po zhig tu 'phangs pas/
sa der thog 'phos nas rdzong 'khor bcas la gnod pa ma byung ba de dus kyi skye bo thams cad kyis mthong ba dang / bo dong rdzong btab pa'i dus 'tshub shed yin nam/ dus
de nas gnas gsar ba gong 'phel la song gda' bas dge mtshan yin ni ma shes/ gnam lcags kyi thog chen po zhig sku gzhogs rang du babs pa na/ thag ring po na yod pa'i 'u lag
pa kha cig shi /gla ba mgo bya ba sku drung na yod pa dran med du brgyal ba sogs phal cher rod rod por gyur kyang / sku nyid lta stangs las ma g.yos par zhal 'dzum ye re
bzhugs/

sku la gnod pa lta ci smros/ na bza'i sne mo tshun skyon med du sol le/ sku gzhogs na bzhugs pa'i rje sa skya pa yab sras kyi sku nyid thugs dam rten du bzhengs pa zhig dang
/ de'i drung na yod pa'i thugs dam gtor ma rnams kyi rtse rgyan tsam yang ma zhu bar gnas pa sogs thams cad kyi mthun grub tu byung ba'i/ sku lder byin rlabs can de rnams
da lta'ang dbu rtse na bzhugs/ thugs dam gtor ma de'ang glang lo gling log chen po ma byung bar ye ma nyams pa yod pa yin/ gzhan yang rong chung gi 'phrang la byon pa'i
tshe/ sku'i thad rang la rbab lug ro tsam zhig mchong zhing byung ba la/ sku 'khor thams cad han brdal ba/ sdigs mdzub mdzad pas gyen la rgyang tsam zhig log rjes phyogs
gzhan zhig la lhungs nas ci yang ma nyes pa dang / btsag sa dkar gyi gru la byon pa'i tshe/ gtsang po'i 'jings su slebs pa na chu rba klong dang bcas te 'tshangs byung
ba na/ sdigs mdzub bstad de phaT ces gsungs pa tsam gyis chu thigs pa tsam yang ma lhungs par phyir log pa sogs thams cad kyi mthun grub tu mthong gda'/ bo dong du hor dmag
byung ba'i tshe/ nang gzan kha cig hor rgya tsam gyis 'ba' rtsi kong byas gsod la nye ba na/ rgyang ring po nas sdang mig dang sdigs mdzub mdzad de shA sa na bzla bar
mdzad pas hor de dag glo bur du bros shing 'khyams song nas/ rang phyogs la gnod pa ma byung ba ni bdag nyid kyis mngon sum du mthong / gzhan yang rdo rje chos skyong rnams
la bsnyen sgrub dang bskang bshags rtsal du bton pas/ gzhung nas bshad pa'i rtags rab 'bring thams cad mngon du gyur/ mngon sum du

rtag par gzigs kyi yod gda' bas/ 'phrin 'chol gyi skabs 'gar/ gtso bo rnams cha lugs 'di lta bus rnam 'gyur 'di 'dra ston gyi 'dug gsung pa dang mis bsreg mkhan med par spos
phor stong pa'i nang nas tshil chen gyi du ba 'phyur ba dang / dgun grang sgang gi sman rag gtor ma thams cad khol zhing dri ro phun sum tshogs pa 'byung ba dang / sku
gcig pus dbyangs mdzad kyang nye 'khor nas nyan pa na dbyangs kyi ram bu 'degs mkhan kha yar gyi skad thams cad kyis mthun grub tu thos pa ni shas cher 'byung / bsgral ba'i
zhing zhig la mngon spyod kyi las mdzad de dgug gzhug mdzad pa na bla'i gzugs zhum bu 'dra ba zhig yud kyis thim ma thag lingga 'dar khri li li 'dar byung ba der 'khod
pa kun gyis mthong ba dang / drag po'i gtor ma zhig 'phen par mdzad de/ gtor ma phyir khyer nas bskul mdzad pa na gtor ma gnod kyi nang du khru re tsam lan gsum 'phar ba
dang / mdos gtor gyi gseb nas me chen po bud nas dgra phyogs su 'gro ba sogs thun mong gi grub pa'i mtshan ma mang du yod de thams cad bri bar ma nus/ mnal lam du rje btsun
ti phu pa dang mjal nas sku tshe'i tshad lung bstan pa dang / gzhu mgo thon gyi sgar na bzhugs pa'i tshe/ nang gcig mdun gyi nam mkhar thig le mthing kha 'od kha dog
lngas bskor ba mtheb long tsam zhig gi dbus na/ ma 'dres la yongs su rdzogs pa'i rgyal ba rdo rje 'chang gi sku rgyan dang bcas pa phyi nang sgrib thogs med

pa zhig gsal bar gzigs te 'di ni/ dpal dus kyi 'khor lo'i rgyud 'grel ba rnams dang / rang bzhin rdzogs pa chen po'i rgyud dang man ngag la mkhas pa'i skye bos ltas na ni bsam
gyis mi khyab pa'i lam rtags su gda'/ kha phyir ltas la goms pa'i mkhas grub mang po ni 'khrul snang dag bya yin los gsung ngam snyam/ mdor na de la sogs pa mchog gi
lam rtags du ma zhig mngon du gyur mod/ rang nyid kyang tha mal pa kho na'i tshul 'dzin/ mi rnams kyang ya bo nam mkha' sogs mtshan gyi 'bod phyogs mang po dang bcas dam
pa dang lta ci/ mi gzhung ma'i mthong yang mi byed pa de ga'i ngang la sbas pa'i rnal 'byor gyi brtul zhugs kyis nang gi sa lam bgrod pa la gtso bor mdzad pa zhig gda'/ de
ltar phyi ltar sde pa dpon po'i tshul 'dzin mod/ deng sang gi nang so rnam pa ru nga la dpa' nus zhan pa 'di rnams dang ye mi 'dra ba/ mna' dam tshig /khrel ngo tsha/ gzhung
phyi thag gtso bor mdzad nas/ zan gang chang gcig dang lta ci/ byus kyi khe chen po bsam gyis mi khyab pa'ang khyad du bsad nas mdung gcig 'dzin kho na ma gtogs/ khye
cung zad 'ong 'ong 'dra na dgra mi sha bo'ang pang du blangs nas tsam pag skyong / gus cung zad 'ong 'ong 'dra na pha yang rgyab tu shugs nas rdo char 'bebs/ nyi ma gang
shar gyi cam pa lha mo la dgos pa'i dbang du ming btags pa'i/ khe las gtam ngan thu ba/ mi brgyud kyi bsegs brdar du 'gro ba 'di 'dra dang / dgos med la 'ur shang sa 'tshong
/ gtugs

na wa gros mgo gar 'jug tshang brlag pa 'di 'dra min par/thog mar zhi bas 'pham blangs/ gal te des mi 'dul na zlog tu med pa'i dpa' nus kyis phas rgol de stobs che chung la
ye ma ltos par slar mi skye ba'i chos can du thal bar stong pa sogs 'jig rten gyi phyi mo nyan nges kho na mdzad/ chos phyogs nas/ deng sang gi bla gum spra cal kha cig
dang mi 'dra bar/ spyir chos dang gang zag thams cad la dag snang phyogs med du mnga' bas/ rang rang gi lugs kyi bstan dang bstan 'dzin thams cad la gus pa dang bsti stang
du mdzad mod/ rang gi rtsa ba'i grub mtha' rje btsun sa skya pa'i bstan pa/ de las kyang snying por gyur pa bdag chen rdo rje 'chang yab sras las ston dang bstan pa gzhan
nas mi 'tshol/ ja sig re tsam dang / rta drel re tsam la rtsa ba'i grub mtha' dang bla ma thams cad 'tshong ba'i thugs mnal lam du'ang mi mnga' ba sogs/ chos dang 'jig
rten gnyis ka nas dpe thub pa'i legs tshogs kho nas dus 'da' ba'i ngang nas/ dgung lo drug cu rtsa brgyad bzhes pa'i chu pho khyi'i lo khrums can gyi zla ba'i tshes bcu
la zab mo'i rnal 'byor las ma g.yos bzhin du/ thog ma'i lung bstan ltar na/ sku skye ba gsum brgyud dgos par snang mod/ de'i rjes su lam zab mo du ma zhig gi nus pas/ skye
ba de nyid kyis byang phyogs rgyal ba'i zhing du 'byon pa'i ltas ngo mtshar ba bsam gyis mi khyab pa dang / mkha' 'gro chos skyong gi bsu ba mngon sum du

bdag cag rnams kyis mthong ba dang ma mthong ba du ma dang bcas te zhi bar gshegs pa'i tshul bstan rin thang med pa'i rin po che'i phung po sku gdung de nyid bdag ni/ bsod
nams dman pas phyag phyi ma thub/ chos lung nas mkhan rin po ches mchod sprin rgya mtshos bstabs te zhugs la zhen pa'i tshe me'i tshogs kyis sku la reg par ma nus par re
zhig na thugs ka'i thad nas me rang 'bar te yud kyis zhugs bzhes shing / gdung thams cad ring bsrel gyi phung por gyur/ ches dkar ba'i sa la sku gdung cung zad bsres nas
dpal phyag na rdo rje'i sku khri khrag mang po btab pa thams cad kyang rang bzhin gyis baiDUrya sngon po'i mdog lta bur 'gyur ba sogs/ gzu bor gnas pa thams cad mi phyed
pa'i dad pa la 'god par mdzad pa'i ltas du ma zhig /skye bo mang po'i mthun grub tu byung ba yin no/ /des na rang cag 'di'i rigs su skyes pa rnams/ dus kyis ma khyogs pa
la khag btang / sku yon che bar grags pa mang po'i lad mo byas/ mi chos kyi mna' dang / lha chos kyi dam tshig la rtsi 'jog med par/ dgos pa'i dbang yin pas skyon med ces
gang ngan la ngo sor 'khyer ba de 'dra rmi lam du yang mi bya bar/ pha rgan des ji ltar mdzad pa'i rjes su zhugs nas/ chos dang 'jig rten zung 'jug tu khrig khrig byas/
'di phyi gnyis ka yod pa re mi byed ka med yin pas/ nor su che dang stong 'ur su che la bla ma mi re/ rta drel dang grub mtha' mi brje/ lugs gnyis nas rang lugs zin nges
re dgos so zhes/ phyis 'byung

ba'i rigs kyi tsha bo rnams la btsun rgan 'ba' su ba des kha chems su bzhag pa yin no/ /yid bzhin nor bus gtams pa'i chu gter gyi/ /kha dog mthong bas skrag pa'i rdar ma rnams/
/phyogs de'i gtam yang bdag gir mi byed na/ /rin chen bgo skal thob pa'i skal ba ci/ /ltar snang 'jig rten spyod par mthong ba yis/ /yun ring bsten kyang pad mtsho'i
sbal pa bzhin/ /skal dman phal gyis dam par ma mthong na/ /rgyus med skye bo rnams la smos ci dgos/ /kha cig gzhan zer tsam la tshad mar 'dzin/ /la la sdang bar zhugs pas
yid dbang 'khrugs/ /phal chen yon tan skyon gyi dbye 'byed bral/ /des na dam pa'i yon tan mthong ba nyung / /kha cig de la 'di 'dra ma byung bas/ /khyed la ci 'byung des
na brdzun yin snyam/ /sems yod skye bo phal la mi 'byung ba/ /de phyir dam pa'i yon tan mchog tu grub/ /a ho 'jig rten phun tshogs mtha' dag la/ /rol bzhin 'jig rten spyod
las 'da' 'gyur ba/ /'jig rten 'jig rten 'das pa'i phun tshogs la/ /rol khyod 'jig rten 'di par phal gyis mthong / /bdag ni dus 'di nas bzung byang chub bar/ /bdag nyid
che khyod zhabs rdul bsten bgyid na/ /bdag dang bdag gir byas pa'i spun rnams kyang / /bdag lta'i g.yul las rgyal bar mdzad du gsol/ /de ltar bdag gi pha rgan de bltams
nas ring po ma lon pa na yum de nyid chos kyi dbyings su thim pa la brten nas/ gtsang tshong 'dus mgur mo'i khri dpon lugs gnyis kyi

dbang phyug tu gyur pa de'i lcam sring ma byang sems bu khrid mar grags pa khab tu bzhes pa'i sras kyi thu bo nam mkha' rgyal ba 'jig rten snying po med pa'i rang zhal gzigs
nas/ rje btsun lce ston paN chen las dge bsnyen mdzad/ phyis su mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen pa'i zhabs drung du rab tu byung zhing mtshan rig 'dzin rdo rje bdud 'dul du
grags ba de'ang thugs rab che zhing thugs gsal ba/ gong du smos pa'i dam pa de dag phal cher dang / sprul sku shAkya bzang po/ rig 'dzin chen po tshe bdag rnam rgyal/ gnubs
chen rin chen dpal bzang / rje btsun chos kyi rgyal po mnga' ris rig 'dzin chen po/ rje kun bzang mthu stobs/ grub mchog mchog legs rdo rje/ bla ma rin po che/ dge slong
chen po sogs dam pa du ma'i zhabs la gtugs/ spyir sa kar rnying gsum du grags pa'i gdams pa du ma gsan/ khyad par gsang sngags snga 'gyur gyi chos mang du gsan zhing
sbyangs/ gtso bor mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen pa'i drung du thugs sgrub mthing kha'i dbang lung rdzogs par gsan cing / dus dang rgyun gyi bsnyen pa bsam gyis mi khyab pa
mdzad cing / dpal 'khor lo sdom pa gshed dmar lha lnga/ rdo rje gzhon nu sa lugs/ gu ru drag dmar/ thugs sgrub yang snying 'dus pa/ phyag rdor mdo lugs/ phyag rdor 'khor
can/ 'chi med 'od snang / sgrol dkar sogs yi dam du ma'i bskyed rdzogs bzlas par bcas pa dang / mkha' 'gro chos skyong rnams la'ang gtor bsngos tshar gnyis ma sogs rgyun

dang dus khyad par ba'i mchod gtor mang du mdzad/ byin rlabs kyi mtshan ma mngon gyur ba bsam gyis mi khyab pa mnga'/ mthar dgung lo don gnyis bzhes pa na snyung ba'i rnam
pa tsam yang med par/ mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen pa spyan drangs nas mnyes mnyes kyi zhal ta mang po zhus/ rdzong dgos thams cad ni brdzangs tshar/ 'tshog 'os thams cad
ni 'tshogs/ bla ma 'di lta bu sngas mgor phebs/ sems la 'phreng dgos pa dang / yid theng pa gcig kyang med/ nga las skyid pa su yod ces dang / bar do'i 'phrang la yang hU~M
sgra di ri ba 'di ga la 'gro ba yin gsung pa sogs dga' spro dang bcas bzhin du tshes brgyad kyi tho rangs zhi bar gshegs shing / dbu thod sor bzhi tsam gsal por 'phags/
'ja' 'od dang me tog gi char la sogs pas rtog ge pa rgan po mngon pa'i nga rgyal can kha cig kyang mi phyed pa'i dad pa la 'god pa sogs ngo mtshar ba'i ltas du ma zhig
bstan nas/ nub phyogs ayon chos kyi pho brang padma 'od kyi gzhal yas chen por byon pa'i ltas du ma zhig byung ba yin no/ /ayon chos kyi rgyal po'i sku drin gyis/ /ji ltar
byas kyang bde ba yin no zhes/ /slu med gtam gyis gad brgyangs lan grangs brgyar/ /bsgrags nas ayon sprul sku'i zhing du byon/ /gsar rnying chos la zab khyad 'ga' med kyang
/ /gsar 'grog chos pas rnying mar smod byed pa'i/ /gsar mar rlom pa'i khengs ldan mang po zhig /gsar du dad gus ba spu langs pa mthong / /dam pa khyed gnyis

lugs gnyis dpal 'byor gyis/ /dgyes bzhin dag pa'i zhing du byon lags mod/ /shul du lus pa'i bu brgyud 'di rnams la'ang / /da dung thugs rje'i spyan rgyang gzigs su gsol/ /de
lta bu'i sku mched gnyis kyi khab tu se ston dpal chen 'bum dang nyi ma bzang po sogs yang phur gshin rje dang bcas pa'i zhal gzigs shing / dam can bran bzhin du 'khor
ba'i sngags 'chang zam ma chad par byon pa'i gdung brgyud 'dar chos rdzong pa zhes grags pa'i sa skyong dbang po/ dpal ldan sa skya pa'i dpon don yod rnam rgyal zhes bya
ba'i sras mo tshe brtan bu 'dren zhes bya ba bud med kyi skyon brgyad spangs shing / yon tan thams cad kyis phyug pa/ phongs pa dang sdug bsngal ba dang mgon med pa thams
cad kyi mar gyur pa/ skye bo rnams kyi ma 'dres pa'i mdza' shes/ byis pa'i dus nas bdag chen rdo rje 'chang chen po'i zhal snga nas dang / zur tshe bdag chen shAkya gshin
rje/ 'jims chen kun dga' snying po/ paN chen shAkya mchog ldan sogs dam pa du ma bsten nas chos tshul du ma thob cing / khyad par rje btsun rdo rje 'chang sgo rum pa'i
zhabs la mi phyed pa'i dad pa mnga' bas ci mdzad de phyogs su gtong ba/ rje btsun lce ston paN chen/ mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen pa/ 'khrul zhig kun dga' chos ldan rnams
las gdams pa'i snying po thob nas thugs nyams su bzhes/ dpal gur gyi mgon po'i yi ge bdun pa sa ya gsum song zhing rjes su bzung ba'i mtshan ma yang thob/ nA ro mkha' spyod
kyi thugs dam chag med du mdzad pas mnal

lam du rdo rje rnal 'byor ma zhal gnyis ma gser btso ma'i mdog lta bu gzigs shing / phag skad kyi ngur sgras sa be re re byed pa'ang gsan pa sogs yon tan du mas mdzes pa de
nyid las/ bdag cag ming sring kha yar skyes 'dug na'ang phan thogs pa bdag cag lnga byung ba las/ bdag yab dgung lo zhe gcig bzhes pa shing pho spre'u'i lo/ zla ba bzhi
pa'i yar ngo nyi ma me bzhi'i 'grub sbyor ram gza' da lta ba'i spen pa'i phung po me bzhis bsregs pa'i 'chi sbyor yod pa'i nyi ma rtse shar la lte bas chos gos bzhin du dkris/
a zhes bya ba'i skad drag po 'don bzhin du btsas 'dug /de'i tshe la las btsan gyi zhags pa thebs pa yin mi 'tsho zer ba sogs chal chol mang po lab 'dug na'ang / gso
ba rig pa'i pha rol du son pa'i 'tsho byed rin chen pa zhes bya ba sku drung na bzhugs pa de na re/ 'di'i lte ba'i dkri tshul la dpyad na/ nges par bstan pa la phan pa'i
dge bshes zhig 'byung zhing / rgyud las/ de 'dra gso sla mi nor bkra shis byed/ /ces 'byung bas/ khab tu bzhugs kyang gzhan dang mi 'dra ba zhig 'byung zhes lung bstan de'i
tshe/ sngar bu mo tsam dang ci yang skye ma myong ba'i bud med mang po zhig la bu khye'u kho na btsa' ba sogs bsod nams yod yod 'dra mo ni byung nges su gda'/ bu chung
de yang sha'i mdangs dkar ba/ dpral ba'i dbyes che ba/ sna'i gzengs mtho zhing smin ma 'brel ba/ sme ba dkar po'i ga sha yod tsam byas pa zhig 'dug ces thos/ btsas ston

rgya cher byas te/ rje btsun rdo rje 'chang chen po jo nang na bzhugs pa la thugs dam skyabs 'og dang ming zhu bar btang bas/ ming mgon po bsod nams mchog ldan zhes pa gnang
'dug /dus gsum sgrib med gzigs pa'i mgon po des/ /bsod nams dbang gis mi lus legs thob cing / /mchog gyur lam bzang sgom pa'i skal ldan du/ /gsal bar gzigs nas ming 'di
btags pa 'dra/ /gang ltar gso ba sla ba'i tshad thub pas lha mchod 'dre rdungs ye ma dgos shing skyed che la yid 'dzin pa zhig yod gsung / bdag lus la 'khril tsam nas yum
nyid sha'i dri tshor ba na'ang mi bzod pa skye ba byung la/ bdag rang byis pa'i dus sha kha la mi khyer ba zhig yod 'dug /mis khrid nas 'gro shes tsam gyi dus na nyi tshod
cig la thugs dam gyi khungs re rtag par byed kyi yod 'dug pas/ thengs shig zhal ngo rnams bya rgod gshongs mjal bar bo dong nas zhabs thang du phebs pa na/ nyi ma la
bltas te lam kha de nyid du tsog gis bsdad de ji tsam bgyis kyang ma langs par de ma grol ring zhal ngo thams cad lam kha der cham me bzhugs dgos pa byung 'dug /rtsed mo'i
gnas skabs thams cad na yang dgon pa 'debs pa dang / khri mthon po la 'dug ste chos 'chad pa dang / nag po chen po'i 'dug stangs byas nga mgon po yin zer nyi ma phyed re
tsam de ga la sdod/ za ran pa na'ang gtor gsos gyis zer phye mar dang bu ram sogs khar 'jug dgos pa dang / res 'ga' nyams dbyangs dang / nga'i smon lam

drang po yin zer zhing gar mang po byed/ res rten gsum gyi drung du mchod pa chung chung mang po bshams nas/ yon chab 'di ni sngo la dwangs/ /sngo la dwangs pa bzhes su gsol/
/zhal zas 'di ni rtse mo snyung / /rtse snyung chen po bzhes su gsol/ /zhes sogs mchod phreng mang po brtsams shing gyer bar byed kyi tha mal pa'i spyod pa byed pa cung
zad kyang mi dran no zhes/ nga rang gi ma ma rgan mo dang / a ma rgyal la sogs de dus kyi drung 'khor thams cad mgrin gcig tu sgrog pa thos/ bdag gis lo gcig tsam 'gro
ba na rje btsun rdo rje 'chang chen po las dpal kye rdo rje'i rgyu dus kyi dbang gi chu bo ma nub par thob 'dug go /rigs brgya'i khyab bdag rdo rje 'chang dbang des/ /snod
ldan bu de dkyil 'khor rnam bzhi la/ /'khrul med dbang bzhis sku bzhi'i sa bon btab/ /phung khams dang po dbang gis smin par byas/ /gzhan yang tshe dpag med/ phyag na rdo
rje uu tsarya/ gur gyi mgon po pho rkyang dang / lcam dral sogs rjes su gnang ba mang po zhig thob par snang / smra shes tsam gyi dus bdag gi bla ma rdo rje 'chang chen
po de jo nang nas spyan drangs/ ayon gyi slob dpon chen po padma'i thugs sgrub kyi dbang rgyas pa zhig thob 'dug pa phyis su'ang dbang de gsal po dran gyin 'dug na'ang
/ bka' gter gang yin ma shes par rin po che la zhus pas/ de dran gyi gda' 'am dgod dro/ gu ru chos dbang gi gter ma thugs sgrub gsang ba 'dus pa'i dbang yin gsung / gzhan
yang tshe rta

sogs mang po thob gda' ste gam la zin pa ni mi gda'/ rje bla ma jo nang la thegs pa na phyags phyir 'gro ba yin zer/ kha khrid phyogs ji tsam byas na'ang ma nyan par dam pa
de'i na bza' la 'chang nas ngu zhing / pha ma dang spun zla la'ang 'phreng sems med pa'i gdung shugs chen po byas pa la brten nas phyag sgam sogs sku chas kha cig bzhag
/rin po che bzhugs rgyu ba'i khungs byas pas thub tsam byung / dang mo khyed la de 'dra'i dad shugs shig bdog ste/ zhes rje bla ma nyid kyi gsung las thos te/ dam pa 'dis
ma rungs pa bdag skye ba du mar drin gyis bskyangs pa'i bag chags brtas pa zhig yin nam snyam/ mkha' lding dbang po'i rjes su dga' ma bzhin/ /dam pa'i zhabs phyir 'brang
ba'i gdung shugs 'di/ /sngon gyi las dkar rdo rje'i mdud pa yis/ /nyam chung bdag yid dam du bcings par nges/ /rang gi a ne 'khrul zhig kun dga'i zhabs las/ sprul sku ratna
gling pa'i gter chos thugs sgrub yang snying 'dus pa'i sgrub dbang / tshe sgrub gsang ba 'dus pa'i dbang / zhi khro dgongs pa rang grol gyi dbang rnams ma'i phang nas
zhus pa yin gsung / yab grub pa'i dbang po sku mched las kyang nag po chen po'i gtor dbang yang nas yang du thob/ de dag gtor sgrub mdzad pa'i nye 'khor na yod dus sngags
pa gos lcags nag gser ma'i phod ka gyon pa zhwa theb ban phur dang bcas pa mtho gang tsam mchod bshoms kyi ting so so'i steng na 'cham ral byed pa dngos su mthong ste/

nged rang gi rigs brgyud ma 'khrul ba rnams la byis pa'i dus mgon po'i rnam 'phrul rgyun par mthong ba de yong nges su 'dug go grub dbang ye shes g.yung drung des/ /grub pa
brnyes pa'i dge mtshan las/ /grub pa'i rigs brgyud ma 'khrul bas/ /grub rtags byis pa nyid nas thob/ /nga rang dran tsam gyi dus bo dong rdzong du rje btsun rdo rje 'chang
las bir bsrung thun mong ba thob/ de'i tshe rnal 'byor dbang phyug gi rnam thar zhib tu gsung pa thos pas phal cher gam la zin/ nyal ba'i sgang la/ sdigs mdzub bstan pas
ganggA gyen la ldog /phyag 'tshal mdzad pas dbang phyug tshal par gas/ /thal mo brdabs pas rtse gsum thal bar song / /sngo nag 'bar pa khyed la gsol ba 'debs/ /zer ba'i
bstod pa brtsams pa dang / yang / dpal ldan bla ma'i thugs kyi sras/ /yi dam lha yis rjes su bzungs/ /dam can rgya mtsho bran du 'khol/ /dpal ldan bla ma la phyag 'tshal/
/zer rin po che la bstod pa brtsams pa dran zhing da lta yang ma brjed par 'dug /byis pa'i dus snying rje shin tu che bas sems can bsad pa dang bzung ba thos tsa na sems
la mi bzod pa ci yang 'byung zhing ngu ba kho na byed/ bkra shis sgang na yum gyi zla la yod pa'i tshe gzhu mkhan hor phrug zer ba zhig btson khang nas bros pa btson rdzi
rnams kyis bsad nas mgo bo khyer 'gro'i 'dug zer ba thos pas sdug bsngal bsam gyis mi khyab pa byung / lto bza' ba yang mi dran

par ngus pa sogs gsal po dran zhing / de dus sems can la gnod pa ye mi nus pa'i snying rje can zhig bdog na'ang / da ni drung 'jol mo bas 'brug pa la zhus pa bzhin/ mig la
thal ba btab kyang / snying rje'i sgo nas mchi ma 'chor ba'i na ma bsangs pa zhig byung gda' ba dkor gyi byin rlabs yin nam snyam/ mngal grib g.ya' dang bral ba'i me long
la/ /sngon gyi las dkar gzugs brnyan 'char bzhin pa/ /dkor zas snum gyis byugs pa'i de ma thag /mog por gyur 'di bsams shing yi re mug /sbyangs stobs yon tan gsar 'phel
med kyang sla'i/ /skyes stobs yon tan de rnams ma 'gribs na/ /bla ma'i gzugs brnyan tsam 'di min nges shig /'byung mod da ni mes tshig shing bzhin no/ /byis pa'i dus nas
gos rgyan mchor po gang mthong rung ngas 'di 'dra gyon du mi nyan snyam pa lhan skyes su 'char ba nas dus thams cad du gos dmar ser gang 'os ring gzugs ma kho na gyon/ skra
yang sor gsum las ring ba bzhag pa mi dran/ mi tshos kyang sde pa chos rje zer/ nga rang yang khur bzhes byed/ skabs shig na bo dong rdzong gi tshoms chen gyi ldebs bris
mdzad kyi 'dug pa'i lam 'bras brgyud pa'i rje bla ma rdo rje 'chang gi sku 'dra'i drung du nga rang rab byung gi gzugs maNDal 'bul ba zhig 'dri ru bcug /de'i mkhris tsam
du bu rdzi a skyabs kyang btsun pa lhung bzed thogs pa zhig tu 'dri ba dang / jo nang kun mkhyen chen po'i zhing bkod kyi bsrubs shig na brag phug gcig tu nga rang rab
byung bsam gtan la rtse gcig tu 'dug pa'i rnam

pa can sogs ri mo ba rnams la zhu ba phul nas bris/ zla bo rnams la'ang nga btsun pa byed/ khyed rang tsho yang chos byas pa drag kho na labs pa dran zhing 'dug /lo brgyad
lon pa'i dbyar dpal ldan theg mchog pho brang zhes bya ba'i gtsug lag khang gi logs bris kyi zhal bkod la 'jam pa'i dbyangs mnga' ris bla chen phebs 'dug pas/ rang gzhin
gyi dga' spro dang mos gus byung nas sku mdun du yang yang phyin/ gang srus sogs gang yod kyi phud nas phul/ lha khang der bris pa'i bla ma yi dam chos skyong thams cad kyi
mtshan saM skr-i ta'i skad du bslabs/ gzhan yang 'phral gyi zla bo'i ming / spyad dngos yo byad phal cher rgya skad du shes pas shin tu thugs gtsigs che bar mdzad/ de'i
skabs shig tu rje btsun rdo rje 'chang chen po dpal ldan lcang lo can na bzhugs pa'i drung du phyin pas/ sde pa mgon po pa mgyogs po btsun pa byed rgyu yin/ yang na shes
bya rab 'byams la mkhyen pa'i spyan mnga' ba'i mkhas pa chen po zhig bya/ yang na tshe dang sgrub pa mnyams te phug sgo phye ba dang 'phur thub pa mnyam po zhig byed dgos/
gang byed dam gsung ba na snying la brjod du med pa'i spro dga' bsam gyis mi khyab pa zhig skyes/ bdag gsung ba de gnyis gang byed lags zhus pas/ yang yang bzhad cing

ma thag /ring nas goms pa'i

yid kyi bung ba de/ /lhan skyes spro ba'i bro gar ci yang rtsen/ /khyod kyis byis pa'i dus su gang bsams pa'i/ /khur de phyed tsam khyer na'ang mkhas grub cig /'byung la the
tshom med mod da lta'i bar/ /don med las 'di gang gi skyon yin kwa ye/ /kwa ye sems la sems kyi gros thob dang / /dang po'i dus nas yid la smon pa gang / /gang de don med
gyur na ma legs kyi/ /gyi nar ma 'dug blo skyed mi 'don nam/ /rang lo brgyad lon pa lcags mo yos kyi lo ston zla 'bring po 'bru bcud thams cad phun sum tshogs pa'i dus
bkra shis kyi gtsug lag khang dpal ldan theg pa mchog gi pho brang du mkhan po dus gsum rgyal ba thams cad kyi bdag nyid don gyi slad du mtshan nas smos te kun dga' legs
pa'i zhal snga nas/ gtsug phud 'breg pa'i dge slong gnas brtan mkhas pa nam mkha' gzi brjid/ 'dul ba 'dzin pa nam mkha' don grub sogs dad pa'i dge 'dun lnga'i dbus su rab
tu byung ba'i sdom pa blangs/ ming mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po zhes btags/ dga' ston rgya cher bsgrubs te/ shAkya'i sras kyi khongs
su chud pas snying la sim pa ci yang thob par gyur to/ /me dang dug dang sgram chen sbrul gyis 'khrigs pa'i nags na rtse ba bzhin/ /rnam mang skyon brgyas nye bar 'khyud
pa'i khyim gyi dga' ba spangs nas 'dir/ /yid 'phrog ga bur gzegs mas bran pa'i ha ri'i nags klung 'jam po dang mtshungs pa/ /thar pa'i them skas so so thar zhes ming tsam
gyis kyang snying la sim pa ster de bdag

gis thob/ /kwa ye 'di na kham phor dum bur ni/ /thal med chu tsam 'thung bzhin sdug bsngal brgyas/ /rab gtses dbul po'i khyim yang btang dka' na/ /ches mtho'i rgyal srid spong
ba e ma mtshar/ /gzugs dang lang tsho blo gros phun tshogs shing / /'khor dang longs spyod mnga' thang bsam yas kyang / /bzhi mdo'i rtswa bzhin ring du dor nas ni/ /shAkya'i
sras de'i rjes su dad pas zhugs/ /grogs dag gang du btang dka' rgyal po'i khyim gyi 'byor pa phun tshogs mi zad de dang ni/ /mkhur tshos dmar snum nu ma'i khur gyis
dub pa'i mdzes ma gser gyi rna cha g.yo ba dang / /ru dar sprin gyis nam mkha' sgrib byed dpa' bo'i dpung bcas rgyal srid mchil ma ltar spangs nas/ /ngur smrig gos gyon
nyam chung gyi nar rgyu ba 'di ni bdag gi legs tshogs dang po yin/ /de nas rje btsun rdo rje 'chang chen po dpal bo dong e'i bla brang dkar por bzhugs pa'i phyags phyir
bsnyen nas/ gnas kyi slob dpon 'jam pa'i dbyangs mnga' ris bla chen la zhus te bslab sbyangs byed pa'i khungs byas/ der sleb nas ring po ma lon pa na rmi lam du nga rang
gi a ma yin snyam pa'i bud med cig gis stod thung sngo khra zhig bkab/ spos shin tu dri zhim pa brgya khres mang po bcug pa'i sgam zhig dang / thod pa nas smug pos phyur
bur gang ba zhig byin/ tshigs bcad cig 'don gyi 'dug pa yid la ma zin/ rmi lam de zhabs drung du zhus pas bo dong gi lha mo 'di mnyes pa'i mtshan ma yin

nam snyam/ spos de la ltas na tshul khrims gtsang sing ba a tho ba zhig yong ba yin nam gsung / rgya bod kyi klog thams cad zla ba gcig la legs par shes mod/ bla chen sku drin
can des khyod bla ma byed pa la klog phyed tsam gyis mi chog gsungs nas/ dkon mchog brtsegs pa dum pa bcu drug pa tshang ba tshar gcig dang / sngags 'bum par ma rgyal
rtse na bzhugs pa de tshar kha yar 'don du bcug pas deng sang gang klog kyang ngal dub med tsam 'di byung ba lags/ rje btsun birWa pa nas rdo rje 'chang yan gyi sku bstod
rnams dang / mtshan brjod/ bzang spyod/ sgrol ma/ sher snying / ltung bshags/ byams smon sogs nyer mkho'i chos spyod thams cad gsung spor mdzad nas bslabs pas tshegs med
par shes/ yi ge ni bslab pa'i khung byas byang shing la yig 'phreng gcig bris/ de nas ham pa byas bris pa'i rtsal yig ma gtogs/ rgya bod kyi yi ge gang shes 'di gcig kyang
bslabs pa mi bdog /klog kyang dbu med 'di zhor la shes pa yin/ ri mo'ang cha tshang ni mi shes/ gzhan bris sku shob be ba nyan nges 'di yang rang rdol la shes pa lags
shing / snyan ngag sgra don gyi rgyan gang brtsams kyang brtsam stan la ma ltos par bris tshad snyan ngag du yong ba'i gu yangs po 'di rang shes kho na lags/ de'i skabs
shig srod la phyir khams gseng du phyin pas/ kha sang rmi lam du byung ba'i bud med des mda' dar zhig dang / tshe bum zhig khyer gar stabs byed cing slebs byung ba la/ zla
bo

zhig der yongs ma thag de 'ja' yal ba ltar song nas bred zhum me ba zhig byung drung du zhus pas/ lha mo des tshe'i dngos grub cig ster ba yin shas 'dug na'ang cung zad bar
chad du song 'dug pas tshe sgrub cig gyis gsungs nas/ lo tshes pa'i zla ba dang po la grub rgyal lugs kyi tshe dpag med kyi sgo nas a mA ra Ni 'bum phrag bcu bgrangs/ rmi
ltas 'di yin ni gang yang ma byung / dngos su 'od 'khyug pa dang / gzugs 'di yin med pa'i za nge zi nge mang po mthong zhing de la bred snang yod pa de 'dra mang po byung
nas zhus pas/ khro bo'i dbang po mi g.yo ba dkar po'i rjes gnang zhig mdzad nas/ gnyid sad ma thag sngags brgya rtsa re zlos/ nges par bar chad kyis mi tshugs gsung ba
bzhin rjes gnang thob pa nas bar chad de rnams gang yang ma byung / de nas bzung ste mi g.yo ba dkar po/ phyag rdor dkar po/ sna tshogs yum/ ri khrod lo ma can/ 'jam dpal
nag po rnams la nyin re bzhin mngon rtogs bzlas pa brgya rtsa la nyung mtha' byas pa re chag med byed kyi yod na'ang dus phyis gzhan 'dras kha dog khyer song / dgongs re

gi gzungs smon lam dang bcas pa byed dgos kyi yod pa rta nag la phyin pas rang grol du song ba yin no/ /de'i skabs shig mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen pa'i zhal snga nas 'khor
nyung shas dang bcas dbus nas gtsang la phebs/

dang / bla ma'i dga' ba la bsam pa dung dung ba byung / rje 'dar phyogs la phebs khar bdag yod sar thol gyis byon byung nas gos chen lcags nag kha do pa zhig dang / stong
skud dmar po zhig gnang / 'di la phyag 'phreng thag pa bzhin mdzod/ gos chen 'di la bris sku lta bu mdzad dam gang na'ang mi la ma gnang bar phyag tshags mdzod/ rten
'brel cig yod do gsung zhing zhal mdzum mang po mdzad kyi 'dug pa de dus ni dga' ba la bsam pa tsam las ma byung / da bsams na mgon po che chung 'di rnams thob pa'i rten

bu'ang / /snyan brgyud gdams pa'i snod du'ang rung bar dgongs/ /dam pa'i zhal bzhes rdo yi ri mo bzhin/ /'gyur med bden pas thugs la btags na yang / /rang gis gsol ba
btab pa'ang mi dran pa/ /a ho las nyon dbang gis skyes pas lan/ /bla ma de'i phyags phyi dang / gzhan yang phyogs kyi zhu ba po mang po'i zhor la gsung gi bdud rtsi du ma

khyod gsang sngags rgya mtsho lta bu'i mthar son pa zhig byed dgos/ de'ang chung dus nas bslabs pa rang khye che ba yin/ thog mar tshe'i rten 'brel yin pas 'di bzhin gyis gsung
/ dpal ldan sa skya pa'i thugs dam/ dgung lo brgya nyi shu bzhugs pa'i grub chen dze tA ris bkral ba'i tshe dpag med lha dgu'i dbang gnang nas/ mkhas pa dpal gyi yi
ge'i steng nas phyag khrid kyang zhib par mdzad de/ thog mar snying po nye snying bzhi 'bum re'i bsnyen pa byas rjes sgrub mchod bdag 'jug dang bcas pa brgya tshar gcig btang
/ de nas dpal kye rdo rje man ngag lugs kyi mngon dkyil sems dpa' chen pos mdzad pa la lung bshad phyag khrid dang bcas pa gnang ste ngag thog nas sgrub mchod bdag 'jug

ba nga'i

mthu min nam ste/ bla chen drung phyis su'ang khyod kyis klu bdud 'di la thugs dam re byas na rtags re yong gi 'dug ste ka gsung ba zhig byung / lo bcu la kha ltas tsa na dpal
dus kyi 'khor lo'i sgrub dkyil jo nang phyogs las rnam rgyal gyis mdzad pa la bslab gnyer byas/ zhag bcu bcu na rgyugs re 'bul gyi yod pa la/ thengs shig rtsed mos g.yengs
nas zhag gcig gi rgya 'dzin pa ma byung bar ltag slog byas rgyugs byang bar phul bas/ de skabs ni ma dgongs pa skad mdzad/ khyed shes rab che'i gda' gsung pa las gzhan
mi gsung / zhag 'ga' nas ka li dang spel ba'i gdams pa'i mthar/ sems gzhan yengs pa'i 'don pa dang / /ltag slog mkhas pa'i rgyugs sprod dang / /zin kyang brjed du 'jug
pa gsum/ /dgos med yin pas spang ba gces/ /zhes pa gnang byung bas/ ngo tsha zhing skrag la shin tu 'jigs pa zhig byung nas/ mchi ma mang po shor/ dgos med kyi dran rgyu
chung du song bas 'di gcig pu'i sku drin la'ang khyer thabs mi gda'/ mdor na yongs rdzogs kyi sgrub thabs dpag bsam snye ma bdag 'jug bdud rtsi'i rol mtsho dang bcas pa
mchod brjod nas/ shubhaM gyi bar nag 'byams su zla ba gcig la zin pas dgyes tshor ci yang mdzad/ gsol ja gnang sbyin dang bcas pa'ang stsal/ khyed byas na yong ba zhig gda'
ste gsung ba da lta'i ba ma glang 'di yong ba dgongs pa'i gsung du gda'/ thengs shig gos chen dmar po chung ngu zhig spen rkang bzhi la btags nas bdag gi zhwa mo'i rtse
la phyag la bdar nas btsugs te/ bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan

'dzugs pa yin no/ /bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan tshugs par gyur cig /ces gsungs zhing de la gzigs nas bzhad kyin gda' ba/ nged kyi bla ma 'di gzhan rtsed mo mdzad kyi 'dug pa sus
kyang mthong ba med/ de dus ni kun gyis sku rtsed tsam du go /da bsams dus rje bla ma de'i zhal slob bzang la hrags pa bdog ste/ rgya dang mon gyi dpes da lta dus 'khor
dang gsung ngag rin po che sogs la 'chad nyan byed mkhan bdag gcig pur nges pa 'di dgongs pa'i lung bstan du gda' 'o/ /dngos kun lag mthil gnas pa'i shing tog bzhin/ /sgrib

kyang byas/ lo bcu gnyis lon pa'i dgun mgo'i zla ba'i tshes bcu bzhi la bkra shis kyi gtsug lag khang dpal ldan lcang lo can du mkhan po rje btsun bla ma dam pa de nyid dang
/ grib tshod pa bla chen rin po ches mdzad tshigs snga ma dge tshul gyi sdom pa rnam par dag pa thob/ yun ring po'i bar sngor dkar dang bcas pa'i rang tshugs ngo lkog med
pa'i dge tshul da ma dog che zer ba zhig byas/ de nas zla ba phyi mar rje bla ma grum stod kha'u'i brag rdzong nas rgyal ba'i rgyal tshab grong stod rin po che'i zhal
snga nas kyis spyan drangs pa'i phyag phyir phyin/ yar lam gdong khar nang so rnam pas gzhi len sogs bzabs bzabs mang po mdzad/ khong tsho bka' brgyud pa'i khungs byed kyin
gda' bas/ sdom gsum dang thub pa dgongs gsal gyi phyag rgya pa la dgag pa mdzad pa rnams la brten nas chos skad zir zir gang yang byas mod/ khrom thub rang byung ba med
dam bsam/ de dus ni ngag sgo yangs pa'i thog chod/ de nas gdan sa chen po dpal ldan sa skya'i gtsug lag khang du phebs/ mdun gyi zhing steng zhig nas phyag 'bul mdzad kyi
'dug pa'i dus gnam sa ngo mi shes pa'i zi ding ba zhig ma gtogs gang yang mthong rgyu dang gzhig pa chug rgyu ma byung / bdag chen chos rje khri thog rin po che dang mjal/
brtse skyong yang bzabs ma mdzad/ sgo rum gyi bla ma lha khang / bse 'bag nyid dang bcas pa mjal/ gur gyi sku de zhal ras kyi dpangs mda' gang tsam yod pa'i khro bo
zhi ma khro mthing kha 'od chags pa rgya smin ma la gser shog btab/ shangs kyi rtse sogs la rtsi gogs pa

'ang dum pa yod pa/ zhal 'gram hang nge ba'i steng na spa bas yod tsam byas pa zhig tu mthong / nged kyi zla bo 'dras ni de min pa 'drar mthong ni zer/ rgyal bas rgyal ba'i
bstan pa gnyer du gtad/ /grub pas grub pa'i gtsug lag skyong bar bskos/ /mgon po mgon po'i 'bag tu snang ba de/ /mjal bas mjal ba don dang ldan par byung / /bzhi thog bla
brang gi lha khang gcig kyang mjal/ gzhan gtsug lag khang mtha' dag mjal snying 'dod par byung ste zhag gnyis las ma bzhugs pas long ma byung zhing / rje bla ma gnyis phyogs
der ma byon pa yun rings pas mjal ba dang chos zhu mkhan sogs ches mangs pa'i thugs brel dang / thugs dam gyis g.yengs g.yog drag pa'i khungs 'dra yod pa a ra gog tu
song bas lha khang la zhe 'dod med pa yin nam/ labs kyang do dam ma byas par gzhan ci yang mjal ma thub/ nyi ma gtsang gi phyogs nas sems lhag ma lus pa 'di gcig pu ma
gtogs gzhan ci yang mi bdog /sa skya'i rmongs zhen snying la gcags pa'i mthus/ /sa skya'i lha khang phal cher ma mkhor bas/ /sa skyar phyin nas stong log byas so snyam/ /sa
skya'i phyogs de da dung sems la dran/ /'dod sred can 'gas sred pa zhugs pa yi/ /grogs de ring na gnas kyang snying la 'char/ /de bzhin dpag tshad du mas mtshams chod
kyang / /ma bsgribs yid kyi yul na lam mer gda'/ /de nas drug pa rdo rje 'chang dang dbyer med pa'i rje btsun sa skya pa yab sras rnams kyis rnam par grol ba'i ye shes

brnyes pa'i sa/ stobs 'phrog dbang po 'khor dang bcas pas mngon sum du bsten pa'i ljongs grum stod kha'u'i brag rdzong du phebs/ gzhis bzhugs rnams kyis dar 'phyar ser sbreng
sogs bzabs bzabs ci yang zhig mdzad/ de nub bla ma rje'i phyag phyir 'du khang gong ma der bsdad/ sang nas rje bla ma lam 'bras lha khang du bzhugs/ bdag gis 'bum thang
dang khad nye'i sgrub chen brtson 'grus pa bya ba'i khang chung zhig gi g.yabs su yol ba byas nas bsdad/ rje rin po che gdan sa'i drung gi gzhis len brtse skyong bsam gyis
mi khyab pa lan cig ma yin par thugs la btags/ nged rang gis kyang tshogs su mang ja/ gdan non 'bul 'gyed dang bcas pa bsgrubs/ grub chen rnams kyang nyin re bzhin gnyis
gsum re gdan drangs/ gsol ja tsha bzhes bzabs thag chod re skor ma byas thams cad la zhus/ bdag gi bla ma sku drin can des rgyal tshab dam pas dbu mdzad gzhir bzhugs
kyi dge 'dun dpal ldan sa skya pa'i snyan brgyud kyi zab lam nyams su bzhes bzhin pa lnga bcu tsam dang / bdag sogs phyogs mtha'i grwa pa'ang thogs pa dang bcas pa'i bdun
cu phyin la/ gsung ngag rin po che zla ba gsum gyi bar smin rgyas su sku drin bskyangs/ gsung ngag dang 'brel ba'i dbang byin rlabs phal che ba dang / dpal dus kyi 'khor
lo'i dbang sogs so so'i bzhed pa dang bstun pa'i dbang lung du ma zhig gnang gi 'dug pa phal cher thob/ khyad par brag sgo'i drung du stobs 'phrog dbang po bsnyen dus kyi
rjes gnang zhig

gnang ba'i tshe ye shes phab tshar mtshams la zhabs drung gi dbu thog gi bla bre'i thad nas ba thag cig brkyang ba'i sna la sdom chung ngu zhig babs nas rjes gnang ma grol
gyi ring nged kyi pang na phar rgyug tshur rgyug byed cing bsdad 'dug mod/ rjes su gar song ni ma shes/ rjes gnang zhu grogs la yod pa'i sgrub chen kha re khyod kyis rjes
gnang zhus pas bsnyen rtags byung zer ngo mtshar mtshar ni byed kyi 'dug /de 'dra'i bshad tshod 'dug pa ni ma mthong / yang nged rnams bla brang nas gnas tshang der bskyas
pa'i tshe bla brang pa'i khrol khyi rgya bo zhig gda' ba de nged kyi phyi la sleb byung nas sgo 'gag tu sdod/ bdag gsung chos la phar 'gro dus 'du khang gi 'gag thub skyel/
slar gnas tshang gi gnam sgo'i 'og tu nyal nas sdod/ gsung chos gyes gdong du 'du khang 'gag tu nged bsu ba la sleb yong / nam la nged sdod sa de la skor ba byed kyin
'ba' dir byed pa zhig byung ba bo dong la phyir 'gro dus mdun gyi zam chen bud bud phyi la 'brangs de nas phyi mig lta zhing log song bas sems 'phreng po zhig byung ba
gang yin ni mi shes phan thogs la dgod bro ba zhig byung ngo / /tshur lam gdan sa chen por zhag 'ga' bzhugs rtsis gnang gi 'dug na'ang bo dong nas gdan 'dren ngos drag tsam
byung ba la brten gar gzhung brgyud nas phebs/ de rjes bo dong bla brang dkar por zla ba gsum gyi bar gsung ngag rin po che'i dbang gong ma gsum gyi lam khrid rje btsun
nyid la ji ltar bzhugs pa'i yi ge'i lung byin rlabs sgrub pa lung byin gyi bar

brgyud pa gsum las 'ongs pa'i man ngag thams cad yongs su rdzogs par thob/ grol ston tshogs kyi 'khor lo/ bsags sbyang gi maNDal gyi nas khal lnga bcu lhag pa/ gser zho gsum
gyis gtsos pa'i 'bul ba dpangs gang che dang bcas pa'ang phul/ bdag la rten khebs ma Ni ma hor dus shig /'jam dbyangs kyi gser sku zhig /dar dur kha kha gru yangs pa zhig
rnams gnang / chos 'di'i bdag po re ba yin pas thos bsam dang nyams len la 'bungs/ dpe tsam ltas pas shes pa'i chos ma yin pas bla ma'i gsung sgros la nan tan mdzod/ ster
byin 'di la gnang dpangs shig mi gda' ste go ba zhig yod pa yin gsung ngo / /rgya chen mdo rgyud rgya mtsho bsrubs pa'i bcud/ /rgya bod mkhas grub bye ba'i snying gi
nor/ /rgya chen zab mo'i mthar thugs gsung ngag chos/ /rgya lam rnyed par dka' de bdag gis rnyed/ /bla ma'i gsung ngag dbyangs snyan lha yi rnga / /yid dang rna dbang tshim
la mi ngal ba'ang / /byis pa'i blo yi gam la cher ma zin/ /da dus snying nas dran kyang ci zhig bya/ /yab rje'i zhabs pad bsten dus byis pa'i blo/ /mno bsam cung zad rnyed
tshe bdud dbang song / /rang dbang thob tshe dam pa chos dbyings byon/ /ji ltar bgyis kyang bsod nams bgo skal zhan/ /'on te dad pa'i zhing sa mchog tu gshin/ /'bral
med mos gus dam tshig chu yis brlan/ /yab gcig gsung gi sa bon skyon med thebs/ /nam zhig 'khrul med 'bras bu 'byung ngam snyam/ /de'i dus lam sbas bshad nyams khrid yid
ches par zhus/

gsung ji lta ba'i zin bris kyi dpe chung zhig byas pa chos mdzad legs bshad pa zhes grags pa'i g.yog gi khungs la dpon po'i sems/ sdang sems dgra dang gnod sems bgegs las che
ba zhig bdog pa des bsams bzhin du shog ro'i zla la chur bcug nas gong bu gcig tu byas pa 'dis mtshon/ 'di nyid kyis 'phral dang yun gyi rten 'brel la gnod pa mang po
zhig byas te/ tshe rabs sngon ma zhig nas las ngan gyis 'brel ba'i dngos grub kyi gegs la chas pa zhig tu gor ma chag go /de nas rang lo bcu gsum du slebs pa'i tshe skeg
gi rnam pa byung dogs pas de la dmigs pa'i mtshams shig byas na legs/ zhes yab yum rnams gsung ba la rje btsun mchog la thugs dam brtag pa zhus nas aShta'i gzhi bsnyen zhig
byed snyam pa la/ bka' lung la da lam aShta las gur gyi mgon po'i bsnyen pa byas na legs pa 'dug /de'ang thog mar yi ge bdun pa'i bsnyen pa gyis/ grangs ni rje btsun rin
po che'i gur rgyan du gsung pa'i dgongs pa yin pas 'bru re la 'bum phrag brgyad brgyad de 'bum phrag lnga bcu rtsa drug zlos gsung / dkar shAkya grags kyis mdzad pa'i
khro bcu'i srung 'khor gyi lung dmigs dang bcas pa zhig gnang nas/ rje bla ma bo dong bla brang dkar por sku mtshams la bzhugs/ bdag gis bo dong rdzong gi bya 'dabs bde gsal
rab brtan zer ba'i dgon chung skyid po zhig bdog pa der 'ongs nas zla ba drug gi bar mtshams byas/ bla chen thugs rje can des kyang grogs mdzad de yi ge bdun pa'i grangs
ni ji ltar bshad pa bzhin song / byis pa ham can zhig bdog pas/ zhal mthong yong ngam bsams dung dung byas

te rmi lam bzang ba re tsam las mthong ba'i grabs kyang ma byung ste/ da bsams dus sangs rgyas mthong ba la tha na'ang sa dang po tsam thob dgos pa 'dug pas sngar mthong rgyu
ma byung ba 'os chod/ da dung mthong mthong la thag rgyang chen rgyang pa yod nges su gda' 'o/ /'on kyang 'dre mthong ba kha cig ngas mgon po mthong / lha mo mthong zer
bred bred mang po byas yong gi 'dug pa bden bsam pa ni mi gda'/ bden na ni sngags bgrangs pa las zog che ba ngos byin rlabs myur ba e yin te/ phal cher de dag gis mgon
po mthong na bya rog dang 'ug pa dga' mgur rol bar nges so/ /rgyal ba kun gyi mthu stobs gcig bsdus nas/ /rgyal ba'i bstan srung dbang por skur bzhengs pa/ /rgyal ba khyab
bdag rdo rje nag po che/ /rgyal ba thugs rje can de kho bos bsgrubs/ /rtog btags rang bzo'i rlung gis ma bskyod pa'i/ /snyan brgyud zhal drod ma nyams gdams pa'i sprin/
/byin rlabs chu khur lci ldan 'khrigs pa'i tshe/ /dngos grub char rgyun 'babs las 'os ci yod/ /drag sngags dbyar gyi rnga gsang sgrags pa'i tshe/ /bdud bgegs bya dkar skrag
nas ga shed song / /nus mthu'i rma bya dga' bas gar byed pa/ /'di ko dngos po'i gnas lugs ma yin nam/ /bsnyen pa gegs med du mthar phyin/ yum rgan mo sku drin can des/
skeg las thar ba'i gtang rag gyis gsung / nas khal brgyas gtsos pa'i gnang byin dang tshogs 'khor kyang bzabs po gnang / gtang rag gi gtor sgrub kyang bzabs

bzabs dpe med byas te mtshams grol/ lo bcu bzhi lon pa'i dpyid ka de 'od zer can lha lnga la gtso 'bum 'khor khri bzhi gyur gyi bsnyen pa zhig byas/ lo de'i ston slob dpon
padmas bdud po pra ma ra dza'i sprul pa bod kyi bde skyid 'joms mkhan gcig tu lung bstan pa'i bo dong mkhan po sher rgyam pa dang / gnas gsar ba ma 'cham par bun ne byung
ba'i byus rim du 'od zer can lha lnga'i sgrub mchod byas pa'i tshar nyer lnga song ba'i tshe dung chos kyi chu blug pas bum nang gi ye shes pa gshegs dam tshig pa 'od du
zhu ba'i chus bum pa gang bar gyur zhes brjod ma thag bum chu lud nas chi li li babs shing / kha dang mchu gnyis nas babs pa de 'dra ba'i ngo mtshar byung / gtso bor rje
bla ma'i sku drin dang yab sras rnams rang gi nus pa los yin mod/ kham mchu yang rtseg ste legs/ lha mo 'od zer can 'di la gsol ba btab na mi bslu nges pa'i thugs rje che
la myur ba zhig gda'/ 'grub nges shes pa'i dge sbyor rgyang bsrings nas/ /mi 'grub nges pa'i 'jig rten ban ling gis/ /gal chung chos la byas pas bslus pa las/ /tshul bzhin
bsgrubs kyang slus pa su yis thos/ /ma bsgrubs 'bras bu 'dod pa'i 'dod can tsho/ /cung zad mno bsam slong las sgrub pa mdzod/ /rgyu med 'bras bu 'tshol ba'i 'gyogs skor
gyis/ /yi chad thang la yun ring 'khyams nyen gda'/ /de'i ston de tshe sngon ma'i lan chags 'jal mkhan cig yin pa 'dra/ kho rang blos lings kyis btab

nas bdag gi g.yog byed pa'i blo gros bzang po 'di zla la sleb/ de nas de'i bar la skabs 'gar grogs ngan pa'i mig ltos kyis dgos med la 'ur ba ni thor re ba byas/ gzhan rdzas
dngos po chung chung nas bzung dgon pa khams chen gyis bar tshang ma kho rang la gtad pas/ ma 'phyugs ma rlag gong 'phel gyi 'dzin skyong mthun grub 'ba' zhig byung ba
la brten nas nged rang chos 'chad nyan dang kha ton kho na byas pas chog pa ma gtogs/ gdan re 'ding ba tshun du sleb pa'i ban ling mi dgos/ kho rang gzhis la yod dus sgor
ma nas tsha hrug ge yong ba thams cad kyis mthong ba 'di yin mod/ bcol na phyags ma rgyag pa'ang mi shes la/ /gzhag na bshad ra shug ras lung pa 'geng / /gar btang shes
pa 'tshub pa 'ga' zhig gis/ /sgro skur gshed smod 'ur lugs 'di bsams na/ /btang na gar btang sa der blo mi 'tshag /sgor na gar bzhag gnas su gong 'phel yong / /zhen che blo
shed ldan la 'gyur ldog chung / /khyod rang lan brgyar 'ur kyang a'u tsi/ /lo 'di rje bla ma'i dgung lo re gcig pa'i skeg yin pa dang / sku dog kyang che bar yod 'dug
pa nas sku mtshams kho na la shas cher bzhugs pas gsung chos phran bu ma gtogs 'gangs che ba ni ma thob/ de'i dgun kyang gur gyi yi ge bdun pa 'bru 'bum gcig dang / phyag
na rdo rje utsarYa'i sngags 'bum gcig mtshams dam po byas nas bzlas/ lo bco lnga lon pa'i khyi lo'i dbyar bdag gi yab dang / gcen thu bo de'u ri'i sgar thog tu byon pa'i
sku rim la/ yang 'od zer can gyi bsnyen pa

bsos la sgrub mchod gyis gsungs nas bgyis pas tshar lnga bcu tsam song ba'i tshe rmi lam du 'od zer can gyi sku nam mkha'i khams khengs pa zhig gi phyal gyi nang spang ri khyon
yangs po zhig gi ldebs la rang re'i sgar de khra hrug ge 'dug pa zhig gsal po rmis/ de'i ston btsas ma 'go byed tsam la bdag bsod nams kyi dpal gzhal du med pa zhig
'bar te/ /de'ang mkhas pa'i mkhas pa chos kyi rje nam mkha' dbang phyug pa'i drung dbus nas zhabs gtad byon/ 'bul ba ni srab mo'i sku chos legs po zhig las mi 'dug ste/ bstan
pa la phan pa'i dge bshes chen po bsam gyis mi khyab pa yin pa dang / zhal slob rnying par song bas dgyes bzhin du zhal gyis bzhes/ bdag cag gzhi byes kyis grwa pa bcu
gsum la dpal dus kyi 'khor lo la sogs pa'i bla na med pa'i rgyud thams cad kyi rdzogs rim/ zla lam zhag gis gcod pa sangs rgyas la zhag dus thebs pa'i khrid zab lam sbyor
ba yan lag drug pa'i nyams 'khrid gnang ste/ thog mar rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor du bsod nams kyi tshogs kyi slad du byis pa 'jug pa'i dbang bdun gnang ste/ thun mong
dang thun mong ma yin pa'i sngon 'gro zla ba gcig bskyangs/ yig brgya dang maNDal khri tsho bzhi bzhi btang / me tog nas khal nyi shu rtsa lnga lhag pa phul/ de mtshams
rdo rje slob dpon lus kyi dkyil 'khor du tshul khrims dang ye shes kyi tshogs kyi slad du 'jig rten dang 'jig rten las 'das pa'i dbang gong ma gnang ba'i bgegs sprod kyi
skabs

rje bla ma chas zhugs mdzad/ rdo rje'i gar dang bcas srung ma drug cu'i bstod dbyangs kyi bskul mdzad pa na/ sngon chad kyi zhal mdog zla ba shar ba lta bu de ma yin par mthing
shun gyi mdog lta bu la 'od zer mig gis ye mi bzod pa zhig tu thog mar bdag gis mthong / de nas yum dang dpon sa nam mkha'i drung / o lo ming sring / a skyabs/ gnyer
pa tshe 'dzin pa rnams rim bzhin slebs nas/ a tsi 'di 'dra 'dug zer thams cad gcig la gcig gis yus bzhin du smra'i 'dug ste nged mi drug po de'ang bsod nams bsags par gda'/
byin rlabs kyi zi langs pas byis pa mno mi shes yan chad sa 'phag gnam 'phag byas/ gnam sa ngo mi shes pa'i 'gyur ba chen po thams cad la byung / a ho rgyal ba dngos
su byon pa'i tshe/ /tha mal byis pa'i sems la'ang ye shes 'bar/ /drag rol gu gul dpung du mi dgos par/ /bsam med bems po rnams kyang mgul snyam byed/ /gzhan du yun ring lo
zlar bsgoms pa las/ /gang zhig gsung thos tsam yang don che ba/ /yab gcig rdo rje 'chang dbang de yi gsung / /phyin chad thos pa'i skal ba i yod na//bsams shing bla ma'i
zhal bzang snying la dran/ /dran mod dngos su mjal ba'i skal ba med/ /med bzhin 'khrul pa'i 'khor ba 'dir gnas phyin/ /phyin chad khyed 'dra'i mgon dang mjal ba dka'/ /dka'
mod las dkar dbang gis dngos su mjal/ /mjal tsam ma yin gsung gi bdud rtsi thob/ /thob bya'i snying po thugs yid

gcig tu 'dres/ /'dres khyer bla mas ma bslus nga re skyid/ /de nas dben gsum la zhag bdun dang / sor sdud la bdun te mun mtshams zhag bcu bzhi shin tu dam pa mdzad/ nged rang
la khyer kha med kyang bla ma'i byin rlabs dang gdams ngag gi zab gnad kyis nyams myong yang cung zad skyes/ kha phyir bltas kyi zar zir tsho la zhen pa med pa zhig byung
/ nyin mo'i rnal 'byor bsam gtan sogs kyang nyams khrid kho na mdzad de/ zla ba gsum la yan lag drug gi dngos gzhi grol ba mdzad/ sems 'grel skor gsum dang / sbyor drug
gi yi ge rgya bod kyi dam pa mang pos mdzad pa sogs mdor na rje nyid la ji ltar mnga' ba'i lung man ngag thams cad bum pa gang byor gnang / rje bla ma dam pas mdzad pa'i
sbyor drug la zhen pa byas/ mun mtshams kyang zhag gsum re mdzad pa'i khrid du gnang / de thams cad rdzogs pa'i mthar rdo rje slob dpon bdag po dang bdag po chen po'i
dbang bskur te bstan pa'i rgyal srid gtad/ de dag gi skabs su yang tha na lha bshos 'jog tshul dang rdo rje dril bu 'dzin tshul tshun chod la zhib cha'i phyag 'khrid gnang
/ lung mang po gnang ba'i skabs su'ang bdag gcig pu la gzigs shing / yengs pa'am/ gnyid bro'i 'dug na brda tsam mdzad/ chos grol ba dang / tha'i khyer kha la dpa' der bsdad
pa tsam gyis thob na ka ba dang chab ril sogs thams cad kyis thob mod/ de 'dras ci yong khyod la 'di'i bdag po re ba yin

mod/ sems ma 'khrul ba bgyis la nyon/ dka' ba'i gnas su ngas labs pa 'di tsho'ang ma brjed pa gyis gsung pa dang / skabs 'gar nga khyod la re chen po zhig yod de gsung thugs
chad de ba'i gsung yang byon nas mdor na lan cig ma yin par legs pa'i lam la sbyar ba 'di gcig pu'i sku drin la'ang khyer thabs mi gda'/ a ho srid lam dub pa'i mgon med
bdag /bdag nyid chen po khyod kyi sku drin las/ /las bzang zab lam sgom pa'i skal bar ldan/ /ldan grol can du byed pa'i rang dbang thob/ /thob kyang ngan goms dbang du song
ba bdag /bdag nyid chen po khyod 'dra'i drung du yang / /yang dag ma yin sems kyi gya gyu dang / /dang po'i lha yis byin rlabs gnyid rmugs 'thibs/ /'thibs te gtam rgyud
snyan pos sems rab yengs/ /yengs tshe se gol sgra yis gcig tu gcun/ /gcun kyang yar bskyed med pa'i tha shal sems/ /sems can dud 'gro'i khyu ru gtogs la khad/ /gzhan yang
de'i lo dpal sdom pa chen po dang / gsang ba 'dus pa 'jam rdor sa lugs/ mkha' 'gro rgya mtsho sogs zur bka' mang po dang / rdo rje 'phreng ba dang kr-i ya bsres pa'i
dbang la sogs pa dbang mang po/ phyag rdor gos sngon can dang / rdo rje shugs sogs rjes gnang mang po/ brtag gnyis 'grel pa skor gsum sogs lung mang po ste/ mdor na zla ba
bcu'i bar nyin re bzhin bar ma chad par gsung chos kyi sku drin bsam gyis mi khyab pa zhig thob/ sbyor drug

gi thun mong gi sngon 'gro rnams la brjed byang chung ngu zhig kyang byas/ lo bcu drug lon pa'i phag lo yang gtso bor sgom byed pa'i lugs byas/ gur gyi mgon po'i yi ge bdun
pa 'bru 'bum gnyis tsam dang / dgra nag zhang lugs kyi dkyil 'khor rgyas pa'i thog nas hrIHShtrI gtso 'bum 'khor khri bzhi 'gyur gyi gnya' mnan/ dmag zor re ma tI'i bhyo
raka bzhi 'bum gcig bzlas pas/ bsnyen rtags za re zi re dgod bro mo de 'dra kha re byung / lar gnas gsar ba'i mi bo dong du skyo mkhan sngon ma rang bdag yin pa dang / yul
lha lta bur song bas yin nam/ bsnyen pa ma byas gong nas su re 'go zhig gi legs po zhig yod de/ bo dong rdzong 'jig pa'i tshe/ rdo rje 'chang chen pos rdzong bdag la khong
bskos pa'i kha bstabs 'di las ma byung bas/ dga' mod byung dogs med snyam yi chad chen po byung bas gyes/ bdag gis kyang mchod gtor rgyun chad/ bar skabs su tshur btud
pa 'dra ba byung na'ang spang blang ma byas par bzhag /da bsams dus sems can gyi las sangs rgyas kyis kyang bzlog mi thub pas/ bcom ldan 'das nyid bzhugs bzhin du shAkya
rnams kha dag pa dang / sngon chad byas pa gang yin pa ni ma gtogs so/ /zhes mdo rgyud phal cher las gsal bar gsungs 'dug pas 'di rigs la lha dang srung ma la yi chad
dang khag 'dogs byed rgyu rdul tsam med cing le lan 'ded rang 'ded na skye ba sngon ma

bsags pa'i las ngan tsho la 'ded dgos rgyur 'dug na'ang mno bsam drag shos rjes su las/ rtab rtab la lung ma bstan re byas 'gyod kyang rgyugs thebs med pa kho na yong ba 'di
spra chal la spu sud pa'i spre'u'i grogs mched rnams kyi khyad chos su 'dug pa bzhin sngar yang mang po byung mod/ des mi thub da dung yong zer ba'i mo ngag gi tshan du
gda'/ lo de'i mjug la nyang stod bsam sdings nas grub thob kyi 'khor los sgyur ba lce ston paN chen rin po che sde pa nas spyan drangs/ bdag gi bla ma de la gsung chos gsan
pa dang sgo bstun dgyes bzhin du phebs byung / de'ang bla ma 'di pa bod yul gyi sngags 'chang thams cad kyi dbus na nyi zla ltar gsal ba lce thams cad mkhyen pa mdo sde
seng ge zhes bya ba rgyud sde brgya rtsa brgyad la mkhas shing grub pa des 'a zhwa'i pha mes zhu 'brog a mes chen po'i bla ma mdzad/ sku drin bsam gyis mi khyab pas skyabs
pa nas bzung / gdung rabs dgu'i bar bla rabs mchod rabs zam ma chad par byon pa'i bla ma drin chen gyi brgyud pa zhig yin/ rje 'di nyid kyang nges par grub pa'i dbang
phyug rtsod med cig lags pa ltar/ nged rang yon mchod kyi pha chos dpal phyag na rdo rje gtum po chen po lha nyer gcig gi dkyil 'khor chen por dbang bzhi yongs su rdzogs
pa dang / tshe dpag med lcam lugs/ nag po chen po lha chen dpal 'bar gyi rjes gnang thun mong dang thun mong ma yin pa man ngag

gi lung phal che ba dang bcas pa sogs gsung chos khams chen po nyung ngu zhig thob/ lo bcu bdun du sleb pa'i zla ba dang po de'i nang du bde gsal mgon khang du mtshams byas/
lha chen pad gdong ma'i bsnyen pa zhig byas pa yid ches po zhig byung ba yin/ a ho grub pa'i rigs su skyes tsam gyis/ /nag po'i mtshan ma phal cher rdzogs 'gyur na/ /bla
ma'i lung gis legs par mnga' gsol tshe/ /'phrin las kha lo sgyur bar cis mi 'grub/ /dpal ldan 'a zhwa ye shes g.yung drung nas/ /'a zhwa mthu chen mgon po rin chen 'bar/
/zhal mthong gsung thos dgra bgegs chom la phab/ /grub pa'i lag rjes gsal pa kho na yin/ /khyad par pha rgan grub pa'i dbang phyug des/ /lan cig min par zhal gzigs bran
du bkol/ /thugs kyis brtse ba'i bran khol rnams kyis kyang / /lha 'di'i cho 'phrul mthong ba mang du byung / /pha de'i gdung gi thig le las skyes shing / /pha rgod bla mas
yang yang bka' bsgos pas/ /pha nor bu yi spyod pa 'os yin zhes/ /pha mes brgyud pa'i lha 'dis kho bo bskyangs/ /'di la gtam gyi sbyor ba 'ga' yod kyang / /'di na gsal
bar smra ba'i snod ma rnyed/ /'di dang mtshungs pa'i gsang ba'i gtam phal cher/ /'di bzhin nam mkha'i dbyings su phaT cig rgyob/ /da dus 'byung ba'i rigs kyi dpon rnams kyang
/ /khas phyug gang che'i rjes

zlos ma byed par/ /lha 'di bsten la glo snying brang gsum khol/ /grub pa'i rigs brgyud ma bcod snying gi bu/ /bsnyen pa de'i sgang tsam la nged rang gi dgra'i skal ba rgya
'dre khong btsun pa chen po 'jigs su rung ba'i rnam pa can rta la rgyud tsam zhon/ snam sbyar ber thul sogs bzabs sprod/ rma bya'i sgro zhwa gyon pa'i btsun dmag gcer bu
mtshan ma mdung tsam sgrengs pa brgya phrag mang pos bskor te sleb byung ba na nag po chen po'i nga rgyal brtan pos gtso bo de'i ske la ral gri zhig bsnun pas thal bar bun
gyis song / 'khor rnams skad cig la du ba yal ba bzhin gyi gar song cha med la song ba na gnyid sad pas dngos su du chom deng ba zhig tshor/ nang thams cad bseb dris khengs
'dug /'di rgya 'dre'i g.yul las rgyal ba thog ma yin/ bsnyen pa phal cher rdzogs pa na pha rgan grub pa can de'i drin gyis nged rang la lus dang grib ma bzhin 'grogs/
legs nyes phal cher lung ston pa'i lha mo zhig yod pa de'i cho 'phrul yin pa 'dra/ bud med gzhon nu zhig gis nyang stod rgyal khang nas dpon sa'i drung gis skyel du btang
ba yin zer/ smyug ma'i gzeb chen po zhig 'khris su khyer byung ba yam ste sprad pas yong ba med/ nyan mi nyan ni mi shes go rim zhig yod zer/ thog mar me long g.ya' yongs
su dag pa la 'khor lo bris pa zhig gtad nas 'di 'bral med du chongs shig zer/ de nas gras kha bcu gras tsam byas pa'i dpe cha po ti chung nge ba zhig sprad nas 'di skye

bo thams cad la thun mong du sbyin rgyu'i chos yin zer/ yang po ti de tsam legs po zhig sprad nas 'di snod dang ldan nges ma gtogs kun la bshad rgyu ma yin/ rang res sgrub
rgyu yin zer/ de nas yang me long g.ya' yongs su dag pa 'od lam me ba zhig sprad byung nas/ dpe cha de gnyis kyi bdag po byas na 'di dang 'dra ba zhig yong ba 'dug ste zer/
de nas mda' tshad par ma zhig bton byung nas/ 'di phar phyin gyi 'grel pa don gsal yin/ tshang ni bdog ste par gsal po mi 'dug zer/ yang par ma mda' tshad cig bton byung
nas 'di rnam 'grel gyi 'grel pa kun bzang yin/ par gsal po mi 'dug pa'i khar phyed tsam ma tshang ba 'dug pas 'di gnyis kyis ha cang gi phan thogs shig ni mi yong ba 'dra
dgos sam mi dgos zer/ dpe cha de gnyis lag tu blangs pa nas bu mo des shugs ring zhig phyung nas me long de blangs nas ras nag po zhig gis gril nas bdag gi pang du bzhag
/dpe cha rjes ma de gnyis kyi zla bo la 'di yod zer spre'u'i pags pa mnyes pa zhig dang / bul tog 'dra ba la ngo shes rgyu cher med pa'i skya bo le ba bre do tsam zhig
gtad byung ma thag gnyid sad byung / bsam dus tha'i dbang zhig byung ba yin na de dang de 'dra zhig yin pa 'dug ste snyam pa'i go ba zhig byung ngo / /ma las brtse ba'i
lha mchog khyod kyis 'dir/ /ma 'ongs gnas 'di mngon sum bzhin du bstan/ /ma bsgribs go zhing sems la shar mod kyi/ /ma rabs

kho bo gzhan gyi dbang du song / /de'i dbyar a mi lags rnam rgyal dpal bzang po'i nang rten rje btsun chen po grags pa'i gser sku chen po bzhengs pa'i gzungs kyi do dam byas/
sems la mi med kyi lung stong zhig tu phyin nas rdzogs rim sbyor drug 'di dang / skyed rim mkha' spyod ma 'di la chig dril byas/ shi ma thag mkha' spyod du 'gro ba zhig
byed snyam pa thun mong ma yin par byung mod/ zhal ngo tshos mdo phyogs bslab dgos gsung gi gda' ba la zhe med de byas na 'jog tsam e yong snyam bsams bzhin du gshis kha
lod po byas su la'ang cher ma nyan/ dgos med la'ang tho re ba 'ur/ 'ur dgos nges shes pa'ang kha re byung mod/ mi la la kho lang tsho brdo ba'i smyo spyod yin ze ba dang
/ gser sku'i 'tshub yin zer ba sogs sna tshogs lab cing 'dug mod/ sems la mnong med pas su la'ang 'jigs po ma byung / dgongs pas khrol na dang ma khrol na ga shed du gcig
la bud nas 'gro'am snyam pa byung na'ang / pha rgan grub pa can de bla ma yin pas de'i bka' bcag na dge sbyor lam du ma song gi dogs nas bsdad/ ston de rdo rje rnal 'byor
ma'i bsnyen pa bzhi 'bum bcu cha'i sbyin sreg dang bcas pa yid ches pa zhig byas/ de'i mjug tsam nas rkang pa g.yon pa'i nad gzhi 'di langs byung ba la lha rje rnams
kyis bstan pa'i thabs de dag lhur blangs kyang phan rgyu gang yang ma byung / de'i skabs shig rgya gar nub phyogs nA girkoTa'i rgyal po'i sras ma Ni ka nA tha zhes bya ba
'chi med grub

pa'i dzo ki zhig phag lo dpyid ka byon nas dbus la bzhud/ yar lam bdag can 'byon par byas pa de phebs byung ba nas mtshams khongs su mjal/ des gu ru 'tshol ba la bod du lan
gsum yongs/ sngon ma'i dus ma'i rum na byas nas ma mthong / bar ma'i dus byis pa chung ngu zhig skyes pa zhig gis bzung nas 'dug pa rgyang nas mthong ba tsam byung / da
lam 'phrad pa 'di yin gsung / bdag la byams po dang dgyes po yang dag par mdzad/ de nas bzung rgya gar shar nub gung gsum gyi dzo ki su byung yang de dag gi skad phal cher
go /yul mi gsha' ma dang phrad pa lta bu'i dga' tshor 'byung / /ro Ti sogs kyi kha zas dang / bhu Du ba sogs kyi yo byad la zhen pa chen po yod zhing 'dug /kha che'i yi
ge dang / nA ga ra gyob be ba 'di yang rang rdol shes byung bas a tsA ra ltogs 'khyams pa zhig gi skye ba zhig yin pa 'dra bsam pa yong gi 'dug /snying nas sgrub pa don
gnyer bsam sbyor gyis/ zhe med 'ur po'i spyod pa thog gcig byas/ /'di la mi rnams kun gyis smad lags kyang / /rgyal ba sras bcas dbyings nas dgyes sam snyam/ /'chi med grub
pa'i dzo ki sgo nyal byas/ /sngon dus byas pa'i bag chags gsal bar dran/ /gnas sar gu ru ma hA ta pa sI/ /'phags yul skye bo phal cher thal mo sbyor/ /dzo ki de las ayon
padma sku gsum gyi sgrub thabs dang / /a bhi dha nar gsungs pa'i phag mo'i byin

rlabs/ /bhru rlung sogs man ngag mang po zhus/ khong nged la drin yang che/ legs gshad gser thur na bris 'dug pa'i rnying ma'i dgag pa de tsho mthong ba dang / rnying ma'i
sngags rnams dang / rgya skad bod skad kyang cher mi 'grig pa mang / deng sang gi grong sngags 'di rnams kyang ral pa theg tshad re khud pas khyad byas pa ma gtogs bsam sbyor
mi nag pa gzhung ma dang khyad ye mi 'dug pa la brten/ rnying ma 'di gsha' ma zhig min pa 'dra snyams pa'i log rtog chen po yang skyes/ kha 'di rlung langs pa zhig ma
gtogs tshod zin par mi bdog pas skur ba'ang tho re ba 'debs/ bdag gi bla ma sku drin can des/ chos rje pa'i kha 'di me 'bar 'khrug ma ru gda'/ 'di 'dra ye ma gsung / tshig
legs nyes ci 'dra na'ang don zab po yin/ rdo ring rin po che rang gi sku ngo la yang rnying ma pa 'ja' lus la song ba bdun gzigs gda' las ngan ka ma gsog gsung yang yang
skyon/ pha grub pa can de dang khu bo sngags 'chang dbang po des kyang khyod kyis chos 'di'i bro ba ma myong ba yin/ nam gzhug rnying ma kho na byed dgos yong gsung ba
'phral du phebs pa nas de dag gi ngo bsrung phyir kha ma btang tsam las gding gi log lta gra ma nyams par gdog pa'i tshe/ dzo ki 'dis slob dpon padma'i sku rgyal po lugs
lta bas chog mi shes pa slob dpon nyid kyis phyag nas ma yin zer ba zhig khyer gda' bas gu ru rgyal po lugs pe kar gyis bod du sprul pa yin zer ba'i rdzun phugs der rdib/
slob dpon

padma'i sku gsum sgrub thabs zhus pas ratna gling pa'i gter ma dang don la khyad ye mi 'dug pas gter rdzun yin zer ba'i log rtog der khegs/ sngar skur zhus byas pa la 'gyod
pa bsam gyis mi khyab pa byung / da byed re snyam pa'i zhe dam drag po yang skyes/ de'i sdig sbyong la rnying ma bka' gter gyi chos 'chad nyan yod do cog zhus nas spyir
gzhan la rgya cher spel/ khyad par gang rnying ma la sdang ba'i sa phyogs su grub mtha' rkang 'then byed pa'i dam bca' byas/ ngan 'gro'i lam nas bzlog pa 'di khong gi drin
yin/ dpe rul 'ga' yis mi dge'i bshes byas shing / /sngags rul 'ga' yis spyod la sems khrel bas/ /mi rul kho bos las ngan tshabs chen bsags/ /bu rul bdag nyid dmyal ba'i
lam du chas/ /de tshe 'phags pa'i yul nas gangs can 'dir/ byon nas zab mo'i gdams pa stsal ba'i mthus/ /zab mo'i chos la yid ches dad pa thob/ /bsams shing sku drin mi chung
che bar 'khums/ /mgo bo la ya ma'i nad tshabs che bas zhwa gyon du ye mi 'dod/ mgo phyogs yo la skrangs nas tsha dpal mi bzod pa tsam yod/ mgo bo'i pags pa srab mo mang
po ling gis zhus yong ba sogs yang mo zhig yod pa yang 'dis gnang ba'i bhru rlung la nyams len byas pas gzhi med du bud song ba yin no/ lo de'i dbyar zhabs drung bstan
pa'i drung gis gsol ba btab pa'i zhor la pha rdo rje 'chang chen po'i drung du nag po chen po'i srung

'khor thun mong min pa dang bogs 'byin nyams khrid du zhus/ mtshams dam po byas sgom dang bsnyen pa stabs gcig tu byas pas ngo mtshar ba'i ltas kyang kha re byung ste yi ge
bdun pa 'bru 'bum gnyis song / de ma thag zangs gri can gyi gtor ma la bsten pa'i bsnyen pa byas dus rgya 'dre shed ka yin nam rgyal po'i cho 'phrul du ni gda'/ sprel kham
pa che tshad cig dngos su byung ba brdungs pas ming med du song ba zhig kyang byung / thun gtor 'bul mkhan med par gar song ma byung ba'ang lan gnyis tsam byung mod/ byi
