ba bzhin gyis khyer ba yin nam gang yin ni mi shes lo de'i btsas chod g.yul dbar la bdag gi bla ma dam pa de kog chung ma bya ba'i chab tshan la phebs kyi gda' ba nas/
bdag gi'ang rkang pa la phan zer phyags phyi byas 'gro ba'i khungs su yod skabs chos mdzad legs bshad pas/ spyir nged la rnam pa kun tu log sgrub rkang 'dren rten 'brel
'phyugs thabs grangs med pa zhig byed bzhin pa'i mu dang / bdag gis sde pa'i nang gzan byis gzhon zhig la skye ba sngar ma'i las lta bu yin nam/ dga' tshor chen bo zhig yong
gi 'dug pa nas byams po byas pa la mi theg pa'i khungs byas/ thabs du ma nas smad cing zhu log phul nas yab yum gcen dang bcas pa'i bka' bkyon yang lan mang du phab/
khyad par bla chen sku drin can de'i drung du skur zhus byed kyi 'dug zer gzhi med kyi zhu log khams chen po zhig phul gda' bas thugs 'ur/

chab tshan la phebs pa'i lam bar gyi sde pa zhal ngo dpon g.yog rdzong zhol pa sogs gshegs skyel dang byin rlabs zhu ba'i khrom dmar smug tu 'khyil ba zhig gi khrod du bdag
gi mtshang nas brus pa'i bka' bkyon drag po yun ring la dos drag pa zhig gnang / gdings na gnod ye med na'ang 'jigs pa dang ngo tsha bas da lta rang sa 'di la dim na dim
na bsam pa ma gtogs/ bla chen drung la log lta dang yi chad cig kyang ma skyes/ de nas chab tshan khar phebs/ gzims gur du bzhugs pa na bla ma rdo rje 'chang de'i drung
du shog gsungs phyin pas/ zhal mdzum mdzad nas drung bla ma pa 'khrungs sa mnga' ris par song ba'i skyon gyis 'di yin gyi brtag dpyad bya long ye med par mi mang de'i gseb
tu sma phab sgyu blug kha g.ya' tsag tsag pa mang po zhig gsungs song ste/ khyod kyis rlog tshan byed pa lta ci smos/ ngas ga le ltas pas bzhin 'gyur ba tsam yang mi 'dug
/a tho yin thugs la btags/ dam tshig dang drin som par gda' bas bzang gsung / bya ba 'di dang 'di 'dra byed par rtsom pa las 'di dang 'di dag lan brgya phrag byas pa'ang
skyon chung ba yin gsung ba sogs bdag gi bag la nyal dang bstun pa'i bslab bya mang po zhig mdzad/ bdag rang yang yus kyis bsnags nas mchi ma mang po shor/ snga phyi'i
byung tshul 'ga' zhig kyang zhus pas/ ngas los go /da byon/ yang khos rin po che'i drung na dug shags byas zhu log 'bul gyi 'dug zer labs na drung bla ma pas rang

re gnyis ka la skyon du yong / mchi ma phyis la byon gsung ba bzhin bla chen rin po che'i drung du phyin/ sngar 'khyud bzhin gyi phyags phyi byas/ bdag gi bla ma drin can 'di
khro ba mnga' la 'dzin pa spangs pa zhig bdog pas myur du thugs 'ur ba de sangs nas bka' lung gnang ba sogs brtse skyong mdzad/ lar da bsam dus 'am bus de'i tshe bla chen
dam pa de'i drung du paN chen ma ti'i chos spyod rab gsal gyi lung zhig ma gtogs dbang dang lta ci gzhan chos kyang ye ma thob mod/ de skabs gang shes pa'i yon tan de
thams cad khong gis bslabs pa dang / lo brgyad nas bcu bdun gyi bar pha ma'i tshab/ blon chen gyi tshab/ g.yog po'i tshab thams cad mdzad nas tha na za lugs tshun chod bslabs
pa'i drin can bla na med pa zhig yin pa la yin par ngo shes par byas nas khong gis nga gsod na'ang 'os yin bsam pa ma gtogs 'di'ang min bsam pa sems la ma shar/ ding
sang 'di na dbang brgya phrag mang po zhus/ chos 'chad tshad la sba tshangs byed/ 'phral gyi lto gos thams cad sbyangs/ 'gro na rta skyon/ sdod na gdan bting / gar phyin
kyang legs legs zhu zhu kho na yong ba sogs bdag gis drin tshad med pa bskyangs pa 'dras khong rang tshos mngon sum du ma 'os pa byas pa la cung zad labs pa na lag na yod
na brdeb/ bla ma pa la rgyal 'gong zhugs bya ba dang / smyo 'dug zer ba sogs gtam mang po lab/ yid chad ye dgos pa med bzhin du yid chad mang po

byed/ gzhi byes phyi nang med du skur pa kho na 'debs pa 'di tsho mthong tsa na nga rang gi de dus kyi bsam sbyor de la skyon ye ma byung ba 'dug go bcad snyam dga' spro dung
dung ba skye'i gda'/ de ltar byas pa'i rten 'brel ma 'phyugs pa yin yong / bla chen dam pa 'di las phyis su chos kyi sku drin bsam gyis mi khyab pa zhig thob pa yin no/
skye bo dman dang dam pa'i khyad par dag /byas pa shes dang mi shes 'dis 'byed ces/ /sngon byon mkhas pas bsgrags pa la dpags na/ /tha chad bdag kyang dam pa yin tshod
'dug /'dug mod khyod kyi yon tan nyin skar mtshungs/ /mtshungs mod skyon gyi rnam grangs bsam las 'das/ /'das kyang dam par rlom pa'i ma rabs khyod/ /khyod la skur 'debs
byed mkhan 'di rang mkho/ /mkho yang mkho ste mang yang mang nges shes/ /shes ldan gzur gnas kun gyis bkur stir byas/ /byas shes dam pa du mas lan brgyar bsngags/ /bsngags
'os mkhas pa'i drung na bdag re mdzes/ mdor na lo 'di yan gtso bor bla ma rdo rje 'chang chen po de nyid zla re zla gnyis ma gtogs skad cig kyang ma bral bar bsten/ bla
chen 'jam pa'i dbyangs nyid lus dang grib ma bzhin du bsten nas ci byas chos su song ba zhig yin la/ bdag gi bla ma 'di nyi ma phyed yan chad thugs dam kho na la bzhugs/
de nas gsung chos gsung pa sogs mdzad/ rgyun

gyi thugs dam mtshan phyed tsam la thun gtor phul tshog pa dang / gtor sgrub sogs kyi tshe grol ba dang / nam langs pa mnyam po byas pa'ang mang po byung / tho rang lhag pa
ni rtag par 'gor/ thun mtshams thams cad du phyag dpe bris zhus kho na ma gtogs zhabs 'chag dang / bzhugs gral dang / bzhugs yong la zhal 'phros dang / ri skor sogs ye mi
mdzad pas bdag kyang gar gnas su rdzog ge sdod/ chos kyi bya ba gang la'ang sems mi dub tsam 'di de dus nas goms pa'i lag rjes su gda' ste mdor na 'di yan chod skyid nges
shes la chos 'phel ba'i skabs so/ /brgya phrag bskal par mtshan yang rnyed dka' ba'i/ /bla ma brten nas theg mchog zab mo'i chos/ /thos dang bsam pas nyin mtshan 'da'
ba 'di/ bgrang pas bsod nams bsags pa'i lag rjes lags/ gzhan yang lo de'i sos ma rgan mo drin chen de'i phyags phyi byas/ nged rang sku mched bzhi char dpon g.yog shin tu
mang ba dang bcas jo nang mjal du byon/ zhag kyang kha cig bzhugs/ rgyal ba'i mchod rten dpal yon can la zhabs skor yang nyin mtshan du ngal ba med pa dang / dgon pa la
bsnyen bkur yang bsam gyis mi khyab pa mdzad/ rten gsum rnams kyang zhib par mjal tshe rten bshad mdzad mkhan gzims dpon sgrub chen pa bya ba des/ rdo nag po la ma Ni dkar
po 'bur dod yod pa zhig bstan nas 'di kun mkhyen chen po'i phyag shan rdor ba'i brdar la ma Ni rang byon du byung ba yin gsung ba la/ dang po ni 'di 'dra

sgam 'di na mi bdog /kun mkhyen chen po sdor dkar ba de la phyag shan yong ba dgod bro zhus pas skyengs nas mun ne bzhugs 'dug /de'i tshe gdan sa la chos rje nam bzang pa yod
pa khong gis gzhi len bzabs shoms mang po byas/ khong 'di pa 'jig rten rgod yang rgod la gtso bor yang 'don/ dgra sbud pas 'dul mkhan du gda' bas ston shoms de tsho bza'
chen po gda'/ bab thob tu song na khong nged kyi bla ma dam pa de'i gdan sa dngos yin pas phyag 'bul chos zhu ba sogs byed dgos rgyu yin na'ang phyis su nye gnas ngan
pa zhig gi dbang du song / bdag gi bla ma de'i thugs mang po dkrugs/ skyid sbug la tsha len byed pa sogs dgos med mang po zhig byas yod pas tshig pa log sbam me bzhag pa
yin no/ /bzhugs gral der khong dpon slob tshos re mos su chos skad kyi khungs 'dra byed kyi 'dug pa na/ ngas rnying ma ba rnams la dam tshig sa ma ya 'bum sde bya ba yod
zer/ rang re gsar ma ba'i dam tshig rtsa ltung bcu bzhi po 'di ga yin/ da srung mkhan ye mi gda' bas grangs ka mang nyung gang yod kyang khyad cig mi gda' byas pas/ khong
la 'phog thengs shig sbob be bzhugs dgos pa'ang byung / khams pa dkon cog rin chen zer ba'i sgrub pa po bdag gi bla ma las zab lam thob nas rtse gcig tu bsgoms pas mngon
shes thogs med du mnga' bar grags pa zhig yod pa des/ nged cag chog yin nyog yin zer ba'i lung bstan kha re byas/ sgrub chen ma byings kyi'ang mos gus dag snang nyams 'ur
sogs mang po mdzad/ nga rang yang

bsams tsa na 'di yin med pa la snang yul lam lam mang po byas pa zhig ni byung / nged der sdod ring sku 'bum chen mo'i dril bu rlung pos nam bskyod dus/ oM AHhU~M hoHzer ba
'dra mo'i gsum brdungs kho nar nges par byung ba ni de dus kyi mi phal cher la rgyus yod pa de yin mod/ jo nang dam pa'i gnas de bdag gis mthong / /mthong ba'i mod la dad
gus spu long g.yo/ /g.yo med sems la dga' bde'i ting 'dzin skyes/ /skyes chen gong ma'i byin rlabs yin nam bsam/ /bsam gtan gyis myos sgrub chen pho mo'i tshogs/ /tshogs
gsum lam la brtson pa de kun yang / /yang srid spong la the tshom mi 'dug snyam/ /yid ches dad dang spro ba lhag par 'phel/ /la las dam pa yin zhes lung bstan byed/ /la
las spyi bos btud nas gsol ba gdab/ /la las 'khral 'chong lding zhing gar stabs sgyur/ /la las ngu zhing 'chang nas kho bo bzung / /phal cher grub pa'i gnas 'dir bdag gis
sngon/ /dal 'byor don yod las 'ga' byas sam snyam/ /da dung ljongs 'dir tshe dang sgrub pa'i rgyun/ /snyom rgyu byung na bsam pa'i re smon byung / /de nas lo de'i mjug
nas snang tshul 'di 'dra zhig shar te/ bdag chen chos ky-i rje khri thog rin po che dang / bdag gi thu bo lugs gnyis la mkhyen pa'i spyan rnam par gsal ba'i sa skyong chos
kyi rgyal po'i drung gnyis bka' gros mdzad/ mgyogs pa'i bskul ma cung zad gzims byang slob dpon sngon po zhes pa'i rtog ge ba rgan po zhig yod pa des ri sgul mtsho bskyod
'dra mo byas/ rta nag po'i

mnga' ris pa tshang gi mi sna/ zha lu pa rab rgyas zhu ba'i ham pa dang blo shed mtshungs pa med la chos kyi skal bas 'phongs pa zhig 'dug pa de rdzong du yang yang yongs nas
zhu'i 'dug pas kyang rkyen byas te/ mtshan nyid bslab gnyer byed dgos pa'i zhal ta lan cig min par byon byung ba/ spyir nged la chos 'di'i las 'phro med nges shig yin
gda' bas/ pha yod tsa na bu'i dpes nga rang lo bcu gcig bcu gnyis kyi dus dang po'i gnas gsar chos mdzad pa de'i skad cha thos pas gang gi sgo nas mi mnyam rgyu med/ ngas
kyang de las lhag pa zhig byas la skad ston pa tsam gyis phyir rgol tsho 'gyel yong ba zhig byed bsam pa'ang byung / bgro gleng mdzad mkhan 'dra mthong tsa na'ang dga' mo
zhig yong gi 'dug pas mtshan nyid cig bslab dgos snyam/ sdom gsum/ rigs gter/ mdo sde rgyan/ mngon rtogs rgyan/ tshad ma rnam 'grel gyi gzhung rnams sbam 'dzin byas yongs
su rdzogs par bzung yod pa la/ de dus ni sngags smyon bgrangs pa'i byin rlabs can cig dgos rgyu yin/ chos rje chen po yang thugs gnyer gyis g.yengs thugs dam ma mdzad
pas sku tshe bar chad du song ba yin/ sngags sgrongs gsung mkhan kho na byung / phyis su sbyor drug zhus pas da sgom zhig byed dgos pa 'dug bsam pa zhe thag pa nas skyes/
sngar bshad pa ltar rmi lam la brtags na'ang shes shing phan thogs pa zh-ig ye mi yong bar go /mtshan nyid pa'i bla ma slob dpon 'ga' zhig

gi rnam thar 'dra mthong thos byung bas kyang hu hu de tsho na yang stong pa ka 'dug /stabs nyes na dge 'dun gyi dbyen khams po che mi gsog pa'i nges pa mi 'dug pas/ da rang
mkhas pa i yong mi shes pa'i ban ling las grub pa yong nges shes pa'i thugs dam zhig dga' ba 'dra snyam blo thag chod song ba nas zhu khrol dum pa go le zhus te/ spyir
yang sde pa dpon po'i rigs 'di la ma zhus par byas na gnang chen gang byas tshabs su 'gro/ zhus na sbeg btang bas e yong zhus kyang mi yong gsung ba de srol du gda' ba dang
/ khyad par nged cag byis par song bas bslab gnyer 'di mthar thon zhig mi yong ba 'dra tshul sogs zhus pas ni/ 'brug dang 'brug ris su song nas bslab gnyer ma nus pa'i
snyad 'dogs yin dgongs pa las mi gda'/ bdag gi rogs byed pa'i dbang yod ni su'ang med pa la brten de las 'os ma byung / de phyin grwa sa gang du phyin kyang yags po kho
na ma gtogs lod po su la'ang mi 'dug mod/ 'on kyang rta nag na bdag chen 'jam pa'i dbyangs ngag gi dbang phyug bzhugs kyi 'dug pas gtso bor de kho na la bsams/ rta nag der
gsang sngags kyi 'chad nyan byed kyi yod 'phros thos pas zhor la sngags chos 'dra thob pa srid snyam nas cis kyang byed dgos na rta nag la 'gro zhus pa bdag chen gyi bka'
bkod yin gda' bas de gcig pu dgongs pa mthun nas ma zhus kyang thag chod tshar gda'/ tha mal rgan po 'bum phrag 'dus pa las/ /sngags rig byis pa chung

ngu khyad par che/ /rgyu skar lus stobs rdzogs pa mtha' yas pa/ /zla dbang tshes ma thag pas zil gyis gnon/ /'on kyang sprang po'i glu la nyan mkhan med/ /med bzhin ban ling
byas pas a thang chad/ /chad rgyu gang yod chad pa'i bdag sems de/ /de ltar yid mug ngang nas gzhan dbang song / /zla ba bcu gcig pa'i nang du bdag gis phag tu thab chas
kyi bshas mang po bsam gyis mi khyab pa byas/ mnga' zhabs la 'u lag mang po bskul ba rnams la nas sogs cha rkyen bkal/ bdag dpon slob btsun pa'i khungs slob gnyer ba sum
cu tsam dang / nged rnams skyel mkhan gzims dpon sangs rgyas zhes dbus gtsang na grags thon pa'i yags po zhig yod pa des gtsos drung 'khor mchor la rags pa'i rta pa rkang
thang mang chen mang ba dang bcas sde srid chen po dbyar mthong la 'byon pa 'dra mo zhig byas nas phyin/ de nub mkha' rur bsdad/ rmi lam dga' mo zhig ma byung / tshig
pa za se ba zhig la langs nas phyin rnga mo 'phrang gi de na mar/ sra brtan brag la yid kyis bris pa'i sgo/ /sgo de'i nang na chu gter chen po'i ljongs/ /ljongs der de dang
de 'dra 'dug pa mthong / /mthong mod tshe 'dir skal ba de las med/ /de nas chu 'gram zhig na mar skyo chod de yi mug long nge / 'a'i 'a'i bsam pa zhig gi ngang la yongs/
/nyi ma'ang ze re re bzhud 'gro'i 'dug /rlung po drag po zhig gis rgyab nas 'ded pa 'dra ba byas/ thams cad kyang mgo phur gyin bzabs

sprod tsho thal ba tshub be byas/ rta mgyogs po gtong gin 'dug pa na bdag rta thog tu sdug gnyid rib be ba zhig byung ba'i tshe/ dbang sngon mdog mtshungs bong bu'i sras chibs
shing / dbang sngon ltar gsal phying pa'i na bza' can/ /dbang sngon lhun po nyi mas 'khyud pa'i gzi/ /dbang sngon la sogs nor bu'i rgyan cha can/ /grangs med rkang thang
phub mdung 'dzin pas bskor/ /rtsol med shugs kyis bgrod pa'i gom stabs can/ /thogs med dbyings nas khyod la skyob tu yong / /snying med po khyod 'jigs par ma byed kye/
/pha rgan grub pa can des nga yi bu/ /bdud kyis khyer na mi rung myur rgyug ces/ /bskul nas 'ongs kyi sems la gzengs bstod la/ /bla ma sgoms la gsol ba thob cig gsung /
/las kyi rlung gis ded nas yongs pa'i tshe/ /dam nyams grib kyis nyams rtog mgo bo phur/ /gyag khyer thal tshub kha cig 'byung nges zhes/ /brda ston 'di ltar byas la gor
ma chag /de nub rta nag ri khud du bsdad/ /gzhi len dang 'bul ba byed mkhan 'ga' re 'dug pa gar song ma shes/ der yang rmi lam ngan po zhig byung / sang thub bstan rnam
rgyal du sleb/ bdag chen 'jam pa'i dbyangs kyis sku drin la khyer ba med pas skyong ba'i 'go tshugs/ /tshogs der mang ja/ spyi 'gyed/ rin po che'i drung du 'bul ba bsam gyis
mi khyab pa phul/ nged rnams grwa pa yar ma rgan mar ma gzhon sum cu nas bcu drug gi bar gzhon hrags kyang bdog pa dang / gnas

gsar ba stobs ches pas phugs phan thogs yong snyam/ lha 'dam klu 'dam byed kyi 'dug na'ang phyogs su lhung na bstan pa la gnod nges su 'dug pas spyi lding ba byas mod/ gsar
'grogs dang phugs khugs la re yin yod/ khams mnga' ris khang tshan so so ja 'dren 'bul ba khas phyug legs legs mo ji snyed cig byas/ sang de nas bsdus chen pa'i khrod du
zhugs/ skyor mgo yang ngas byas dgun chos dang po de shin tu 'phel ba zhig byung / de nas ring po ma lon pa na sde 'khrug cig byung ste/ rgyu ni slob dpon padmas/ bdud sprul
gnyis kyis bstan pa de: ming med nyid du byed par 'gyur: ces lung bstan pa'i slob dpon bkras brtan pa dang 'khur nag pa bya bas khams mnga' ris kyi 'du long khams chen
zhig gi rgyun tshugs pa star chags song ba de las byung / rkyen ni btsun gzhon skyes gzugs pa kha cig gis byas te/ nyin gcig ba zings rta zings la 'khrugs/ nged snga chos
zhu mi rnams dmag gseb la mi thar ba tsam yang byung ste/ de nyin 'khrug yun ring po rang ma byung / yang bskyar nas sde 'khrugs langs/ nyi ma rtse shar tsam la 'dzings/
dka' bcu rab 'byams su mtshan gsol ba mang po dang slob dpon tshos khog tu zhugs/ zhen pho rus su brtags pa'i bdud zhugs pa'i shar shar mang pos srog 'bul ba byas/ nyi
ma phyed yol tsam gyi bar 'khrugs/ chos rar rab byung gcig thang ro la btang /

gzhan kha re'ang bsad grag /brang khang so so la 'tshang drag byas skad cha shod thebs med pa mang po zhig byed kyi gda'a'o/ /sde 'khrugs mi bsad rta sgyel zhe sdang dang /
/btsun gzhon grogs su bsten pa'i 'dod chags dang / /nga mkhas nga che nga rgyal 'gying 'gros 'di/ /gti mug mun ne 'thibs pas lan nam snyam/ /mi tshe gzhung lugs sbyangs
pa'i lag rjes la/ /che 'dod grags 'dod phan tshun skor sdebs kyis/ /dge 'dun dbyen byas thar med dmyal bar mchong / /las stabs 'di 'dra bsams shing snying rlung ldang / /bdag
chen 'jam pa'i dbyangs thugs 'ur/ /phyag rdzas rnams chibs drel mdzad rdzong bda' grub/ /chibs sga tshun sgron grub 'dug pa la/ nged 'khor bcas dang skyang 'dur ba sogs
spyi lding ba'i khungs kha cig yod pas zhu ba byas kyang chibs drel ni sgor ma thub/ zhabs drung nyid du'u thug mang po zhus pas thugs lhod tsam gnang / dmag rnams spe'u
zhig la 'tshang zhing 'dug nas/ bdag gis 'di pa la gande zhig gnang ba zhu zhus nas dzam dzam mdzad pas gyes tsam byung / de nub bdag snang tshul de dag mthong bas stod
'tshangs khams chen po zhig 'chi ba la thug pa zhig byung skabs bdag gi bla ma de yid la dran pa tsam gyis nad de las grol mod/ de nas bzung yun ring po'i bar nad de 'phral
du langs nas zhe sun la nyen che ba zhig byung / bdag chen rin po che'i gsung gis bdag la do dam gyis gsungs ltar gang shes kyis lab lob byas pas chings 'dra

mo zhig 'grig skabs/ zhabs drung rin po che byang stag lung pas gdan 'dren byung ba nas dbus la byon/ bdag la dbu zhwa zhig gnang / nged tsho ma slebs bar yar byon/ re zhig
ya tshor thugs gnyer gzhug skyong mdzad pa ma gtogs/ blos btang na le mi yod bas 'bad pa mdzod gsung ba sogs bslab bya mang du mdzad/ spyan chab phyungs nas thegs/ bla ma
de'i phyags phyir phyin na bsams pa kang kang byung zhing / phyin na mnyes pa'i gsung mang po byon te/ bo dong nas grol cha ma byung ba nas bdag tsho sems 'phreng po zhig
la yar log /bo dong bon gnas zhes bya ba na dgon chung sdod mkhan tsam med pa'i bla brang 'du khang spyil chung sogs shoms la sdod spro ba zhig yod pa der ming thub bstan
chos 'khor gling du btags nas bsdad/ mnga' zhabs kyi drag pa 'dras thug tshul yang phul/ rgyun pa'i thug tshul dang dus ja sogs sde pa nas gnang / ma rgan mo des grwa
pa rnams la phogs kha re'ang gnang / bdag gis cher mi shes kyang gra ma 'thor na legs pa 'dra snyam 'chad nyan gyi khungs byas/ spyi chos la bka' gdams gzhung drug dang
/ rigs gter rang 'grel sogs lung mang po byas/ bsdus ra che chung thams cad ngas btang / slob dpon gnas chung pa bya ba bgro gleng bde la pra chal ba zhig bdog pa des so
so la phar tshad kyi thal 'phreng spyi don sogs btang / 'phral gyi sgrigs rnam gzhag thub bstan pa sor bzhag byas bsdad pa'i

tshe/ sa de grub thob 'dar phyar gyis bon po phung bar byas sa yin pas bon po'-i mchod rten dang sgrub khang mang po yod/ bon skyong ma bya ba'i gzhi bdag bdud mo shin tu thu
ba zhig yod pas der dpe mtshams byas tshad tshe yong gi med zer bred bred mo byed/ 'tshub kyang shin tu 'tshub pas nam la 'bod pa sogs dngos su'ang cho 'phrul thor bu
yong gi 'dug pa nas gzhan du spos pas dga' ru mi 'gro btul dgos snyam/ grwa pa thams cad la gcod gdan thog gcig ma'i khrid phog /nga rang gis kyang dmigs pa drag po mang
du btang / bon skyong ma'i spyan rten yin zer ba'i na thog chung ngu zhig yod par mtshan mo phyin zhing gcod byas pas zhag lnga tsam nas je 'jigs je 'jigs la song nas mi
tshugs pa tsam byung / chu kha na mar tshom tshom brad pa'i ngu choms kyi zer len thos pas snying don 'gro ba 'dra ba yong ba'ang byung / nub cig dngos su rkang pa nas brud
byung ba la gces 'dzin gtong ba'i khungs byas bzhag pas brgyal ba skad byung ba yin nam re zhig dran rgyu ma byung / cho chad nas rkang pa 'khyags nas dran pa rnyed byung
ba zhing shas gsum tsam zhig brud nas chu khar slab 'dug pa rkang pa chur song bar 'dug /de gar bsdad nas dge sbyor byas pas blo bde 'bol gyis song / tshar tshad kyang
yid ches pa 'grig /'tshub dang cho 'phrul thams cad rgyun chad pa zhig byung / rang sems bdud du langs pa ma gtogs pa/ /phyi rol bdud du grub ba ci yang med/ /dam chos

bdud kyi gcod yul bsgoms pa'i tshe/ /phyi nang bdud kyi dpung de dbyings su yal/ /bdag 'dzin a 'thas zhes pa'i phung po 'di/ /bdag gzhan 'gro ba'i glud du byin pa'i tshe/ /bdag
dang gzhan du 'dzin pa ma grub pas/ /bdag med 'di la 'khyer mkhan ngas ma rnyed/ /der bla chen thugs rje can spyan drangs/ chos chung brgya rtsa sogs dam pa'i chos bsam
gyis mi khyab pa'i sku drin thob ste/ mdor na glang lo zla ba gsum pa nas dgu pa'i bar bon gnas dang bla brang dkar por chos gzhi bteg nas bslab gnyer 'phel zhing thams
cad la blo bskyed yang chen po byung / lo de'i dbyar mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen pa'i zhabs las gsung gi bdud rtsi thob pa yin na'ang 'di'i tshul rgyas par 'og tu 'byung
ngo / de nas thub bstan du 'dug pa'i nub cig nyang stod rgyal khang de rmi lam du gsal po byung / skor dgos pa'i ltas 'dra'ang 'dug pa dang / bdag gi bla ma de'i gsung
gis ngas bod na yod pa'i sbyor drug thams cad thob pa zhig bya snyam pa la paN chen nags rin lugs de ma thob/ da ngas zhu mi thub khyod kyis thob na de gas chog pas 'brug
pa la zhus shog gsung ba nas de thams cad sgo bstun ston btsas ma ma tshar tsam la nyang bar rtsis kyi lha khang bskor ba la phyin/ rim gyis gnas der sleb/ a jo brtan pa'i
drung gis nu bo dang byis pa yin snyam pa'i bsnyas pa gtan nas ma mdzad/ dpe med kyi bla chen khams po che phyogs nas byon pa zhig yin pa tsam gyis mthong dang bsnyen

bkur dus khyad par ba dang nar ma thams cad du de las skyid pa byed ma myong ba 'dra ba sku drin bskyangs/ lha khang rnams su'ang dkar me snyan dar stobs cher phul/ smon lam
btab/ khyad par rgya phubs shar na mgon po 'bur dod shin tu ngo 'tshar ba zhig bzhugs pa'i drung du tshogs gtor rgyas pa phul ba'i dus snga rting du sku de la mtho tshad
zhus pas je che je che la song ba thams cad kyis mthun grub pa'i ngo mtshar yang byung / bka' brgyud bstan pa'i bdag po khyab bdag 'brug pa gcung smyon me tog la phebs
pa dang mjal/ gtum po ras chung lugs kyi rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor du dbang bzhi rdzogs pa dang / phag mo khams gsum ma'i byin rlabs lung dang bcas pa/ paN chen lugs kyi
sbyor drug rgyal dbang rje'i gsung la jo bzang bde legs pas zin bris mdzad pa rnams thob/ zhang dbon thugs yid gcig tu 'dres pa lta bu'i dgyes tshor brtse skyong mang po
mdzad/ grub thob kyi 'khor lo sgyur ba lce ston rin po che spyan drangs nas pha chos gtum chen dang / 'khor lo chen po'i rgya bod kyi yi ge rab tu mang po'i lung zhus/ grwa
pa rnams kyis spyi bsod grol/ dgun chos 'dzugs ran zer 'bod mi byung ba nas log 'gro bar brtsams pas/ lha mo de 'phreng ba'i rnam pas zhon rta sde pa'i chibs pa drag
shos gser bya zer ba zhig yod pa'ang glo bur du 'chi ba la thug /gzhan yang 'tshub kha re byung nas mchod gtor rgya cher phul/ dpe cha drag pa zhig gte ba'i tshul du mgon
khang du bzhag /lo phyi ma la'ang yong ba'i

khas len byas pas snang ba rang sems kyi rten 'brel gyis phan par byung / pha gir sdod pa'i ring lha mo'i gtor khang du mtshams dam po byas mgon po'i bsnyen pa kha gso dang
/ lha mo'i gzhi bsnyen cig byas pa yid ches par byung / mdos bskang rgyas pa tshar gcig kyang phul/ nye bar brten na slu med lha 'di yis/ /nye bar bskul nas grub pa'i bsti
gnas su/ /nye bar sleb tshe chos ldan rgyal po des/ /nye bar mchod cing bkur sti phud dud mdzad/ /grub pa'i slob dpon padmas byin rlabs shing / /grub brnyes la zhwa'i
gdung gis brten pa'i gzhi/ /grub pa'i gnas 'dir bde skyid dpal 'byor dang / /grub dbang gnyis las gdams pa'i dpal 'byor thob/ /ya mtshan 'bur du dod pa'i bris sku'i drung
/ /dge mtshan gong 'phel yong ba'i ngo mtshar mthong / /dus mtshan lha mo gnas pa'i pho brang du/ /rtags mtshan gzhung dang mthun pa'i bsnyen pa byas/ /de nas bo dong du
phyir 'ongs/ der yang ser sbreng gzhi len sogs bkur sti phud dud phun sum tshogs par gnang / bdag gi bla ma dam pa de las thugs rje chen po'i dmar khrid sbyor rtsa ma'i
khrid dang / skye med do pa'i lugs kyi gcod khrid cig zhus/ slar bo dong bla brang dkar por phyin dgun chos cho 'phrul gyi smon lam sogs kyang srol ji lta bar byas/ bdag
gi bsam pa la nga rang gis chos 'di shes pa zhig dang phan thogs pa rang yong ba mi 'dug na'ang / 'di 'dra byas nas grwa pa 'di tsho'i gseb tu yon

tan can bstan pa la phan pa 'dra'ang e yong / tha na'ang re zhig chos mgo thon 'gro ba 'dug snyam dad dos byas/ sde pa la zhus nas bdag chen rin po che byang stag lung na bzhugs
pa'i drung du gdan 'dren pa'i bang chen yang yang btang / lo bcu dgu lon pa'i stag lo zla ba gsum pa nas zug 'di yin med pa la dran med du yun ring po brgyal 'gro ba
de 'dra nyin re la'ang lan kha re byas pa zhig byung ba nas bo dong rdzong du shog gsung nas der phyin sman pa rnams la ni byed rgyu 'di yin zhig ye mi 'dug /bying ba chen
po'i 'phreng yin pa 'dra gsungs/ gegs sel 'dra gnang byung na'ang phan rgyu cher ma byung ba'i khar je lod la brgyal ba de sad yong khar stod 'tshangs 'dra ba'i zug chen
po bzod glags med pa yong ba la de kha'i ngang nas brgyal 'gro ba nyin re'ang lan bco lnga nyi shu tsam yong gi 'dug /brgyal ba'i tshe zla bo rnams kyis rol mo byas rna
ba'i rtsar ting shags brdungs pa dang re zhig nas dran pa rnyed yong ba de 'dra zhig gis zla ba drug mnar ba'i mthar nub cig chu me la th-im pa'i rtags kyang byung / drung
chen ser po bas rtsa ltas nas cang mi gsung bar bdag la gzigs te shugs ring zhig bton spyan chab phyungs nas thegs song mtshams/ bdag gi bla ma de gdan drangs phebs
nas mgo la phyag bzhag nas 'am bu la gzigs la thugs lhod de bzhugs shig gsungs cung zad thugs dam la bzhugs nas da rtsa zhig gzigs dang gsung ba la rtsa dang dbugs gnyis
char sor chud nas shi tshar tshar ba la bla ma dam pa'i thugs

rjes bsos pa ma gtogs thengs shig gi bar la yab yum drin can de dag gis dbu mdzad pa'i ming sring gnyen bshes thams cad thugs khral la gtad/ sha sdug 'bu sdug mnar yun ring
ba'i thag chod pa zhig byung na'ang de'i sang de nas je bde la song nas sing nge drag /de'i bar la sdig pa dag pa yin nam phan gnod byed pa'i lha 'dre thams cad thogs med
du mthong gi 'dug /nad yun de tsam gyi bar la bdag gi nu bo nor bzang drung des nyin mi dal mtshan mi gnyid skyo dub ngal ba cung zad kyang med par nad g.yog mdzad pas
drin che bar bdog /las ngan tshabs cher bsags pa'i rgyu byas shing / /rkyen ngan dam nyams khor yug bsten pa'i mthus/ /nad ngan de yis mnar yun de tsam byas/ /zungs ngan
'chi bdag kha ru yud kyis chas/ /mkhyen ldan sman pa'i mdzad dgos thams cad zad/ /brtse ldan gnyen gyi tshogs rnams thugs khral kyang / /tshad ldan bla ma'i byin rlabs gcig
pu yis/ /skal ldan kho bo ma shi tshe thar byung / /yun ring de la nyi na mtshan khyad med par/ /brtse bas bskyangs pa'i drin can gcung po khyod/ /bsod nams 'di yis bdud
btul chos 'khor bskor/ /nyon mongs nad chen gso bar gyur ces smon/ /de nas bla brang dkar por 'dag sbyar byas/ oM gsum ma bzhi 'bum zhig dang gur gyi yi ge bdun pa 'bru
'bum zhig kyang bzlas/ khams bde zhing dge sbyor kyang 'phel bar byung / de grol nas slar nyang stod la phyin/

dpal lha mo'i gtor khang du mtshams bsdams lha mo'i sgrub bsnyen zhig dang / tshe sgrub kyi bsnyen pa rtags thon pa zhig byas/ rin chen sgang gi rdzong 'debs pa'i sa chog gis
gsung / de la dmigs nas gur gyi bsnyen pa kha gso zhig byas pa 'di yan la yi ge bdun pa 'bum phrag brgya dang nyi shu tsam song gda'/ der nyang stod rgyal khang chos sde'i
mkhan po gyis gsungs nas byas/ sgrub mchod dga' mo zhig 'dug pa de'i mkhan po'i dkyil 'khor kye rdor yin zer man ngag lugs kyi rdul tshon du sgrub mchod rgyas par byas/
klang sder gyi mar khal du ma byung ba thams cad rgya phub shar nub tu mar mer phul/ cho 'phrul dang thug byung bas mtshan mo yun ring po bskor ba dang smon lam zhe dag
pa nas byas/ nya'i nyin skya ser shin tu mang po zhig la dbu ma lugs kyi sems bskyed rgyas pa zhig bsgrubs/ slar lha mo'i gtor khang du mtshams byas nas bde mchog lU hi
pa'i bsnyen pa zhig byas/ de phyogs kyi brel ba phal cher chod nas yos lo la bo dong duu sleb/ der bdag gi bla ma de'i zhal nas da lo bsnyen rdzogs zhig byas pa drag /bdag
chen rin po che spyan drangs nas mkhan po zhus/ ngas las slob byed gsung ba la bslab gnyer 'di ma rdzogs ring bsnyen rdzogs then tsam byas na ji ltar yong / byed par
shar na rje btsun chen pos rje sa chen la zhus pa bzhin bsnyen rdzogs kyi mkhan po thub dbang rang byon byung na'ang / rje nyid la zhu ba min pa gzhan la mi 'tshol zhus pas
spyan chab gnang zhing yun ring du bzhad nas/ bsnyen rdzogs de

da lo ga cis kyang grub na ma grub na mdzod/ dgongs pa de yin na ngas mkhan po los byed/ las slob de rin po che tshar pa 'os gsung pa ltar mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen pa'i
zhal snga nas spyan drangs/ rang lo nyi shu lon pa mdzes byed kyi lo chu stod zla ba'i tshes brgyad/ grib tshod rkang pa gsum/ nyi ma gung tshig ma yol tsam la bkra shis
kyi gtsug lag khang dpal ldan lcang lo can gyi pho brang du mkhan po don gyi slad du mtshan nas smos te gnas brtan chen po kun dga'i zhabs dang / las kyi slob dpon mkhan
chen thams cad mkhyen pa tshar pa'i zhal snga nas/ gsang ste ston pa'i slob dpon mnga' ris bla chen/ grib tshod pa mkhas pa'i dbang po rje btsun dbon rin po che ngag dbang
bstan pa'i rdo rje/ zhu ba po sde snod 'dzin pa'i gnas brtan sangs rgyas bzang po dang bcas pa'i dbus su bsnyen par rdzogs pa dge slong gi sdom pa legs par thob ste/ 'di
na sangs rgyas bstan pa rin chen sgron/ /'bar ba'i snod ni dge slong nyid yin la/ /bla med sngags kyi ston pa rab mchog kyang / /dge slong rdo rje 'dzin pa nyid du gsungs/
/de ltar shes nas bstan pa mtha' dag la/ /bshad dang sgrub pa'i bya ba lhur len phyir/ /zhugs la yongs su rdzogs pa'i sdom pa mchog /bsod nams bgo skal nyid du bdag gis
thob/ /bdag chen rin po che yang dbus nas yar phebs byung ba ltar/ nged cag nyang stod dang bo dong sgrags pa'i slob gnyer ba drug cu phyin dang bcas slar rta nag

la phyin/ sngon ma'i slob dpon des gsang yum grangs med bsten pa sogs phyogs du ma nas mdor bstan byung bas cam ste bzhag /rje btsun dbon rin po che spyan drangs / dbyar chos
dang po'i thog nas rigs 'bring la zhugs/ bdag chen rin po ches gsung ngag rin po che zhig 'dzugs pa gnang byung ba ltar dga' bzhin du zhus na'ang shin tu bsdus pa zhig
las ni ma byung / 'bad pa cher byas thos bsam sgom pa stabs gcig gi khungs byas/ 'jam pa'i dbyangs des rgya chen chos kyi bcud/ /bcud bzang nyung ngu'i tshig gis bzungs
ba'i tshe/ /tshe rabs sngon nas bsags pa'i bag chags las/ /las 'di bdag gi yin snyam dga' spro thob/ /phyogs der phyin pas mdo sde 'di yin mod/ /snyam nas dga' spros rgyud
phyug ba spu langs/ /dgos med zar zir dbang du ma song bar/ /gang gsungs de la dmigs pa rtse gcig bsgoms/ /ston de'ang rta nag nyid du bsdad kun mkhyen rta nag pas mdzad
pa'i sde bdun rab gsal dang / paN chen kong pos mdzad pa'i rtags rigs blo rigs la sbam 'dzin byas/ sngar sor gnas chung pa des skyon can yin zer ba'i chad de chod de mang
po bslab dus skyon da lta'i 'dis chog pa yod/ /gsar slob ye dgos pa med snyam ma bzung / mkhas pa chen po gzhung lugs kyi gnad dgongs pa'i dbon rin po che 'dis gzhung
gi go don longs pa mang po bslabs pa rnams 'bad pas bzung / khyad par tshad 'bras de sgom phyogs dang mthun po zhig 'dug

pa nas nan tan byas pas dga' mo zhig shes/ dgun chos dang rting sogs kyi dus/ spyan yin par thal/ lha'i spyan yin pa'i phyir zhes sogs tshul gsum pa can gyi rtags tshig la
skyon can gyi thal 'gyur gtong mkhan sogs go ba med pa'i skya phye sngo phye tsho'i lan ni mi shes/ gzhung tshig rtags bsal du bkod pa'i bgro gleng byed pa la rab 'byams
pa chen po don ldan tsho'i gya po pher ba tsam byung / de'ang sgrigs la skyur khar bdag phar phyin la rtsa slob byed zhus pas/ khyod kyi shes rab kyi sgra la sems ma byas
pas mi yong gsungs mgas na/ grwa pa rnams kyis rgan mo phar phyin byas na 'phongs zer bkag /tshad ma mi byed ka med byung / sems la de ga yin phar phyin byas na 'phro la
mi lus pa zhig yod de bsam pa tsam byung ste/ gzhung gi dgongs pa rtogs pa phar zhog gis/ tshig gi brda tsam yang mi shes pa'i/ /rdo bcal sgrigs sogs zar zir mang po 'di/
/yon tan ming tu btags kyang skyon du go /mchod brjod skabs su 'bras bu sku gsum bstan/ /yang dag rtags kyis rgyu 'bras gtan la phab/ tshad 'bras sogs kyis phyi don bden
grub bkag /snga phyi mang po bdag gnyis rtsad nas phyung / /bstan bcos che 'dis lam rim zab mo bstan/ /bstan mod phyir ltas rnams kyis mthong ba med/ /med nges dbyangs
su len pa'i rdo bcal sgrigs/ /sgrig pa 'di la bstad so ci 'dug soms/ /kha

cig ki shar dos drag dwags po'i mda' rtsed bzhin/ /rkang lag sogs 'gyur bro pa'i sa bro bzhin/ /yar mchong mar mchong spre'u'i zlos gar bzhin/ /sngon byon mkhas pas 'di 'dra
e ma mdzad/ /dril ba'i lo ngo lnga'i bar mtshan nyid pa'i khungs yin/ rta nag rang du ni zla ba hril po bcu bzhi las ma bsdad/ der sdod pa'i bar gsung chos snga phyi chos
spyod/ rigs lung / mang ja sogs thams cad la 'tshog pa'i sngon ma gyes pa'i rting ma byas/ ras chod du a cang / chos khrims pa la zhu ba byas pa'i brel spyod kyang ma
byas par chos ra rigs lung thengs gcig tsam yang gcog ma myong / bdag rang a cang / nged rang gi grwa rigs tshun la mtha' 'doms byas/chos sde'i sgrigs la gnod pa cung zad
kyang ma byas pa bla ma dkon mchog gi thugs kyis ma khrel bar byas pa bzhin gzhi byes kyi dge 'dun thams cad kyi'ang dgyes tshor dang / bzang bzang gsung tshig gi gtang
rag dang / mthong cha 'jog kyang lhag par mdzad/ tshogs su'ang gsum gdan snyes 'bol dang bcas pa bzhugs khri'i sku gzhogs g.yas na yod/ gsol ja ba zur khyer dkar yol dang
bcas pa gsung chos la'ang chos gdan sogs dpe med kyi mthong / bdag chen rin po ches nges kyi dbon po yin pas gsung nas gnang ba sogs thub bstan pa spyi sgos kyi thad du
nged rang ya gir sdod ring la skur pa zhu rgyu ye med/ slob gnyer nus la shes rab che khungs btsun pas gdan sa'i 'os yin zer

phal cher lab/ zhabs drung rin po ches kyang khyod yon tan mgyogs po slobs/ 'o cag tsam slong la 'byon ni mi dgos/ bgro glengs sad sud bde mo ma byung bas bzod/ gzhung gi don
ni go'i 'dug po ti sbrel las grwa skor zhig kyang gang mgyogs kyis/ zhe sun ne yong ste mtshan nyid bslabs pa'i mdo don 'di ga min pa gzhan ni 'di yin cher mi 'dug /gdan
sa'ang byas pa dga' 'am gsung pa lan kha re phebs byung na'ang thugs brtse bas gsungs pa'i lan zlog par mi nus pas/ sku drin che ste bdag gis mi zin bsam zer ba tsam gzhus/
gzhan snga gong sde 'khrugs langs pa'i nub 'khor los sgyur ba'i rgyal srid kyi dpal thob kyang dgon pa 'dir lo gsum las mi sdod pa'i dam bca' byas yod pa dang / mtshan
nyid shes 'chad nyan byed rgyu byung na chags sdang med par dgon pa rgyab byas pas chog snyam pa kho na ma gtogs gdan sa'i 'dod ci yang ma byung / phyis su zhabs drung
de mi bzhugs pa'i rting la'ang slob dpon 'bum rams pas 'dir shog yon tan slobs gdan sa gyis zer yi ge mang po bskur byung ba'i lan du/ sngon gyi smon lam las 'phros mtshams
sbyar ba'i/ /snod ldan slob ma nam byung rjes su 'dzin/ /snang shas dbang gis ma dad mi 'dod bzhin/ /slob 'khor sdud pa'i shes 'dod mi bdog lags/ /zer ba bskur bas khong
la 'phog nas yig 'brel kyang

bcad so bsod par byung ngo / /'brug lo dpyid chos grol nas bdag chen rin po che rtse gdong la thegs pa ring po ma lon par zhi bar gshegs/ der 'das ma 'ongs da ltar gyi gshis
tshul gang la ltas kyang yi mug la snying rlung ldang pa zhig min pa mi 'dug /bdag gi bla ma de'ang gnas skabs 'di lta bu'i tshul zhig ston par gor ma chag /de 'dra ba
ma byung gi bar zhabs rdul bsten gsung chos lhag ma rnams zhus byas na dga' ba 'dra snyam/ yi mug gi 'phreng ba mang po spel ba'i zhu yig kyang phul/ zhal ngo so so la'ang
gsed bkrol zhu sna 'gyod med cig phul na'ang / rdo rje 'chang chen po nas brgyud pa'i gsung chos phal cher chad snying 'dod pa dang /nged rang la bsod nams kyi skal ba
de las med gda' bas yon mchod thams cad kyis la las zhi ba/ la las drag po/ la las ngo tsha bsher ba'i phyag dam mi sna dang bcas gnang nas dgongs pas ma khrol/ der nged
rang grwa ba dang bcas pas bdag chen rin po che'i gsol 'debs kyi thog tu sger gyi mang ja gdan non 'gyed bcas grwa pa rnams bsdus nas mang ja skol/ me tog gi char zhag mang
po kha ba lta bur babs/ las rgyu 'bras ngo shes shing dad pa yod pa'i dge 'dun thams cad kyis ngud mo'i sgras sa g.yo ba tsam byung / slob dpon bkras brtan sogs dar 'phyar
dang gtang rag gtong mkhan yang kha re 'dug /de ltar gsol 'debs

grub mtshams/ yang zhu yig nan cher 'u thug dang bcas pa zhig phul ba'i lan du yi ge bskur bas mi go na dngos su bslab bya byed/ grwa pa dang chas ka der zhog las khyod rang
hrug tsam zhig shog gsungs nas bo dong du slebs/ bla ma dam pa de dang mjal/ da gang la'ang snying po mi 'dug pas tshe phyi ma la phan pa'i chos shig zhu dgos 'dug zer
ba zhus na'ang zhal ngo tshos phug rdo rgyab tshar 'dug pa dang / gsung chos kyang rdzogs par ni gnang mi thub pa 'dug dgongs pa 'dra/ bla ma gshegs rjes dgon pa bor bas
ci yong / phar rgyug las slob gnyer gyi 'phro gyis zhes dang / bla ma gshegs bstan pa nyams dma' ba'i skabs su ka bstan pa'i khur 'khyer dgos pa yin gsung nas dgongs pas
ma khrol zhing / zhal ngo rnams kyi'ang bla ma'i bka' bcag pa'i thugs dam gyis grul ci btub sogs 'dra 'dra mang po'i bka' bkod nan chags pa mdzad de zla phyed tsam las ma
'gor bar phyir brdzangs/ 'gro khar bdag gi bla ma de dang 'bral mi phod pa tsam gyi sdug bsngal chen po byung / phyi phyag phul gdungs ba'i mchi ma char du babs/ skad kyis
brnangs pa tsam du ngus pas ma bshum par 'dir byon/ ngas byin rlabs byas kyi gsung nas byin rlabs bka' bsgo rgyas po zhig mdzad/ nga la'ang soms las thos bsam sgom gsum
la g.yel ba ma byed gsung / bdud rtsi

ril bu bdun gnang / sgo nang du slebs nas yar log ste dus dang gnas skabs thams cad du skyabs mgon re sa gzhan mi bdog pas thugs rjes gzigs dgos zhus pas/ zhal 'dzum mdzad
de thugs rjes los gzigs/ ngas dus thams cad du khyod ma brjed pa byed kyi yod gsungs te gsung gi tha ma thos pa 'di yin/ de nas sems 'phreng bzhin du phyir phyin nas de nub
dar sdings su bsdad/ sems had de ba zhig min pa 'di yin zhig mi 'dug /rim bzhin rta nag tu slebs/ rje btsun dbon rin po ches gsung chos thun gnyis ma gsungs/ nged rang
dpon slob tshos slob gnyer 'phel po yod pa'i zla phyed cung ma song pa las bdag gi bla ma rdo rje 'chang chen po de zhi bar gshegs tshar 'dug na'ang snyung gi yod zer ba'i
bang chen sleb 'phral mjal ba e srid snyam rta nag nas nyi ma phyed yol la yongs pas la rtser nyi ma rgas tsam la sleb/ na rdzab kyi gsab la 'grel zhing bog zhing yongs/
dar sdings/ kog chung ma'i gru kha sogs na thab 'dzin pa rim bzhin 'jog pa mdzad 'dug na'ang nged rnams mtshan 'grims byas pas tshor mkhan ni su yang ma byung / mtshan
la ko ba 'don rtsis kyis mgyogs par yongs pas gzhong gong bya ba'i lung stong zhig tu mtshan snga phyed tsam la slebs gang tsam phyin kyang de khar 'khor nas thor cha tsam
zhig lam sgor/ de dus ni yi mug la bya thabs med pa byung /

phyis bsams pas der ma 'gor na dbyar gtsang rgyas pa'i chu la mtshan ko btang / /gang la'ang lta rgyu med pa zhig yong ba 'dug pas bla ma dam pa de'i thugs rjes skyabs par
'dug /'jigs skrag rings par chas pa'i bu rul bdag /'jigs bcas chu bo'i 'jings su shor dogs nas/ /'jigs med bla ma de yis gnas der sgor/ /'jigs rung chu bo'i 'jigs las de
ring skyabs/ /skyabs khyed slu med lags zhes 'dis kyang mtshon/ /mtshon mod skal ngan phal gyis ji ltar go /go yang dad pa med pa de bas mang / /mang po'i khrod na shes ldan
nyin skar tsam/ /ka sbug sogs kyi zhing tshigs tsher mas ltabs pa'i bar yur po ske nub pa tsam chus gang ba mang po sgrol ba'i tshe/ bkra shis sgang pa dpal 'byor zer
ba'i mi gzhon hur thag cig yod pa de dang /blo bzang gis lam bcags srog 'tshor la khad bzhin du lam sna byas phyin pas nged rnams bde bar chu khar nam zi la sleb/ chu mthong
bas thams cad sems khongs su chud kyang nyes med du thon te tshes gcig gi nyi rtse la rdzong du sleb/ snang tshul mthong dus kha sing nga rang gis thab bzhog gang la'ang
ma 'dzems par 'ongs pa des mjal thub tsam byung 'dug snyam pa shar mod/ nged byis par song bas khyed kyi de e tho byung zer mkhan tsam yang mi gda'/ dgung zhag gi bar
dus 'khor yongs rdzogs dang bde mchog llu hi pa'i sgrub mchod

byas/ sku gdung rin po che'i drung du rgya dril/ rgya chol/ hong ting bdun cha/ mchod rnga/ dkar dung / dbu thog tu bla bre/ na bza' rten khebs gcig rnams phul/ de nas zla
ba bcu pa'i nang du nged kyi bla ma grongs pa kho'i mthu yin zer/ lha sa rdzong pas tshag po lnga drug dang bcas pa'i tshogs 'khor dar 'phyar byed kyi zer thos pas nga'i
bla ma bde ba nas bde bar gshegs pa la gtam 'di dang byed pa 'di shin tu ma 'os snyam/ bla chen thugs rje can dang nged dpon slob kyi mtshams bsdams/ bla chen rin po ches
'jigs byed kyi thugs dam drug cu pa mdor bsdus te nub re bzhin mdzad kyi 'dug pas zhag bdun tsam nas rtags byung gsung ba ltar/ kho'i mthu pa sngags 'chang rin rdor ba kha'u'i
sbo log gis tshig nas shi /bdag gis brag rdzong ma'i zlog bsad kyi 'khor lo kho na gnad du bsnun pas/ zla ba gcig nas nub cig dred yin snyam pa'i sems can 'jigs pa
zhig mchongs byung ba bdag gis mgo nas mnan brdungs pas/ de shi song tsa na 'khris der mgon po'i gtor ma rgyas pa zhig bshams 'dug pa la khrag gi rgyun yur chu tsam 'bab
kyi 'dug /de'i mdun na mgo bo ni mi 'dug sha tshag po bubs 'dra ba'i gsar pa bsad ma thag khrig khrig 'dar bzhin pa zhig 'dug pa na mi mang pos khyod btsun pa byas nas sems
can gsod mkhan yong ngam zer bzhad gad byed pa'i rmi lam gsal po zhig byung / gnyid sad nas

kyang nang thams cad khrag dris khengs gda'/ rmi lam de byung nas zla ba ma 'gyangs pa la lha sa rdzong pa'i dpon po phyogs las zer ba de pho log sgang tshal gyis btab nas
gdungs pa'i skad ngan 'don bzhin du zhag gcig la shi /lo phyi ma'i zla ba drug pa'i nang du mi kha cig gis pha zhig khrid byung nas sha dgos zer ba de ni 'di yin zer nga'i
'khris der bsad song ba zhig byung ba'i 'phral du kho'i chung ma zhig shi song zhing / de dus kyi mthu byed po ko chag pa bya ba'i sngags pa mi drug tsam yang gri kha kho
na ru song nas rkang stongs te mi bdog /bstan la sdang ba 'di dag mi sgrol na/ /bstan srung bsnyen cing bsgrubs nas ci zhig byed/ /bstan dang bla ma'i ched du byas pa
yis/ /bstan srung dbang pos myur mgyogs mthu rtsal bstan/ /bstan dgra su byung da dung sgrol byed mod/ /mod la bde chen zhing du mngon 'tshang rgya/ /rgya chen rgyud las
gsungs pa'i man ngag kun/ /kun gyis shes na sa steng bsregs kyi dogs/ /mdor na de yan chad ni bdag gi bla ma rdo rje 'chang chen po des sku drin kho nas bde bar 'tsho ba'i
skabs so/ /de nas bsams pas bdag gi bla ma de las gsung ngag rin po che zhig thob kyang byis par song ba snyan brgyud bzhi ldan zhig ma byung ba 'dug /gzhan snying por
gyur pa'i gdams pa ni cher ma thob da ni bla ma de'i tshab mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen pa la zhu snyam pa

thun mong min par shar te/ 'di'i tshul zhib bar bshad na sngar smos pa ltar byin pa'i dus kyang rje nyid kyis rten 'brel bsgrig pa gnang ba dang / nged rang yang shin tu dad
pa zhig byung nas/ glang lo rin po che drung bdag gi bla ma de mjal ba dang rong phyogs la phebs pa sgo bstun bo dong du phebs byung skabs gsung chos zhus chog pa'i zhu
ba zhal ngo rnams la zhus pas dgyes bzhin du grol mod/ 'on kyang rang re'i byed pa'i dkyus yin pas zhabs drung du brtag pa zhig zhus gsungs nas zhus pas kyang shin tu bzang
bar babs/ bdag rang gis nan gyis zhus kyang / bla ma'i slob ma slob mar min gsungs nas zhal gyis ma bzhed pa'i tshe/ rje btsun rdo rje 'chang gis bka' lung nan gyis gnang
/ bla ma'i slob ma slob mar min/ /zer ba'ang bdog ste/ bla ma mnyes byed gang yin bya'ang zer ba mi bdog lags sam cis kyang gnang mdzod gsung ba la/ gnas gsar ba mi
min zer ba bden par 'dug /bla ma la thel 'bebs sogs sngar med kyi srol btsugs gsung sku rtsed dang bcas zhal gyis bzhes/ thog mar sgrom dkar gyi tshe khrid zla ba'i chu rgyun
'od zer drug bsgrag gi rjes gnang / chag lo'i lugs kyi tshe dpag med dkar po/ dbyangs can ma dkar mo ste dkar lha gsum gyi sgo phye nas zhag drug gi ring la byin rlabs
rjes gnang nyi shu rtsa drug lung mang po dang bcas pa thob/ de'i skabs 'phros shig la khyod tsho nga la chos zhus na zer brtag pa

byas pa e yin gsung ba la/ nged rang yab sras ma gtogs su la'ang rgyus ni med ci yin snyam 'jigs zhum pa zhig byung / nged rang tsho gang byed kyang brtag pa zhus nas byed
pa'i dkyus shig gda' bas brtag pa zhus lags zhus pas/ bzang po byung ngam gsung / shin tu bzang gi gda' zhus pas bzhad cig mdzad de/ nged kyi rmi lam du nga rang gi pha yin
snyam pa zhig nas gnas gsar pa'i chos rje 'di khyed la chos zhu zer brtag pa byed kyi 'dug chug pa byed dam/ mi chug pa byed gsung gi 'dug pa la bstan pa la phan na ni
chug pa mdzod/ mi phan na ni mi chug pa mdzod zhus te bstan pa la phan pa yin nam chug 'dug pa gsung bas dga' ba dang bred pa lhan cig pa byung / rdo rje 'chang la bzhugs
pa rnams/ zhabs drung nyid du gang thob thob gyis/ der mi bzhugs pa'i sa stongs ngas 'gengs pa yin mod gsung nas/ grol khar dpal mgon dkar po tshe 'phel gyi tshe dbang
thun mong min pa de legs par gnang / yos lo bsnyen rdzogs kyi las slob la gdan drang pa'i dus/ gur gyi mgon po'i dbang lnga po rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor du zhus shing /
khyad par srung 'khor brag rdzong ma snyan brgyud thun mong min pa'i khrid nyams khrid yid ches par zhus/ bdag gi shes rab dang 'dun pa la mnyes pa'i gsung yang byon/ 'brug
lo bdag gi bla ma rdo rje 'chang de'i sku gdung rin po che mjal ba la phebs byung skabs/ da nga

yang gang byed mi shes pas mgon po dmar po skor gsum sogs khag che ba 'di rnams myur du gsan pa drag /'di pa ji lta ba shes mkhan da gzhan ye mi bdog gsung ba sogs thugs brtse
bas dgongs pa'i bka' lung bslab bya mang du gnang bas sems ngal gsos/ zhabs drung rig 'dzin chen po'i zhor la dkar bdud sogs rjes gnang kha cig kyang thob/ der 'phral
du spyan 'dren pa'i rtsis kyi dus bsgrigs zhus na'ang / ngo bo ni chos bsgugs byed du 'jug par 'dug /ltar snang thugs brel glo bur ba 'dras g.yengs pa'i khungs mdzad/ sngar
gyi dus tshes las zla ba gsum tsam 'gyangs/ de'i bar la gong du smos pa'i mtshams de byas/ de grol 'tshams bla chen thugs rje can gyi drung du gsar ma'i rgyud 'bum phal
che ba'i lung zhus/ 'dar zhabs drung du gdan 'dren rting bskul yang yang phul ba'i rting ma la/ dpal bdag chen chos rje'i sku yi dbon/ /zhes sogs bsngags brjod kha cig
gi mthar/ sa dbus gtsang khams gsum gyi sman ljongs na/ /chos zab mo 'dod pa mang na yang / /ngas rdal por gtad pa khyed nyid tsam/ /pha rdo ring pa'i bstan pa 'dzin du
re/ /zhes sogs kyi gsung bzang po dang bcas dus nges gnang byung ba'i thog tu spyan drangs/ rang lo nyer gcig lon pa 'brug lo la zla ba bcu gnyis pa'i tshes bzhi la phebs/
de nub nas gsung chos btsugs te/ mgon po che chung dmar po skor gsum cha lag dang bcas pa'i rjes gnang yig

lung rdzogs pa/ man ngag phal cher dang bcas pa gnang ba'i nyin re chos thun gnyis gnyis/ 'chams dbyangs kyi bslab sbyangs sogs dpyis phyin par thugs la btags te/ mtshan snga
phyed tsam dbyangs bslabs/ de nas sgom thun yod tsam dang gtor bsngos sogs byas/ de nas mar me'i 'od la mgon po'i phyag dpe khag che ba tsho yi ger bris pas zla ba gcig
la shog bu bcu dras sum brgya tsam tshar byung zhing / nged kyi mgon po'i dpe drag shos rnams la skyer thig gar po byas pa kho na yong ba'i rgyu mtshan de yin/ dpon slob
gnyis car la mnal lam mtshan ltas ngo mtshar ba'ang byung / gser gyi maNDal/ tshogs kyi 'khor lo sogs kyang 'bad pas bsgrubs/ grol ston la 'chi med 'od snang ma'i dbang
zhig gnang nas rje bla ma bsti gnas su byon/ rgyal ba sgo rum pa de'i sku drin gyis/ /rgyal tshab nyid las mi zhan bla mas bskyangs/ /rgyal bstan srung ma'i dbang po che
chung dang / /rgyal dbang dmar po skor gsum gdams pa thob/ /phyi rol dregs pa'i gsung brnyan ji snyed pa/ /rdo rje lus kyi rten 'brel kho nar bstan/ /de yang gsal stong
zung 'jug blo 'das su/ /rang ngo sprad tshe 'khor ba hrul por song / /rang bzo'i rnyog ma spangs pa'i bdud rtsi'i chu/ /byin rlabs lbu 'phreng ma nyams 'di 'thung tshe/ /nyon
mongs skoms nad sel ba lta ci smos/ /grub gnyis kun dga'i myos pa ci yang thob/ /sa skya'i rjes 'brangs phal gyis ma thos pa'i/ /sa skya'i bla chen snyan brgyud

mang du thos/ /sa skya'i bstan 'dzin mchog de'i sku drin gyis/ /sa skya'i bstan pa nyin mor byed la dbang / /de nas zla phyed kyi bar gtang rag tu gtor sgrub bzabs thag chod
pa zhig byas rjes rje bla mas phyag bris su mdzad pa'i mgon po lha bcu gnyis ma'i dam tshig bris sku zhig yod pa de la thun mong ma yin pa rab gnas zhag bdun ma byas pas
mar me khor yug tu 'dzin pa sogs ye shes pa dngos su zhugs pa'i ltas du ma zhig byung ngo / /lo nyer gnyis pa'i sbrul lo zla ba gnyis pa'i nyer dgu nas bde gsal mgon khang
du mtshams bsdam mal 'og gsang rdzas dang / gtor ma gsum man ngag bzhin bshams/ nang khrid kyi bsnyen pa zla ba bdun gyi bar du man ngag bzhin bgyis pa'i tshe/ shA sa
na 'bum phrag gnyis tsam song ba'i tshe/ gegs kyi rnam pas smyo la khad chen byung ba na bdag gi bla ma rdo rje 'chang tshar pa'i zhabs de gdan ma drangs par 'dar nas bo
dong rdzong du glo bur du byon byung nas mjal ba'i tshe/ zhal ras byu ru ltar dmar zhing gzhon sha chags la zhal rgyan sogs ye med pa'i rnam pa can zhig tu 'dug nas/ dgod
gro sngar phan ni zhal rgyan ye gzhor gyi mi 'dug /da lam gang yin nam bsam pa tsam byung / mjam ma thag sems la dga' spro dang mos gus chen po skyes/ gegs de la gegs sel
tsam yang zhu ma dgos par de nub nas rang grol du song / sems bde thag chod

cig byung 'dug /sang de'ang mjal bas sku sha'i mdog zhal rgyan sogs rgyun pa ji lta bar 'dug nas shis tshul zhus pas/ khyed rang la gzigs snang zhig byung ba yin nam gsungs
te/ thogs med gzigs pa'i ye shes spyan zur gyis/ /tshad med gegs kyi nyen pa de dgongs nas/ /sgrib med brtse bas byon nas mjal ma thag /dpag med sems kyi gdung ba ga shed
song / /gzhon nu lang tsho rgyas pa'i 'dzum zhal dang / /res 'ga' dar yol brjid chags 'dzum mdangs can/ /rdul bral ye shes sku yi 'dzum zhal ni/ /skal ldan mig la rnam
'gyur du ma bstan/ /bslu med 'di 'dra'i mgon gyis bzung ba kun/ /ji ltar byas kyang gol sa ma mchis mod/ /brjed ngas log lta'i dbang du ma song ba'i/ /gsol 'debs nus na de
gas chog par go /zla ba bcu pa'i yar ngo la mthar phyin gtang rag kyang shin tu rgyas pa zhig byas shing / slar dpal mgon bsnyen dus gyi bsnyen pa zhag nyer gcig pa zhig
bgyis pa'ang yid ches par byung / zla ba bcu gcig pa la mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen pa'i drung du mjal ba dang / gsung chos kyi 'phro 'ga' zhig zhu ba la 'dar stod grang
mo che'i chos grwar phyin/ lugs gnyis nas brtse skyong bu las lhag pa mdzad/ /'dar pa drung chen chen mo de bzhugs kyi yod pa ltar gzhis len zur sos sogs gang ci nas re
ba khengs nges shes pa thugs la btags/

der zhag nyi shu rtsa drug gi bar la thams cad mkhyen pa rdo rje gdan pa'i lugs kyi dpal mgon stobs 'phrog dbang po'i gtor ma drag po'i 'chams dbyangs phyag len thams cad mkhas
par sbyangs/ zla ba de'i nyer dgu la gtor chen gnang ba'i las pa bgyis te thog bcad/ gur gyi man ngag gi 'phro kha cig chig brgyud du zhus/ dud sol lha mo'i skor gsung
chos kha cig kyang thob/ gtor chen thongs pa'i nub mnal lam gyi tshul du rje btsun rdo ring pa chen po dang / chos rje rdo rje gdan pa zhal rgyas su bzhugs pa dang mjal
nas/ dpon slob gnyis kyi sku skye ba sngon ma kha cig lung bstan gsal bar byung / da lam gtor chen 'di rgyas par byas pas chos rje rdo rje gdan pa chen po mnyes pa yin
nam gsung ba nas/ dga' zhing spro la ba spu langs/ mchi ma mang du shor/ re zhig had de lus pa zhig byung / mnal lam ming tu btags pa'i 'od gsal ngang / /rgyal ba rdo rje
'chang gnyis mngon sum gzigs/ /lkog gyur sngon gyi gnas 'ga' lung bstan thob/ /ngo mtshar 'di dang 'di 'dra gsung ba thos/ /a ho srid par 'khyams pas ches dub pa/ /bdag
la nyid kyis ring mo zhig nas bskyangs/ /sngon gyi zhal bzhes bslu med bden pa'i mthus/ /'dir yang slob bshad snyan brgyud lhug par stsal/ /da dung khyed dang mtshungs par
ma gyur pa/ /de srid mgon skyabs dpung gnyen gzhan med pas/ /yid ches dad dang gus

pas gsol ba 'debs/ /bslu med thugs rjes sngar bzhin bzung du gsol/ /de nas mang mkhar mu gu lung mjal gnas 'brel gyi tshogs 'khor thugs dam gyi rim pa dge sbyor rgyas par byas
nas zhag gcig bsdad/ rje btsun chen po'i sgrub phug cha lung dang / phu dgon sogs mjal du 'gro rtsis phu na 'bum pa 'dug zer ba nas zla bo 'dra han brdal nas 'gro ma
nus par ma 'khor phyir 'ong khar 'khon rog shes rab tshul khrims kyi gter nas byung ba'i phur cha'i phur pa zhig /rje nyid kyi dbang bum/ phyag dril rgyun ring du gnang ba'i
shing khun ma shubs bcas/ seng ldeng gi kha TwAM ga /bde mchog rtsa rgyud kyi TIkka mu tig phreng ba/ 'phags pa rin po che'i thugs dam hor sku gur gyi mgon po'i sku zhig
sogs gnang byin kyang rten 'brel gyi sgrig phyogs dang bstun pa bsam gyis mi khyab pa gnang / 'dar du sdod skabs nub gcig rmi lam du lung pa ri klungs thams cad rdo pha
wang kho nar byas pa zhig gi khrod na sbra nag chen po thog drug thog byas pa zhig gi steng ma na mgar ba snum bag chags pa'i bag bron po zhig 'khor mang po dang bcas
'dug pa'i rtsar sleb/ de na re bande chen po byon pa legs kha sang nas mjal snyam kyang khyed grib cig gis nyogs nas 'phrad ma thub/ gdan 'di la bzhugs zer stag 'bol chen
po zhig la bzhag /kho rang ni rnam par 'gying / kho'i bud med 'khor g.yog mchor la rags pa rnams phyag 'bul du bcug /'khur ba gtso bor gyur pa'i bza' btung mang po drangs
nas khyod la 'di

man tsam gyi re zhig yod pa yin na'ang grib kho nas rmugs nas shes rgyu dang dran rgyu ci yang mi 'dug /khyod kyi cha lugs dge sbyor sogs 'di kho na rang min tsam zhig yod
pa yin/ da thabs cher mi 'dug cis kyang ru lag rgyang la rgyug /nga'i sring mos zhabs tog kyang byed pa yod byung na zhag kha yar sdod la kha ton gyis zer ba sogs bslab bya
mang po byas/ nga yang mgar ba 'dis sngar nga la phyag 'tshal gyi yod de da lam ldang ba tsam yang ma byas snyam/ snyas dogs kyi khungs byas gtam lan cher ma bcal/ de
ga'i ngang la gnyid sad/ dgod brog gang yin nam bsam pa tsam byung / de nas zhag 'ga' nas btsun pa zhig gis khrid nas rgyang yin zer ba zhig la phyin pas sa 'og nas shel
gyi sba tshigs brtsegs pa ring po'i kha na da lta'i rgyang dmar 'di 'dug nas mi thar ram snyam pa'i tshe bud med gcig gis lag 'then btab nas sleb skabs/ nang de nas sngags
pa rgan po zhig byung nas nga la 'khyud de ngu zhing bod bsod nams dman/ khyod grib kyis bslad/ khyod rang gang yin yang ngo mi shes pa 'di 'drar byung 'dug /'di na khyod
ra'i pha nor yod pas ltos zer/ gser khang gi gdung ldebs la shing chol 'dug pa'i nang nas po ti chung nge ba zhig /ril bu dmar po sran tshos tsam gyis phyur bur gang ba'i
thod pa kha sbyor zhig /shel gyi rdo rje sems dpa'i sku mtho gang tsam zhig rnams 'dug pa'i sgo rtsa na bram gzugs 'dra ba gnyis kyi mdung rtse sprad nas mnan pa'i 'og
nas lanytsa'i yi ge 'di u tsa ra Na

bya ba bris 'dug pa zhig mthong / sngags pa des nga'i lag nas bzung ste mi phod pa'i rnam pas gtam mang po labs/ shugs ring phyung nas bud med de la 'di la bsnyen bkur gyis
zer/ des kyang za rgyu mang po byin mtshams su gnyid sad/ de la brten nas de nub rgyang gi gtsug lag du bsdad de rten mjal byed par brtsams pas rgyang gra tshang gi rgyugs
sgyur byed pa dang thug /lha khang so so na gnyer tshang chang tshang sogs byas yod pas mi yong zer ba la/ bla ma de'i nye gnas pher pher mo byed pa'i theb shog pa zhig
gda' ba de bos ja chang gsol ba bzabs nas zhus pas dgyes bzhin du khrol te phyin pa na/ 'khyams gra de na chang 'thung ba skya ser pho mo mang po'i khrod na/ gdan chung
kha yar brtsegs pa'i khri steng na/ /bla chung chos pa'i gzugs brnyan hor 'dra zhig /bem chung gsar rnying brtsegs ma mang po gyon/ /blo chung rang mthong langs pas 'gying
zhing 'dug /de tshe dkor gyis myos pa'i nye gnas 'gas/ /sbyin bdag chang gis myos pa kha cig la/ /skor zhal phor chen myos byed kyis gang ba/ /'dren rim 'phyugs pas myos
ldan de dag 'khrugs/ /de tshe skrag pas stabs pa'i bla chung de/ /gdan nas lhung zhing phyogs bcur phyag 'bul byed/ /sbugs 'thums yon mchod de pa'i rnam 'gyur te/ /mthong
bas gad mo'i ngang du re zhig lus/ /de nas gser khang sogs lha khang rnams mjal/ rgyang ma mnyes pa'i rtags 'dug zer dkon gnyer de lab kyi 'dug /lha khang de dang

ha cang mi ring ba na slob dpon padmas rgyang ma gtul dus phur pa brgyab pa'i shul yom po lung bya ba'i brag phug phur pa'i dbal gyi dbyibs 'dra mo byas pa zhig 'dug pa de
mjal du phyin/ de nang chu shu gsar pa chus ldem gyis gang ba zhig 'dug pa rgyang ba'i mi 'dra yod pa tsho na re 'di na deng zhag bzhugs mkhan med nas zla ba bzhi tsam song
'di ci yin nam zer/ gcig na re ngas da nang rang yongs te ni mi 'dug zer ba la slob dpon padma'i sgrub khang yin pas dngos grub kyi mtshan ma zhig yin nam snyam/ chu de
nas yog tshad btung / bla ma sku gsum gyi gsol 'debs dang / hU~M ring hU~M thung bar ma 'ur ma byas/ chu shu de khyer 'gro byas pas chos mdzad legs bshad pas mi'i lung
pa'i sa char bdag pos bzhag pa'i chu shu 'khyer bas rgyab 'dre nyo ba yin nam zer bsgyur sbyang dang bcas mkhur ma 'dod/ brag phug de'i logs la g.yung drung ris dang / rdo

/ de nas bo dong rdzong du slebs/ re zhig mtshams dam po byas pa'i kha ton byas/ bla chen thugs rje can de las bka' rgyas 'bring bsdus pa sogs lung gi tshogs rab tu mang
po'i sku drin zhus/ lo nyer gsum par slebs pa'i rta lo zla ba dgu pa'i nang du slob dpon byams pa ba dpon slob rnams byang phyogs ri bo bkra bzang la rje sngags 'chang chen
po chos skyong bsod nams spyan 'dren

pa'i snyan gsan 'bebs pa la brdzangs / bar chad sel phyir bka' srung e ka dza ti thang lha dam can dang bcas pa la gsol kha rgyas pa nyin re bzhin byas pa'i nub cig rmi lam
du bo dong gi khang pa'i steng nas bltas pas byang phyogs thag ring po na thang lha'i gangs yin zer ba'i shel dkar po zur brgyad pa 'dra ba'i gangs ri mthon po dwang sang
nge ba zhig 'dug pa'i mkhris sprin zam 'dra mo zhig brgyud nas sleb gangs de la sgo zhig 'dug pa na yar zhugs te phyin pas dung gi khog pa'i khrem nyer lta bu zhig la sgor
sgor rim bzhin phyin pas rtse'i nang na khang pa bkod pa phun sum tshogs pa longs spyod kyi bye brag brjod kyis mi lang bas gang ba/ de'i dbus na thang lha la slob dpon
padmas phur pa'i dbang gnang dus kyi dkyil 'khor yin zer ba'i rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor khra yal le ba zhig gi drung na mar me khrag lta bu dmar ting nge ba zhig yal
la la 'bar gyi 'dug /de nas skyes pa brjid chags shig 'dug pa des bdag la bande chen po la gzhis len gyis zer 'khur ba shas che ba'i bza' btung mang po byin/ shel dkar po
khru gang tsam zhig kyang byin pa rmis/ skabs shig bud med smug tshon ma chen po zhig byung nas byang pa yong ba yod zer ba zhig kyang rmis pas don grub par go /slob dpon
pas rim bzhin byon bkra bzang du tshes bcu'i nyin sleb/ rin po che 'du khang na tshes bcu grol dngos grub 'gyed kyin/ nyi ma zla ba lta bu'i

gu ru rin po ches/ /ma rig mun pa sel ba'i dngos grub stsal du gsol/ gsung zhing byon pa dang slob dpon nang du zhugs pa thug nas byin rlabs zhus pas dngos grub dang gtor dbang
gnyis ka thob/ de nas gzims chung du byon skabs zhu yig rten bcas phul gshis tshul zhus pas/ mdang rmi lam du shar 'di nas nyi ma zhig shar byung nas lung pa thams cad
'od kyis khengs pa zhig rmis/ da lam dngos grub 'gyed kha'i rten 'brel kyang legs/ bstan pa la phan pa zhig yong shas 'dug gsung ba sogs dgyes bzhin du zhal gyis bzhes
dus sgrigs byas khong rnams 'khor byung / slar yang gtang rag dang 'phrin 'tshol rgyas par byas gdan 'dren la btang bas zla ba bcu pa'i tshes bcu la bde gsal nyid du phebs
byung / de snang snga ma 'di rig 'dzin sangs rgyas byams bzang bya ba'i byang gter gyi bdag po de'i sku skye/ rta mgrin gyi sprul par lung bstan/ rnying ma gter kha nyi
shu tsam gyi dbang lung mnga'/ chos nyid mngon sum gyi snang ba la mnga' brnyes/ slob dpon padma dang khri dngos su zhal gzigs/ gter mgon phyag bzhi pa dang bza' bdud rA
hu la sogs bran du 'khol/ lhag par byang chub kyi sems 'byongs shing phan sems che ba'i mthar thug /'phral sbas pa'i rnal 'byor du bzhugs pa zhig yin/ bla ma de zla ba
bzhi'i bar du bsten nas byang gter gyi chos tshan lnga brgya pa phrag gcig gtso bor gyur pa'i gter kha bcu tsam gyi dbang lung phal che ba zhus/

khyad par sgrub chen drag po rang byung rang shar gyi rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor du dbang zhus pa'i tshe/ bum dbang gi skabs su glo bur du sprin 'khrigs nas bum chu ster ba
dang mnyam du kha ba lhag par che ba zhig gsang dbang thug babs/ dbang bzhi pa'i maNDal phul ba na nam mkha'i mthongs sing nge gyes nas nyi ma dwangs shing dro ba'i tshad
thub pa zhig tshogs 'khor ma grol gyir bar du byung / de nas mtshan yal kha ba chen po ri klungs thams cad dung phyis pa lta bur gyur pa sogs ya mtshan pa'i ltas kyang
byung / rdzogs pa chen po dgongs pa zang thal nyams khrid yid ches par zhus/ snga phyir gser gyi maNDal bdun phul/ tshogs 'khor drug cu tham pa skor/ chos che chung gang
la'ang dar kha la chung mtha' byas pa'i phyag rten re phul/ bla ma'ang shin tu mnyes/ bdag cag dzam bha la'i nang du bcug gda' gsung dgyes drags pa'i gsung mang po byon/
gos chen gyi paN zhwa legs pa zhig gis gtsos pa'i na bza' cha tshang ba/ phyag dril/ ting sogs bla chas tshang ma dpus gtsang ba sogs 'bul ba'ang gya nom pa phul te dgyes
bzhin du phyir byon/ slar phebs bzhed kyang 'dug pa bzhin/ gdan drangs pa'i gsung chos lhag ma thams cad rdzogs pa zhig zhu snyam na'ang dus kyi zing log gi dbang gis ma
grub mod/ bla ma 'di la thob pa'i chos rnams dpe med du ye ma bzhag pas thugs dgongs rdzogs par byas pa yin no/ /snga 'gyur

/ /rgyud sde rgya mtsho'i snying po grub chen brgyad/ /yun ring dus nas bsnyen pa'i lha yin la/ /'dir yang chos 'di phyogs bcur rgyas byed pa'i/ /rten 'brel zab mo kun gyis
mthun grub byung / /drin can sngags 'chang dbang po dgon gsar bas/ /bskyed rdzogs gdams pa'i rgyal srid bdag la gtad/ /nges don rtsol med theg pa'i rang ngo sprad/ /bsams
bzhin bka' drin dran no thugs rjes skyobs/ /lo nyer bzhi lon pa'i lug lo zla ba drug pa'i tshes bcu'i nub/ khang pa phu mda' byas pa zhig na/ bud med cig gis dkon gnyer

bro gang la lta'am snyam tsa na/ rje btsun chos kyi rgyal po mnga' ris rig 'dzin chen po spyan 'dren zhu mkhan med par bo dong du byon 'dug pa

nas/ thos pa tsam gyis/ rmi lam de'ang 'di yin pa 'dug snyam nas mos gus thun mong min pa skyes/ dka' las che bar byung na'ang / zhabs la gtugs te gsung chos gsol ba btab dgyes
bzhin du zhal gyis bzhes nas/ thugs rje chen po rgyal po bka' 'bum lugs kyi tshe dbang gis sgo phye/ khyed rang gi skyeb sngon ma nas kyi chos skal 'di yin gsungs nas

no skyobs/ /de'i tshe nub cig gi rmi lam du/ mdun gyi nam mkhar lha dmar smug zhal gsum phyag drug pa yum

can phyag gnyis nyi zla cha lang rdeb pa'i rnam pa can zhig 'dug pa la/ de thim rang zer rgyu ni ma byung /nga rang yang de lta bu'i lha zhig tu song nas rnam pa gsal la zil

byar nyan pa med/ /rjes su 'bul ba byed/ babs ni dngos dang rmi lam gyi khyad ma gtogs mthong snyam du ni 'dug gsung / lha de ni phyis su mthong smon na yod skabs chos
skyong gi rjes gnang zhig byas pas 'khu ldog gi rmi lam shin tu 'tshub pa zhig byung ba na/ rang nyid lha der gyur pa'i dbu gtsug na rta mgo dang bcas te 'dug pa thams cad
sdigs pas rang grol du song ba zhig kyang byung la/ lha de'i sgrub thabs sogs rgyas par gsung rtsom mdzad nas rjes su gnang yang byung mod nyams su len pa ni ma byung
ngo / /lo de la dus kyi 'khrug long drag po bsam gyis mi khyab pa byung bas/ phal cher sku rim dang / gtor bzlog kho na la gnad du bsnun/ me mo lug la bod khams g.yo: dmag

pas phan nam snyam/ gu ru drag dmar nyang lugs kyi dkyil 'khor bzhengs nas sgrub mchod tshar bco lnga tshogs 'khor dang bcas pa zhig kyang byas/ rig 'dzin chen po'i gsung gis/
'gong po ar gtad cig bsgrubs nas mnan na phyogs 'dir bde gzar mi 'byung gsung mod/ bdud dbang ches pas byedadagos zhu mkhan med pa'i khar/ rje btsun dpon slob tshos shan
khong bon khongs kyi rnam pas bka' bkyon mang po mdzad/ de'i zhor zhal ngo nang bzan tshos bteg nas/ phyogs der dad pa byed mkhan nged gnyis gsum las ma byung gsung las
yar lam g.yung pa la 'gong po ar gtad sgrubs kyi byas kyang khas ma blangs/ 'dir yang mi mdzad 'dug /bde gzar langs na khe yod dgongs par gda' na'ang / gus subs thebs

sngon gyi smon lam

mtha' btsan pas/ /bdud dbang ma song dam pa'i thugs mdzod longs/ /gang zer dbyangs su len la ma nyan par/ /rig 'dzin sprul sku'i zhal bzang mthong bas dad/ /dad med skye bo'i
rjes su ma zhugs shing / /zhing 'dir rnyed dka'i mgon de mnyes par byas/ /byas pa don yod dam chos nying khu thos/ /thos lo ma yin nges shes mtshan ma mthong / /lo de'i
zla ba bcu pa'i tshes bcu gcig la/ hor smad pa'i dmag dpung che ba brgyugs/ tsher ma mang po bsregs/ g.yag lug mang po yang dag par ded/ /mi bsad ni ma byung / lo gtor
kha cig brdabs pas/ de nub brda' zhogs byas yud kyis bros nas mi 'dug cing / phyis su dgon pa'i stabs nas 'di pa dang spyod lam 'dres/ nged rang gi gra pa'i khungs 'dras
kyang bskang gso bzhin byas 'dug pas 'gyangs se ni byung mod/ 'ga' zhig ni mtha' gtsang song / nged kyi pha mes nas bzung deng sang gi bar nged dang 'gras pa tsho rtsad ma
rdzogs pa ye mi gda'/ bla ma rdo rje 'chang de bzhugs pa'i bar la mi lo chen po nyer bdun tsam gyi bar/ zhal ngo sku tshe bar chad du song ba dang / byus kha dma' ba tsam
yang ma byung / bde zhing skyid pa de yun rings pas gyen lan thur gyi tshul du mi bde ba mang du langs/ mdung thad 'dzin drags pas yon tan skyon du song nas mtha' bzhi
dgras 'khor/ nyang shab gnyis char du bun ne zing nge ba'i ngang la song / gnas pas

seng ge rtse phrogs/ dmag bo dong la chas grub 'dug pa la/ dpal nag po chen pau'i gtor chen zhig brdabs pas/ lam du zhugs tshar ba glo bur du phyir log nas bde bar gyur mod/
lha sa rdzong pa'i dmag sngon mo rdzong bya bar byung skabs kyang / gtor ma sogs 'phangs na rtags thon nges bdog ste rjebatsun dbon de skabs gnas gsar pa'i gtsug rgyan
'di phyi'i skyabs gnas su bzhugs pa des/ rdzong nas lha sa pa'i dmag la ja 'dren gnang ba sogs sgo du ma nas rten 'brel 'phyugs pa 'dra bas yid ches pa zhig ma byung / gang
ltar de nas bzung 'di yin med de ba zhig gi ngang la 'gro'i gda'/ lo nyer lnga lon pa'i dus/ bdag gi bla ma drin can mnga' ris pa de bsnyung ba'i tshul bstan pa zla ba
gcig dang zhag nyi shu'i bar du byung ba la/ nyin mi dal mtshan mi gnyid pa'i tshul du gzims 'gab tu nyal/ zhabs snying ga la sbyar zhing bsros/ bshang gci thams cad kyang
phyag phyi byas pas sdig pa dag pa'i rtags mang po byung / gsung gi tha mar/ chos rje khyed skyid chos dang rnam g.yeng du ma song bar dge sbyor la 'bungs/ dkon cog brtsegs
pa dang 'dul ba lung gzhi cis kyang zhu thub pa gyis/ las 'bras la chung ngu nas 'dzem dgos gsungs/ de nas gsung ye mi 'byon par spyan nam mkha' la had de gzigs pa
kho na'i ngang nas/ sa ga zla ba'i tshes brgyad kyi srod la dgongs pa chos

dbyings su thim nas/ tshes bco lnga'i bar sku'i gzi 'od zla ba ltar dwangs shing 'od 'phro ba gzhon nu lang tsho la babs pa'i rnam pa can du bzhugs/ de nas gzhan rtags ni ci
yang ma byung / sku'i gzi mdangs bsnyung ba'i sgang gi de tsam du 'dug nas/ zhag gsum bzhag kyang gzhan khyad ma byung ba nas/ tshes bco brgyad kyi nyin sku gdungarin po
che nged rang gi phyag phyi byas pa'i tshe'ang shin tu gtsang zhing dri zhim la yid 'phrog pa zhig gda'/ chab ser re tsam yod na'ang byin rlabs rten yong ba 'dug pa la
snyam pa byung ma thag cor sgra dang bcas chu gtsang dwangs pa 'dra mo ting gang byon pa de khengs ma thag rbad kyis chad/ sku'i gnas 'di 'dra nas byon yang thams cad kyis
bltas pas mi shes la/ de'i srod la dpal kye rdo rje'i rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor du zhugs la zhen pa na/ me thams cad dum bu gcig tu gyur pa'i rtse mo/ nA ro mkha' spyod
ma'i dbyibs 'dra ba 'bar/ 'ja' dkar po bsam gyis mi khyab pa 'dus/ de nub ma shes mod/ sang nyin thab ka'i nye 'khor nas me tog dkar po sil ma lhag par rnyed/ me mchod
kyi sgang tsam la thag sgra dang bcas thugs ka'i thad kyi bug pa nas bdag gi pang du sku sha mtheb sor tsam zhig byon/ sku gdung thams cad ni shel ltar dwangs pa'i gdung
log tu phal cher gyur/ ring bsrel kyang mang du byon/ me mchod phul grub nas pur khang la mgo gtad nyal

ba na/ bla ma de sku thang rkyang du bzhes pa'i sku'i dbyibs ji lta ba zhig sngas 'gor byon nas chos rje yar bzhengs dang gsung ba la/ bdag thugs kyis gtong ba lags sam zhus
ngus pas/ ngu mi dgos nga 'og min du sleb/ 'og min 'di ga yin mod gsungs phyag spyi bor bzhag byung ma thag gnyid sad byung bas/ mchi mas sngas bangs 'dug cing / slar yang
skad kyis brnangs par ngus/ pha yis yang yang bor ba'i dwa phrug bdag /bdag gzhan don gnyis sgrub par rlom lags mod/ /mod la bla ma dran pa'i mchi ma lhungs/ /kyi hud
bsams shing bla ma yab sras dran/ /de nas dgung zhag gi bar thugs dam gyi snying po dpal kye rdo rje'i rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor bzhengs te/ zhags bdun bdun nas dkyil 'khor
bsdu ba dang / sta gon skyor ba sogs gzhan phan bdud rtsi ji lta ba'i lugs bzhin bdag cag bzhis dgung zhag ma grol bar cho ga tshar gnyis re byas/ gsol ba btab/ bdag
gcig pus dpal rdo rje 'jigs byed ro langs brgyad skor gyi rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor du dgung zhag gsum pa'i bar mchod cing gsol ba btab/ nged kyi bla ma de na bza' tshun
'theb yong mi nyan par gcig byung ma thag gcig mi la gnang tshar 'gro bas phyag rdzas ni mi bdog /'phral gyi rdo rje 'dzin pa dang dge slong gi mkho ba'i yo byad cung zad
yod pa de rnams dang / bdag rang gi chas ka'i lugs drag pa rnams

mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen pa'i drung du thugs dam la 'dogs par zhu ba la phul/ dgung zhag gsum pa'i thog tu dgongs rdzogs dngos gzhi'i khungs dge 'dun brgyad brgya tsam la
nyin thub kyi bsnyen bkur gang ci thams cad sde pa nas sku drin bskyangs te shin tu rgyas par bsgrubs/ nged rang gis bdag tu bzung ba'i dngos po thams cad phongs pa med
par btang / dgung zhag de grol 'phral nas bzung dge sbyor zhig byed dgos snyams yod kyang 'gyangs pa'i skabs shig rmi lam du/ bde ba can na bdag gi bla ma rdo rje 'chang
de bzhugs 'dug pa'i drung du sleb/ byin rlabs zhus pas/ nga khyod la re chen po zhig yod de/ khyod ri khrod 'grims zer sgug sgug nas/ klungs khrod du tha mal du 'chi ba
'dra zer drung bla ma ba'ang thugs khral du gyur gda'/ da dung bu tsha'i spyod pa ka byed dam/ khyer kha la gsung mgo la thal lcag cig skyon byung bas gnyid phrad kyi sad/
bla ma de'i zhal ras mig sngar gsal drag nas skad thon par ngus/ da thabs med/ da nang rang nas dge sbyor sgrigs bcur zhig byed dgos snyam/ de nas bzung nyi ma phyed yan
kha ton gyi khungs/ lto gdan gcig tu sgyur/ gtor bsngos thun gnyis/ brgya rtsa/ za byed mkha' 'gro'i sbyin sreg satstsha 'debs pa sogs g.yeng ba dang / gnyid dbang du mi
gtong ba'i dam bca' drag po zhig bgyis na'ang / dam bca' 'dus byas yin pas 'phral du zhig /dam pa'i spyod pa bslabs kyang mi shes la/ /dam pa min

pa'i kun sbyor zhor la shes/ /dam pas khrel gnas bdag la bla mas gzigs/ /gzigs pa sgrib med de yis dus kun du/ /du ma'i gsung gis dge la bskul na yang / /yang dag ma yin rnam
rtog kho nas g.yengs/ /g.yengs med bsam gtan sgom dus nam yong na/ /na rgas 'chi skye'i sdug bsngal bzod par dka'/ /dka' bas btsal ba'i chos ni de bas dkon/ /dkon mchog
skyabs su 'dzin pa ches dkon mod/ /mod la bsam mno thong la dge sbyor 'bungs/ /sku gdung rin po che la gdung tsha khri tsho brgyad btab pa sogs rang gi nus pa dang bstun
pa'i sku drin khyer thabs de tsam las ni ma grub/ bla ma 'di'i phyogs su lus longs spyod gtang na'ang chungs ba las mi bdog ste/ ji srid ma shi'i bar du ma brjed par gsol
ba 'debs pa las thabs gzhan mi gda'/ lo de'i nang du sde chen 'ga' zhig gis sbyar dug ma rungs pa zhig btang ba la brten nas/ zug gzer la sran pa'i thabs med cing / sems
'khrul nas gnam sa mgo gzhug mi shes pa zhag lnga tsam byung / nang gcig shin tu ma bde bar 'chi ba yin nam snyam/ 'pho ba lta bur 'gro bsam lam zab cig bsgoms pas/ bla
ma dran drags 'chi ma mang du shor bas/ blo bzang 'khris na yod pa'i mno bsam la nga zug ma bzod par ngu ba yin nam bsams pa 'dra/ bla ma yin pa la thugs dam la 'jog dgos
zer chos bshad mang po byas byung /

de 'phral slob dpon padma la gsol ba zhig 'debs dgos snyam/ gtor ma bshams/ byang gter gyi 'phrin las 'bring po gyer bas/ spyan 'dren yan la ni zla bo tshos gyir ba ma gtogs/
skad thon rgyu'ang mi gda'/ spyan 'dren nas shes pa 'ur/ skad 'bod pa rgyag pa tsam thon/ drag rol yun ring la dos drag pa byas/ de ma thag nad khrus nas/ khrus skor khor
bcu gsum byung bas nad sing nge thon nas/ deng sang gi bar du zo mdog bzang la byung tshad bzhes chog pa'i phag pa la 'gran btsugs chog pa 'di ga lags mod/ dug gsum nad
sel ayon byin rlabs kyis/ /dug nad ma lus bshang ba'i lam nas bud/ /dug ro tsam yang med pa'i gdengs chen thob/ /dug chen bdud rtsir bsgyur ba'ang bla ma'i drin/ /'di
nas bzung ste/ brag sna ba'i sgos g.yog a zhang bya ba zhig gis gzung thud rdo char dang bcas pa bya ba'i bar dang / des mtshon nas glang lo gling log chen mo'i bar gyi byas
byung rnams zhib par bris na/ snang tshul thos na dgra yang mchi ma 'chor/ /mno bsam btang na snying rlung glo bur lang / /gnas tshul bsams na yi mug tshig pa za/ /de
phyir de dag brgyang du skyur las zhog /sdug po nyams su myong ba des chog gi /sdug gtam yi ger bris nas dgos pa med/ /sdug bsngal rtsa ba dmyal bar ma skyes na/ /sdug po
de tsam sran na'ang thub par mchis/ /bo dong nas bud pa'i tshe'ang / sde pa rnams kyang rta khrom bzabs sprod dge rtsa lo gsar

la 'byon pa 'dra mo ma gtogs mi gda'/ nged rang gi sems la kyag de ga yin/ pha yul spong bar byin gyis rlobs/ /zer gsol ba 'debs dgos pa'i tshod na thog tu byung gnas mang
po zhig 'khor nyan che/ blo phugs chos dang / chos phugs sprang / thugs dam pa dga' mo zhig nga byung snyam pa ma gtogs/ gzhan 'di yin cig ma byung / bsam 'grub rtser sdod
skabs/ brag dmar mkhan rin po che dang mjal/ byang gter gyi dug dbang de bzhugs kyi 'dug nas gsol ba btab pas/ dngul phor dang / gser zho gang / ka gdan sgril ma lnga sogs
cha rkyen mang po dgos gsung pa/ mi yul don pas de tsam mi 'byor pa 'dra snyam nas ma zhus/ ri chos shig dgos zhus pas zla ba lnga drug 'gor gsungs 'jigs 'jigs mo mdzad
kyi 'dug nas ma gnang / phyag 'bul byas grub pas de phyin chos 'brel zhig thob na dga' ba 'dra snyam phyag bzhi pa'i rjes gnang lung kha cig dang bcas pa zhus shing gnang
ngo / /sdug pos chos shor ba med zer ba bden por gda' bas/ de thams cad kyi bar du nges rang gi dge sbyor sgrigs ma che phra thams cad ye ma chag mod/ phyis skyed du
song ba nas 'chag pa mang du song byung ste/ skyed po mi theg pa'i tshan cig e yin bsam/ zla ba lnga drug gcig gi bar mi mang po'i gseb tu khyom khyom sdod dgos pa byung
bas sun pa lta bur gyur te/ myug tu sleb ma thag rang re la lugs gnyis

nas re mkhan su yang med pas skyid par yang byung / khang pa chung ngu 'os tsam zhig 'dug pa de/ myug rtsis len pa'i mi sna tshos/ nges kyi sdod sa yin zer gyi 'dug pa/ gzhan
phyag phyi drag pa tsho ni der bzhugs mi nyan 'dug pas/ za ru ma nyan pa dkon cog mchod byas gnang bar gda'/ tshe 'di'i dpon dang phyi ma'i bla ma las/ /'phral gyi sgos
dpon 'dam pa'i dad gus can/ /'gro mgon gzhon nus khong ra'i bsod nams las/ /ches chung khang chung zhig tu sdod gnas byin/ nged gnas mal zas gos gang la'ang rung mo zhig
mi bdog pas de gar 'dag sbyar byas mtshams dam po la bsdad/ 'a'i gang la snying po ye mi 'dug /sngar phan gyi za ri zi ri de dag don med 'ba' zhig la song / dge sbyor kyang
gtso cher rgya 'dre 'dis chos sgrub pa la bar chad byas kyi dogs mgon po kho na la bgyis mod/ da ni de bas kyang phyi ma phan gyi thebs shig dgos pa 'dra snyam/ gtso
bo bla ma'i rnal 'byor dang bstun nas rje bla ma'i sku stod 'bum ther gcig ngag thog nas btang / de nas bzung lo re la sku bstod 'bum ther re gtong ba'i dam bca' byas pa/
res gnyis 'bum tsam dang / phyed dang gnyis 'bum tsam song ba mang ba byung / nub cig rmi lam du/ 'dar nas rin po che'i phyag dam yin zer ba'i yi ge zhig mi zhig gis sprad
byung ba bklags pa na/ kun rdzob lha sngags ting 'dzin gyi/ /srung ba'i 'khor lo ma lus pa/ /rdo rje brag rdzong mar 'dus pas//'di nyid kho na sgom par zhu/ /bya ba zhig
'dug pa na ngo mtshar che snyam mgon po'i

sngags rnams kyang sngar kho na bzhin bzlas/ lo de'i zla ba bcu gcig pa'i nang du nub cig sa sribs tsam la rkang pa g.yon gyi na tsha yod pa 'di na sngar dang mi 'dra ba'i
tsha dbal drag pa sran mi thub par 'khyug cing 'khrig /khab btsugs pa ltar kar kar ba dang / chu khol ba ltar long long byed pa zhig 'dug pas lag pas byugs pas sreb thug
thug 'dug /mtshan phyed tsam la dge bshes phur pa bya ba zhig yod pa thun gtor 'bul du byung ba na mar me bteg nas bltas pas/ sbom phra smyug gu sbom shos tsam 'bur po rnams
kyi mdog dmar shig ge ba/ kyongs rnams nga rang gi sha'i mdog tu yod pa bzhag 'khyil ba lta bu'i sgor mo me long chen po tsam zhig 'dug pa de mthong ma thag /dge bshes
phur pa'i byad sbob kyi skrangs/ de nas rim bzhin lus thams cad skrangs pa la tsha dbal byas/ mtshan yal le a tsa 'bod dgos pa'i na tsha zhig thebs byung ba/ ngas dbang
chung zhig byas pas phan song bas/ dgod bro/ nga rang gdon gyis zin bzhin du gzhan la phan pa snyam pa'ang byung / sbrul lta bu de zhag kha cig nas je yal la song nas mi
snang bar gyur mod/ lar nged rang la chag sgo che tsa na rkang pa'i nad 'di thu ru 'gro/ chag sgo med dus tsha ber re ba tsam las mi 'byung ba zhig gda' ba/ nA ga rakSha
sogs kyi thugs dam dang / lha rje kyis zer tshad byas kyang phan rgyu ni mi gda'/ zla ba bcu gnyis pa'i tshes gnyis la drin khyer thabs med pa'i ma rgan mo de

zhi bar gshegs/ dgung zhag zhe dgu'i bar/ dpal kye rdo rje'i dkyil 'khor du dbang nyin re bzhin phul/ sku gdung la zhugs 'bul ba/ gdung tsha rnams zab phur spyan 'dren pa lo
ma 'khor gyi bar/ zla ba byung ngo cog gi tshes gnyis la sgrub mchod gang 'os re rgyas par sgrub pa sogs drin lan gyi khungs cha tsam 'khyor bar byas mod/ bsams na ma 'di'i
drin 'khyer ba la dka' mo zhig yod de/ nam zhig bdag gis byang chub mchog thob nas/ /nam mkha'i mthas klas 'gro ba sgrol nus pa/ /de tshe ma 'di drin lan 'khor lags
mod/ /de 'dra'i gnas skabs smon pa tsam du zad/ /lo nyer drug tu sleb pa'i bya lo zla ba gnyis pa'i tshes lnga la lam du zhugs zab bu lung mjal du phyin skabs/ yar lam zhong
zhong du gnas skor la phyin/ gnas mjal zhus pas/ btsun ma 'dre kha ma zhig gis khang thog nas bsgyur sbyang dang bcas sgo 'byed du ma nyan/ nan tan du zhus pas sgo phye
tsam byung / rin po che gdan sa ba bya ba yin zer ba'i btsun rgan zhig gis rten bshad byas/ ngas khas phyug mang po dang / snyan dar kha re phul bas mnyes pa 'dra gnas
tshang yang btang / khyed la ne gu'i phyag dpe 'dra yod dam zhus pas/ yod gsung / g.yar po dgos zhus pas/ ci zer do nub lta ni mi thub/ sang ni khyed 'gro/ gnas skor ba
la dpe cha bskur bas nga'i dpe khungs med du 'gro'am gsung ba la/ mi skyon nged shangs chos 'di la mos po zhig bdog na'ang de snga ma thob/ zhong zhong 'di

bla ma'i gnas yin zer bas rten 'brel cig brtag pa lags byas pas dgod cing po ti zhig khyer byung nas/ chos drug rdo rje tshig rkang dang / phyag drug pa'i gtor chog cig sprad
byung ba/ nged rang la dpe cha 'dri chas khyer khyer ba yod pas 'phral du bris pas khong mnyes/ 'dir gnas skor ba mang po byung ste thang chad skum ste nyal mkhan rkyang
min pa mi yong ba 'dug /khyod don gnyer byas dpe cha 'dri lugs dang / kha ton byed lugs sogs a tho zhig 'dug /dbyibs 'di la bltas na skye sa drag pa zhig kyang yin pa
'dra gsung ba la/ chos rje tshar ba bya ba zhig gi grwa ba/ stong mthon po ya nas kyi bla chung ngan dag cig lags/ gnas gsar ba dang na ning nas yon mchod 'brel po yod pas
rta 'di khong gis rta skyel mdzad pa yin byas pas go /khyod kyis de tsam nus nas ngas shing byin gyis gsungs yi ge ma tshar bar ong kong btang nas skyid du bcug /phar yang
zhabs tog 'bul bas mnyes par byas/ mgon khang chung ngu de'i sgo la sngas bstad nas nyal bas/ nam langs khar rmi lam du khang pa de nas mi zhig 'thon byung nas/ skad
go rgyu med pa'i pir pir 'dra zer zhing / nga'i chos gos kyi dra rnams su li khris thig le re re byas song ba na gnyid sad/ rim bzhin phyin stag sna na gung tshigs byed kyi
yod pa'i tshe/ pha rgan grub pa can de bsnyung bas/ phyir shog zer ba'i bang chen sleb/ zla bo byings yar brdzangs/ nged mi bzhis bza' btung ci yang yid la ma byas par
stag sna nas nyi ma phyed yol la

yongs pas myug tu thor cha zin pa la sleb/ pha rgan kyang sku khams gzhi med du dwangs 'dug pas go bcad par byung / thugs kyang mnyes mnyes mdzad/ slar zab bu lung la phyin
nas mkhar chen rtse'i mdun de na yar sa sribs pa la sleb/ 'o cag rnams la ngo shes ni ye med/ sa phyis pas gnas tshang mi 'byor ram zer grogs rnams sems khral du song /
bdag gis rta 'di la za rgyu zhig byung na/ nged rang rnams nub re tsam gar nyal yang chog zer zhing 'gro'i yod tsa na/ sde phyogs de nas bud med lo bco lnga tsam 'gro ba'i
spa lo ma zhig dang / btsun ma de tsam zhig bsdongs nas sleb byung ba/ nged tsho dang 'phrad ma thag 'o de ga yin zer nas/ nged tsho dang bsdongs log 'gro'i 'dug pa la/
nged kyi zla bo 'dras gang la ni 'byon byas pas don mi gcig bdog ste da yong ba gda' zer zhing dgod/ nged rnams la gnas tshang zhig gnang dgos byas pas/ nged gnyis la khang
pa med rogs byas nas g.yar gyi 'dir shog zer khrid nas/ khyim zhig tu gnas tshang g.yor rogs byas/ nged rta babs tsam la de gnyis la bzang lan cig byed snyam tsa na gar
song rtsad ma chod pa zhig byung / rim bzhin me tshor du sleb nas zhag gcig bsdad/ zab bu mdar zhag lnga bsdad nas lha khang bar pa de la skor ba gang 'gro dang / sku
