'dra'i drung la nyin re la le bdun gsol 'debs dang bstun pa'i phyag brgya tshar re bgyis/ gangs ches pa nas gter lung sogs bskor ba'i spros pa ni ma byung / sgrub chen 'dras
chos skad 'dri ba la rang

re'i go tshod dang bstun pa'i lan btab pas mnyes/ chos 'brel zhu ba'ang mang po byung / de'ang zla bo sngon ma tsho gnas su slebs nas zhag kha re song / nged mi yong ba yin
nam snyam dpa'o rgan po zhig la lkog mo btab pas de na re/ ci yin/ mo 'di la phas brag la lam dod nas/ bus bye ma la lam ma dod pa'i mo zhig babs zer smras 'dug pa/ kho'i
mo de mngon shes su 'dug snyam pa'i yid ches gting nas skyes/ padma rgyal po'i sku drin rjes dran nas/ /padma'i sgrub gnas zab lung dad pas bskor/ /padma'i gsung gis nam
yang mi slu ba/ /padma'i byin rlabs rgyud la 'jug gam snyam/ /mar lam lcags po rtse/ po tog /srin 'dul/ 'jag rnams su phyin/ gnas 'brel smon lam yid ches pa re byas shing
myur tu sleb/ lo de'i zla ba lnga pa/ chu dbar nyi sbug tu 'bro'i sngags 'chang mkhas grub dbang po 'jam dpal blo gros kyi drung du chos zhu bar brtsams pa na shangs chu
shin tu rgyas pas bgrod mi thub zer bshol bar brtsams pa'i nub rmi lam du lung pa kha lho bstan ri skya khrob be ba zhig gi ldebs la khang pa nyis thog rab gsal yod pa/
de'i g.yab 'khor zhig na bla ma 'ber mo byin can raksha'i phreng ba bzung ba zhig gi drung na nga 'dug pa na/ gzhon pa zhig gis rgya raka gi phreng ba rnying pa zhig gtad
nas/ 'di khyod rang gi dang po'i thugs dam yin/ da dung bzung na khe che ba 'dug ste/ blo the tshom las mi 'dug /da res ma bzung na/ de nas mi zin zer ba zhig rmi ba

nas/ de'i sang nyin de ga drung du phyin pa'i tshe/ lung pa sogs rmi lam ji lta bar 'dug /bla ma 'di 'bro'i gdung brgyud rnying ma mtha' dag la mkhas/ ayAai ring 'bum phrag
nyi shu rtsa drug bgrangs/ zil gnon dngos su zhal gzigs/ grub pa'i dbang phyug tu gyur pa zhig yin/ de dus lam bar du skyes pa dar ma grir bsad ma thag pa'i ro chen po zhig
dang phrad/ rten 'brel legs snyam pa byung / bla ma des kyang thugs rjes lhag par bzung nas/ gnubs lugs kyi gshin rje dmar nag gi dbang lung rags pa thob/ sras po sku
skye bas spyan tshab mi nus par bar chad chen po byas/ zhag bdun tsam bsdad nas phyir yongs/ slar zla ba gcig tsam song ba'i tshe rmi lam duu bla ma de dang mjal nas lung
phyag khrid mang po gnang ba zhig rmis/ chos bka' de zhib por thob pa yin nam snyam/ sang de slar yongs chog pa'i zhu ba skyel du btang ba dang / zhi bar gshegs pa'i gtam
ngan skyel mi lam du 'phrad nas/ yid kyi re bas rdzogs pa'i mthar thug pa zhig byung ngo / /de nas re zh-ig myug nyid du mtshams la bsdad pa'i dge sbyor byed kyi yod pa'i
nub mo zhig rmi lam du/ sde pa ngag dbang rnam rgyal gyi bka' shog yin zer ba'i dbyibs rtag shun pang khebs 'dra mo byas pa'i gser gyi yi ge mtho re tsam byas pa zhig
gda' ba de'i stod na rgyas rgyas mang po 'dug pa brjed nas mi gda'/ 'gab de na da lam la gshin po 'di snying rje ba gda' bas byon/ phyis su rim bzhin ti shrIr 'khur zer
ba zhig 'dug pa ci la lta'am snyam pa

na/ 'o yug sdings ma sde pa nas la/ sde srid rin po che rin spungs pas gnang / nged la bsko 'ja'i phyag dam dang bcas pa 'byor byung na'ang / bdag dang mo dar zhing rgyas dus
dgon pa 'dzin 'dod ye med pas da ci zhig 'dzin/ da bar 'di tshor bsdad pa'i dgos pa'ang / yab bgres po 'di gnyis 'o brgyal skabs zur khyer mangs kyang thugs 'khrugs kyi
dogs bsdad pa ma gtogs da khyed rnams brtan brling zhig khel na tsa ri lta bu ga shed cig tu 'chi ba sgug pa ma gtogs 'di med zhus kyang pha rgan grub pa can des lo kha
cig gyis gsung nan tan phebs pa nas bdag tu bzung / babs su 'di 'dra zhig las kyis bskos yod gda' bas/ nged lo bcu drug lon pa'i dus rmi lam zhig la bu mo na gzhon ras sngon
po'i yug gyon byas pa mdzes po zhig gis bdag gi lag pa nas bzung ste yud kyi nam mkha' la phyin pas/ mtha' gangs ri dang / brag ri chen po mang po ye le ba byas pa'i
lung stong yangs chod de ba zhig gi dbus na/ lung pa kha byang bstan sribs che se ba zhig gi gshongs shig na/ khang chung se khrib ber ba byas pa'i dgon chung / lha khang
dang mchod rten la rdza'i gandzi ra btsugs pa/ rtsi dkar dmar spel nas btang ba'i dgon pa'i rgyab na/ rdo'i gdugs byas pa'i mchod rten rgad po mi gang lhag tsam byas pa
zhig bstan nas/ 'di khyod kyi dgon pa yin zer ba la/ sems skyo mo zhig kyang byung / gandzi ra'i kha stabs dang / dgon chung 'di

'di 'dras don med zhus pas/ thog mar 'di yin/ de nas 'dod na gser gyi gandzi ra bcu gsum gtsugs pa'i bdag po byas pas chog zer ba zhig byung ba'i dgon pa de 'di yin par gda'
bas/ 'o yug tu sleb dus gzhan thams cad rmi lam bzhin 'dug pa la/ 'du khang dmar por byas pa la sa khra dang / rgyab kyi mchod rten de mi 'dug pas ci yin snyam/ rgan po
'ga' la dris tsa na/ dang thog sa khra dang mchod rten gnyis car yod zer gyi gda'/ gang ltar kyang zla ba bcu pa'i tshes bcu bdun gyi nyin sdings ma nas 'bod mi sleb byung
mod/ kha ba chen po nyin mtshan med par babs nas/ khong tsho'i dus thog tu mi sleb par thag bcad pa'i nub rmi lam du mi mang pos mar me bteg nas ja 'dren byas/ a pho don
grub lags yin snyam pa zhig gis dar sngon po kha gang phul ba rmis te gzhi byes kyi lha 'dres bsu skyel gyi khungs yin pa 'dra/ nam mkha' glo bur du yer nas dus thog tu
bteg /myu gur bsdad pa'i nub/ mi chen po 'chams sku tsam phrog zhu gyon pa/ mi'i lag pa 'bu ljig ge ba'i do shal byas pa zhig na re/ nga'i khang pa lam kha na yod pas yar
lam khor tsam 'byon dgos zer ba zhig byung ba nas/ gos sngon la shog zer ba yin nam snyam mjal tsam byas/ dam can gyi sku la dar kha gang phul bstan pa bsrung dgos pa'i
'phrin 'chol byas dus/ dkon gnyer de na re phyag mi 'bul ba nam zer ba la/ phyag khong gis tshur 'bul rgyu'i khungs lags/ nged su yin la phyag 'tshal

gyi mi bdog byas pas khong mgu mo mi gda'/ nyer gnyis la khri thog tu bskos/ de tshe 'ja' gur dang me tog gi char pa/ 'brug mdun ri'i steng na nyal ba sogs 'dug ni zer mod
bdag rang gis ma mthong bas tig po med/ bkra shis kyi dus smugs pa thams cad 'du khang gi sgo nas gshong tshad du sleb byung ba ni mthong bas rten 'brel legs pa yin nam snyam/
de res zla ba phyed dang gnyis tsam bsdad/ drung pa dkon 'phangs pa bya ba'i bgres po jo bzang chos pa rang zhig gda' ba sogs gra rigs kun gyis byams po mdzad mod/
phal che bas gnas gsar pa'i bu yin zer ar gog gi mthong dang / bred zhum me ba ma gtogs/ dge ba'i gshes gnyen rang du ni de skabs ma mthong ba 'dra mo zhig gda'/ dgon pa
de na rgyud 'bum zhig bzhugs kyi 'dug pas/ nged rang gi zla bo bka' bcu pa byams rab zer ba deng sang rnam rgyal rab brtan gyi slob dpon mdzad po 'di la bla med kyi rgyud
kyi lung rdzogs pa zhig byas/ sdings ma ba rnams kyis kun rig mdzad pa mthong bas/ cho ga 'di tsam la'ang bcas bcos dgos pa mang po zhig 'dug snyam pa byung ngo / /'di na
blo chung bdar ma'i skye bo rnams/ /rgya mtsho'i kha dog mthong bas skrag pa bzhin/ /nged kyi ming tsam thos pas skrag gyur pa/ /rgyus med skye bo khyod las bden pa su/
/'phrad ma thag tu rang mtshang mi ston la/ /rim gyis bstan tshe nges shes skye 'gyur ba//'di 'dra skye bo ya rabs

kun gyi srol/ /khyod rnams tshur gshegs rim gyis lta bar gyis/ /sa phyogs de'i skye bo phal chen dad pa che ba/ dad pa'i rjes 'brang kho na shas che bar gda' zhing dge 'dun
phal cher tshul khrims gtsang po sha stag 'dug pa'i zhing dag cing gda' na'ang / dus kyi dbang las/ hor dang khad nye zhing / de pa dang yon mchod yin zer 'brel chen po
byas pa zhig 'dug pa dang / khams pa'i yon bdag rnams la'ang bzhugs gral sogs 'phral du dgos pa'i bsun po zhig 'dug pa nas/ myur du bor dgos bsams pa kho na byung mod/ gang
mi yog pa'i do'i dpes/ slar bsreg shing rin cen sgang yang lo de la ga 'dzin dgos pa byung na'ang / de lo ni der ma sleb/ lo tshes pa'i dbyar chos kyi thog tu sleb/ po
po dgra lha bya ba khas 'phyug dang shes sgo che ba'i tshad thub/ gyod rgan gtam lab pa zhig 'dug pa de sogs/ grwa rigs kun gyis gzhis len bsnyen bkur spyi sgos nas gzabs
thag chod pa mang po byas/ tha na snga chab phyi chab tshun 'dul ba'i phyag len khrig khrig pa dang sing sing zhig gda' bas dga' ba la bsam pa'ang byung / der sleb pa'i
nub g.yag rog po chen po zhig rgol ba'i khungs byas byung ba mgon g.yag byed zer nas bzung / phye mar byin/ mgon po'i gtor ma mgo thog tu bzhags nas bka' bsgo byas pa'i
rmi lam gsal po zhig byung / lar nged gar sdod sa de'i gzhi bdag phal che bas rmi lam du dbang re nges par zhu'i gda' bas yin nam/ gang phyin sar skyid pa de ga

min pa/ 'tshub byung / mi na/ rta na zer ba rang cher yong ma dran/ 'dul 'dzin mkhas pas bskyangs pa'i 'dul grar sleb/ /mthu chen gzhi bdag drags pa dam la btags/ /phyogs de'i
gnas tshul nges pa tsam bgyis te/ /dgung zhag bdun bsdad rang gi gnas su 'ongs/ /de nas bka' brgyud bstan pa'i bdag po 'brug pa gcung smyon de la mi phyed pa'i dad pa
zhig yod pa dang / thugs kyang mnyes po zhig yod pa nas shog gsungs pa'i bka' lung bka' dam/ dngos dang rmi lam du yang yang byung ba nas/ lo nyer bdun lon pa'i khyi lo
zla ba lnga pa'i nang du ra lung la phyin nas zla ba phyed dang gsum tsam bsdad/ bla ma des lugs gnyis nas rang gi sras la ji ltar mdzad pa bzhin gyi brtse bas bskyangs/
bde mchog snyan brgyud dang / nA ro chos drug nyams khrid du gtso bor zhus/ ro snyoms dkor mdzod le'u drug pa sogs zhor nyan gyi tshul du'ang gsung chos mang po zhig thob
la/ nA ro chos drug la gsung ji lta ba'i zin bris shig kyang byas/ de tshe rgyal dbang sprul sku gsum pa spos skya tshe ring ma na sgar mdzad bzhugs pa'i drung du/ rten
'brel rdzogs pa dang / dkon mchog brtsegs pa'i lung / rje yab sras kyis gsan pa'i phyag phyi byas thog skabs shig sprul sku rin po che'i drung na phyogs kyi bka' bcu rab
'byams pa mang po zhig tshogs pa'i gral chen ja bur gyi bkod pa rgyas pa dang bcas pa zhig gi tshe khong rnams phyag rgya chen po dang / ayon bsnyen sgrub kyi nyams len rtags
bsal du bkod pa'i sgro gleng

mang po mdzad/ rab 'byams pa khams chen du rlom pa zhig gis/ rtag pa'i dngos po yod/ de bde gshegs snying po yin/ jo nang kun mkhyen chen po de ltar bzhed zer brgyal 'gro ba
tsam byed kyi 'dug pa la/ mi 'thad zer mkhan su yang mi 'dug pas/ sems la tshe ring tsa na skad cha ci yang zhig tshor gyi 'dug /kun mkhyen chen pos bde gshegs snying po
rtag par zhal gyis bzhes bdog ste/ dngos po yin par mi bzhed/ khong gis gsung rab kun na/ stong gzhi rang bzhin 'od gsal 'dus ma byas/ /gsung pa kho na yod mod/ 'di mi
'thad tshul 'dra labs na rung ba tsam 'dug ste g.yem ma mu cor gyi rgyal por 'dug pas dgag sgrub kyi yul du'ang mi 'dug la/ lar chos rje thams cad mkhyen pa bu ston gsung
pa de kho na mad/ kho bo gzhung lugs la thos bsam ma nus par sgom la yongs pa yin pas sgro gleng byed pa'i bab thob med/ de nas kyang phyag rgya chen po brjod bral de brjod
byar byas pa'i sgro gleng sogs dgod bro la yid mug pa zhig byung nas kha rog par bsdad/ a ho sems kyi rang zhal lta ba'i tshe/ /tha snyad tshig gi zir long 'di ci dgos/
/tha snyad bslab tshe stong nyid don du gnyer/ /stong nyid sgom dus tha snyad ra mdar 'bod/ /rgyal bas lung bstan kun mkhyen jo nang pa/ /'ga' 'dus skyon med grub mtha'
bzhed lags mod/ /gtsang dag bde dang rtag pa'i mthar thug pa'i/ /bde gshegs snying po dngos por bzhed re skan/ /der gsung chos rnams re zhig rdzogs/ nged phyir 'ong khar/
khyab bdag gcung smyon chos kyi rgyal po nyid kyi bzhugs

gdan la nged sdod du bcug /gnang sbyin mang po mdzad/ gos can gyi sgom zhwa legs po zhig phyag la dar nas mgo la sbran te/ da lam 'bul ba'i gtso bo 'di yin/ mi mang sa dang
khrom dbang sogs kyi tshe nges par bzhes par zhu gsung ba dang / sems la nga rang la rtsa ba'i cha lugs zhig yod pa bor bas yong ba med snyam pa shar na'ang / bla ma gcig
dang rten 'brel 'phyugs na bla ma thams cad srog gcig pas sbal pa rma can bzhin 'gyur bar bshad pa de dran nas da lam khas blangs/ phyis su mi nus gang yin tshig gis sbyangs
pas chog snyam nas/ de ga bgyid zhus pas thugs mnyes pa'i rnam 'gyur mang po zhig mdzad kyi gda'/ bka' brgyud bstan pa'i gtsug rgyan gcung smyon des/ /don brgyud phyag
chen gnas lugs rang ngo sprad/ /sgrub brgyud bstan pa'i bdag po khyod 'os zhes/ /chig brgyud gdams pa'i gnad 'ga' lhug par bstan/ /bstan pa rtags kyis 'dzin phyir 'di
gyon gsungs/ /gsung nan dang bcas sgom zhwa legs par stsal/ /stsal mod rtsa ba'i grub mtha' ma zin na/ /na tshod rgas kyang byis pa yin nam snyam/ /bla ma de drin che ba
zhig yin pas bka' bcag tu mi rung snyam/ de skabs tshur lam rin spungs zhabs drung sogs mi 'tshogs che sa thams cad du sgom zhwa de gyon pas/ zhwa mo tshun 'gyur ba 'dra
gsung sku rtsed mdzad pa kha re byung ba na de ga'i 'dod lan btab/ sems la grub mtha' 'gyur ba mi bdog pas sla'am snyam pa kho na byung mod/ nged rang gi gra pa

khog chung la kha rdar ba blo mi brtan la 'gyur skyen pa zhig yod pa des/ rje sa paN la 'bod pa dang bcas/ nged la skur 'debs zur za mang po byas mod/ sngon tshe dpal ldan
chos kyi grags pa yis/ /ral pa can gyi cha lugs bzung lags mod/ /skyabs gsum bka' rtags phyag rgya ma bor bas/ /mu stegs yin zhes smod mkhan su yang med/ /kho bos bla ma'i
dam tshig gzhung srong phyir/ /re zhig sgom zhwa'i cod pan bcings lags mod/ /nyams len grub mtha' gzhan du ma 'gyur bas/ /shes ldan skye bos ltas na ci zhig smod/ /rta
drel tsam la grub mtha' blos gtong zhing / /sdom gsum thob pa'i bla ma rgyab bor nas/ /lto phyir dung dung brgyug pa'i dad can khyod/ /mkhas blun skye bos khrel gnas ma yin
nam/ /blo chung gdan chung mthon por bzhag pa'i tshe/ /nga rgyal dbang gis dpon po khyad du gsod/ /rtsa ba'i grub mtha' dar tshe snying rlung lang / /lugs gnyis phyi thag
mang tshe snying re rje/ /phyis su bla ma 'di nged la gsung chos mang po zhig gsan gsung bka' lan cig min par phebs byung mod/ ye ma phul/ cis kyang ma gsan par 'bul
dgos byung na de dang bstun zhu grol cig zhu snyam pa ma grub pa'i ngang nas zhi bar gshegs/ ji ltar drag snyam sems la mi bzod pa chen po byung ba'i tshe/ stag lo zla ba
brgyad pa'i tshes bzhi'i nub rmi lam du bla ma de dang mjal zhwa mo dmar po yug shin tu legs pa zhig gnang byung nas/

da phyin dbu zhwa 'di bzhes nas/ gzhan phan mdzad pa zhu/ gdul bya yang 'di rang che ba yong ba gda' gsung 'dzum mang po zhig mdzad cing thegs song ba na/ gnyid sad pa'i tshe
bla ma grub thob de'i zhal ras mig sngar 'bral mi phod pa lam lam shar/ skad kyis brnangs par ngus/ khyod kyi bde chen ye shes sku/ /brnyes tshe skal dman bdag gi bsam
pa ji lta bar/ /legs par 'doms pa'i brda dang gsung dbyangs bstan/ /sku drin dran no da dung thugs rjes skyobs/ /mos gus lta phyir khas phyug ma song bas/ /rmi lam zhal
mthong brda thabs zab mo bstan/ /lto phyir mos mos byed pa'i zog rgan 'gas/ /da phyi bskal par zhal bzang mthong re skan/ sngar gnang ba'i sgom zhwa de glang lo shor/ zhi
bar gshegs pa'i dus byin rlabs rten la gdung brgyud rin po ches dbu zhwa sgom zhwa zhig gnang 'dug pa'ang / mi sna tshos lam bar du skyur nas lag du 'phrod ma byung mod/
bla ma bslu ba med pa 'di nyid kyis rten 'brel cig sgrigs par gor ma chag /'on kyang kho bo cag /deng sang gi bla sgub kha cig ltar/ lto ba na ma re dang / rdzogs pa'i byang
chub tshod mi byed pas/ bla ma de'i sku drin bsab phyir bla ma de las thos pa'i gdams ngag rnams la thos bsam dang / bshad sgrub la sogs pa bstan pa gsal bar byed pa'i
bgyi ba ni ma nyams par bgyid pa 'di yin no/ /ra lung nas 'khor nas ring po ma lon par khyi lo zla ba bdun pa'i tshes bcu la pha rgan grub pa

can de ngo mtshar ba'i ltas dang bcas chos kyi dbyings su gshegs/ gzhan yang mi 'dod pa'i rkyen mang po spungs pa bzhin byung na'ang / ci nus kyis dge sbyor du bsral/ dgung
zhag gi bar dpal phyag na rdo rje 'khor lo chen po'i rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor bzhengs te zhag bdun na sta gon skyor ba sogs gzhan phan bdud rtsi lta bur gsol ba btab/
lo de'i dpyid ma drin chen de'i nang rten/ rgyal ba rdo rje 'chang sgo rum pa chen po'i sku 'dra gser sku zhig bzheng pa'i srung 'khor dang / gzungs thams cad lag ris su
bris/ rten gyi bya ba yongs su rdzogs nas/ dpal 'khor lo sdom pa lU hi pa'i rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor la brten pa'i rab gnas rgyas pa tshar bdun phul ba'i tshe/ me tog gi
char kha ba ltar babs/ mar me'i phreng ba khor yug tu bzung / zhi rgyas kyi sbyin sreg gi thab nang gi rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor cho ga phyed tsam ma tshar bar bkra lam
me gnas pa dang / rgyas pa'i thab khung du ye shes pa spyan drangs pa'i dus/ rje btsun rdo rje 'chang de nyid mchod tshogs rgya mtsho lta bu'i dbus na gzi brjid dang bcas
ye re re byon byung ba pha grub pa can des mngon sum du gzigs pa sogs ngo mtshar ba'i ltas du ma zhig byung ngo / /lo de'i dgun sdings ma dgon par phyin/ dad pa can de
dag gis nan tan du gsol ba btab pa'i ngor/ byang gter gyi thugs sgrub rnam gsum gyi dbang lung khrid dang bcas pa zhig gzhir gnas kyi skya ser rnams la 'bul gyi yod pa'i
tshe/ grub chen

bsod nams legs pa bya bas zhus nas skya ser shin tu mang po la zhi khro dgongs pa rang grol gyi dbang khrid ngo sprod rgyas par byas pas/ srog gcod spong ba sogs dge sdig gi
'dor len byed pa mang po byung / der yod pa'i skabs su rmi lam la myur du 'gro ba'i ltas shig gsal bar byung ba dang / snga mo zhig gi dus kyang lo nyer bdun la 'chi ba'i
lung bstan gsal po zhig kyang yod/ de lo mo phya pra mkhan kun yang dog cha che zer gyi yod 'dug na'ang / de rigs la brtsi ba'i tshan min te/ sgor ma nas legs po zhig
mi 'dug pa nas/ myur bar myug tu 'ongs pa'i mtshams bsdams/ rtsa ba'i bla ma rnams la dus min 'chi bzlog gsol 'debs shig kyang bgyis bdog pa'i dngos po thams cad gtso bor
pha bla ma mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen pa'i zhabs sogs bla ma rnams kyi drung dang / dge 'dun gyi sde la spong dag la btang / mtshams dam po la bsdad pa'i dge sbyor bgyis/
'chi chos gsha' ma ma byas chos pa rnams/ /'chi ltas byung tshe tshe sgrub ma byas na/ /'chi ba 'od gsal gsal bar mi zin phyir/ /'chi dus bred dngangs dngangs skrag 'byung
bar nges/ /lo de'i mjug nas phag lo zla ba bcu gcig pa'i bar te lo khyir ba zhig mtshams la bsdad/ kha ton kyang shin tu 'phel/ lugs gnyis nas zir lang ye med dal la
skyid pa zhig byung / lo nyer bdun lon pa'i phag lo'i sos de/ pha grub pa can des theg mchog pho brang du lam zab brgyud pa bzhengs pa/

dus kyi dbang las zhig pa'i sku tshab tu chug /phyogs 'di na rje btsun sa skya pa'i bstan pa'i gzugs brnyan tsam yang dar po mi gda' bas bstan pa rin po che me dar chu dar
gyi rten 'brel la dmigs/ lam zab brgyud pa'i bla ma nyi shu rtsa gcig /mgon po che chung dmar po skor gsum dang bcas pa dang / byang gter pa'i ghu ru zhi drag /sangs rgyas
stong sku sogs bris sku sum cu rtsa lnga tsam zhig bzhengs shing rab gnas kyi bar mthar phyin pa dang / bzo bo rnams la'ang re ba rdzogs pa'i 'bul ba zhabs tog bgyis/ mtshams
de grol mtshams rin chen sgang du phyin/ rab 'byams pa mang thos bya ba'i bgres po thugs dam pa chos mthun zhig gda' ba des kye rdo rje'i dbang zhig gsol ba btab mod/
lo kha yar chos mi bshad snyam pa zhig bdog pa des khas blangs ma byas pa'i nub/ rje bla ma rdo rje 'chang de dang rmi lam du mjal/ chos rje pa'ang dbang byas pas yong
tsa na mi byed/ 'o cag ka 'di 'dra da yong gsung ba zhig byung ba nas rgyu dbang rgyas pa zhig phul/ de nas bzung dbang dgos zer tshad la dka' las la ma ltos par 'phral
bsgrubs byas pa yin no/ /mtshan nyid mi ldan bdag gi dbang bskur la/ /rgya chen phan yon 'byung ba ci zhig srid/ /'on kyang mchog gi bla mas rjes gnang nas/ /rab 'byams
dbang gi chu bo kho bos spel/ /de'i ston shangs mthong smon na mtshams dam po byas yod pa'i nub cig rmi lam du thugs rje chen pos byin gyis brlabs pa'i skyes bu dam pa zhig
dang 'phrad bas the tshom ma byed zer ba'i lung bstan gsal ba zhig byung /

ci yin nam snyam yod pa'i dus/ sang dgongs de nged rang la chos 'brel yod tsam gsan pa'i chos rje smon lam pa bya ba zhig yod pa de byon byung bas gsang stabs su mtshams khog
tu mjal/ rdo rje gling pa'i gter chos thugs rje chen po ngan song kun skyob kyi dbang lung rnams yid ches par zhus/ de'ang bla ma 'dis bla ma brgya dang gnyis bsten nas
bka' 'gyur ro cog la sogs pa/ gsan pa rgya mtsho'i pha rol tu byon pa lta ba nam mkha' lta bu klong du gyur kyang bde mchog gi yi ge bdun pa dang / ma Ni dung phyur kha
re bgrangs gnam lcags kyi thog dbu gtsug rang du babs pa brdar nas tsog pur bzhugs pa'i gsum phrag nas thal song kyang ba spu bzhob tsam las ma byung ba sogs lung rtogs
kyi yon tan du ma mnga'/ 'phral kyang 'jig rten chos brgyad hrul por zhig pa'i sbas pa'i rnal 'byor chen po zhig yin la/ bla ma 'di las snga phyir chos kyi sku drin bsam
gyis mi khyab pa zhig thob pas bdag la drin shin tu che bar byung bas lung bstan gyis ma bslus pa yin no/ /de'i dgun nges par grub pa'i dbang phyug dkar rtsi rtogs ldan sde
pa nas kyis spyan drangs mthong smon du phebs skabs de snga'ang gsung chos thor bu thob pas dad po yod na'ang / nged sdings mar sleb pa dang thug mjal ma thub dogs pa
la/ bla ma de'i zhal nas nged kyi ni gu 'di kho la sprad nga 'chi ru 'gro rgyu yin gsung bsgug sdod mdzad kyi yod 'dug pa nas 'phral du 'ongs/ shangs chos rje nyid la mnga'
ba phal

cher zhus shing nyams su myong / gzhan yang dgongs pa kun 'dus sogs chos bka' du ma zhag nyer lnga'i bar zhus so/ /lo nyer brgyad lon pa'i byi lo'ang zla ba brgyad kyi bar
mtshams kho na la bsdad pa'i dge sbyor bgyis/ de lo'ang bdag gi nu bo dad gus kyi zhing sa gshin la/ mkhyen rab kyi sdong po rgyas pa/ dpa' rtsal gyi g.yur za ba zhig bdog
pa de/ sku tshe lo nyer lnga las mi thub pa'i lung bstan byung ba nas/ tshe dbang brgya tshar zhig phul bas zla ba drug sku tshe bsrings/ de tsam nas tshe dbang 'dra byas
na nur sgyong yong re na'ang / gzhan dbang gyur nas bya thabs ma byung ba ltar/ dus las yol ba sogs snang tshul mang po zhig gis sems skyo ba'i tshad thub pa zhig byung
/ dpal 'khor lo chen po'i rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor du dbang zhag re dgu'i bar phul/ zhag bdun bdun nas dkyil 'khor spod pa dang mnyam du zhi ba'i sbyin sreg kyang ci
mang re sogs sdig pa sbyong ba'i thabs yid ches pa zhig bgyis/ lo de'i zla ba bcu gnyis pa sdings ma dgon par/ grub pa'i dbang phyug snar mo chos rjes nan gyis bskul nas
padma gling pa'i gter chos tshe sgrub rdo rje'i phreng ba'i sgrub chen zhag bdun pa zhig bgyis pa na/ zhag gsum song ba'i tshe 'gong po'i cho 'phrul blo las 'das pa zhig
kyang byung / sman sgrub kyi shar gyi thod pa de'ang mandza'i steng nas 'dril 'dug pa sogs bar chad kyi mtshan ma kha re byung ba na/ 'jigs pa dang the tshom med par/ dbang
drag padma'i drag

po'i sbyin sreg cig byas pa de'i nub rmi lam du/ sbrang bu nyam chung rid po bcu gsum lcags sder zhig na bcug pa shi 'dug pa de thams cad ngas bsad pa'i khungs la/ gnyis la
dbugs gyu tsam 'dug pas da dung drag po'i sbyin sreg gcig grub na/ phyogs der phan pa 'dug ste da bar ma thub/ gang ltar bar chad de legs par thul/ thod pa'ang sngar bzhin
sleb 'dug cing / de'i sang nas sman langs nas gling khongs thams cad dri bzang pos khyab/ ril bu rnams thod par 'jug pa'i dus skam thag chod chen bdog cing / thod pa kha
sbyar mtshams kyi zan rnams 'khyags nas mi phed pa tsam 'dug mod/ ril bu thams cad rlon pa khol nyams yod pa dang bcas shing 'phel yang chen po byung 'dug la/ phyis su
zla ba lnga tsam gyi bar ril bu rnams ye ma skam par 'dug pa la/ hor rgyal mtshan bya ba de myur du byung ba'i dus/ /snod de nas ril bu byin pas/ de nub nang rang skam thag
chod song ba/ bstan dgra 'di rigs la gtam 'dres na'ang dngos grub yal 'gro ba der gda'o/ /gang na'ang der sgrub pa cha lag tshang ma byas/ gtor ma'i sbyin sreg gi dus
bud shing gi nus pa rdzogs nas kyang / thab kyi dbus su me mar me 'bring po tsam zhig 'bar ba ja sbyor cig tsam gyi bar byung ba dang / gtor ma zor du 'phang ba'i tshe/
thog mar gdong lhags mi tshugs pa tsam byung ba la/ 'du khang gi sgo thon ma thag rlung kham nag chen po zhig rgyab nas

langs te zor gtor brdeg long med par dgra phyogs su sgyel ba dang / dam sri sgrol ba'i mtshams kyi skabs su/ nged kyi lag na rtse sag bzang po zhig yod pa des/ ltad mo ba btsun
ma zhig gi lag pa star mo'i ldebs la sbyar ba'i thog tu thag sgra dang bcas phog song na'ang / zhur ma tsam yang ma byung ba ni thams cad kyis dngos su mthong ba de
lags/ ril bu de ni nad gdon grib thams cad sel bar nus pa'i byin rlabs can zhig byung ba yin no/ /dad ldan slob ma'i tshogs kyis gsol btab nas/ /tshad ldan gdams pa'i go
rim ji bzhin du/ /bcud ldan sman gyi sgrub pa mtha' ru phyin/ /skal ldan 'gro ba'i re ba rdzogs par byas/ /lo nyer brgyad lon pa'i glang lo dpyid/ myug tu byang gter nas
gsungs pa'i phyi sgrub sman gyi bcud len zhig zhag bdun bsgrubs pa'i dus dri bzang po'ang cung zad dang 'phel che ba sogs rtags ni yid ches par byung mod/ bkra rtags thams
cad legs po zhig ye ma byung bas/ de la dmigs pa'i thabs 'dra dgos pa yod na'ang grub pa zhig ma byung / lo de'i zla ba gnyis pa'i nang du bdag gi bla ma mkhan chen thams
cad mkhyen pa'i zhal snga nas spyan 'dren ma zhus par phebs byung ba nas/ sa dang po la'ang mi smon pa'i dga' spro byung / da lam gzhan don spyod rgyu ye med/ khyed la
chos shig bshod du yongs pa yin gsungs pa na/ dga' zhing mgu la ba spu langs/ mchi ma'ang lhug par shor/ zhabs la gtugs pa'i phyag bgyis te/ gang gnang

zhus pas da lam 'jigs byed 'di byed gsung ba ltar 'o yug sdings mar spyan drangs/ dpal rdo rje 'jigs byed rwa lugs thun mong ma yin pa'i dbang lung man ngag bshad pa thams
cad yongs su rdzogs pa dang / khyad par rwa khrid mkha' 'gro snyan brgyud nyams khrid du stsal bas bskyed rdzogs zab mo'i lam gyi gnad gsang thams cad khong du chud/ rdo
rje theg pa'i gnas thams cad la klong du gyur pa zhig byung ste/ dran pas gdung sel khyab bdag ma he'i zhal/ /ngur smrig zol gyis rol pa'i pha rgod des/ /'khrul med gnad
kyi lam gsang 'di bstan tshe/ /mtha' yas chos kyi rang zhal rjen par mthong / /padma dbang chen yang gsang khros pa'i dbang lung man ngag thams cad rdzogs par gnang / slar
phyags phyi byas zab bur phyin/ der zhag lnga bzhugs nas thugs sgrub kyi dbang bsdus pa dang / nA ro mkha' spyod kyi byin rlabs sogs dbang lung kha cig kyang gnang / slar
myur du zhag lnga tsam bzhugs te stod la byon/ de nas ring po ma lon pa na mnga' ris chos kyi rgyal po sprul sku chen po chu bo ri nas gtsang du phebs 'dug pa spyan drangs/
zla ba lnga tsam gyi bar bsnyen bkur te/ rje nyid kyi gter chos phal che ba dang tshe brtan rgyal mtshan dang ratna gling pa'i bla ma zhi drag /padma gling pa'i bla
ma nor bu rgya mtsho rnams sgrub chen dang 'brel ba'i dbang lung / ma Ni bka' 'bum skye bdun sgrub chen dang 'brel ba'i dbang lung / khyad par

byang gter gyi sgrub chen bka' brgyad drag po rang byung rang shar chen po'i sgrub chen sman sgrub dang bcas pa'i sgrub dbang thun mong ma yin pa sogs gdams pa du ma zhig thob/
'bul ba'i dngos po'ang ci 'byor pa zhig phul te phyir byon/ skabs shig sdings ma dgon par dge 'dun kha cig la ni gu chos drug dgos gsungs pa nas bshad pa'i zla la yon
bdag khams pa rgan po kha cig kyang zhugs/ sgyu lus kyi dmigs pa'i sgang la myug tu mi yong kha med cig byung nas khrid pa rnams la nged ma sleb bar dmigs pa rnams chig
'gril du sgoms shig ces smras nas/ myug tu slebs pa'i zhag gnyis gsum nas ga re de tsho sgom gyi yod dam med/ yod na 'phro la gzhag na 'phangs/ mi sgom na ngal ba las mi
'dug pas phar mi 'gro dgos snyam/ nub cig rmi lam bzung nas ltar phyin pas/ khrid pa de dag gi kun spyod/ za 'grogs nyal lugs tshun gsal bar mthong / skal dman gnyis gsum
zhig ma gtogs khrid pa byings dang khyad par khams pa rgad po de rnams sdug rus byas sgom zhing 'dug nas zhag lnga las ma 'gor ba phyin/ ming gsal ni ma byas gnas tshul
rnams bshad nas ched du sgom dgos tshul byas bogs thon pa cung zad kyang byung gda'/ de nas yun mi ring ba zhig nas/ dus kyis zings log kham po che zhig langs/ bdag gi phu
bo lugs gnyis nas 'gran zla thams cad dang bral zhing / 'gran par 'dod pa rnams kyi gzi brjid 'phrog pa la dpa' ba

zhig yod pa de dus kyi mthar lhung ba la brten/ glo bur du 'jigs shing stabs pas yul 'khor nor rdzas thams cad bor te gtsang po lho brgyud du mtshan mo gcig la slebs par bgyis/
rim gyi dam pa'i bsti gnas chos lung dgon par slebs/ mkhan chen rin po che dpon slob rnams kyi/ nged de pa'i dus kyi snang tshul la ma snyas/ dang thog gi tshul dgongs
nas brtse skyong bsam gyis mi khyab par mdzad/ gzungs sgrub khang pa bya bar bsdad/ zhi bar gshegs pa de'i thugs dam gyi snying po dpal 'khor lo sdom pa lU hi pa'i ras
bris kyi dkyil 'khor la brten nas dgung zhag gi bar dbang bskur ba rgyas par 'bul ba sogs sku sdig sbyong ba'i thabs bgyis mod/ 'di nyid bskyed rdzogs kyi thugs dam la gsal
snang thob pa zhig yod pas/ mtshams sbyor ngan pas rgyud dkrugs kyang / gsal dngas rdzing bur rdo rgyab bzhin/ /sngar gyi gnad kyis bar ma dor/ /zhes gsungs pa bzhin/
bar dor grub mtha' snyog par/ dam pa bslu ba med pa gsum zhal 'dzom byung bas de la ltos par mi gda' na'ang / nged rang gi sku drin gso ba phyogs su 'dug pas bgyis pa tsam
yin/ chos lung der shas cher mtshams byas/ pha bla ma tshar pa chos rje de'i sku drin gyis/ skyid sdug thams cad dge sbyor du bsrel thub tsam bdog pas skyid pa yang byung
/ lugs gnyis nas rnam g.yeng med pas dge sbyor kyang shin tu 'phel

ba zhig byung ba yin no/ /der mkhan chen rin po che las/ tshe dbang dang rnam sras kyi rjes gnang zhig thob/ rje bla ma kun bzang mthu stobs kyi zhabs las mi tra khrid drug
sogs chos kha yar thob/ lo de'i zla ba bcu gcig pa'i gnam gang la rje bla ma nges par grub pa dkar rtsi rtogs ldan de zhi bar gshegs pa'i zhal chems su bdag pos gsung ba
yod 'dug pa bzhin 'bod du byung bas bla ma'i dam tshig la bsams nas phyin/ sku gdung rin po che zhugs la 'bul ba dgongs rdzogs kyi gsol 'debs sogs/ gang ci thams cad thugs
dgongs rdzogs nges shes pa bsgrubs mod/ de'i tshe rtogs ldan pa rnams kyi mdzad spyod/ mos gus thams cad kyi snang tshul nges par byung ba de lags so/ /der khong rnam
pa za ba la ma 'cham par nang 'thab mang po byas pa'i grib kyis khams nyog la rgyud 'khrug pa shin tu ma bde ba zhig nas phyir log /bres gshongs su zhag sdod byas pa'i gnas
tshang de/ rig 'dzin chen po bstan gnyis gling pa'i dbon po yin par gda' bas/ khong gi phyag na rig 'dzin chen po'i sku 'dra phyag nas ma zhig 'dug pa de la byin rlabs
zhus ma thag ma bde ba thams cad sbrul gyi shun pa brjes pa bzhin sangs kyis dag /sems la 'gyur ba chen po zhig kyang byung

bas/ phyis kyang lam zhor byung res kyi mjal snyan dar re phul byas pa yin no/ /de nas 'o yug tu phyin nas bla ma de'i dgongs rdzogs la dmigs/ sngags 'chang dbang po 'o bran
rin po che'i drung gi dbu mdzad dge 'dun lnga bcu tsam la shangs pa'i phyag chen chos drug gi nyams khrid dang / gzhan gser chos lnga'i dbang lung rje de nyid las gang
thob pa tshang ma dang / skya ser sum brgya tsam la dgongs pa kun 'dus kyi dbang khrid lung sogs bgyis pa las/ zhi khro'i dbang gi ye shes phab pa'i tshe dge bshes byams
pa chos dbang bya ba zhig la ye shes phebs te/ skyil krung bcas bzhin du mi rnams gral la 'dug pa'i steng nas yud kyis 'ongs te 'phag pa la sogs kyang byung / bum pa/ nang
mchod/ gtor ma thams cad 'du khang der ci gar bzhag pas cung zad kyang ma 'khyags shing / ne gu'i dbang zhig gi ngo sprod kyi skabs su mdun gyi nam mkha' 'ja' 'od sna lnga'i
dbus na pha bla ma rtogs ldan gyi rgyal po de 'dzum ye re bzhugs nas ngas byin gyis rlabs kyi yod gsung ba'i nyams snang gsal po zhig kyang byung / slar chos lung du
'ongs nas lo so gcig lon pa'i stag lo zla ba dang po nas zla ba bzhi'i bar mtshams nges pa can gyi dge sbyor byas de rjes sde pa rin po che dbang rgyal de chos dbyings
su phebs 'dug pa nas/ sde pa rin po che zhal bzhugs pa 'dis bdag la lan mang por thugs la btags/ brtse bas bskyang / byams po yang dag mdzad pa'i drin can zhig yin pas/ gsol
ja zhig ma zhus na mi btub snyam mjal du

phyin pas/ mnyes bzhin du sdod gsungs nas zla ba bzhi'i bar du zhabs phyir bsdad/ phyag dpe dpe khang na bzhugs pa'i po ti stong phrag phyed gnyis tsam bsgrigs gdong dar dkar
chag sogs kyi phyags phyi byas/ rje bla ma grub brnyes sdom brtson chos kyi 'byung gnas dge slong ngag dbang zhabs las gsar rnying dang 'brel ba'i dbang lung mang po zhus/
phar kyang dgongs bzhed dang bstun pa'i chos bsam gyis mi khyab pa phul/ gzhan yang rje 'ug pa lung pa dang / sham bhar mkhan rin po che nang so mtsho bo nas sogs dad
ldan mang po la so so'i bzhed pa dang bstun pa'i dbang lung man ngag nyin mtshan mi phyed par phul/ kun mkhyen chos kyi rgyal po rdzong dkar ba'i zhabs las kyang rgyu lam
sogs sku drin cung zad thob cing mi phyed pa'i dad pas rgyud brlan par gyur/ lo 'd-i nang du rong po byang chub dpal dang / sbyin pa dpal sogs kyis zhus pa'i ngor/ mgon
po dmar po skor gsum gyi thun mong man ngag ci rigs pa'i lung dang / dpal dus kyi 'khor lo'i dbang tshar gnyis/ mkha' 'gro rgya mtsho'i dbang tshar gnyis/ sdom chen/ sbyangs
pa'i yon tan/ gdugs dkar zhe gnyis ma/ kr-i ya'i dge legs su byed pa'i dkyil 'khor gsum phur pa sa lugs 'jam pa'i rdo rje sa lugs sogs dbang mang po dang / dmar mo
skor gsum/ dmar po skor gsum/ dmar chung ma skor gsum sogs rjes su gnang ba dang byin rlabs mang po/ ro snyoms sgang sgril/ ne gu'i chos drug /phyag chen ga'u ma/

thugs rje chen po'i dmar khrid/ skyo lugs kyi rwa rtse sems 'dzin sogs khrid mang po/ thugs sgrub rnams gsum dang / rta mgrin yang gsang khros pa sogs rnying ma'i dbang lung
bsam gyis mi khyab pa zhig kyang bgyis la/ lo de'i zla ba bcu gcig pa la g.yang yul skyid pa'i ljongs su sleb zhal ngo'i drung du zab pa dang rgya che ba'i chos mang du
'bul zhing gnas pa'i tshe/ bdag gi bla ma mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen pa'i zhal snga nas spyan drangs pa bzhin bde bar phebs nas der zhag lnga bzhugs/ slar myug tu phebs/
bla ma de'i sku drin gyis rnam rtog ngan pa thams cad rang grol du song ba'i mthus/ lo so gnyis lon pa'i yos lo zla ba dang po la sde pa nas kyang myug nyid du gzhi phab/
der zhal ngo rnams kyis gtso mdzad bdag cag nyi shu tsam phyin la rje btsun rdo rje rnal 'byor ma'i rtsa dbu ma slob bshad thun mong ma yin pa zhig gnang / a ho rgyal
yum dbang mos mngon sum du/ /du ma'i skye bar rjes bzung bla ma mchog /mchog 'dis zab mo'i nye lam 'di bstan tshe/ /tshe 'dir mkha' spyod 'grub la the tshom bral/ /slar bsreg
shing rin cen sgang gi dgon par spyan drangs zhag nyer lnga'i bar bsnyen bkur nas/ dpal gshin rje'i gshed dmar po lha lnga'i smin grol yongs su rdzogs pa/ dpe nag bltas
pa'i bshad yams tsam ma yin par thugs nyams su ji ltar myong ba bzhin bstan pas sems kyi sgro 'dogs

thams cad der chod/ slar grub thob tu rtags pa'i blun po kha re'i rkang pa la gtug dgos bsams pa'i blo rtsa ba nas bud/ lam dang lam ma yin pa'i shan chod pa zhig byung ste/
'jam dpal khros pa dus dgra'i dbang po des/ /'jam pa'i dbyangs kyis thugs bcud 'di bstan tshe/ /'jam dbyangs bzhed pa'i don de kho bos rtogs/ /'jam dbyangs dngos su byon
kyang zhu rgyu med/ /de nas rim bzhin pha bla ma 'o yug sdings mar spyan drangs nas/ rje btsun yab dang thun mong ba'i rtsa dbu ma nyams khrid du zhus/ bla ma de'i gsung
gis da lo cis kyang zhwa lu phyogs la rgyug las gnas skor gyis khyad par zhwa lu ba'i lugs kyi dbang lung 'di dag rdzogs pa zhig thob na ma thob na yin pas/ de zhu ba'i
khungs zhwa lu'i shar chos lung zer ba na khrid khang nas kyi chos mdzad ma zhig bzhugs pa de rang btsun pa yod 'dug pas de la zhus zer ba dang mo ru zhus te lag tu ma longs
par 'dug da sgos zhu sa ji ltar yod dang / rnam sras kyi dbyangs rol mkhas po shes pa 'dra rtsad chod pa gyis gsungs nas pha bla ma dbus la byon/ khyod kyis dus gsum
gsal bar gzigs pa'i mthus/ /ma 'ongs gnas 'di gsal bar lung bstan mod/ /bdag gis dus de gsal bar ma rtogs kyang / /dus phyis bsams tshe gsal bar nges shes skyes/ /der zhag
kha cig bsdad nas grub pa'i dbang phyug 'o bran chos rje dang / rdzogs chen byams pa ba dpon slob sogs gzhi byes kyi dge

'dun rnams la dgongs pa kun 'dus/ thugs sgrub rnam gsum/ shangs chos gser chos lnga rnams kyi dbang khrid lung smin rgyas thugs yid ches par phul/ pa rnam na/ dpal sa'i dbang
po lugs gnyis kyi 'khor lo bsgyur ba'i dbang phyug nor bu padma bzhugs pa'i drung du sleb/ brtse ba chen pos bskyangs/ de na gtsang tshong 'dus mgur mo'i khri dpon lugs
gnyis la mkhyen pa yangs pa sde pa gra lnga nas bzhugs 'dug pas mjal 'phrad mdzad/ zhwa lu sogs su sne sbyor gyi mi sna zhus/ thog mar sman lung mjal du phyin nas zhag
gcig khyams ra chen po der lcog bu phub nas bsdad/ dpal mgon stag zhon 'di nged rang gi pha mes dang / slob dpon gnyis kar brgyud kyi srung ma blo bstad na mi bslu nges pa/
mthu che la rtsal drag pa zhig yin pas/ tshogs gtor bskang gso rgyas par phul/ rdor dbyings kyi lha khang dang / smr-i ti'i gdung 'bum sogs mjal/ bla brang pas kyang ja
'dren gnang byin 'os 'gro thugs la btags/ sang snga bar thar par phyin kha che paN chen gyi sku/ gsol lhung mkhar gsil rwa gnyis ma/ rje nA ro pa'i rgyan drug /rdo rje
gdan pa nIShka langga'i phyag dril sogs byin rlabs rten mang du bzhugs pa rnams dang / dngul gyi rdo rje sems dpa' sogs bla brang 'du khang na bzhugs pa'i rten thams cad
mjal smon lam yid ches par btab/ mgon khang na 'cham sku legs po gnyis bzhugs kyi gda' ba la zhal khebs bsal

nas bltas pas 'tshub yod zer dkon gnyer de 'jigs 'jigs byed kyi gda' bas thugs 'tshab mi dgos lha 'di'i rgyus nged che ba zhig yin byas/ thar dgon sman lung dam pa'i gnas su
slebs/ /dpyal ston mkhas grub dam pa'i phyag rjes mthong / /bcos min mos gus dam pa snying nas skyes/ /slu med byin rlabs dam pa zhugs sam snyam/ /gam la bya ba'i la chen
po de brgyab nas 'ongs pas/ zhwa lu ri phug tu gung tshigs phyi ba la sleb/ bla chen rgyal mtshan pa bya ba'i gsang sngags pa chen po zhig bzhugs pa de mig ngo shes tsam
zhig yod pas khong la gnas tshang zhus/ ri phug gi rten gsum rnams dang / shar chen bla brang gi rten rnams mjal smon lam yid ches par btab/ shar chen nas drung chen des
gzhi len gzabs ma thugs la btags/ de'i tshe ri phug bla brang na mkhan chen 'jam dbyangs pa bzhugs kyi gda' ba/ khong gsung chos bzhin gnang rgyu yod pa zhig yin na mjal/
phyag 'bul zhu snyam na'ang / de'i spros pa ni chod 'dug /mjal phyin khong go sa gzhan dang mi 'dra bas phyag 'bul ba dang gzhir bcas na'ang / khong phyag rdzas phyug
la gtong phod che ba zhig grags/ nged rang sprang por song bas ltogs lha yin dgongs 'khrungs dogs gang gi'ang sgros ma btang bar spam me bsdad mod/ khong pas sku 'dra rin
po che'i drung der sum gdan snye 'bol bzang po zhig bting nas ja bzang po sun cig

gnang byung / rgyal ba bu ston yab sras dgon par sleb/ /rgyal dbang thugs rje can de'i sku brnyan mthong / /rgyal bstan gsal mdzad khyod kyi gsung bzhin du/ /rgyal ba'i bstan
pa 'dzin par smon lam btab/ /de nub rmi lam du gzims mal sku 'dra'i pad gdan la mgo bo gtsugs nas bdag khyed kyi nye gnas yun ring du byas pa'i dge slong de yin mod thugs
rjes gzigs zer gdung shugs kyi yus mang po byas pas/ sku 'dra rin po che'i phyag g.yas pa bdag gi spyi bor bzhag byung ba zhig gsal bar rmis/ de'i sang zhwa lu gnas su
sleb/ khri khang nas chos rje a byin drung bya ba zhig gnang byung ba dang / lcags stod nas nang so drung gi sne sbyor gyi phyag dam zhig yod pa bzhin zhwa lu nas slob
dpon chen po rnam sras pa'i drung gis gzhi len grogs dan yang dag par mdzad/ jo legs pa sogs kyis 'jigs pa med par rten mjal zhib la yid ches pa byung zhing zhwa lu pa'i
ban smyon tsho bred por byed kyi 'dug na'ang / nged la de dus nas phal che bas byin rlabs zhus shing byams po yang dag par mdzad/ chos skyong ba'i rgyal po chen po rnam sras
zhi drag /'chi bdag gshin rje'i dbang phyug sogs bzhugs pa'i mgon khang der gtor ma phul zhing bstan pa rgyas pa'i 'phrin las zhus/ chos skyong de pa nged rang gi rtsa
ba'i srung ma yin pa'i don gyis zil che la nyams dga' ba zhig byung zhing / tshur yong ba'i dus rgya phibs steng nas bya rog zhig

'phur byung ste rags nag po'i 'og tsam nas bsus/ phyir 'gro dus bya rog zhig gis rgyan gong bar bskyar ba ni de skabs kyi zla bo gzhi byes thams cad kyis mthong ba de yin mod/
de nas khri khang zhabs drung du shog gsung ba ltar/ spyir sde srid 'di pa dang / gnas gsar ba gnyis sku nye thugs nang gtsang la phan thogs pa re che sa zhig yin na'ang
/ nged sprang po rtogs 'khyams par song bas/ de 'dra'i ham pa byas shan mi 'dug mod/ 'on kyang bza' gang che sar rgyug pa 'di ban sprang spyi'i srol yin pa dang / khri
khang nas nged kyi kha stabs la ma gzigs/ dang mo'i khungs la gzigs nas thugs nang gtsang la thugs mnyes pa dang bcas/ sde pa rin po che mched drung dang / sde pa sku mched
thams cad dang mjal kha gnang / zhag shas sdod gsungs na'ang / rkang pa g.yon 'di'i nad de langs 'dug pas/ mtshams shig mi byed kha med yod nas zhag gcig bsdad/ skyid
po bsam gyis mi khyab pa byung / tshur lam pa na nor bu gling na da ti jo shag gis bzhengs pa'i dpal chen po zhig bzhugs pa de mjal zhing byin rlabs zhus/ myug tu sleb
ma thag dgon pa dkar por mtshams bsdams pa'i dge sbyor yid ches pa zhig byas/ de'i lo pha grub pa can yab sras gsum gyi nang rten/ bla ma rin 'byung / rdo rje mi 'khrugs
pa/ tshe dpag med/ slob dpon chen po padma/ bde mchog lhan skyes shig rnams gser skur bzhengs par

gnang ba'i srung 'khor/ gzungs kyi do dam sogs byas pa'i mthar/ rten gyi bya ba yongs su rdzogs nas dpal kye rdo rje'i rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor bzhengs te/ rab gnas shin
tu rgyas pa zhig byas/ de nas nyin re bzhin sgrub mchod sngon du 'gro ba'i rab gnas rgyas pa nyin re la tshar bzhi bzhi phul nas zhag nyer bdun la rab gnas rgyas pa brgya
rtsa brgyad/ thog mtha' bar gsum du zhi rgyas kyi sbyin sreg re dang bcas pa phul ba'i tshe'ang me tog gi char pa cher babs nub re mos su rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor dang
/ rab gnas kyi rten gyis mar me bzung ba stong ma chag par byung zhing / des mtshon pa'i bkra shis pa'i dge mtshan bsam gyis mi khyab pa zhig byung ba ltar dus de nas sde
pa rtsis gnas gsar ba dar rgyas bkra shis mkha' khyab tu 'bar ba 'di byung ba lags/ de grub ma thag myug gi dbu rtse 'di dang thog dpon chen grags pa rgyal mtshan gyis
bzhengs 'phro la gshegs/ bar skabs su sde pa nas zhig bsos mdzad pa'ang 'phro la lus pa zhig byung ba nas/ mi phal cher rnam rtog byed kyi 'dug pas de la dmigs dbu rtse rang
du mtshams zla ba gcig bsdams nas lhag pa'i lha la gsol ba btab pas bgegs mi 'byung ba'i mtshan ma brtan po zhig thob de grol rjes gtsang gi tshong 'dus mgur mo nas sa
skyong nyin byed dbang po'i bka' lung bzhin/ der phyin nas gshin rje gshed dmar po'i dbang / dmar po skor gsum/ phyag chen ga'u ma'i khrid sogs spyi

sger du chos mang po phul/ zha lu'i shar chos lung dgon pa na bzhugs pa'i rgyal yum dbang mo dang mjal ba'i sne sbyor zhus pa bzhin/ sku mtshams dam po yod 'dug na'ang brtse
bas bzung ste mjal kha byung / mjal ma thag sems 'di yin gyi tig po ci yang med pa'i hang nge ba la lus kyang yang chod de ba mchi ma bun bun pa zhig ma gtogs gang yang
ma byung / bdag gi lag pa gnyis nas bzung ste ngas na ning de nas bsgugs te khyed da bar mi 'byon pa la ngo tsha la gsung ja sbyor kha re'i bar lag pa phyag gis ma btang
sems nyid ngal bso zhig zhus pas/ bu nyon khyod gang rnam par rtog ces sogs kyi sho lo ka 'di la brgyad stong pa dang sbyar ba'i bshad pa rgyas pa zhig dang / bla ma'i rnal
'byor zhig gnang lta ba nam mkha' lta bu'i ngang nas chos spyod sgyu ma lta bu bya ba yin pas thugs dam spros bcas gtso bor bton pas spros med kyi ye shes shugs las 'byung
/ ngas brgyad stong pa la rgyun du ngag 'don byas pas gnas lugs la nges pa rnyed pa yin/ bstan pa nub la thug gda' bas 'chad nyan gtso bor mdzod bstan pa la sus phan
mi shes pas sprang po dang bla chen tsho chos skal mnyam por sbyin/ lta grub mthon po'i kha khyer gyis las 'bras ma mthong na bslu bas phyi tshul theg dman gyi spyod pas
gzhi bzung nges don gyi thugs dam la 'bungs rgan mo'i snying gtam yin no gsung zhing spyan chab byon nged der 'dus thams cad bla ma de'i mdun na yod ring sems rtog med
du had de mig mi 'dzum

par mchi ma bun ne ba kho na gda' ste mi phyed pa'i dad pa chen po zhig thob myur du 'ong bar zhus nas phyir log /slar myug tu 'ongs pa na pha bla ma thams cad mkhyen pa'i
zhal snga nas dbus na phebs 'dug pa bzhin/ gser dngul sogs khri khang du byung ba'i dngos po thams cad phyag tu phul/ 'khor lo sdom pa nag po lugs kyi dbang dang / stobs
'phrog dbang po'i gsang khrid sogs gsung gi bdud rtsi cung zad kyang thob/ zla ba bcu gcig pa la 'o yug sdigs mar cho ga mkhyen pa'i dge 'dun sum cu la bsnyen bkur zhus/
'dzab skor ba lnga brgya tsam bcas te tshe sgrub rdo rje 'phreng ba'i sgrub chen zhag bdun pa zhig bstan pa spyi'i rim gror bsgrubs pa'i tshe/ 'phrin las tshar brgyad brgya
dang sum cu song ba/ lnga brgya pha bla ma'i sku rim/ brgya phrag gcig bstan 'dzin spyi/ brgya phrag gcig bod khams spyi'i rim gro/ brgya phrag gcig de las kyang bstan
pa'i sbyin bdag spyi'i sku rim du bsngos/ sum cuu po de cho ga mdzad po rnams la dmigs/ ril bu yang dri bzang zhing 'phel shin tu che ba sogs mtshan nyid dang ldan pa zhig
byung / gzhan yang skyes stobs dang sbyangs stobs kyi yon tan mi dman pa/ myug pa slob dpon karma pa la rgyud sde lnga smin byed duu btang ba'i shangs pa'i gser chos lnga
smin grol lung bcas shin tu tshang ba zhig kyang phul/ rje bla ma thams cad mkhyen pa'i zhal snga nas kyi sku 'dra brgyad kyis gtso byas pa'i dkyil thang che chung 'dres
pa lnga bcu

lhag pa bzhengs shing rab gnas kyang rgyud sde dang mthun par bsgrubs/ lo so gsum lon pa'i 'brug lo dpyid/ gtsang gi tshong 'dus nas sa skyong dbang po rgyal ba'i bstan pa
bla mar mdzad pa des do dam dang ched gnyer mdzad/deng sang chos rje thams cad mkhyen pa bu ston rin po che'i bstan pa rdzogs par 'dzin zhing spel ba la sa'i steng na 'gran
pa'i zla thams cad dang bral ba'i rdo rje slob dpon chen po rje btsun 'jam pa'i dbyangs byang gling chos rje'i zhal snga nas dpal 'khor bde chen nas spyan drangs ba dang
bstun tshong 'dus khri khang du phyin nas/ dam pa de las dpal gsang ba 'dus pa mi bskyod rdo rje/ rdo rje 'jigs byed dpa' bo gcig pa/ bcom ldan 'das rdo rje dbyings rtsa
ba lugs rnams kyi rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor du dbang bskur ba zhus shing mi phyed pa'i dad pa thob/ bu ram shing pa'i rgyal tshab bla na med/ /bu ston bla ma de yi bstan
pa'i rgyun/ /legs par spel la mkhas pa'i bla ma de/ /legs par mjal bas re ba'i shing rta gang / /der zhal ngo drung la shin tu spros pa med pa'i de kho na nyid kyi myong
khrid lung sogs cha lag rdzogs pa'i thugs yid ches pa zhig dang / gzhan dbang lung thor bu phul/ slar zha lu ri phug shar chen bla brang du nag nya dang bstun nas/ rje
bla ma 'jam pa'i dbyangs de mnyes par byas nas dpal dus kyi 'khor lo sku gsung thugs yongs su rdzogs pa'i rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor chen por byis pa 'jug pa'i dbang bdun/
dbang gong ma/ gong chen dang bcas pa rdzogs par zhus pa'i

tshe/ kha ba shin tu che bas ri lung thams cad dung gi maNDal ltar dkar sing ges byas pa zhig byung ba/ mtshan ldan rdo rje 'dzin pa'i sku drin gyis/ /skal ldan kho bo smin
par byas pa'i tshe/ /dpal ldan dus 'khor bstan pa bod yul 'dir/ /rdzogs ldan dus dang mtshungs par byed do zhes/ /bgrang yas bstan la dga' ba'i lha rnams kyis/ /dpag yas
'dzin ma dkar 'jam gos kyis g.yogs/ /bsam yas dge ba'i mtshan ma gzhan yang mthong / /mtha' yas legs tshogs rten 'brel lhun gyis grub/ /de nas slar chos lung du rgyal yum
dbang mo de mjal du phyin dus kyang sngar kho na bzhin thugs mnyes mnyes mang po mdzad/ chos du ma zhig gi gsol ba btab pas khyed 'byon pa'i dus ma byung / nga lo brgyad
cu rtsa bzhi lon/ dpe sgrog tu mig mi gsal/ 'phar lung byed du rna bas mi thos/ chos ji ltar byas 'chad du 'dug pas rgya cher 'bul mi thub do nub 'dir bzhugs/ khyod zhwa
lu'i mkhan po byed rgyur 'dug /de'i tshe zha lu ba'i chos bdag ma 'di mi dgos ka med yin/ nged kyi chos bdag ma 'di dga' gcig bdog /ngas sang 'di'i rjes gnang byed gsungs/
bdag la zha lu'i mkhan po byung dogs med/ byung kyang zin dogs med de rjes gnang ni sku drin bskyangs zhus pas/ mkhan po byed rgyu yin par 'dug mi zin ma zer/ da lam
dus 'khor gyi bdag po chen po'i dbang zhig kyang cis kyang zhu thub pa mdzod gsungs/

sang de rdo rje rab brtan ma'i rjes gnang shin tu rgyas pa zhig mdzad/ do nub nas bzlas pa re dang gtor bsngos kyang ma chag par mdzod gsungs/ tshe dpag med 'chi med rnga sgra'i
dbang zhig gnang rjes chos rje ka bzhi pa'i thugs dam gyi dkyil thang zhig kyang gnang / rin po ches brgyad cu gya bzhi bzhugs pas khyod tshe ring ba'i rten 'brel mdzod
gsungs/ gzhan yang ngo mtshar ba'i ltad mo dang zhal 'phros mang po zhig gsung gi 'dug ste/ mkha' 'gro'i dbang mos dngos su rjes su bzung / /mkha' 'gro'i gsang tshig
ngo mtshar mang du thos/ /mkha' 'gro'i bu khyod skal ba rab yin zhes/ /mkha' 'gro'i gtso des gsal bar lung bstan mdzad/ /bla ma 'di dpyal kun mkhyen chen po'i sku skye gnyis
pa/ gsang rnying mtha' dag la mkhas pa'i tshad/ lo sum cu bug sgo la bzhugs nas thugs dam mdzad/ 'phral bgres mo de tsam du song nas kyang chos gos rnam gsum dang mi
'bral/ phyi dro'i kha zas 'jam tsam yang mi bzhes/ dang po sku gzhon pa'i dus ni nyin re la tshar re/ da lta zhag gnyis kyi khongs su brgyad stong pa tshar re zhal 'don
mdzad pa zhig yin/ phyag gi mdzub mo gnyis la oM gsum ma'i sngags 'phreng nA ga ro'i yi ger gsal po byas pa zhig gda'o/ /de nas dbon shrI byang chub sems dpa' chen po rgyal
ba bzang po'i gdung brgyud rnam par dag pa lcags stod nang so nam mkha'i drung gis shog gsung ba ltar lcags stod du phyin dgongs

bzhed dang bstun pa'i bka' dbang 'bul gyin gnas pa'i dus/ rin spungs nas gnam sa'i dbang phyug 'khor lo sgyur ba'i rgyal po des bka' shog pho nya dang bcas pa phebs pa ltar
myur du phyin te/ rgyal po'i pho brang de na/ bod yul gyi dregs ldan thams cad kyi cod pan brtul zhugs spyod pa'i rdo rje bcu gcig pa glo chen thams cad mkhyen pa'i drung
gdan chags 'dug pa bzhin/ ched du 'bod par gnang bar 'dug /bdag rang la sgos chos su dpal 'khor lo sdom pa nag po'i lugs kyi dbang bzhi sngon du 'gro ba rim bzhi'i nyams
khrid cha lag dang bcas pa zhig gnang / sde pa rin po che'i phyags phyir tshe khrid rgyas pa dang / do ha'i bshad pa shin tu zhib pa/ gzhan yang mgon po che chung / dmar
po skor gsum/ rgyud sde lnga'i dbang rgyas pa smin byed du btang ba'i shangs chos kyi gser chos rnam pa lnga'i dbang lung khrid sogs chos kyi sgo du ma'i sku drin thob/
grub dbang spyod pa'i rdo rje bcu gcig pas/ /grub brnyes nag po'i bzhed gzhung gsal bar bstan/ /grub gnyis mngon du byed la gegs med ces/ /grub pa mchog des gzengs bstod
dbugs dbyung mdzad/ /rje bla ma chos kyi 'byung gnas chos rdzong pa'i zhabs las kyang bla ma dgongs pa 'dus pa'i don dbang bsdus pa sngon du 'gro ba'i chos skor po ti brgyad
kyi lung sogs chos du ma zhig thob/ snga 'gyur bstan pa'i bdag po 'ug pa lung nas chos kyi rje zur haM rgyal ba'i sras po yab sras kyis zhus pa'i ngor/ dpal

sgrub chen bka' brgyad drag po rang byung rang shar chen po'i rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor du rtsa dbang / sgrub dbang thun mong dang thun mong ma yin pa/ sgrub phran gyi dbang
/ rjes gnang / yi ge phra mo tshun rdzogs pa dang / sgrub chen bka' brgyad bde gshegs 'dus pa dang / gsang ba yongs rdzogs kyi dbang yongs su rdzogs pa/ rdzogs pa chen
po kun tu bzang po'i dgongs pa zangs thal du bstan pa dang / rang byung rang shar chen po'i dbang myong khrid/ lung / rdo rje slob dpon gyi gtad rgya'i bar yongs su rdzogs
pa/ gu ru tshe brtan rgyal mtshan nas brgyud pa'i bla ma zhi drag /thugs rje chen po yang snying 'dus pa sogs so so'i bzhed pa dang mthun pa'i dbang / rjes gnang / lung
gi rnam grangs bsam gyis mi khyab pa zhig bgyis/ khams pa rin cen byang chub sogs kha cig la shangs chos yongs su rdzogs pa zhig kyang bshad/ lo de'i zla ba bzhi pa nas
bzung / bstan pa'i sbyin bdag gnas gsar bas bla ma rdo rje 'chang de'i thugs kyi dgongs pa rdzogs pa'i thabs su lam 'bras lha khang khyad par 'phags pa 'di bzhengs pa'i
dbu tshugs pa ltar/ de'i srung 'khor dang gzungs kyi do dam gnod sbyin 'khor lo sgrub pa/ logs bris kyi dkyil 'khor rnams la zhu dag sogs nyin mtshan ngal dub med pa'i dge
ba'i bya ba zla ba phyed dang lnga'i bar bgyis pa'i mthar/ bdag la bla ma 'di mchog tu sku drin che ba zhig yin na'ang zhal bzhugs pa'i dus zang zing gi 'bul ba mang po
bgyis mod/

pha ma drin chen gyi nor/ nged kyi lag la rdar phul ba tsam du 'dug pa nas bsam pa ma rdzogs/ 'di tsam gyis kyang blo kha khengs pa med na'ang re zhig ci 'byor du zad pas/
de snga yan rang nyid la gang yod kyi rten gsum mchod cha thams cad dam tshig gi rdo rje dril bu tsam zhig dang / byin rlabs rten gyi dbang bum cha gcig /ting bdun tshar
gcig ma gtogs tshang ma gtsug lag khang du phul/ des mtshon pa'i dus der lag tu yod pa'i bdog pa'i dngos po thams cad ltos med du phul zhing / slad nas mchod cha'i rigs gang
byung de 'bul bzhin pa 'di ga lags/ de skabs mnga' ris dkar rum pa chu phug dbon po kun dga' rnam rgyal ba sogs kha cig la dpal phyag na rdo rje 'khor lo chen po'i dbang
dang / rje btsun gong ma gsum gyi bka' 'bum gang thos de tshang ba'i lung yang phul de'i rab gnas la pha bla ma thams cad mkhyen pa'i zhal snga nas spyan drangs nas rab
tu gnas pa rgyas par mdzad/ rten bzhengs mdzad pa'i dpa' rtags la gur gyi mgon po'i gsang khrid thun mong ma yin pa zhal ngo drung la gnang gi 'dug pa'i phyag phyir thob/
bsnyen sgrub las gsum gyi khrid dmigs so so'i thad du/ de dang de'i rtags/ nyams dang rmi lam gang rigs su gsal por thob/ sa skya'i bstan la dad pa mang na yang / /sa
skya'i rje la chig dril byed pa nyung / /sa skya'i sbyin bdag khyad can khyod yin pas/ /sa skya'i chos srung dbang po gtad kyis long / /zhes

gsungs gdams pa'i nying khu gnang ba'i mthus/ /yid ches mtshan ma mang po kho bos mthong / /a ho grub pa'i zhabs lung ma nyams pa/ /thos tshe snying la kun dga' ci yang thob/
/de nas pha bla ma dpal zhwa lu gser khang gi seng ge'i khri la mnga' gsol ba ltar/ /bdag kyang de dang mtshungs par ma he mchod pa'i ltas mo zhus rim bzhin gsungs ngag
rin po che gsol ba 'debs pa'i khungs byas de ga'i dus sgrigs zhus yod na'ang / sde srid rin po che'i sku mtshams kyi srung 'khor dang / de grub mtshams zam 'tsher gyi bla
ma gyis gsungs pa'i bka' ji tsam 'bad kyang zlog ma nus par mi byed kha med byung ba nas cung zad 'gyangs/ slar rang lo so bzhi pa sbrul lo zla ba dang po'i tshe bzhi
la zhabs drung du sleb pa bzhin ri phug chos kyi mngon par mtho ba'i grub gnas su gsung ngag rin po che tshugs sa gnang / de mtshungs rje bla ma 'jam pa'i dbyangs byang gling
rin po che yang dpal 'khor bde chen nas spyan drangs te rnal 'byor rgyud kyi dbang bcu gsum po yongs su rdzogs pa rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor du zhus/ de snga yan bla
ma'i drung du chos 'chad pa sogs ye byed kyi med na'ang / der bla ma yab sras gnyis ka'i bka' ma chogs par zur 'chad par bgyis te/ rje bla ma 'jam pa'i dbyangs kyi zhal
snga nas dang / mkhan chen brag dmar ba/ ri phug dbu mdzad chen po sogs gzhis byes kyi bla ma dge ba'i bshes gnyen mang po la/ dpal mkha' 'gro rgya

mtsho/ bde mchog sbyangs pa'i yon tan/ kye rdo rje man ngag lugs/ dus 'khor sdom chen/ phyag na rdo rje gtum chen/ kun rig sa lugs/ tshe dpag med lha dgu/ tshe dpag med lha
gcig sogs dbang mang po/ bde mchog dkar po/ nA ro mkha' spyod/ phag dkar/ 'chi med rdo rje lha mo sogs byin rlabs mang po/ rgyal sras bka' 'bum dang / pha bla ma'i bka'
'bum sogs lung mang po/ bde mchog dkar po dang / thugs rje chen po'i dmar khrid sogs khrid mang po/ dpal gur gyi mgon po lcam dral/ phyag bzhi drug /rnam sras zhi drag sogs
rjes gnang gi tshogs rab tu mang po so so'i bzhed pa dang mthun par phul/ grub pa'i dbang phyug skyo ston rin po che yab sras sogs la rang bzhin rdzogs pa chen po kun
bzang dgongs pa kun 'dus/ drag po dmar chen/ tshe sgrub rdo rje'i 'phreng ba/ padma dbang chen yang gsang khros pa/ gshin rje 'char ka /ma Ni bka' 'bum rnams so so'i dbang
/ lung / khrid/ cha lag dang bcas pa dang / chos rje rang byung pa dpon slob kha cig la ras chung snyan brgyud gsar ma smin grol yongs su rdzogs pa zhig kyang bshad de
mdor na zla ba gsum gyi bar nyin mo rje yab sras la gsung gi bdud rtsi zhus/ mtshan mo gzhan la 'chad pa gtso bor byas/ phyir lam pa rnam lhun grub rtser mkhas pa'i dbang
po dpal sgang pa la rta mgrin yang gsang khros pa dang / dbyangs can ma dmar mo'i rjes gnang sogs gdams ngag kha cig phul/ zla ba

bzhi pa'i nang du dpal sbug padma bkod par mtshams zla ba phyed dang gnyis kyi bar bgyis/ de'i tshe dus chen sgrub mchod 'di 'dzugs par bzhed pa'i skabs yin pa bzhin/ phag
mo so bdun ma dang / 'khor lo chen po gnyis la nag 'gros legs pa re yang bcos/ gsang 'dus 'jam pa'i rdo rje'i dkyil chog gi nag 'gros shog bu phag gdong bcu bzhi pa zhig
/mtshan snga phyed tsam nas nam zi ba tshun la grub pa zhig kyang bgyis/ de nas zla ba drug pa la bsreg shing rin chen sgang gi dgon par chos rje bya ston sprul sku bas dbu
mdzad dge 'dun rnams la rgyud sde lnga'i dbang rgyas pa smin byed du btang ba'i ne gu chos drug gi nyams khrid/ gser chos phyi ma rnams kyi'ang byin rlabs lung rnams phal
cher rdzogs pa dang / dpal mkha' 'gro rgya mtsho'i dbang tshar gnyis/ 'jam pa'i rdo rje/ phag mo mngon 'byung / rnam 'joms ma Ni badzra rnams kyi dbang bgyis shing /
cho ga rnams la so so'i phyag len yang legs par bslabs/ slar myug tu kye rdo rje yab yum bde mchog lU hi pa/ 'jigs byed bcu gsum ma/ 'khor chen/ gdugs dkar zhe gnyis ma/
kun rig /dze tA ri'i lugs kyi tshe dpag med rnams kyi dbang bskur bgyis te/ so so'i cho ga dang lag len la sbyangs pa'i rdo rje slob dpon gtso 'khor lnga lngas rgyud sde
dang mthun pa'i sgrub mchod/ bla ma dam pa'i thugs kyi dgongs pa rdzogs nges 'di legs par 'dzug pa'i do dam dang / rdo rje slob dpon bgyis te rdo rje theg pa'i bstan pa la
bya ba bgyis pa'i khungs

yin/ dus de nas 'o yug sdings ma dgon par kye rdor yab yum 'jigs byed bcu gsum ma/ gdugs dkar/ kun rig /tshe dpag med rnams dang / bsreg shing rin cen sgang du/ 'jam pa'i rdo
rje/ phag mo mngon 'byung / 'jigs byed bcu gsum ma/ gshed dmar lha lnga/ rnam 'joms ma Ni badzra/ kun rig tshe dpag med rdul tshon la brten pa'i sgrub mchod kyang legs
par tshugs pa bzhin/ 'dzugs pa'i dus bdag rang gis rdo rje slob dpon bgyis pa'i phyag len phra mo tshun bab chol du ma song ba bgyis so/ /zla ba bdun pa'i nang du 'o yug
zam 'tsher du dbang cha lnga la dpal rdo rje gzhon nu sa lugs kyi dbang legs par byas pas/ phyogs de na grwa pa rgan gzhon thams cad dbang gi brda chad tsam yang ma chags
par sngags par khas len zhing / tshogs 'khor du ming btags pa'i chang 'thung mang po byed pa zhig gda' ba de la cung zad phan nam bsam/ de nas 'o yug sdings mar mnga' ris
chos kyi rgyal po sprul sku rig 'dzin chen po spyan drangs dpon slob nyi shu phyin la zhag nyi shu rtsa 'dren bsnyen bkur zhing / gser/ g.yu/ rta/ khrab/ khro/ g.yag sogs
dgongs par gang yod kyi dngos po phul te/ dpal bde mchog e ka dza ti'i smin grol yongs su rdzogs pa rdo rje slob dpon bdag po chen po'i bar rje nyid la ji ltar mnga'
ba thams cad yongs su rdzogs par thob/ rgyud sde'i nying khu mkha' 'gro'i snying khrag 'di/ /kha ba'i ljongs 'dir nub la nye ba'i dus/ /rgyal yum dbang mos lung bstan ji
bzhin du/ /legs par 'bad

pas chos 'di'i srog rtsa zin/ /gzhan yang dad pa can stong tsam dang lhan cig tu dong sprugs kyi dbang zhus pa'i tshe dbang tshugs nas ma grol bar nyin re bzhin me tog gi char
'bab pa sogs ngo mtshar ba'i ltas du ma'ang byung zhing / yang dag mkha' 'gro rgyun gtor gyi dbang lung sogs gdams pa zab la dkon pa du ma zhig thob/ de nas re zhig myug
nyid du mtshams la bsdad pa'i kha ton bgyis/ rang lo so lnga pa rta lo'i nang du dpal rdo rje phreng ba'i dkyil 'khor zhe gnyis/ kr-i ya'i dge legs su byed pa'i dkyil
'khor gsum rnams dang / mi tra brgya rtsa'i dkyil 'khor phal che ba bzhengs shing gtso bor mtshams nyid la bsdad/ chos kyi rje khro phu rin po che nyi zla ba dang / dad
pa dang yon tan gyis rgyud phyug pa'i chos rje shar pa bsod nams chos 'phel ba sogs la bde mchog e ka dza ti lam yongs su rdzogs pa zhig phul/ zla ba brgyad pa la 'o yug
sdings ma dgon par dad gus kyis rgyud phyug pa'i slob dpon buddha ba dang / sde snod dang rgyud sde'i don smra ba'i drung pa bslab gsum pas gtso byas nyung ngu zhig la dpal
rdo rje 'jigs byed chen po'i rdzogs rim thun mong ma yin pa rwa khrid mkha' 'gro snyan brgyud kyi myong khrid/ rwa pod kyi lung rnams dang / don gnyer mang po la bde mchog
nag po pa dang / dril bu pa'i dbang / nA ro mkha' spyod kyi byin rlabs/ rtsa dbu ma'i khrid lung dang bcas pa/ gcod zab don lugs kyi dbang khrid lung dang bcas pa dang
/ chos rje kyur rtsegs dbon po sogs la byang gter thugs sgrub

kyi dbang lung yongs su rdzogs pa sogs so so'i bzhed pa dang bstun pa'i chos kyang mang du bshad rjes/ ra gong brgyud 'brog rgya mtsho chos kyi 'byung gnas su phyin/ rje btsun
rwa lo tsA ba'i gdung brgyud rnam par dag pa bla chen chos dpal bzang po'i sprul pa'i sku bla chen rin po che bsod nams rgyal mtshan gyi zhal snga nas mnyes par byas
nas/ dpal rdo rje 'jigs byed chen po rwa lugs thun mong ma yin pa'i dbang / sdong ston gyis mdzad pa'i yi ge mang po'i lung / skyo lugs rwa rtse sems 'dzin gyi khrid/ rdo
rje gzhon nus lugs kyi dbang lung / sbyong rgyud dkyil 'khor bcu gnyis kyi dbang sogs gsung gi bdud rtsi kha cig zhus/ las kyi gshin rje dang / dkar bdud lcam dral gyi rjes
gnang ma zhus kyang dgyes bzhin gnang ba sogs lugs gnyis nas brtse skyong dpag tu med pa mdzad/ brgya tsho nas sde pa'i drung gis kyang bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i sku drin
gyis bskyangs/ bla ma de'i gsung nan ches pa ji tsam 'bad kyang zlog par ma nus par padma dbang chen yang gsang khros pa'i dbang lung man ngag thams cad rdzogs pa zhig
phul/ dge slong bkra shis dpal zhes bya ba mang du gsan zhing gzigs pa mkhyen ldan zhig gda' ba des zhus nas/ bde chen ral gcig gi smin grol yongs su rdzogs pa/ thugs rje
chen po padma dra ba'i dbang / thugs rje chen po yang snying 'dus pa/ /rgyal ba rgya mtsho mun sel sgron me/ mi tra bcu gsum ma rnams kyi dbang lung rdzogs pa sogs chos
mang du bshad cing zhag nyer lnga bsdad/

de nas zla ba dgu pa'i tshes bzhi la/ bdag gi bla ma grub thob kyi 'khor lo sgyur ba lce ston rin po che chos kyi dbyings su gshegs pa'i bang chen sleb pa nas nyin mtshan bshad
nas 'ongs te/ sku gdung rin po che'i phyag phyi dgung zhag gi gsol 'debs sogs bsgrub cing pa rnam bsam sdings su re zhig bsdad pa na/ 'khris kyi rgyal po des cung zad
bar chad byed kyi 'dug nas rmi lam du legs par btul/ de tshe sde pa a brtan drung phebs te dgongs pa rdzogs thabs kyi gsol 'debs/ gdung brgyud rin po che la che 'don/ phyag
phyi rnams la gang la gang 'os kyi bdag rkyen sogs phyis kyi mig ltos la phan pa zhig mdzad song na'ang / nang de na bcud 'phrog ma'i mtshan nyid thams cad tshang ba
zhig gda' ba de khams bzang ring bar tshogs khang pas ji tsam 'bad kyang lugs gnyis nas go tshugs mi yong ba thag chod gda'o/ /de nas rin cen sgang du sleb snod ldan bcu
gcig la dpal rdo rje 'jigs byed kyi rwa khrid snyan brgyud kyi myong khrid dang / tshogs pa byings la grub chen brgyad cu'i rjes gnang sogs chos du ma so so'i bzhed pa bzhin
bshad/ nged yon tan gyi cha shas khyi la 'dug kyang len/ yon tan med pa'i blun po gos bem can rta drel mang po can la blo mi 'gro ba zhig bdog pas/ dge slong zla rgyan
pa zhes bya ba phur pa'i rtsa 'chams dga' mo shes pa zhig yod pa de las sa phur gyi 'chams mthar phyin pa zhig kyang blangs/ rang lo so drug pa'i lug lo zla ba dang po
la/ rin spungs rgyal po'i khab tu/ lce'i sngags 'chang grub brnyes dge slong

chos bzang bkra shis pa'i zhal snga nas byams chen nas spyan drangs/ pha chos 'char ka sgrom bu ma'i dbang lung man ngag thams cad rdzogs par thob/ byin rlabs kyi mtshan ma
ya mtshan pa zhig kyang byung zhing / gzhan yang tshe sgrub nyi zla kha sbyor sogs dbang lung kha yar zhus/ phar yang dgongs bzhed dang bstun thugs sgrub kyi dbang 'bring
po phul/ zla ba de'i tshes bcu gnyis la myug tu sleb pa bzhin/ de dang rtse bstun zhwa lu nas rje bla ma byang gling 'jam pa'i dbyangs spyan drangs myug chos sde'i bla
brang du zla ba gnyis kyi bar chos rje thams cad mkhyen pa nas brgyud pa'i bya spyod dang / rnal 'byor bla med kyi dbang rje nyid la ji ltar mnga' ba thams cad rdzogs par
zhus/ phar bde chen ral gcig gi smin grol rdo rje slob dpon bdag po chen po'i bar yongs su rdzogs pa dang / mi g.yo ba bla med/ tshe dpag med nyer sgrub rnams kyi dbang
/ khyung khra/ sna tshogs yum sogs rjes gnang kha yar dang / phyag phyi ba rnams la/ sgrol ma bla med/ mgon po beng / phyag bzhi pa rnams kyang phul zhing / zang zing gi
'bul ba zhabs tog kyang thugs kyi shing rta yongs su khengs pa bgyis so/ /de nas rang nyid dge sbyor gang 'phel zhig byed snyam pa/ rje mi la ras pa ltar ltogs gugs la ni
mi tshugs/ mi gzhan la re ba las/ a jo drung 'dis skyo ngal med par lto gos thams cad bzabs yang dag gnang ba 'di zab rang khye mod/ ga shed du bsdad kyang lhag por 'u lag
'phel ba las mi 'dug pas nye 'khor shig tu dben dgon chung ngu zhig btab pa'i dge sbyor dang / dad pa dang skal ldan byung na 'chad nyan gong 'phel yin pa la/ khur 'khur
dgos mang po'i sdug po de 'dra ma

yin par rang dbang 'dus la so bsod pa zhig byed snyam pa ltar/ pha bla ma thugs dam brtag pa zhus pas 'di nyid babs byung ba bzhin/ zla ba gsum pa'i nang du dpal sbug 'debs
pa'i 'go tshugs/ zhal ngo bgres gzhon tshang mas las byed rnams la skabs chang / thug pa/ bzhes spro sogs 'phral 'phral du sku drin bskyangs/ nang gzan skya ser rgan gzhon
thams cad kyis las chos su mthong ba'i mos gus kyis dpung pa sa 'og tu bcug pa'i las ka shugs drag tu mdzad/ mnga' zhabs pa rnams kyis las ka blos longs la bzhun pa byas
pa bzhin zla ba lnga pa tshun la shing rtsi tshun zhabs su chud la/ de'i skabs pha bong g.yag drug 'gyur tsam gyi chen po sgril ba sogs drag rngal kho na'i ngang la song
mod/ su la'ang rmas zhur tsam yang med cing legs tshogs kyi rten 'brel mang du byung / de'i tshe rje btsun dam pa pa rnam na phebs 'dug pa nas mjal du phyin/ rdo rje 'jigs
byed zhe dgu ma'i dbang sku drin gyis bskyangs/ pa rnam lhun grub rtse'i zil gnon du slob dpon chen pos lung bstan zhing rigs 'dzin chen po bstan gnyis gling pa'i thugs
sras chos rje dpal 'byor lhun sdings pa'i drung la rang bzhin rdzogs pa chen po dgongs pa zang thal gyi dbang rags pa/ lung shin tu zhib pa/ khrid dmigs kyang yod tsam
dang bcas pa phul/ de nas zla ba bzhi pa la mkhas pa'i 'byung gnas dpal zhwa lu gser bkang gi chos grwar pha bla ma mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen pa chen po'i zhal snga nas
kyi drung du sleb/ nyin re bzhin gsung chos thun gsum ma sku drin bskyangs te/ gsang 'dus rim lnga sogs khrid che chung 'dres pa brgyad so so'i lung dang bcas pa sogs
chos kyi tshul bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i sku drin thob/ brag dmar mkhan chen sogs

dge bshes mang po la/ 'jam dbyangs smra seng / gtsug tor 'bar ba/ sman bla bde gshegs brgyad/ rta mgrin/ sgrol dkar sogs rjes gnang mang po dang / ma Ni bka' 'bum sogs lung
bsam gyis mi khyab pa'ang so so'i thugs bzhed dang bstun nas bar ma chad par phul/ de'i tshe gsang 'dus mi bskyod pa'i dbang ma thob pa mang du 'dug na'ang / pha bla ma
thugs brel gyis gnang ma thub par/ rim lnga don du gnyer ba po rnams kyis nan gyis gsol ba btab/ pha bla ma'i gsung gis cis kyang dbang bskur gyis/ de'ang dpe thog nas lta
ci/ 'gyur mi 'dra ba tshun thams cad mkhyen pa rang gi yi ge na gang yod ma gtogs rigs mthun sbyor ba sogs ye ma byed phebs pa'i bka' ni zlog par ma nus/ de snga slob gnyer
byed pa lta ci smos/ dpe cha yang ma mthong mod/ khong rang tshos dpe cha bskyal byung ba ltar/ nyin mo ni gsungs chos kyi g.yengs nas lta long ye ma byung / mtshan
mo dge sbyor tshar rjes mar me la bzung bas zhag gsum la gtor chog ma gtogs lhan thabs dang bcas pa blo la chud byung ba ltar/ dpal zhwa lu'i drung chen grags pa rgyal mtshan
pa dang / lhun grub pa sogs chen slob phal che ba dang / chos rje brag dmar mkhan chen pa/ e chos sde brag mo che'i chen po/ grwa tshang chen mo ba'i slob dpon sogs
gzhi byes kyi bla ma dge bshes drag bsdus dbang cha gnyis la rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor du dbang rgyas par phul/ de nas sems nyid ngal gso'i khrid gnang ba na sngar phan
dbang dang nges par 'brel ba rang cung ma byung ba 'dra na'ang / spyir yang smin grol ya ma bral ba legs shing / khyad par 'di da lta 'di phyogs bka' chad 'dug pa gso thub
pa na legs phebs pa la/ bka' rgya 'jigs 'jigs gang yang 'dug

pa nas sngar phan ni gsum las mang ba la ma bgyis/ ji ltar bgyid/ 'tshub bzhin ni mi yong ngam zhus pas da lam ngas bka' rgya bkrol bas skyon ci yang med gsung ba nas bka'
ltar bsgrubs/ spyir 'di zhwa lu pa'i chos khams che sa zhig yin pa dang / bka' shin tu dam pa'i stabs kyis ches dkon/ khyad par bka' nub nas yun ring po song ba'i stabs kyis
chos nyams yod pa thams cad mas bu stor ba rnyed pa tsam du dgyes/ dge bshes chen po bgres po yon tan gyi dregs pas 'gying ba rnams kyang byon pa la brten/ dpal bde ba
chen po ral pa gcig pa lha nyi shu rtsa lnga'i rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor chen por/ chos grwa de'i bla ma slob dpon rnam pa brgyad/ srad brag dmar dang / bsam rtse mkhan
chen pa sogs dbang cha gsum la dbang rgyas 'bring bsdus gsum rdzogs pa dang / bla ma 'chad nyan pher ba bcu gsum la byin rlabs gnyis/ rdo rje slob dpon bdag po chen po'i
dbang rnams phul pas thams cad thugs yid ches shing dgyes par bgyis so/ /de nas gong du smos pa bzhin nged rang bo dong na yod pa'i dus nas zhwa lu ba phyogs kyi chos sgor
thams cad ma tshang ba med pa zhus gsung ba dang / yos lo'ang ched du rting bskul gnang gi 'dug pa ltar pha bla ma nyid kyis snga mo'i dus nas dgongs par 'dug cing /
zhwa lu ba'i byis pa chung ngu yan chad mgrin gcig mthun snang grub pa la brten/ sde srid rin po che rin spungs pas kyang dgyes bzhin du grol ba yin gsungs/ nan gyis bka'
gnang ba zlog ma thub/ rang ngos nas chos phyogs nas spangs rtogs kyi yon tan/ 'jig rten phyogs kyi shes myong rgyu cha rkyen sogs gang nas bsam kyang blos lcogs pa'i yul
mi 'dug kyang / bla ma/

dge 'dun dpon slob rnams kyi bka' gcog ma phod par lo gcig gi khas len phul bas/ ngas lo gsum/ khyed kyis lo gcig /de 'dra byas na zhwa lu pa tshos phyag rten kyang mi 'byor
ram/ lo gsum nges par gyis/ de bar skyid na legs/ sdug na bsran/ de nas bong sha za mi za bong bu'i kha stabs kyi dpe/ skyid po byung na tshe dang mnyam par byas na'ang
legs/ sdug po byung na nam byung dus zhog thong / spyir 'di na bstan pa la bsams nas bya ba byed na dgon chung gzhan dang ye mi 'dra byed rgyu gang yang yod cing / 'chad
nyan byed nus na/ sngar phan khyed rang gi dgon chung tshor 'chad nyan byas pa skad sgra nam mkha' la rang dengs mi 'gro/ lag rjes 'jog thub/ 'jig rten nas bsams na skya
ser 'di tsam zhig nar mo ril mo gang byed kyang rang re dbang che/ bza' cher mi bdog ste/ pho rab gtam za zer ba yin/ gnas gsar pa pho rab yin pas gtam dga' mod gsung ba
dang / chen slob zhal rgyas thog tu mtha' bkod mang du phebs pa nas/ nged rang gi legs nyes thams cad khong la re ba yin pas 'di man 'di tshun ni zhu ma spobs/ sems hang
nge ba/ 'jigs zhum me ba zhig la/ bka' bzhin bgyid pa las thabs ma rnyed/ bdag gis chos phyogs nas 'chad nyan sogs dkon cog thugs ma khrel bar bgyid par zhu/ 'jig rten phyogs
nas zhi drag gang dgos kyang chen slob drung rang gis thugs 'gan bzhes/ bdag kha mi 'jug pa zhig byung na ma byung na zhus pas pha bla mas kyang de ga'i bka' nan rgyas
par mdzad/ chen slob drung gis kyang zhal zho mo che'i zhal bzhes mthun grub cig mdzad/ de nas nged kyi pha mes kyi srung ma 'di rung mo zhig bdog pa nas/ yul gsar 'dzin
pa sogs bya ba khams che ba gang byed kyang

gnang ba zhu ba'i tshul re dgos kyis yod pas na rang gnas su 'ong / de tshe char pa shin tu chung ba'i gtsang po sogs kyang chen po ye mi gda' ba la/ nged cag zhwa lu phyogs
la chas tsam nas glo bur char chen po rgyun ring du babs/ gtsang po ba log rta log la rgyas/ shangs chu ni nged 'grul pa rnams snga rting la'ang cher 'gro ba shes nges
kyi tshad bzung med pa bde bar sgrol nas bsam rtser zhag gcig bsdad/ brag dmar nas drung chen gyis gzhi len sogs bzabs po thugs la btags/ zhwa lu pa'i drung chen lho pa thab
'dzin la byon 'dug cing / de skabs sdug chas sprad phyin na zhwa lu pa'i gzi brjid la gnod kyi dogs/ rta khrom/ rkang thang / khal ma sogs mchor la rags pa'i bkod pa
phun sum tshogs pa zhig byas nas phyin pa'i tshe nyin mo nam mkha'i dbus dwangs shing mtha' sprin gyis gtibs pa zhwa lu phyogs nas 'ja' sprin dkar po du mas bsu ba'i tshul
du byas pa kho na byung zhing / thob rgyal dang zhwa lu nas chen slob drung sogs rta bsu'i bkod pa bsam gyis mi khyab pas bsus rim bzhin/ dge lung / khri khang sogs su
bsnyen bkur gya nom pa la rol bzhin du/ pha bla ma'i drung du sleb/ mnyes pa'i gsung dang gzhi len gyi bkod pa dpag tu med pa gnang / zla ba drug pa'i tshes gcig lha'i bla
ma rgyal sar byon pa'i 'grub sbyor dge ba la/ lha dang bcas pa'i 'jig rten pa thams cad dang / phyogs bcu dus gsum gyi nyan thos dang byang chub sems dpa' thams cad kyi
spyi bo'i padma la zhabs sen gyi nyi gzhon gar byed pa'i chos rje thams cad mkhyen pa bu ston rin po che'i zhabs stegs kyi seng ge'i khri la bzhag ste chos kyi 'khor lo
sgyur bar mnga' gsol ba'i tshe dge 'dun rgya mtsho lta bu de'i dbus su seng ge'i khri gnyis bshams pa la

yab sras lhan cig tu bzhugs te/ pha bla mas lugs gnyis nas gdan sa ba dge 'dun dang bcas pa la lugs gnyis kyi blang dor gyi gnas mang du gsungs/ ber thul ne ser bzang po dang
/ sku chos khyad du 'phags pa zhig gis gtsos pa'i gnang sbyin kyang blos mi 'khyud pa gnang zhing rab gnas kyi me tog 'thor bar mdzad pa'i tshe yang char zim bu'i rgyun
lhag par babs/ rin spungs nas sde srid rin po che'i bsko 'ja' khri ston dang bcas pa khri khang nas sde pa rin po ches khri ston mang ja nas 'gyed phun sum tshogs pa dang
/ sde pa gnas gsar nas dang lcags stod nas kyang khri ston rgyas par sku drin gyis bskyangs shing / phyag 'tshal ston mo'ang phun sum tshogs par bsgrubs/ sbyor drug zhu
ba po bla ma slob dpon drag bsdus shig gi gtsos pa'i dbang cha gnyis la dpal dus kyi 'khor lo'i sku gsung thugs yongs su rdzogs pa chos rje thams cad mkhyen pa'i bzhed
pa ji lta ba zhig kyang phul te/ rgyal ba rigs brgya'i khyab bdag bla ma des/ /rgyal tshab sras kyi thu bor dbang bskur tshe/ /rgyal ba sras bcas nam mkha'i khams gang bas/
/rgyal bar gyur ces me tog bsil ma 'thor/ /mchog gi bla ma dus gsum gzigs pa des/ /zhing 'di'i bstan pa spel bar mngon dgongs shing / mthu ldan srung ma'i dbang pos bskul
ba'i mthus/ /seng ge'i khri la de ring dbang bskur thob/ /snyan grags nyi 'od phyogs kun khyab pa'i tshe/ /skal ngan 'byung po'i bya rnams nyon mongs gyur/ /gzur gnas
shes ldan dgyes pa'i padma las/ /legs so'i sbrang rtsi ci yang rgyas par gyur/ /der sbyor drug gi khrid

gsung ba sogs la yun ha cang mi ring ba zhig bzhugs nas yab sras lhan du/ sde pa gnas gsar bas myug tu spyan drangs/ ser sbreng / gar 'chams/ gzhas rgyag /chibs bsu sogs bsu
ba'i bkod pa sngar phyogs der 'ong ma myong ba lta bu'i rgyas pa ci yong dang bcas te bsnyen bkur phun sum tshogs pas mchod/ rgyal ba rdo rje 'chang sgo rum pa chen po'i
dus dran mchod pa grub ma thag /dpal sbug tu spyan drangs/ rje gha ya dha ras bla chen 'brog mi la gsung ngag gnang ba'i gnas la rnam par grol ba zhes grags pa bzhin/ 'dir
yang skal ldan mang po grol ba thob pa zhig yong re bas ming rnam par grol ba'i ri khrod du thogs gsung dgyes bzhin du zla ba bdun gyi bar chos lung nas mkhan chen rin
po che'i zhal snga nas kyi dbu mdzad/ bdag cag skal ba rab tu gyur pa bco brgyad tsam la gsung ngag rin po che lam 'bras bu dang bcas pa'i gdams pa slob bshad thun mong
ma yin pa nyams khrid du gtso bor gsungs te/ dregs ldan bye bas ming yang ma thos pa'i/ /gsang chen slob bshad zab mo'i gnad mtha' dag /nyid kyis gzigs shing legs par stsal
ba'i tshe/ /skal bzang snying la phan bde'i dga' ston thob/ /'khrul med chos kyi snying po 'di thos tshe/ /rab 'byams shes bya'i rang zhal tshur ston byung / /yongs rdzogs
bstan pa'i nyams len rgyud la khel/ /zab zab phal cher ming kyang tsam du song / /zhar byung / mchog sgrub pa'i dmar mo skor gsum/ thun mong sgrub pa'i dmar po skor
gsum/ dmar chung ma skor gsum/

nag po chen po gur gyi mgon po'i phyi nang gi man ngag ci rigs pa dang bla ma shangs pa'i gser chos las chos drug gi byin rlabs khrid lung la sogs pa shin tu zhib rgyas su
gnang ba rnams thob/ de nas re zhig rje bla ma chos lung mkhan rin po ches spyan drangs nas byon/ bdag gis zha lu'i rnam sras mchod pa grub rjes/ zha lu'i mkhan chen rnams
dang sde srid rin po che mjal phrad kyi dkyus shig yod 'dug pa bsrang ba'i phyir/ rta khrom la sogs pa gzi brjid kyi bkod pa dang rnam gzhag mtha' yas pas phyogs lhung
kha cig gi sems mun par byed bzhin du phyin/ thab 'dzin zhal ngo'i chibs bsu sogs sngar 'khyud gang yod las ma zhan pa'i bdag rkyen dang bsnyen bkur sku drin bskyangs te/
khrims gnyis kyi mdun sa chen po pho brang bsam 'grub rtser zhag bcu gsum tsam bsdad pa'i bar sde srid rin po che'i sku rim la tshe dpag med 'chi med rnga sgra'i rdul tshon
gyi dkyil 'khor bsgrub cing mchod pa nyin re bzhin bgyis shing / chos rje brag dmar mkhan chen dpon slob rnams la dpal 'khor lo sdom pa nag po pa dang / kye rdo rje/
rdo rje 'jigs byed chen po lha bcu gsum ma rnams kyi dbang bskur ba dang / rjes su gnang ba dang lung gi bye brag du ma'ang bshad de thugs kha rdzogs par byas nas/ zam 'tsher
'di bstan pa la phan rgyu ye med la/ rnam g.yeng che/ sa phur 'di nged rang gi dge sbyor gyi snying po

zhig yin pa la/ rtsa 'chams sogs bro ba'i rtsed sna ltar song ba'i dam can rnams kyang mnyes rgyu med pa'i ltas kho na yong ba zhig 'dug pa nas nan gyis phul/ slar zha lu nyid
du rang lo so bdun lon pa sprel lo zla ba dang po nas gnyis pa'i bar bsdad de/ sde snod dang rgyud sde'i don la smra ba bslab gsum pa dang / slob dpon rtse mo ba'i drung
sogs gzhi byes kyi snod ldan kha cig la dpal gsang ba 'dus pa mi bskyod rdo rje'i dbang sngon du 'gro ba'i zab lam rim lnga'i dmar khrid shin tu rgyas pa nag khrid sogs
lung rdzogs pa dang / lce'i sngags 'chang dbang po lugs gnyis nas mkhyen pa rgyas pa don yod rdo rjes zhus nas skal ldan kha cig rang bzhin rdzogs pa chen po dgongs pa
zangs thal gyi dbang / khrid lung / bka' srung dang / rdo rje slob dpon gyi gtad rgya'i bar yongs su rdzogs pa bum pa gang 'byor phul ba'i dus nub cig rmi lam du bud med
smug mo 'jigs su rung ba rma bya'i sgro thul khra bun ne ba gyon pa zhig byung nas 'di pa sgom ni gcig kyang mi sgom par 'dug /dmigs pa'i gnad zhib po bstan nas ci byed
zer cung zad khro tshul ston gyi 'dug pa/ bka' srung e ka dza ti'i cho 'phrul du go /khong rang rnams la'ang lha 'dre 'di tshugs zer gyi gda'o/ /ma bsgoms pa min nam byas
pas kun skyengs par gyur/ dmigs pa'ang zhib po ma bshad zom me bzhag pa yin no/ /gzhan yang dpal don yod zhags pa lha nyer lnga'i dbang tshar gnyis/ rdo rje 'jigs

byed zhe dgu ma sogs dbang mang po/ phag dkar dang seng ge gdong can/ las kyi gshin rje/ rdo rje rab brtan ma/ rnam sras zhi drag sogs rjes gnang mang po/ dpal gsang ba 'dus
pa 'phags lugs kyi rgya gzhung phal che ba sogs lung mang po so so'i bzhed pa bzhin bshad/ rje bla ma 'jam pa'i dbyangs byang gling zhabs spyan drangs nas/ kye rdor 'grel
pa sa lugs sogs dbang kha yar dang / chos rje thams cad mkhyen pa'i bka' 'bum gyi lung tshugs pa tsam bgyis rjes/ myug tu 'ongs nas/ dben shrI byang chub sems dpa'i gdung
brgyud du 'khrungs pa'i mtho btsun chos kyi rje sems dpa' chen po bsod nams dpal 'byor pa'i drung sogs la gsang ba 'dus pa 'jam pa'i rdo rje'i dbang / phra mo brag pa'i
dregs 'dul/ padma gling pa'i drag dmar/ rdo rje gling pa'i thugs rje chen po ngan song kun skyob/ gu ru tshe brtan pa'i bla ma zhi drag /rdzogs pa chen po rang byung rang
shar rnams kyi dbang lung man ngag rdzogs par phul/ de nas 'o yug tu rje bla ma zab bur phebs pa'i lam zhor la spyan drangs/ bdog pa'i dngos po ci 'byor phul/ phyag phyi
bgyis zab lung legs par mjal zhing / rim bzhin myug tu phebs chos sde'i bla brang du bzhugs nas/ sgrub thabs rgya mtsho/ shangs chos lhag ma rnams yongs su rdzogs pa
dang / rgyal khang du phebs nas sgrol dkar gyi tshe khrid dang / grub rgyal lugs kyi tshe khrid thun mong ma yin pa rnams sku drin gyis bskyangs te

pha bla ma stod phyogs su phebs mnga' ris rdzong kha'i dge bshes zhig la padma dbang chen yang gsang khros pa dang / rdzong chung ba lugs kyi mgon po che chung rdzogs pa zhig
/bod spyi'i skyabs/ lha btsan po'i gdung brgyud bdag mo mnga' ris ma'i bkas bskul te bshad/ de nas 'o yug tu phyin te/ snga sor zab bur ltas shig mthong ba la brten/ tshar
ma 'ur mar/ dpal sgrub chen bka' brgyad drag po rang byung rang shar chen po'i rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor du rtsa dbang rgyas pa sngon du 'gro ba'i sgrub pa cha lag
shin tu tshang ba'i sgrub dbang thun mong dang thun mong ma yin pa/ tshe lha/ nor lha/ khyung chen/ bstan srung yongs rdzogs te sgrub phran so so'i dbang dang bcas pa zhig
bgyis pa ltar/ nged rang la byin rlabs kyi mtshan ma shin tu che ba zhig byung la/ gzhi bdag lha chen sku mched kyang dgyes pa'i rnam 'gyur mthong / nag pa'i zla ba la/
zhwa lu'i ri phug tu chos rje thams cad mkhyen pa'i dus kyi mchod pa'i skabs su/ de snga yan mkhan pos khro spro mdzad kyi yod 'dug na'ang / mkhan chen chos grub pas gshed
dmar gyi steng nas yo ga'i khro spro sogs ci rigs kyi ngang nas rim bzhin chag 'dug pa la brten/ sa chog gi gar yang 'chag la nye ba 'dug pa dang / khams gsum rnam rgyal
