gyi sgrub mchod kyang chag 'dug pa nas/ khams gsum rnam rgyal gyi steng nas khro spro bgyis pa ltar grwa tshang gsum ga'i gar pa bzabs mchor bton pa'i sa chog

dar rgyas su song ba zhig byung / lo de nged rang gi rang lo yin pa bzhin rmi lam sogs kyang dga' mo med pa kho na dang / 'phral gyi gshis ka'ang cher 'gyur ba'i myur po 'gro
ba la phyogs pa zhig yin na'ang / zla ba bdun pa'i tshes bco lnga nas dpal spug rnam par grol ba'i ri khrod du mtshams bsdams/ lo phyi ma zla ba gsum pa'i tshes bzhi tshun
bcad rgya gang dam dang bcas/ dpal kye rdo rje'i rtsa sngags dang snying po'i gzhi bsnyen kha skong gi sbyin sreg dang bcas pa gegs med du mthar phyin pa ni bla ma dam
pa'i thugs rje'i byin rlabs gcig pur shes par bya'o/ /rang lo so brgyad pa'i bya lo nag zla la ri phug tu chos rje thams cad mkhyen pa'i dus chen thog sleb/ sa chog sngar
bzhin dang / de snga mchod gar 'di rgyun du mi 'dug pas/ bdag gis sbyin sreg pa bgyis/ grwa tshang gsum po'i gar pa bzabs mchod dang bcas pa'i mchod gar lo ltar chags
su 'dzugs pa'i sgrigs bgyis/ de nas zha lu gnas nyid du zla ba gsum gyi bar gtsug lag khang gi zhig bsos dang / bla brang gi mkhar las dbu btsugs/ nged rang ni sde pa khri
khang nas kyi bzhed pa dang bstun/ rgyal po'i khab der yun ring du gnas nas zab rgyas kyi dbang bka' 'bul ba dang sku rim sogs dgongs bzhed bzhin sgrub pa dang / zha lur
slebs nas kyang rje bla ma 'jam pa'i dbyangs kyis dbu mdzad/ dbang cha gnyis la sbyong rgyud dbang tshar

gnyis dang / yon tan du ma la dbang 'byor zhing sde dang bstan pa'i khur gyis mi ngal ba'i chen slob zhal ngo rnam pa brgyad sogs gzhir bzhugs kyi dge 'dun du ma dang / rgyud
sde'i don la dbang 'byor zhing / gar dbyangs bris thig la mkhas pa'i rin lding slob dpon lha mchog pa dpon slob sogs gzhi byes kyi dge 'dun mang po la bde mchog sdom 'byung
/ gshed dmar lha lnga dang bcu gsum ma/ rdo rje 'jigs byed dpa' bo gcig pa/ thugs rje chen po padma dra ba/ tshe dpag med so bdun ma/ gzungs gra lnga/ gur gyi mgon
po lha brgyad sogs dbang mang po/ rgyud sde lnga'i dbang rgyas pa smin byed du btang / khog dbubs kyi bka' gnyis/ gzhung shing gi bka' brgyad/ phyag chen bka' lnga/ mkha'
spyod bka' lnga/ gsang sgrub gsum/ rig gtad dkar dmar/ rta mgrin gsang sgrub/ mgon po bar chad kun sel dang / yid bzhin nor bu sogs skabs bab tu sbyar ba'i ni gu'i phyag
chen chos drug gi myong khrid/ yi ge mtha' dag gi lung ma tshang ba med pa dang / mi tra khrid drug sogs khrid byin rlabs mang po/ sgrol dkar/ 'jam dkar/ sman bla/ 'jam
dbyangs/ a ra pa tsa/ rnam rgyal / rnam 'joms/ rta mgrin nag po zla rgyal lugs/ phyag na rdo rje u tsarya/ gos sngon can/ gtsug tor 'bar ba/ gur gyi mgon po lcam dral/ stobs
'phrog dbang po bsnyen dus/ phyag bzhi pa/ mgon po beng dmar po/ las kyi gshin rje/ rnam sras zhi drag /rdo rje rab

brtan ma sogs rjes gnang mang po/ chos rje thams cad mkhyen pa'i rnam thar sogs lung mang po dang / grub pa'i dpal gyis phyug cing / byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa lhur mdzad
pa skyo ston rin po che yab sras kyis dbu mdzad/ phyogs de'i gsang sngags rnying ma'i gzhung lugs 'dzin pa drug cu tsam la sgrub chen bka' brgyad bde bar gshegs pa thams
cad 'dus pa'i rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor chen por sgrub chen mtshan nyid tshang ba'i sgrubs dbang rgyas pa dang / drag bsdus shig la gsang ba yongs rdzogs kyi dbang dregs
pa'i srog dbang rdo rje rgyal po bka' rab 'byams kyi dbang dang bcas pa rgyas par bgyis la/ de'i tshe yang byin rlabs kyi ltas chen po zhig nged rang la byung / bde gshegs
'dus pa'i rgyud lung nyi shu sogs lung phal che ba'ang bgyis/ rtogs pa'i yon tan bsam gyis mi khyab pa la mnga' brnyes shing drag sngags kyi nus pa mthar phyin pa'i
gnyags ston rin po che dpon slob kyis zhus nas dad ldan mang po zhig la sprul sku padma gling pa'i gter chos bla ma nor bu rgya mtsho'i sta gon dbang chog rdo rje go khrab
nas rnam sras dmar po'i bar dbang thams cad yongs su rdzogs pa dang / padma dbang chen yang gsang khros pa'i dbang tshe dbang dang bcas pa dang gzhan yang byang gter thugs
sgrub rnam gsum gyi dbang lung / gter mgon phyag bzhi pa/ tsa ri zhing skyong seng ge'i gdong can sogs so so'i bzhed pa dang bstun pa'i dbang rjes gnang lung / phyag
len

sogs gang la gang 'os dpe mkhyud med par nyin re bzhin chos thun gsum gsum ma chag par phul zhing / rje bla ma 'jam pa'i dbyangs kyi zhabs las kye rdor bka' babs phyi ma gnyis
kyi dbang / chos rje thams cad mkhyen pa'i bka' 'bum gyi lung yang thun ma chag tsam zhu ba sogs 'di dag gis g.yengs nas zhig bsos rnams la lta long tsam yang ma byung
mod/ nye bar gnas pa'i blo bzang nyid kyis lus ngag yid gsum gyi 'gan khur bas nged rang la rnam g.yengs ci yang med par gang dgos thams cad ma chad la ma lhag pa khrig
khrig legs par grub yong gi 'dug cing / cha rkyen yang bla brang na ni stong pa nyid la stong pa nyid kyis glags rnyed par mi 'dug mod gtso bor myug nas sde pa'i drung gis
yang nas yang du/ nas/ sha /ja/ tha na sbyin tshun lhug par gnang ba dang / chos sde bar sgo bas nas kyi brgya 'bul dang / sde srid chen po khri khang pas brgya 'bul/
chos rje rin po che dge lung pa dang / myug la nye gnas mas kyang nas mang po phul bas rgyu byas tshe dpag med kyi lha khang du tshe dpag med kyi sku stong tsam bzhugs pa
mchog tu bkra ba'i tshon dang bkod pas khyad par du byas pa dang / gsung rab lha khang na bzhugs pa'i po ti brgya phrag mang po legs par sgrigs/ bzhugs khri la bzhugs su
gsol ba dang / gtsug lag khang so so'i gnam rgyan gyi 'degs sogs gang dang ci thams cad la shes ldan gzu bor gnas pa thams cad dga' mgur ngas thub nges 'di grub 'dug pa
bzhin/ rab tu gnas pa'ang rgyud

sde dang mthun par yid ches par bsgrubs/ sde pa gnas gsar bas yo byad mang du gnang ba la bzhi rten rab ston yang rgya cher bgyis la bzhin bkra shis pa'i dge mtshan du ma yang
lhun grub tu byung ste bstan pa la bya ba bgyid pa'i dbu 'di nas brtsams pa yin no/ /tshur lam lha lnga rdzong du zhag gnyis tsam bsdad de/ lugs gnyis la mkhyen pa yangs
pa sde pa rin po che sku skye yab sras me dbon rnams la dgongs bzhed dang bstan pa'i gu ru drag dmar sogs dbang rjes gnang mang du phul zhing / bsnyen bkur 'bul ba'ang
rgyas par mdzad/ myug tu slebs ma thag nas bzung ste/ zhal ngo drung sogs la rje btsun rdo rje bdag med ma/ phyag na rdo rje gtum chen/ bde mchog lU hi pa/ rdo rje 'jigs
byed chen po lha bcu gsum ma/ 'od zer can ma lha lnga/ thugs sgrub kyi dbang rgyas 'bring bsdus gsum dang padma dbang chen yang gsang khros pa/ tshe sgrub nyi zla kha sbyor/
gsang ba 'dus pa/ spyan ras gzigs/ bcu gcig zhal so bdun ma/ a ra pa tsa lha lnga sogs dbang mang po/ sgrol dkar/ rta mgrin/ gtsug tor 'bar ba/ 'od zer can/ mgon po
lha chen dpal 'bar sogs rjes gnang mang po/ gu ru chos dbang gi gter 'byung chen po sogs lung mang po 'bul bzhin pa'i ngang nas/ rje bla ma gnubs sgom sbas pa'i rnal 'byor
las mi tra brgya rtsa'i rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor du dbang rdzogs pa dang / thugs rje chen po'i sgrub thabs brgya rtsa'i rjes gnang sogs

dam pa'i chos mtha' yas pa'i sku drin zhus/ zla ba bdun pa'i tshes nyer gcig nas bstan pa'i bdag po rdo ring rin po che'i dbon du sku 'khrungs pa'i lha btsun chos kyi rje bsod
nams dpal bzang pos dbu mdzad/ 'chad nyan pher nges kyi bla ma lngas gtsos pa'i skal ldan nyi shu tsam la gsung ngag rin po che lam 'bras bu dang bcas pa'i khrid legs
par btsugs/ de dag gi khrod nas rags bsdus shig la dpal nag po chen po gur gyi mgon po lha brgyad kyi rjes gnang dang / mgon po khro bcu zangs gri can gyi rjes gnang sngon
du 'gro ba'i snyan brgyud slob bshad las 'ongs ba'i phyi nang gi khrid/ bdag chen rdo rje 'chang chen po nas brgyud pa'i mgon pod me 'bar ma kha skong dang bcas pa/ ngor
lugs kyi ser pod/ rdzong chen pa lugs dang / gong dkar rdo rje gdan pa'i lugs kyi yi ge rnams ma tshang ba med pa'i lung sogs 'bul bzhin pa 'di yin la/ zla ba dgu pa'i
tshes bzhi nas bzung ste/ dpal sa'i dbang phyug stobs kyi 'khor lo sgyur ba'i sde srid rin spungs nas bkas bskul zhing / rgyal srid chos kyis bskyangs te thub bstan bla
mar mdzad pa'i sbyin bdag chen po gnas gsar nas kyi gnas khang / 'tsho ba'i yo byad thams cad ma tshang ba med par sbyar te/ mtho btsun chos kyi rje myug mkhan rin po che'i
drung dang / lha btsun chos kyi rjes dbu mdzad pa'i bla ma slob dpon blo gsal zhing 'dun pa dang brtson 'grus

kyis mdzes pa'i dge 'dun drug cu tsam la sa chog rgyas pa dang bcas pa'i dpal dus kyi 'khor lo sku gsung thugs yongs su rdzogs pa'i dkyil 'khor du dbang bskur te/ rgyud kyi
rgyal po 'grel pa dang bcas pa'i lung dka' ba'i gnas su bshad pa dang / spyi don gyi bshad pa shin tu rgyas pa cho ga'i lag len dang bcas pa legs par 'chad bzhin pa 'di
yin no/ /de'ang bla ma rdo rje 'chang de'i sku drin gyis bu lugs kyi rgyud kyi bshad bka' dang / jo nang pa lugs kyi phyag len phra rags thams cad la gzhan dring mi 'jog
tsam yod kyang / bu lugs kyi phyag len phra rags bslab phyir/ rje bla ma byang gling 'jam pa'i dbyangs kyang nye bar spyan drangs shing / chos rje sgrom bu pa bya ba'i bla
ma gar 'chams mkhas pa'i tshad ngor chen pa de las lha mo bcu gnyis kyi mchod gar bslab pa sogs nyin mtshan du rang gzhan bslab sbyangs kyi bya bas dus 'da' bar bgyis so/
/de nas zla ba bcu gnyis pa'i nyer drug la pho brang rin spungs su dpon slob rnams chibs bsu la sogs pa'i bsti stang gya nom pas bsus te sleb/ nyer dgu la sa chog gi gar
rgyas pa bgyis pa'i tshe/ me tog gi char kha ba lta bu babs/ sde pa rgyal bu khri thog pa 'di sku gzhon nur gyur pa des/ kho bo cag 'jam pa'i dbyangs dang / slob dpon
padma'i rnam par rim pas gzigs nas 'khor 'dus pa rnams la gar pa'i gtso bo pha gi ni 'di dang

'dir 'dug ces gsungs 'dug /de ltar rim gyis dpal dus kyi 'khor lo'i rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor chen po dpe bya ba'i 'os su gyur pa zhig sgrub cing mchod pa dang / mchod gar
ba drug cu tham pa rgyan dang cha lugs gzhan gyis 'gran par mi bzod pas der 'dus pa'i skye bo rnams snying dga' bar byas/ rab gnas dngos ni/ rje btsun thams cad mkhyen pas
kye rdo rje'i ras bris la brten pa'i rab gnas 'bring po shar tsam zhig gnang / rab ston sha'i phung po spungs pa'i srin po'i grong du sleb pa 'dra ba'i 'jigs zhum me ba
gda'/ de skabs kyi rten 'brel legs nyes ni slob dpon bzang ring gi jag par gda'o/ /de nas rje dam pa dpal byams chen du phebs pa'i drung du brten nas/ dpal sgyu 'phrul
chen po snying rje'i stobs kyi dbang zab mo sngon du 'gro ba'i dbyibs sngags chos kyi bdag nyid can gyi rdzogs rim rgyud kyi bshad bka' dang bcas pa zab mo gtso bor zhus/
zhor nyan gyi tshul du phyag rgya chen po bsam mi khyab/ thugs rje chen po rgyal ba rgyal mtsho sogs dbang byin rlabs du ma lhug par stsal ba rnams zhus/ cho 'phrul chen
po'i tshes bcu bzhi la rong ngur smrig gi gtsug lag khang na bzhugs pa'i rje btsun ma 'di slob dpon thams cad mkhyen pa'i bshes gnyen gyi thugs dam/ paN grub mang po la
gsung byon pa'i ngo mtshar can du 'dug pa'i gsol ba 'debs par phyin te/ sgrol ma maNDal bzhi pa'i gsol 'debs tshar

bdun dang / rje btsun ma lha bcu bdun ma'i rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor du bdag nyid 'jug cing dbang blang ba rgyas par gyis/ de skabs dad ldan mang po zhig gis gsol ba btab
pa'i ngor/ 'dus ba brgya tsam la dbang bskur ba yang bsgrubs te zhag gcig bsdad/ de nas slar yang byams chen du 'ongs nas/ rje dam pas drung du gsung gi bdud rtsi zhu bzhin
pa'i ngang nas/ rje bla ma grub pa'i dbang phyug rong pa'i zhabs spyan drangs te/ 'joms byed 'char ka nag po ri bo che ma'i dbang lung rdzogs par zhus/ byams chen shar
chen pa dang / bde rgyas pa'i dpon slob zhal ngo rnam pas dbu mdzad dge ba'i bshes gnyen du ma la/ dpal 'khor lo sdom pa nag po pa'i dbang / 'jam dbyangs dkar po/ dpa' bo
stobs 'phrog dbang po bsnyen dus sogs so so'i bzhed pa dang bstun pa'i chos du ma zhig bshad de zhag nyi shu rtsa drug bsdad/ de nas rim bzhin yur gur 'ong ste rje bla
ma grub pa'i dbang phyug dge slong chen po ra snga nas dpon sa bdag mo'i ti shrir bzhugs pa sku nas byon pa dang / nged rang kyang da phyin rong 'di la rgyu 'grul cher e
byed mi shes pas da lam mjal ba zhig nges par skabs su bab snyam nas/ ra sngar zhu khrol zhus pas/ nyin 'khor cig khrol byung ba nas yur gur gdan drangs/ tshe dpag med nyer
sgrub kyi dbang dang / gur gyi mgon po lha brgyad kyi rjes su gnang ba zhig zhus/ bsnyen bkur 'bul bas mnyes par bgyis/ sang de rje btsun rong pa'i

zhabs kyang spyan drangs te/ ba do na mnga' bdag mar pa lo tsA ba'i thugs dam dang / mes ston tshon po'i zhal go bzhugs par grags pas mjal du phyin skabs/ rgyal po kho rang
tha mal ba'i btsun pa gra pa brjid chags kyi rnam pas spos phor khyer nas bsu bar byung ba bzhin thams cad kyis mthong bar rlung tshub chung ngu zhig gtsug lag khang gi
mkhris nas byung ste nges kyi thad du sleb nges gdong la phyu ru ru 'gro'i 'dug /byin rlabs rten bzhugs pa'i gdung rten dang / rigs lnga'i li ma sku tshad chen po 'dra 'dug
pa rnams mjal/ sgam zhig na rgyal po'i rten rdzas shel gyi seng ge sogs kha yar 'dug pa rnams kyang bltas/ bstan pa bsrung dgos pa dang / mtha' dmag bzlog dgos pa'i bka'
bsgo rgyas par byas dus kyang / da gi'i btsun pa de shin tu gus pa'i rnam pas nyan zhing bsdad 'dug /de nub nub chos lung nas mkhan chen rin po ches 'bod mi yang yang
gnang byung ba dang / khyad par rje bla ma shar gling pa'i zhabs dang yang da lam tsam ma mjal na slar mjal dka' ba'i 'dun pas chos lung du phyin te/ rje bla ma 'bul bas
mnyes par byas/ tshur kyang dus 'khor kyi rdo sku hor bzo ma zhig gis gtsos pa'i gnang sbyin sku drin tshad med bskyangs/ chos lung bla phrang nas kyang bsnyen bkur rgya
cher mdzad de/ rang byon 'phags pa dang / nub gnas gsar na bzhugs pa'i thugs rje chen po rnams kyi drung du smon lam yid ches pa re btab/ rim bzhin 'o yug gos sngon du slebs
nas dam can mjal ba na/ rje

bla mas de snga ma gzigs pas zhal ras sogs la thugs gzhig 'jug bzhed pa la/ mar me chen po khyer sa ni mi gda'/ rgya mthongs kyi nyi ma yol bas cher mthong rgyu mi 'dug pas/
'di las gsal ba zhig mdzad na 'thad smras ma thag zhal ras kyi thad du me long gi 'od brgyab pa 'dra ba'i 'od dang khyi le ba zhig gzigs rtog ma tshar ring byung ba der
'dus thams cad kyis mthong mod/ rje btsun rong pa'i zhabs de dam can bran du 'khol ba zhig yin pas de'i sku drin yin no snyam/ de nas sdings mar sleb grwa pa sbyin bdag
thams cad dang / gtso bor blo gros bzang pos rgyu sbyar zhing gsol ba btab nas/ thugs rje chen po 'gro ba kun sgrol gyi sgo nas skye bdun ril bu zhag bdun bsgrubs pa'i tshe/
ril bu'i bum pa la gter bdag dang / gzhi bdag rnams skor ba byed pa nged rang gi nyams snang la byung ba bzhin/ gzhi byes kyi gsal snang ba kha res kyang mthong 'dug
/bum pa zhal phye ba'i tshe/ 'ja'i gur phub me tog gi char kha ba ltar babs/ dri bzang pos gling thams cad khyab/ ril bu dril bu bdun 'phel/ gzhi byes kyi skya ser stong
phrag lnga tsam la dbang bskur zhing ril bu bkye nas thar ba'i sa bon skyon med pa btab/ de grol ma thag sgrub chen bka' brgyad bde gshegs 'dus pa chen po'i sgrub pa zhag
lnga bgyis te dbang bskur ba'i tshe yang 'ja' 'od dang me tog la sogs pa ngo mtshar ba du ma zhig byung / rje btsun rong pa'i zhabs las sprul sku

bstan gnyis gling pa'i gter chos gu ru zhi drag /rnam sras/ sprul sku chos kyi rgyal po ratna gling pa'i phur pa sogs dbang lung du ma'i sku drin zhus/ phar yang dgongs bzhed
dang bstun nas/ rang bzhin rdzogs pa chen po bla ma yang tig yid bzhin nor bu'i khrid dang / rgyab chos su rgyud bcu bdun gyi lung rnams dad ldan mang po zhig la phul
ba'i tshe/ nyin re bzhin chos tshugs ma thag chos ra de dang khad nye ba'i rgya skar gyi smin ma'i steng du bya rog re babs nas bdag la phyogs pas chos ma grol bar lhod de
sdod/ grol ba'i bsngo ba tshugs ma thag 'phur 'gro ba ji srid khrid lung ma rdzogs kyi bar byung bas thams cad ngo mtshar du 'dzin gyi 'dug /der rgyun kyang zla ba gcig
tsam bsdad nas/ rje bla ma bdog pa'i dngos po gya nom pas mnyes par bgyis te phyir byon/ bdag gis grogs dag dal 'byor 'di ni g.yo ba dang / 'jig rten skye bo dam pa 'phrad
rnyed dka'/ /zhes gsungs pa ltar dge ba'i bshes gnyen dang yang yang phrad pa ni dus kyi mtha' 'dir ches dkon no snyam nas/ ra gong rgyud/ 'brog pa rgya tsho spang sgang
na rje btsun ra chen dam pa bzhugs pa la mjal du phyin pa na/ dam pa de nyid zhing 'di'i mdzad pa phal cher rdzogs pa zhig pas sku khams shin tu ngan pa zhig mthong nas
yid la gdung ba chen po yang skyes/ gzhan thabs ni cher ma rnyed/ gdan bzhugs bzhin bgyis na bsams kyang / brgya tsho nas nang so ni pa rnam na bzhugs/ gzhir bzhugs kyi

dpon g.yog rnams nged yun ring na mnyes rgyu med tsam 'dra zhing / nged ni lam zhor bar song bas chas rkyen mi 'dug pa zhag gnyis bsdad nas ci shes kyi gsol ba btab/ dngos
su dbang zhu ba la ni zhal 'phros gnang ba'ang shin tu dka' ba zhig 'dug pas zhu ma spobs ting nge 'dzin gyi dbang rgyas pa du ma blangs shing gsol ba btab nas phyir 'ongs
te bsreg shing rin chen sgang du sleb/ sgrub pa zhag gcig kha gso snyam ril bu'i snod kyi dar khug gzhal bas snga sor 'jug dus ril bu snyim pa nyer gsum bdog pa lam bar
du bzhi 'phel 'dug pa bzhin/ dad ldan shin tu mang pos 'dzab skor dang bcas dbang bskur ba na/ gzhi bdag gal cang ba de tha mal pa'i khams 'brog sgang yol gzi brjid can
zhig gi rnam pas dbang zhu ba dang / gter bdag rnams kyang so so'i gzugs kyis skor ba khrims pa sogs byed kyi 'dug pa bzhin/ dad ldan gsum stong tsam la dbang bskur ril bu
bkye dus/ nam mkha' la 'ja' sprin ngo mtshar ba 'dus/ me tog gi char babs rdul dang khrom 'jam zhing thams cad mi phyed pa'i dad pa la dgod par byos/ a ho ayon mkhan po'i
thugs rje dang / /rgyal sras pad dkar 'dzin pa'i smon lam gyis/ /myong grol ril bu'i sgrub pa mthar phyin nas/ /grangs med 'gro ba phan bde'i dpal la sbyar/ /snga mo'i
dus shig rmi lam du khyod kyis sems can 'bum phrag gsum

'khor ba las sgrol nus zhes pa'i lung bstan zhig byung ba de'ang / ril bu 'di la brten nas 'grub pa yin nam snyam/ yang yang du sgrub pa'i zhe dam bcas/ ril bu mi phyugs mthong
ngo cog la byin/ yar 'brog dang byang gi gnam mtsho phyug mo sogs mtsho chen po du ma la yang bskyal/ rgyug chu dang 'thung rgyu m-ig gis mthong tshad la btab cing smon
lam btab bgyis pa yin no/ /de nas g.yas su myug gi pho brang du 'ongs te/ sde pa rin po ches bkas bskul nas der yang chos sde'i 'du khang du sgrub pa zhag gcig kha bsos/
dad ldan stong gdal ba la dbang bskur ril bu bkye ba'i dus kyang kha dog lnga ldan gyi 'ja' gur me tog gi char dang bcas pa byung ba thams cad kyis mthong ba de yin/
de rjes myug pa rin po che bsod nams dpal 'byor gyis myug chos sde cis kyang bzung gsung pa'i nan skyed mdzad phul ba ltar/ bstan pa bso ba la bsams nas bdag tu bzung / yong
sgo gang ci chos rje nyid sku khams bzang ring phyag tu phul/ lugs gnyis kyi 'gan bdag gis 'khur ba'i khungs byas/ zla ba bzhi pa'i nang du ri phug gi dus mchod chen
mo la phyin te/ dge ba'i bya ba mtha' dag sngar las mi dman par bsgrubs/ de rjes zhwa lu gnas su 'ongs te/ rje bla ma byang gling 'jam pa'i dbyangs kyi zhal snga nas dbu
mdzad pa'i dge ba'i bshes gnyen lnga bcu phyin la/ dpal rdo rje 'phreng ba dang kr-i ya bsres pa'i dbang rgyas pa sla

chos su ma song ba'i phyag len ji lta bar phul/ dad ldan ches mang po zhig la 'dus pa mi bskyod rdo rje'i dbang sngon du 'gro ba can gyi rim lnga'i myong khrid/ de dang rjes
'brel gyi rgyud dang / skyed rdzogs kyi rgya bod kyi yi ge mang po'i lung la sogs pa'i nyin re bzhin yang chos thun bzhi bzhi gtong ba ma chag pa dang / rje bla ma 'jam
pa'i dbyangs kyi drung du chos rje thams cad mkhyen pa'i bka' 'bum gyi lung yang ma chag par zhus/ slar myug du 'ongs te/ dus gsum gyi rgyal ba thams cad kyi spyi gzugs/
pha bla ma rig 'dzin chen po dbus nas spyan drangs te/ sgar pa nyi shu phyin dang bcas pa rgyas par bsnyen bkur te/ lcog ro klu phug gi gtsug lag khang du/ gsang ba las
kyang ches shin tu gsang ba dpal sgrub chen bka' brgyad gsang ba yongs rdzogs kyi 'di dus bka' brgyad bye brag pa'i dbang mang po gsan pa la/ de'i tshul rgyas par gnang ba'i
dgongs pa yod pa la/ phyag bris 'phro mar lus pas bar 'dir ma tshang ba 'dug pa mchan bu'i 'di rjes su btab pa yin no/ /de dag ni rang nyid skyes nas da lta'i bar gyi
byas byung rags pa ste/ legs tshogs su gtogs sam snyam pa tshun bris pa yin la/ byas so cog bris na ni la la ni byis pa rnams dgod 'chor la mkhas pa rnams khrel bar 'gyur
ba'ang yod/ la la ni thams cad snying rlung ldang la thug pa'ang yod/ skyon gyi khongs su gtogs pa rnams sbed

pa 'di so so'i skye bo kun gyi srol du 'dug pas yi ger ma bkod mod/ nged kyi spyod pa dang rnam 'gyur rnams thams cad kyis mngon gsum du gzigs pa 'di ga yin pas yi ger bris
ma bris la ma ltos shing / sbas pas sbas go chod par yang mi 'dug ste/ thogs med dus nas goms pa'i bag chags shugs/ /bag med spyod pa mkhas pas khrel pa'i gnas/ /grangs
med bgyis rnams yi ger ga la ldang / /sgrib med mngon sum gzigs pa 'dis chog mod/ /mkhas rnams yon tan sbed pa lhur mdzad mod/ /byis rnams yon tan cung zad ngo sor 'khyer/
/de phyir 'bad pas rang gi yon tan tshogs/ /ma sbas yi ger bkod pa 'di yin no/ /mdor na rab tu byung ba'i mdo don/ tshul gnas thos dang bsam gtan pas/ /sgom pa la ni rab
tu sbyar/ /ces gsungs pa dang mthun pa zhig dgos rgyur 'dug pas de'i dbang du bgyis na/ spyir tshul khrims kyi phung po la nyes pa'i dri ma mi 'byung ba'i rgyu/ ltung ba
rnams kyi spyi dang rang gi mtshan nyid gnang bkag gi spang blang rgyas par shes pa dang / bslab pa la gus pa dang / 'jigs pa dang ngo tsha bas bag yod pa dang / nyon mongs
nyung ba zhes bya ba bzhi po 'di yin pa la/ bdag la de dag cher med cing / de dag gi zlog phyogs rnams shas che bar tshang ba'i mthus sdom pa'i spang blang phra zhing
phra ba ni bsrung ba'i sngon la ngo

yang mi shes par 'dug /'on kyang so so thar pa'i rtsa ba bzhi chang dang lnga po 'di ye ma nyams par yod pa'i khungs yin/ phyis su dgon pa chen po skyong dgos byung ba nas/
rmu rgod zhi bas mi thub ba kha cig la chad pa sogs gtong dgos pa byung ba na'ang / bsam pa'ang de nyid la phan pa gtso bor bsams/ gzhan yang sde dang bstan pa kho na las
bsams pa ma gtogs rang 'dod kyi 'dres med pa byas/ sbyor ba'ang dngos po gang byung dge 'dun spyi la phul ba ma gtogs sger du nas dog gcig la'ang longs ma spyad/ sku rgyal
sogs gang ci thams cad kho rang rnams la byin/ tha na de tshan gyi ja sbyor gcig kyang 'thung ma myong bas 'gyod pa ye med/ nged kyis nyes pa ci yang ma bgyis bzhin du
bsam sbyor ngan pa du mas dngos dang brgyud nas gnod pa byed po mang po zhig bzhud song na'ang / mkha' 'gro chos skyong rnams kyis bden rdzun gnam thig drang por btab/
gang la gang 'tsham pa'i chad pas gcod kyi 'dug pa ma gtogs/ ding sang gi sngags pa kha cig ltar/ las 'bras rgyab tu bor ba'i gtad khram/ 'khrul 'khor/ than ngan sngags su
gtogs pa thun gcig kyang 'dren ma myong / ding sang nged kyi zla re bzhin drug cu pa gtong ba dang / skabs skabs su gur zhal dang rnam sras dang / 'char ka sogs mdos gtor
mang po 'phen pa la

phal che bas mthu kho na byed kyi 'dug ces gleng / nged rang gi grwa pa dad pa che yang yon tan chung ba 'dra'ang sku tshe la gnod zer ngan thabs su go yod pa gda' ste/ gshin
rje dgra nag po'i rgyud las/ lo re'am zla ba re re'am/ /yang na zhag ni re re bzhin/ /gtor ma drug cu rtsa bzhi sbyin/ /dbyug gu drug cu rtsa bzhir dran/ /ces dbyug gu
drug cu rtsa bzhi'i bar chad zhi ba'i phyir nyin re bzhin yang gtong dgos par gsungs/ rdo rje gur las/ las rnams thams cad yang dag spyad/ /ces sems can la phan gdags pa
dang / rang gi bar chad zhi ba'i phyir/ zhi rgyas dbang drag gi las thams cad sgrub dgos par gsungs pas/ bar chad bzlog pa kho na la dmigs nas gtor ma drag po 'di dag bgyis
pa yin pas tshe la mi gnod kyi steng du phan pa myong bas thon gyi 'dug /gzhan du na/ rgyud sde dri ma med pa las gsungs pa'i don/ brgyud pa zam ma chad pa'i snyan brgyud
mkha' 'gro'i kha rlangs thul le ba mang po thos/ lag len phra rags thams cad kyang ji lta bar shes/ sngags smyon grangs med pa zhig song bas lha las su rung ba'i mtshan
ma'ang cung zad thob/ drag po'i las la sbyar na lha tshangs pa'ang sgrol thub tsam bdog ste/ 'chi dgos pa 'di bsams nas zi me bsdad pa lags/ 'on kyang sngar smos pa bzhin
nged la rbod gtong dang / byed kha drag po byed pa de dag bden pa dang / srung bzlog nus pas byed po de dag gi steng du bzlog cing smin par 'gyur bas

na/ nged la bsam ngan 'chang ba de dag chag sgo shin tu che bar nges par bya'o/ /'jig rten phyogs nas ding sang gi bla chen 'dra dang / dka' bcu rab 'byams kha cig ltar/ bde
gzar slong ba'i gros dang bang chen/ mi bsad rta sgyel gyi gros dang lag len la ye mi the bas blo bde ba zhig bdog /byis pa'i dus nas bzung bud med dang rtsed mo byed pa
lta ci smos/ mdzes ma ji snyed pa mthong yang dga' ba la bsams pa tsam yang skye ma myong / tha na rmi lam tsam du'ang bud med la dga' ba skye ma myong zhing / nged sgom
chen pa'i tshan 'di grub grub mo zhig 'dod nas mi chos bla ma 'byung nye'i 'dug na'ang / ma mthong ba mthong dang / ma grub pa grub ye ma byas la/ chang 'di la zhim snang
dang / 'thung 'dod chen mo yong gi 'dug na'ang / gnyen po bsten nas tshogs 'khor gyi dus kyang lces reg tsam las 'thung gi med pas/ bslab bzhi lnga po 'di la bla ma dkon
cog gi drung na ngo nong dgos pa mi bdog /dge 'dun lhag ma man chad ni ji ltar yod shes par mi gda'/ byis pa'i dus nas bzung snying rje dang phan sems shin tu che/ sems
can la phan na nga rang bskal pa'i bar dmyal bar sdod pa la sdug rgyu mi 'dug snyam pa dang / nga rang shi na'ang shi /gzhan 'di tsho la phan na bsam pa dus thams cad du
bcos min du skye ba zhig bdog pas byang sems kyi bslab pa rgyud ldan yin/

rig 'dzin sngags kyi sdom pa'ang rgyud sde bzhi po so so'i rtsa ba dang yan lag gi ltung ba rnams kyi rang bzhin sogs cha tsam shes la/ khyad par bla ma yab sras la mi phyed
pa'i dad pa ci mdzad khyed mkhyen rgyun chags su ldan pa'i don gyis/ yan lag tshang ba'i ltung bas ma phog pa'i khungs yin la/ dus rgyun du ting nge 'dzin gyi dbang dang
/ zla ba re bzhin rdul tshon nam ras bris kyi dkyil 'khor gang rung du dbang yang nas yang du len pa 'dis sngags sdom rgyud ldan du 'byung re ba lags/ de ltar sdom pa gsum
gyis gzhi bzung nas/ ris med pa'i chos la thos bsam bgyis tshul mdo tsam bshad na/ sngar smos pa ltar gyi chos mchog tu sku drin che ba'i bla ma lnga nas bzung ste/ rje
btsun dbon rin po che ngag dbang brtan pa dang / bdag chen chos kyi rje rtse gdong pa'i drung du lam dbang re thob pa dang / bdag chen khri thog rin po che dang / chos
rje spre chung rin po che las bla ma'i rnal 'byor tsam dang / gnyag ston chen po bkra shis sgang pa las sme brtsegs kyi khrus dbang zhig thob pa yan chad du bla ma dam pa
sum cu rtsa gnyis mnyes par bgyis te chos kyi tshul ji snyed cig thob mod/ bla ma gang las gang thob pa dang / de dag kyang brgyud pa rnam par dag pa gang las 'ongs pa
dang / de dag gi nang gsel gyi dbye ba phra mo ji snyed yod pa rnams ni bdag gis dam pa'i chos thos pa'i tshul gsal bar ston pa yid bzhin gyi nor

bu rin po che dbang gi rgyal po'i snang ba zhes bya bar bkod zin pas don du gnyer na der gzigs par bya zhing / 'dir rtogs sla zhing yi ge nyung ngu'i slad du tho tsam brjod
na/ thog mar theg pa dman pa nyan thos kyi gzhung la so sor thar pa'i mdo/ tshul khrims dang yang dag par ldan pa'i mdo/ dge tshul gyi tshig le'ur byas pa sum brgya pa dang
/ de'i 'grel pa 'od ldan/ tshig le'ur byas pa lnga bcu pa/ chos rje thams cad mkhyen pas mdzad pa'i las chog dri ma med pa'i phreng ba/ karma sha taM gi TI ka /kun mkhyen
nam bsod kyis mdzad pa'i 'dul ba'i bslab bya rgyas pa rnams legs par thob/ dbu sems lugs gnyis kyi sems bskyed legs par zhus nas/ theg chen thun mong gi chos/ rgyal
ba'i yum rgyas pa 'bum du grags pa le'u bdun cu rtsa gnyis bam po sum brgya'i bdag nyid/ yum 'bring po nyi khri lnga stong pa le'u bdun cu rtsa drug dang / yum bsdus pa brgyad
stong pa le'u so gnyis sa/ rdo rje gcod pa/ sdud pa tshigs su bcad pa/ 'phags pa dkon mchog brtsegs pa chen po sdom pa gsum bstan pa nas bzung ste/ gtsug na rin po
ches zhus pa'i bar mdo'i rnam grangs bzhi bcu rtsa dgu/ 'dus pa rin po che tog rnams dang / slob dpon dpa' bos mdzad pa'i byang chub sems dpa'i skyes rabs so bzhi pa dang
/ dgra bcom pa chos skyob kyis bsdus pa'i ched du brjod pa'i tshoms te dad pa'i gzhung gnyis/ theg pa chen po mdo sde rgyan dang / slob dpon

'phags pa thogs med kyis mdzad pa'i byang chub sems dpas ste lta ba'i gzhung gnyis/ rgyal ba'i sras po zhi ba lhas mdzad pa'i bslab pa kun las btus dang / spyod pa la 'jug
pa ni spyod pa'i gzhung ste/ bka' gdams gzhung pa rnams kyi chos kyi nying khu gzhung drug tu grags pa/ byang chub spyod pa'i sgron ma dang / bden pa gnyis la 'jug pa nas
bzung ste/ skyabs 'gro yan lag drug pa'i bar gzhung chung brgyad cu gya brgyad tsam bzhugs pa la chos chung brgya rtsar grags pa/ bka' gdams glegs bam rin po che dang /
thig le bcu drug gi khrid thun mong dang / thun mong ma yin pa theg pa chen po blo sbyong gi khrid/ rten 'brel snying po'i khrid/ sum pa lo tsA ba'i snyan brgyud kyi khrid/
blo sbyong zhen pa bzhi bral gyi khrid/ skyid sdug lam khyer gyi khrid/ skye med do pa'i lugs kyi gcod khrid/ de dag so so'i yi ge mang po'i lung / blo sbyong mtshon cha
'khor lo/ rma bya dug 'joms/ byams pa'i rnal 'byor pa'i gyer sgom rdo rje'i glu/ sems dpa' rim pa/ rnam dag gtsug gi nor bu/ 'gro mgon dpal yes mdzad pa'i khrid yig dang
/ sems dpa' chen po rgyal mchog pa'i blo sbyong zin bris chen mor grags pa rnams thob/ theg chen thun mong ma yin pa rdo rje theg pa nyid la'ang dbye ba bzhir bzhugs pa'i
dang po bya ba'i rgyud la yang / rigs kyi sgo nas drug tu phye ba las/ dang po de bzhin gshegs pa'i rigs la/ gtsug tor nas byung ba'i gdugs kar mo can zhe gnyis kyi dbang
rgyas pa dang /

gdugs dkar lha bcu bdun ma'i rig gtad kyi dbang / rig sngags kyi rgyal mo srung ba lnga lha lnga bcu rtsa gcig gi rig gtad kyi dbang / padma'i rigs la rigs kyi bdag po tshe
dpag med lha dgu dang / 'chi med rnga sgra'i dbang dang dze tA ri'i gzhung gsum gyi lung / tshe dpag med lha dgu paN chen nags rin lugs kyi dbang / rigs kyi 'khor lo sgyur
ba dpal don yod zhags pa lha nyer lnga'i dbang / 'phags pa bcu gcig zhal lha so bdun pa'i dbang phyag mtshan zhe gnyis kyi rjes gnang dang bcas pa/ rdo rje'i rigs la/
rigs kyi bdag po rdo rje mi 'khrugs pa lha dgu'i dbang zhus nas dze tA ri'i gzhung gsum gyi lung / 'khor lo sgyur ba phyag na rdo rje 'gro bzang lugs kyi dbang dang rjes
gnang / slob dpon 'gro bzang gis mdzad pa'i sgrub thabs sogs yi ge mang po'i lung / bram ze ma Ni badzra gyis bkral ba'i rnam 'joms mthing nag lha bcu dgu pa dang / bram
ze'i slob dpon pa ba ri pas bkral ba'i rnam 'joms dkar po lha bcu dgu pa gnyis kyi dbang dang / ma Ni badzra gyi lugs kyi gtso rkyang gi sgrub thabs sogs rgya gzhung bcu
gcig /rje paNDi ta pas mdzad pa'i sgrub thabs dkyil chog gtso rkyang gi mngon rtogs gsum dang / sa ba ri ba'i gzhung gsum gyi lung / phyag na rdo rje mdo lugs brtag pas che
ba'i lha dgu'i dbang dang / lha lnga'i rjes gnang / gzungs/ gzungs kyi 'grel pa klu sgrub kyis mdzad pa sogs rgya bod kyi yi ge rab tu mang po'i lung rnams thob/ spyod
pa'i rgyud la rigs gsum du bzhugs pa'i phyi ma gnyis kyi dbang ni mi snang la/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i rigs

rnam par snang mdzad mngon par byang chub pa sku mi zad pa rgyan gyi 'khor lo snying rje chen po 'byung ba lha brgya dang bcu dgu'i dbang / rtog pa las gsungs pa'i 'od zer
can lha nyer lnga dang / lha lnga'i dbang / 'jam pa'i dbyangs a ra pa tsa na lha lnga'i dbang rnams legs par thos/ rnal 'byor gyi rgyud la/ rtsa ba'i rgyud kyi dum bu dang
po de bzhin gshegs pa'i rigs dpal rdo rje dbyings rtsa ba'i lha so bdun/ mgron thabs stong dang bcas pa'i dkyil 'khor chen por rtsa ba dang / 'grel pa lugs te dbang gnyis/
dum bu gnyis pa rdo rje'i rigs khams gsum rnam rgyal rtsa ba'i lha so bdun mgron thabs stong dang bcas pa'i dbang / bshad pa'i rgyud la rdo rje rtse mo las gsungs pa'i
gsang ba mchod chen rigs bsdus pa'i dkyil 'khor lha stong dang nyis brgya bdun cu rtsa gcig gi dbang / cha mthun pa'i rgyud dpal mchog rigs bsdus pa lha sum brgya sum cu
rtsa dgu'i dbang / dpal mchog rdo rje sems dpa'i dbang / 'phros pa'i rgyud ngan song thams cad yongs su sbyong ba kun rig rnam par snang mdzad rtsa ba'i lha so bdun/ mgron
thabs drug cu 'jig rten pa dang bcas pa'i dbang / shAkya sengge gtsug tor dgu pa lha so bdun/ phyag na rdo rje 'chi bdag 'joms pa lha bcu gsum/ mi 'khrugs pa jo bo rje'i
lugs lha bcu gsum pa/ yan lag gi rgyud mtshan yang dag par brjod pa slob dpon 'jam dpal grags pas legs par bkral ba'i bcom ldan 'das chos kyi dbyings gsung gi dbang phyug
nam mkha' ltar yangs

shing dri ma med pa lha nyis brgya dang nyi shu rtsa dgu/ slob dpon sgeg pa'i rdo rjes bkral ba'i 'jam dpal gsang ldan lha lnga bcu rtsa bdun/ slob dpon 'jam dpal bshes gnyen
gyis bkral ba'i nam mkha'i dri med rigs bsdus pa'i dkyil 'khor te thams cad mkhyen pa bu ston chen po'i phyag len las 'ongs pa'i dkyil 'khor bcu gsum po de dag gi rdul
tshon kho nar dbang bskur ba dang / kun rig rtsa ba'i dkyil 'khor/ shAkya seng ge sku/ tshe dpag med gsung / phyag na rdo rje thugs/ 'khor lo sgyur ba yon tan/ me ltar 'bar
ba 'phrin las te 'das pa'i dkyil 'khor drug /phyag na rdo rje la lha chen brgyad/ klu chen brgyad/ gza' brgyad rgyu skar dang bcas pa/ 'jigs byed dgu/ rgyal chen bzhi/
phyogs skyong bcus bskor ba 'jig rten pa'i dkyil 'khor drug ste sbyong rgyud dkyil 'khor bcu gnyis su grags pa snur lugs kyi phyag len dang / kun rig rtsa ba'i dkyil 'khor
dang / phyag na rdo rje 'chi bdag 'joms pa ste sa lugs ma yin pa gnyis te/ rnal 'byor rgyud kyi dbang de dag thos shing khong du chud par byas pa yin no/ /rnal 'byor
chen po bla na med pa'i rgyud la'ang / thabs/ shes rab/ gnyis su med pa gsum gyi dang po la'ang rigs drug gam gsum du bzhed pa las/ 'dod chags chen po'i thabs/ rgyud dpal
gsang ba 'dus pa mi bskyod rdo rje lha so gnyis kyi rdul tshon

gyi dkyil 'khor du dbang bskur ba zhus nas zab pa las kyang ches shin tu zab pa mar lugs kyi rim pa lnga dmar khrid myong khrid du thob cing / slob dpon 'phags pas mdzad pa'i
rim lnga'i gzhung / sgrub thabs mdor byas/ mdo bsre/ klu'i byang chub kyi dkyil chog nyi shu pa/ rnam gzhag rim pa/ Arya de ba'i spyod bsdus sgron me/ bdag byin rlabs/
sems kyi sgrib sbyongs/ sgra gcan zin dpal bshes gnyen gyi dkyil chog zung 'jug gsal ba/ gser sdings pas mdzad pa'i brgyud pa'i rnam thar sogs nag khrid kyi yi ge nyi shu
rtsa lnga/ chos rje thams cad mkhyen pas mdzad pa'i dmar khrid kyi khrid yig brgyud 'debs gnyis dang bcas pa dang / lo chen byang rtses mdzad pa'i khrid yig /'dus pa rtsa
ba'i rgyud 'phags lugs thun mong ma yin pa'i bshad rgyud bzhi dang bcas pa thos shing khongs su chud la/ slob dpon ye shes zhabs kyis bkral ba'i 'dus pa 'jam pa'i rdo
rje lha bcu dgu'i dkyil 'khor du bla ma penta pa'i dkyil chog dang mthun par sa lugs thun mong ma yin pa'i dbang dang / bzhi brgya lnga bcu pa dang mthun par brgyud pa du
ma bka' babs 'dus pa'i dbang rgyas par zhus nas sgrub thabs kun bzang / 'jam dpal zhal lung / grol ba'i thig le/ bzhi brgya lnga bcu pa rnams kyi lung khro bcu gnyan lugs
kyi rjes gnang man ngag dang bcas pa'ang thos/ slob dpon chen po mar me mdzad kyis bkral ba'i 'dus pa spyan ras gzigs

lha bcu dgu'i dbang rdzogs par thob/ mi bskyod pa'i byang sems kyi rigs phyag na rdo rje 'khor lo chen po lha bco brgyad kyi dbang bskyed rdzogs kyi khrid dza ba ri pa'i gzhung
bco brgyad sogs rgya bod kyi yi ge mang po'i lung / padma'i rigs/ dpal bde ba chen po ral pa gcig pa lha nyer lnga'i dkyil 'khor du dbang re re la dbang bzhi bzhi sbyar
ba'i dbang rgyas pa/ dbang bsdus pa/ ye shes 'pho ba'i byin rlabs/ yum ral gcig ma'i byin rlabs/ rdo rje slob dpon bdag po chen po'i dbang rnams zhus nas/ rgyud kyi rgyal
po/ spyi 'chings nang 'chings/ slob dpon mi pham sbas pa'i bshes gnyen gyis mdzad pa'i sgrub thabs sogs rgya gzhung mang po/ de dag don 'grel sogs rje khro phu bas mdzad
pa'i mdo gzhung mang po/ 'phags pa thugs rje chen pos gnang ba'i rdzogs rim sems nyid ngal gso'i myong khrid/ de'i rdo rje'i tshig rkang rtsa 'grel sogs yi ge mang po'i
lung / rdo rje mkha' 'gro gnyis kyis gnang ba'i rdzogs rim la/ dbang po rab tshe 'dir 'tshang rgya ba gser bzo mkhan mkhas pas gser la rgyan du bkod pa lta bu'i man ngag
la rdo rje'i lam/ sbas pa'i lam/ gsang ba'i gsum cha lag dang bcas pa/ dbang po 'bring 'chi khar grol ba khyung sgong rgya las grol ba lta bu'i man ngag /dbang po tha
ma bar dor grol ba sha btson khri mon las grol ba lta bu'i man ngag sogs yab kyi skor/ yum gyi skor la/ brgyud pa lo rgyus kyi gdams

ngag gis gang zag yid ches bskyed pa nas/ sku gsum rang chas kyi man ngag gis 'khor ba ma stongs bar du 'gro don bya ba'i bar gyi gser chos bco lnga/ bka' srung gnod sbyin
spun gnyis kyi gdams pa dang bcas pa dang / zhe sdang chen po'i thabs rgyud/ dpal gshin rje gshed dmar po lha lnga'i bdag nyid can gyi dbang bzhi yongs su rdzogs pa/ shin
tu spros med/ rnam rtog 'od gsal bdud rtsi'i byin rlabs rnams zhus nas/ shin tu spros med kyi myong khrid/ rnal 'byor dbang phyug chen po'i sgrub thabs che chung sogs bskyed
rdzogs kyi gzhung brgyad/ theg chen chos rjes mdzad pa'i gzhung bshad sogs bod kyi yi ge mang po'i lung / dpal gshin rje gshed dmar po lha bcu gsum pa'i dkyil 'khor
du dbang bskur ba dang / rnal 'byor bzhi'i byin rlabs/ bdud rtsi'i lha mo 'od 'dzin ma dkar mo'i byin rlabs/ 'khrul 'khor gyi byin rlabs/ phyir bzlog gi byin rlabs/ 'pho
ba'i byin rlabs rnams zhus nas rnal 'byor bzhi'i khrid/ grub thob kyi 'khor lo sgyur ba dpal 'dzin gyis mdzad pa'i rnal 'byor bzhi'i de kho na nyid la sogs pa'i gzhung brgyad/
glo bo lo tsA ba chen po'i khrid yig sogs bod kyi yi ge rab tu mang po dang / yang gshin rje gshed dmar po chag lugs thun mong ma yin pa dbang stegs sogs dang bcas
pa'i dbang bzhi rdzogs pa/ chag lo gsum pa'i yi ge mtha' dag dang bcas pa'i lung / bcom ldan 'das gshin rje'i dgra nag po zhang lugs

kyi dbang yongs su rdzogs pa/ gshin rje gshed 'byung ba grub chen lA li tas mdzad pa/ de'i rnam bshad gshin rje gshed kyi zhing khams bkod pa la 'jug pa'i rgyan gyi lung /
rwa lugs kyi gshin rje zhal gsum pa lha bcu gsum dang / zhal drug pa lha nyer gcig pa'i dbang / dpal rdo rje 'jigs byed chen mo drag po khros pa lha bcu gsum pa'i dbang /
ro langs chen po brgyad kyis bskor ba dang / dpa' bo gcig pa phyag mtshan gyis bskor ba'i dbang rnams zhus nas/ mkhas rlom phal che bas ma thos shing / mos pa tsam yang
skye bar dka' ba'i zab chos rwa khrid mkha' 'gro snyan brgyud kyi nyams khrid/ thun mong du grags pa rdo rje'i tshig gi rnam par dbye ba'i khrid/ rnal 'byor bzhi'i rim pa'i
khrid/ bskyed rdzogs zung 'jug gi khrid/ de dag gi rgya bod kyi yi ge rnams kyi lung / rtsa ba'i rgyud rtog pa bdun pa la rwa chen lo tsA ba'i bzhed pa ji lta ba'i bshad
bka' dang / sngags btu'i byin rlabs/ rgya ston rin po che'i lugs kyi bshad bka'/ bshad rgyud rtog pa gsum pa'i bshad bka'/ dngos grub rtog pa zhi ba'i rgyud/ las mkhan
ti'u lo pa'i rtog pa sogs rwa dpon shes rab rgyal mtshan gyi dkar chag dang mthun pa'i man ngag gi yi ge rwa pod du grags pa/ rgya ldong rnam pa gnyis dang / bod kyi dpal
'dzin gyis sbyar ba'i man ngag yi ge rab tu mang po'i lung / dug dbang rma bya rgyas pa man ngag dang bcas pa/ 'chi bdag gshin rje'i dbang phyug chos kyi rgyal po lha bcu
gsum pa/ dmar po bse bya bzhis

bskor ba/ khrag mdog yab yum rnams kyi rjes su gnang ba man ngag dang bcas pa/ rje btsun sa skya pa las brgyud de 'ongs pa'i rdo rje 'jigs byed lha dgu'i dbang / dpa' bo gcig
pa'i rjes gnang / rtog pa bdun pa'i bshad bka' dang bcas pa/ zhang lo tsA ba shes rab bla ma nas brgyud de 'ongs pa'i rdo rje 'jigs byed chen mo lha bzhi bcu rtsa dgu
zhi khro rnam par rol pa'i dbang dang / de'i sgrub thabs/ rnam par 'phel ba/ sbas pa'i spyod pa bsdus pa rnams grub chen lA li tas mdzad pa/ sbas spyod kyi don bsdus pa/
drag po'i 'khrul 'khor gyi man ngag gi lung / skyo lo tsA ba las brgyud de 'ongs pa'i rdo rje 'jigs byed chen po lha bcu bdun ma'i dbang drag po'i dbang bdun gyi rjes gnang
dang bcas pa/ skyo mi bskyod pa'i yi ge'i steng nas rtog pa bdun pa gsum dang / gnyen rin chen brtan gyi yi ge'i steng nas gtam rgyud kyi rtog pa'i bshad bka'/ rwa rtse
sems 'dzin gyi nyams khrid yi ge'i lung dang bcas pa rnams legs par nos shing khong du chud par bgyis pa yin no/ /shes rab kyi rgyud la rigs drug tu bzhugs pa las/ rigs
drug cha mnyam du ston pa/ dpal sangs rgyas thams cad dang mnyam par sbyor ba mkha' 'gro ma sgyu ma bde mchog rigs bsdus pa lha brgya dang nyi shu rtsa bdun gyi dbang /
he ru ka'i rigs/ rgyud de nyid kyi snying po dpal he ru ka zla gam gcig pa lha lnga bcu rtsa brgyad kyi dkyil 'khor du dbang rgyas bsdus/ grub chen hU~M kA ra'i sgrub dkyil
gyi lung dang bcas pa/ slob dpon rdo rje rnon pos

bkral ba'i mkha' 'gro rgyun gtor lha dgu'i dbang man ngag mtha' dag lung dang bcas pa/ slob dpon brtul zhugs kyi spyod pa nag pos bkral ba'i 'khor lo sdom pa lha drug cu rtsa
gnyis kyi dbang / nag po rim bzhi dang / dpyid kyi thig le'i nyams khrid/ slob dpon des mdzad pa'i bskyed rdzogs kyi gzhung drug /de dag gi sa bcad TIka sogs rje btsun
brtse ba chen pos mdzad pa sogs man ngag 'bum du grags pa'i lung / slob dpon lU hi pas bkral ba'i sgong skyes sbyong byed sa lugs kyi dbang / rtsa dbu ma'i nyams khrid/
bsdu ba gsum pa'i khrid/ bde mchog dkar po'i byin rlabs/ de'i khrid/ dpal mngon par rtogs pa sogs lU hi pa smad lnga'i lung / yang rtag pa'i rdo rje dang dA ri ka pa sogs
kyi gzhung gi don brgyud pa'i bka' babs bdun ldan pa'i dbang rgyas pa/ slob dpon dril bu zhabs kyis bkral ba'i rdul tshon lha lnga dang / zab mo lus kyi dkyil 'khor gyi
dbang dang / dril bu skor gsum gyi lung rim pa lnga pa'i khrid/ de'i byin rlabs/ grub chen lwa ba pas bkral ba'i sbyangs pa'i yon tan lha bcu gsum gyi dbang / grub chen kA
la kalpas bkral ba'i rdo rje mkha' 'gro lha drug cu rtsa gnyis kyi dbang / rdo rje mkha' 'gro'i rgyud 'grel slob dpon bha ba bha dras mdzad pa'i lung / dpal sdom pa 'byung
ba lha bcu gsum gyi dbang / grub chen mai tri pas bkral ba'i lha bcu gsum pa'i dbang / grub chen tai lo pa'i lugs kyi lha

drug cu rtsa gnyis/ lha bcu gsum/ lha lnga rnams kyi dbang bzhi rdzogs pa/ rdo rje phag mo lha mo bco lnga/ lha bdun ma/ lha lnga ma/ lhan cig skyes ma rnams kyi byin rlabs/
ras chung snyan brgyud du grags pa'i nyams khrid/ nor bu skor gsum gyi yi ge mtha' dag gi lung snyan brgyud mgon po'i rjes gnang gi bar yongs su rdzogs pa/ paN chen nags
kyi rin chen nas brgyud pa'i sdom pa bcu gsum pa'i dbang / rdo rje phag mo lha bcu gsum ma'i dbang / dpal mkha' 'gro rgya mtsho 'khor lo bcu gnyis su mngon par brjod pa
lha stong dgu brgya dang bco brgyad pa'i dbang / dpal sdom pa bong zhal can lha so bdun gyi dbang / phag mo mngon par 'byung ba'i rgyud las gsungs pa'i rdo rje phag mo lha
so bdun/ bcu gsum/ lha lnga rnams kyi dbang / rdo rje phag mo zhal gnyis ma/ nA ro mkha' spyod/ mai tri mkha' spyod de/ rje btsun sa skya pa'i thugs kyi nying khu mchog
bsgrubs pas thun mong zhar la 'byung ba'i dmar mo skor gsum gyi byin rlabs/ rtsa dbu ma'i nyams khrid/ mi dbang chos gsum sogs rgya bod kyi yi ge rab tu mang po'i lung
/ phag mo zhal gnyis ma/ dbu bcad ma/ don grub ma ste dpyal lugs kyi phag mo skor gsum gyi byin rlabs/ sgom pa drug pa'i nyams khrid/ rgya gzhung bdun/ thun mong / mchog
/khyad par gyi zhal gdams sogs yi ge rab tu mang po'i lung / phag mo ser mo rus sbal zhabs kyi byin rlabs/ bskyed rdzogs kyi khrid/ yi ge'i lung /

phag dkar shes rab gsal byed kyi byin rlabs/ de'i rjes gnang / rgya bod kyi yi ge thor bu'i lung / phag dkar paN chen lugs kyi byin rlabs/ ras chung pa'i phag mo khams gsum
ma'i byin rlabs/ phag mo sgar lugs kyi byin rlabs/ rlung sems dbyer med kyi nyams khrid/ phag mo'i rin chen rgyan 'dra'i byin rlabs dang / sa ra ha'i bde mchog dkar po yab
yum go ldog pa'i byin rlabs/ go cha'i dpa' bo drug dang / dpa' mo drug gi byin rlabs/ bo dong pa lugs kyi bde mchog dkar po zab pa bzhi ldan gyi byin rlabs man ngag dang
bcas pa rnams dang / dpal sangs rgyas thod pa lha nyer lnga'i dbang / sgyu 'phrul chen mo lha lnga'i dbang rnams thos/ mi bskyod pa'i rigs dpal phyag na rdo rje gtum po
chen po lha nyer gcig pa'i dbang / rdzogs rim gyi nyams khrid/ rgyud kyi bshad bka'/ man ngag gi yi ge mang po'i lung dang bcas pa/ dpal phyag na rdo rje gtum po ras chung
lugs lha nyer lnga'i dbang / lha lnga pa'i dbang / dpa' bo gcig pa'i rjes su gnang ba/ gsang ba bstan pa'i rgyud sogs man ngag yi ge mang po'i lung / dpal phyag na rdo
rje u tsArya lha bcu dgu pa'i dbang / de'i rjes gnang thun mong dang thun mong ma yin pa/ rgyud gsum cha lag dang bcas pa'i lung rnams nos shing / brtag pa'i rigs mi g.yo
ba bla med lha bcu gsum pa'i dbang / rgyud dang / glo chen gyi sgrub dkyil gyi lung / padma'i rigs la mgon po tshe dang ye shes dpag tu med pa grub pa'i rgyal mo'i lugs

lha so bdun ma'i dbang bzhi yongs su rdzogs pa/ de'i nyer grub kyi dbang / lha bcu gsum ma'i dbang bzhi/ de'i dbang bsdus pa/ lha gcig bum gcig gi dbang / tshe zan la brten
pa'i dbang / tshe khrid thun mong dang thun mong ma yin pa'i lung dang bcas pa/ dpal thugs rje chen po padma dra ba lha zhe drug gi dbang dang / rje mi tra'i lugs kyi gsang
sgrub bcu gsum ma'i byin rlabs/ rtog pa las gsungs pa'i ku ru kulle lha lnga'i dbang / rtog pa le'u lnga pa dang / de'i man ngag gi lung rnams thos/ rta mchog gi rigs/
dpal rdo rje gzhon nu lha lnga bcu rtsa gcig gi stod las byang chub sgrub pa'i dbang / rgyud dang / rje btsun sa skya pa chen po yab sras/ rje bla ma rnams kyis mdzad pa'i
yi ge rnams kyi lung / yar phur gyi rdzogs rim zab mo a ti bsam gtan gling pa'i lugs kyi nyams khrid/ de'i yi ge mtha' dag gi lung / rje btsun sgrol ma lha bcu bdun ma'i
dbang / sgrol ma lus dkyil lha nyer lnga'i dbang rnams thob bo/ /gnyis su med pa'i rgyud la/ dpal dus kyi 'khor lo rwa 'bro rnam pa gnyis ka'i phyag len phyogs gcig tu
byas pa/ chos rje thams cad mkhyen pa'i bzhed pa'i dbang bdun/ gong ma/ gong chen dang bcas pa dang / 'bro lugs gtso che zhing / rgyud 'grel sor bzhag las rgya gzhung gi
rjes su mi 'brang ba kun mkhyen jo nang pa'i lugs kyi 'jig rten dang 'jig rten las 'das pa'i dbang bcu gcig /rdo rje slob dpon bdag po chen po'i dbang / dpal sdom pa chen
po lha bdun cu rtsa gnyis kyi dbang /

las rgyas pa'i lha/ sna tshogs yum/ rdo rje shugs/ khyung khra rnams kyi rjes su gnang ba/ bsdus pa'i rgyud kyi rgyal po/ rgya cher 'grel pa dri ma med pa'i 'od dang bcas pa/
chos rje bla ma dam pas mdzad pa'i TIka chen gyi steng nas bshad bka' shin tu rgyas pa/ rdo rje snying po'i 'grel pa dang / bde mchog bstod 'grel/ dbang mdor bstan/ rgyud
phyi ma/ bla ma yongs bzungs kyi rgyud rnams dang / sbyor ba yan lag drug pa'i nyams khrid bu dol rje bla ma'i lugs te gsum/ paN chen nags rin lugs dang / de dag dang
'grel ba'i rgya bod kyi yi ge rab tu mang po mtha' yas pa'i lung / grub chen ayon pas rdo rje rnal 'byor ma las dngos su nos pa'i zab lam rdo rje gsum gyi bsnyen sgrub kyi
myong khrid/ zla seng ba'i lugs ma tshang ba med pa dang / bsod nams 'od zer ba'i gzhung bshad sogs yi ge mang po'i lung rnams thos shing khongs su chud par bgyis/ dpal
kye rdo rje'i phyogs la bka' babs bzhi bzhugs pa las thog mar rje btsun rnal 'byor gyi dbang phyug dpal ldan chos skyong bir wA pa'i gsung gi man ngag rje gha ya dha ra
las brgyud de 'ongs pa man ngag lugs su grags pa'i yab kyi rgyud dang lam gyi dbang gi chu bo ma nub pa/ yum gyi rgyu'i dbang / byin rlabs kyi brgyud pa ma nyams pa rnams
zhus nas/ bstan pa yongs rdzogs kyi nyams len gsung ngag rin po che lam 'bras bu dang bcas pa'i slob bshad thun mong ma yin pa'i

myong khrid dang / tshogs bshad kyi khrid/ brda don gsal ba'i byin rlabs myong khrid dang bcas pa/ lam sbas bshad kyi myong khrid/ lam zab mo bla ma'i rnal 'byor phyi nang
gi byin rlabs/ de'i myong khrid/ nang gi lam zab kyi byin rlabs cung mi 'dra ba zhig bla ma rin 'byung dang / tshar gsum khug pa'i byin rlabs/ rnam 'joms bir lugs lha bdun
cu rtsa lnga'i byin rlabs/ rje btsun bir wA pa'i srung ba gnyis kyi byin rlabs/ brda chig brgyud/ sgrub pa lung byin gyi bar lam yongs su rdzogs pa/ bla ma brgyud pa'i
rnam thar/ glegs bam/ pod nag ma/ po ti dmar chung / gzhung bshad sras don ma/ dmar ma zin bris dang bcas pa sogs yi ge mang po'i lung / rten 'brel gyi srung ba'i byin rlabs
sogs thos shing khongs su chud la nyams su myong bar bgyis shing / grub chen Dombhi pas bkral ba'i 'grel pa lugs su grags pa'i dbang / Dombhi ba'i byin rlabs/ dag pa
gsum gyi myong khrid/ grub chen mtsho skyes kyis bkral ba nas gling mar grags pa'i dbang / nag po dam tshig rdo rjes bkral ba'i sku gsung thugs snying po kye rdo rje ste
dkyil 'khor bzhi'i dbang / gtso che'i chos sna sum cu rtsa dgu dang / theg chen chos kyi rgyal pos mdzad pa'i dag ldan snye ma bka' 'grel dang bcas pa dang / shar chen thams
cad mkhyen pas mdzad pa'i dag ldan kha skong / spyi don lung 'grel/ chos rje rdo rje 'chang gis mdzad pa'i gnad kyi zla zer sogs yi ge rab tu mang po zhig thob la/ dpal
rdo rje gur rigs bsdus pa

man ngag lugs 'grel sa lugs kyi dbang / dpal saM bhu Ta rdo rje dbyings kyi dbang / drag po gdan can lha bdun gyi dbang rnams thos/ rgyud sde spyi'i dgongs pa 'grel pa/ paN
grub dbang po a bhA yas mdzad pa'i rdo rje phreng bar gsungs pa'i dkyil 'khor zhe gnyis dang / grub chen darpaN gyis mdzad pa'i bya ba bsdus par gsungs pa'i dkyil 'khor
zhe lnga/ grub chen mi tra yo gis mdzad pa'i rdo rje phreng bar gsungs pa'i dkyil 'khor brgya dang brgyad rnams kyi so so'i lugs kyi dbang yongs su rdzogs pa/ rgya gzhung
so so'i lung dang bcas pa/ rje btsun ba ri lo tsA bas spyan drangs pa'i sgrub thabs brgya rtsar grags pa'i rjes su gnang ba brgyad cu tham pa gzungs dang sgrub thabs sogs
dgu bcu rtsa drug gi lung dang bcas pa/ shud skye grags pa rgyal mtshan gyis spyan drangs pa'i sgrub thabs rgya mtshor grags pa'i rjes gnang brgya dang bzhi bcu tham pa/
sgrub thabs nyis brgya bzhi bcu'i lung dang bcas pa/ rje btsun khro phu lo tsA bas spyan drangs pa'i thugs rje chen po'i sgrub thabs padma'i 'phreng bar grags pa'i rjes
gnang brgya rtsa brgyad lung dang bcas pa/ jo bo chen po rje'i thugs dam rje btsun sgrol ma phyag 'tshal nyer gcig gi rjes su gnang ba nyi shu rtsa gcig sgrub thabs kyi
lung dang bcas pa/ tsa mi lo tsA ba smon grub shes rab kyis spyan drangs pa'i grub chen brgyad cu rtsa bzhi'i byin rlabs/ so so'i rtogs brjod brgyad cu rtsa bzhi'i lung dang
bcas pa rnams dang / zur bka' rjes

gnang thor bu ba/ rje mi tra yo ga'i byin rlabs man ngag dang bcas pa/ rje btsun sa skya pa'i khyad par gyi man ngag gser chos bcu gsum gyi nang tshan tshe dpag med sprul sku'i
byin rlabs/ chag lo'i lugs kyi tshe dpag med dkar po/ paN chen nags rin lugs kyi tshe dpag med dkar po/ rje btsun mi la'i tshe dbang gong khug ma/ ras chung pa'i tshe
sgrub phyi nang gsang gsum gyi rjes gnang / tshe dpag med stod lugs lha nyer gcig gi tshe dbang / bram ze sdom bzang lugs kyi thub pa gtso 'khor lnga/ sman bla bde gshegs
brgyad/ 'jam dbyangs a ra pa tsa na/ 'jam dpal ye shes yon tan bzang po/ 'jam dpal dpa' bo grub pa/ 'jam dbyangs smra ba'i seng ge /'jam dbyangs shes rab 'khor lo/ 'jam
dpal nag po/ 'jam dbyangs dkar po/ dbyangs can ma dkar mo dbyangs can dmar mo/ bo dong pa'i thugs dam lha lnga/ sher phyin dkar mo/ phyag na rdo rje 'byung po 'dul byed/
u tsa bya rgyud lugs/ phyag rdor mdor bsdus/ gtum chung me'i gra gur ma/ phyag rdor 'gro bzang che bar grags pa'i khyung lnga pa/ phyag na rdo rje gos sngon can/ rnam 'joms
sngo ljang / chag lugs kyi rnam 'joms mthing nag /spyan ras gzigs gtso 'khor gsum pa/ dge slong ma dpa' mo'i lugs kyi gtso 'khor gsum pa/ thugs rje chen po yid bzhin
'khor lo lha bcu drug pa/ bcu gcig zhal/ seng ge sgra/ don zhags dpa' bo gcig pa gso sbyong rang gis blang ba dang bcas pa/ don zhags lha lnga paN

chen nags rin lugs kyi kharsa pA Ni lha dgu'i byin rlabs khrid dang bcas pa/ rta mgrin jo bo lugs zhal gsum phyag drug pa/ jo bo lugs zhal gcig phyag gnyis pa/ byang sems zla
rgyal nas brgyud pa'i rta mgrin nag po/ grub rgyal lugs kyi rta mgrin nag po/ gtsug tor rnam rgyal lha dgu/ gtsug tor 'bar ba lha gsum/ sme brtsegs dud kha/ jo bo lugs
kyi sme brtsegs/ mkhas btsun dge rtag pa'i lugs kyi sme brtsegs/ khro mo sme brtsegs/ mi g.yo ba dkar po/ mi g.yo ba sngon po/ ri khrod lo ma can/ mya ngan med pa'i 'od
zer can/ mkha' 'gro ma seng ge'i gdong can nag mo/ seng gdong dmar mo/ seng gdong nag mo lha lnga/ sa skya pa'i gdams pa khyung nag 'byung po 'ur 'ded/ gnyan sgrol yan lag
drug pa/ sgrol ma dkar mo tshe sbyin ma brgyud pa'i bka' babs bdun ldan/ sgrol dkar yid bzhin 'khor lo'i tshe khrid zla ba'i chu rgyun gyi rjes gnang thun mong ma yin pa/
de'i myong khrid/ yang sgrol dkar gyi tshe khrid thun mong dang thun mong ma yin pa gnyis dang bcas pa/ dbang gi sgrol ma dmar mo nor rgyun ma lha bcu dgu/ kha che paN
chen gyi khyad par gyi gdams pa dzaM nag phyi sgrub sbas pa bum 'khyil/ nang sgrub zhal gsum phyag drug pa lha dgu/ chag lo tsA ba'i khyad chos gsang ba 'dus par gsungs
pa'i dzaM ser zhal gsum phyag drug pa/ rje gha ya dha ra nas brgyud pa'i dzam dmar srog sgrub/ paN chen lugs kyi dzam dmar/ dzam dkar 'brug zhon lha lnga rnams so so'i

rjes su gnang ba/ rgya bod kyi yi ge mang po'i lung dang bcas pa dang / rje btsun sa skya pa'i khyad par gyi gdams pa thun mong bsgrubs pas mchog zhar la 'byung ba/ dmar po
skor gsum du grags pa la/ rje btsun rig byed ma phyi sgrub dpa' mo gcig pa'i rjes gnang thun mong dang thun mong ma yin pa/ gsang sgrub lha lnga'i byin rlabs/ ku ru kulle
dkar mo'i rjes gnang / khro bo 'dod pa'i rgyal po'i rjes gnang / dpal tshogs kyi bdag po khams gsum gyi 'khor lo sgyur ba chen po'i thun mong ba thun mong ma yin pa khyad
par gyi rjes gnang / tshogs bdag chags pa rdo rje lha bzhi'i rjes gnang / de'i man ngag gi tshogs rab tu mang po'i lung dang bcas pa dang / dpal mo snying gi gser thag
can/ lha mo ti nu/ nor rgyun ma dmar mo ste dmar chung ma skor gsum du grags pa'i rjes gnang man ngag dang bcas pa thos la/ de dag gi bstan pa srung bar byed pa/ jo bo rje'i
thugs dam mgon po gsum sbags ma'i phyi sgrub kyi rjes gnang thun mong dang thun mong ma yin pa/ gsang sgrub kyi rjes gnang / lha mo re ma ti'i rjes gnang thun mong dang
thun mong ma yin pa dang / dpal nag po chen po gur gyi mgon po la rtsa ba'i bka' babs bzhi bzhugs pa las/ rje 'brog mi nas brgyud pa gri gug lha lnga'i sindhu ra'i dkyil
'khor du dbang bzhi yongs su rdzogs pa/ dpa' bo gcig pa'i rjes gnang dang bcas pa/ ba ri lo tsA ba nas brgyud pa'i pho rkyang dpa' bo gcig pa/ mal lo tsA ba nas brgyud

pa la/ lha lnga/ lha brgyad/ lha bcu gnyis ma rnams kyi dkyil 'khor du dbang bskur ba dang / pho rkyang / khro bo bcu/ lcam dral/ lha brgyad/ lha bcu gnyis ma/ zangs gri skor
gsum/ pu tra rnams kyi rjes su gnang ba/ phyi nang gsang ba'i man ngag ji snyed pa dang bcas pa/ dpal nag po chen po gyi ljang lugs kyi lha bcu bdun pa'i dbang / rgyud
kyi bshad pa man ngag du mas brgyan pa/ paN chen nags rin nas brgyud pa'i gur mgon lha lnga'i rjes gnang man ngag dang bcas pa/ dpal dud sol lha mo phyi sgrub kyi rjes gnang
thun mong dang thun mong ma yin pa/ gsang sgrub kyi rjes gnang nan chags mar grags pa/ rgyud gsum man ngag du ma dang bcas pa/ dpa' bo stobs 'phrog dbang po/ bsnyen
sgrub/ las sbyor/ spogs chog /dam tshig mgon po/ dkar po tshe 'phel/ ser po bsod nams rgyas byed/ khyung zhal can rnams kyi rjes su gnang ba phyi nang gsang ba'i man ngag
zab cing gnyan pa shin tu mang po/ dpal dur khrod bdag po'i rjes gnang / gsang ba snying gi 'khor lo'i rgyud rgya bod kyi yi ge mang po dang bcas pa/ dkar bdud lcam dral
gyi rjes gnang rgyud dang man ngag duu mas mdzes pa dang / dpal chos skyong ba'i rgyal po chen po rnam thos sras zhi ba bde byed dregs byed dang bcas pa dang / zhi ba bde
byed/ rnam sras stod lugs/ ljang ser be con ma/ drag byed seng zhon ma klu brgyad kyis bskor ba mthing kha zhal gsum phyag drug pa lha bco lnga pa/

rnam sras sprin gseb ma/ mgon po gar mkhan mchog dmar smug zhal gsum phyag bco brgyad pa lha brgyad pa/ gar mkhan mchog ljang gu zhal gcig phyag bco brgyad pa/ nang ma mo ltar
sgrub pa rta sngon can bdud mo dgus bskor ba/ gsang ba gshin rje ltar sgrub pa mdung dmar can lha bcu gsum pa/ yang gsang mdung dmar can phyag mtshan bzhi pa lha bcu
gsum pa/ las mkhan dang bcas pa'i mdung dmar can/ yang gsang drag po rab tu khros pa srin po bzhi skor/ dkar po tshe 'phel lha dgu rnams kyi rjes su gnang ba/ gar mkhan mchog
gi brtag pa dang / snod grub pa'i rgyud sogs rgyud mang po/ bde byed kyi rtog pa sogs rgya gzhung mang po/ mgul khug sro ma can sogs bod kyi yi ge rab tu mang po'i lung
/ mgon po bed dmar lha gnyis pa'i rjes gnang / mgon po zhal dmar can lha nyer drug pa'i rjes gnang man ngag du ma dang bcas pa/ lha mo rdo rje rab brtan ma'i rjes gnang
/ bka' gtad/ ne rkyal mar grags pa'i lung / lha mo dmag zor re ma ti'i rjes gnang nag mo srog sgrub sogs man ngag du ma'i lung / gnod sbyin beg rtse can gyi rjes su gnang
ba rgyud gnyis cha lag dang bcas pa'i lung rnams thob/ gzhan yang slob dpon chen po padma rdo rjes mdzad pa'i gsang ba grub pa sogs grub pa sde bdun/ bram ze chen po'i
do ha mdzod sogs snying po skor gsum/ tog rtse ba'i bsam mi khyab sogs phra mo ste phyag rgya chen po'i don ston pa'i gzhung de dag gi lung dang rdo rje phag mo'i byin
rlabs

dang / shA ba ri dbang phyug gi brda dbang zab mo zhus nas/ do ha skor gsum gyi bshad pa spar phu ba'i lugs shin tu rgyas pa/ phyag rgya chen po'i brda'i man ngag /rgya gar
gsang gcod che chung gi khrid lung dang bcas pa/ thugs rje chen po lha lnga'i dbang zhus nas dmar khrid tshem bu lugs/ byang chub bzang po'i lugs gnyis kyi nyams khrid lung
dang bcas pa/ phag mo dbu bcad ma'i byin rlabs/ so rig pa gcer mthong gi khrid lung dang bcas pa/ zhi byed utpal gser gyi 'dab drug gi khrid/ snying po don gsum gyi nyams
khrid lung dang bcas pa/ thugs rje chen po lha bcu gsum pa'i dbang / rje btsun 'jam dbyangs/ phyag na rdo rje/ tshe dpag med/ sgrol ma sngo ljang / dzam bha la ser po
ste lnga'i rjes su gnang ba zhus nas sku 'jam dpal gyi khrid shes rab blo 'phel rgyan gyi 'khor lo sogs mi tra khrid drug tu grags pa'i nyams khrid yi ge ma tshang ba med
pa'i lung / bka' srung brag lha mgon po'i rjes gnang dang bcas pa/ thub pa'i lha khrid/ thugs rje chen po'i dmar khrid/ sgrol ma rjes dran lnga pa/ mi g.yo ba'i chos drug
ste bka' gdams lha bzhi'i khrid lung dang bcas pa/ khros nag lha lnga'i dbang zhus nas gcod zab don lugs kyi nyams khrid yi ge ma tshang ba med pa'i lung / ma gcig mkha'
'gro sde lngas bskor ba'i byin rlabs zhus nas gcod bka' gso ma rgyal thang lugs su grags pa'i nyams khrid yi ge ma lus pa'i lung / gcod yul ma khrid chen po'i nyams khrid
lung /

gcod gdan thog gcig ma'i nyams khrid dang lung / gtum mo'i me dbang zhus nas rgwa lo'i lugs kyi gtum mo zhag bdun ma'i khrid dang lung / phyag rgya chen po nor bu mthong grol
gyi khrid ma bzhi bu bcu bdun dang bcas pa'i lung / spang lung pa'i sba bzhi'i khrid dang yi ge'i lung / rje btsun mar pa lo tsA ba chen po'i thugs bcud rtsa rlung dra
mig 'khor lo/ 'pho ba spyi rdol/ bar do blo chod/ phyag rgya chen po'i tshig bsdus te shog ril bzhi par grags pa rnams thos so/ /rgya bod thams cad du nyi zla ltar grags
pa'i mkhas grub chen po shangs pa gdub bu'i lugs kyi skor thob pa la/ rgyud sde lnga rigs bsdus pa lha brgyad dang nyi shu rtsa gsum gyi dkyil 'khor du smin byed kyi dbang
bzhi yongs su rdzogs par zhus nas/ byin rlabs khog 'bubs kyi bka' gnyis/ gzhung shing gi bka' brgyad/ mkha' spyod bka' lnga/ phyag chen bka' lnga/ 'pho ba bar do'i spyi
bka'/ byin rlabs dngul gdung ma'i bka'/ chang mchod bka' rgya ma'i bka'/ gsang sgrub gsum gyi bka'/ sU kha siddhi'i bka'/ dug lnga lam khyer gyi bka'/ lus 'chi med kyi
bka'/ nor 'dzin gyi bka'/ rta mgrin gsang sgrub kyi bka' rnams gang 'os su sbyar ba'i rtsa ba phyag rgya chen po/ sdong po ne gu'i chos drug /yal ga lam khyer rnam gsum/
'bras bu 'chi med rang grol rnams kyi nyams khrid/ zhal gdams du mas mdzes par byas pa dang / me tog mkha' spyod dkar dmar/ snang ba rang sems/

sku gsum lam khyer sogs kyi man ngag du ma/ sU kha chos drug gi nyams khrid/ bla ma brgyud pa'i rnam thar rdzogs pa sogs 'jag pas ma lugs gnyis las 'ongs pa'i yi ge rab tu
mang po ste mdor na brgyud pa'i bka' babs bdun tsam las 'ongs pa'i man ngag yongs su rdzogs pa dang / bka' srung myur mdzad ye shes kyi mgon po phyag drug pa'i rjes gnang
bar chad kun sel/ gtor dbang bar chad kun sel/ bla ma mgon po dbyer med de/ mgon po rgyan can/ mchog sgrub mgon po/ mgon po gur gum mdog can zhal brgyad phyag bcu drug pa/
mgon po mchin kha/ mgon po dmar po dbang gi rgyal po/ mgon po ser po/ mgon po dkar po yid bzhin nor bu/ mgon po gzi ldan/ mgon po sna tshogs mkha' 'gro ljang nag lha lnga'i
tshe dbang / mgon ser tshe'i bdag po'i tshe dbang / grib sel/ gnad dbab/ lha bzhi'i dril grub rnams kyi rjes su gnang ba man ngag gi tshogs ci rigs pa dang bcas pa
thos/ bka' brgyud bstan pa'i mnga' bdag rje 'brug pa'i gdams ngag sdong po gsum bsgril du grags pa la/ rtogs pa sgam po lugs la bshad pa gzhung gi skor la/ do ha/ gser phreng
/ sku drin bcu gcig pa rnams kyi gzhung 'grel lhan thabs dang bcas pa/ gdams ngag nyams len gyi skor la/ bsam mi khyab/ bsam gtan thun 'jog /thog babs rnams kyi man
ngag /nyams len byin rlabs kyi skor la/

phyag rgya chen po lhan cig skyes sbyor gyi nyams khrid/ bdud lam khyer/ rnal 'byor bzhi'i rim pa/ gdams ngag ras chung lugs las/ ro snyoms sgang 'gril dang / dkor mdzod le'u
drug pa'i nyams khrid/ rten 'brel kho bo lugs la/ rabs bdun ma'i nyams khrid/ tshig mchog ma dang / phra rgyas sogs yi ge mang po'i lung / gzhan yang zab chos nA ro'i
chos drug gi nyams khrid/ 'khor lo sdom pa bcu gsum ma'i dbang zhus nas bde mchog snyan brgyud kyi dbang bzhi'i lam yongs su rdzogs pa'i nyams khrid/ rdo rje phag mo'i byin
rlabs/ thod dbang me'i 'khor lo/ ka pA la mchod pa'i rjes gnang / mo khrid yongs su rdzogs pa/ bka' srung skong kha'i bka' gtad kyi bar nges pa can bdun gyi sgo nas lam
yongs su rdzogs pa/ bla ma mos gus kyi myong khrid/ khrid chen phyi ma bdun gyi lung khrid/ bka' brgyud gser phreng du grags pa rdo rje 'chang nas/ dbon rin po che'i bar
gyi bla ma brgyud pa'i rnam thar yongs su rdzogs pa/ rje gtsang pa rgya ras pa'i bka' 'bum rdzogs pa/ seng ge dgu tshar gyi bka' 'bum/ rgyal dbang rje yab sras kyi bka'
'bum yongs su rdzogs pa/ yang rje btsun chen po 'ba' ra ba nas brgyud pa'i chos/ rgyal ba yang dgon pa chen po'i thugs kyi bcud ri chos skor gsum las nang sgom chen la dgos
pa'i skor gsum yongs su rdzogs pa/ chos sgo 'byed pa ting nge 'dzin gyi dbang dang bcas pa/ bka' brgyud byin rlabs kyi dbang dang / phag mo'i byin

rlabs zhus nas phyag chen chos drug gi nyams khrid/ de'i yi ge ma tshang ba med pa'i lung / khrid chen phyi ma bdun cha lag dang bcas pa'i lung / sbas pa mig 'byed kyi dbang
dang bcas pa/ chos rje gtsang smyon pa'i lugs kyi bde mchog drug cu rtsa gnyis ma'i dbang zhus nas/ ras chung snyan rgyud gsar mar grags pa yongs su rdzogs pa/ rje mi la'i
rnam mgur gyi lung / gzhan yang mkha' 'gro gsang lam chen ma'i khrid dang yi ge'i lung / rgyal dbang gsang lam skor/ shA ba ri phyi 'gyur gyi skor/ chos sgo 'byed pa
gtor ma'i dbang zhus nas sems khrid yid bzhin nor bu'i nyams khrid/ 'pho ba don gyi gsal 'debs/ gcod yul yid bzhin nor bu sogs yi ge mtha' dag gi lung / bka' srung thal mo
brdabs chog gi rjes gnang man ngag dang bcas pa/ phyag rgya chen po yi ge bzhi pa/ lnga ldan/ sku gsum ngo sprod rnams kyi nyams khrid/ dwags po'i bka' 'bum dang / 'bri
gung dgongs gcig gi lung / de dag gi bstan pa srung ba dpal ye shes kyi mgon po phyag bzhi pa'i rjes su gnang ba rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor la brten pa'i shin tu rgyas pa/
tshom bu la brten pa'i 'bring po/ rong gling lo tsA ba'i lugs kyi rjes gnang / rgwa lo'i lugs kyi rjes gnang / gtor dbang rin po che phreng ba/ khams chen rgan las pa'i
lugs kyi rjes gnang / 'khor lo lnga ma dang bzhi ma'i nyams khrid/ las gsang ba'i rgyud dang man ngag zab bsdus ci rigs pa dang bcas pa/

zhing skyong kun dga' gzhon nu sgar lugs kyi rjes gnang dang bcas pa/ dpal mgon ber nag can gyi rjes gnang / trag shad spu gri gcig shur gyi rjes gnang shog dril bcu gsum sogs
man ngag du ma'i lung / jo mo bkra shis tshe ring ma'i rjes gnang man ngag dang bcas pa rnams thos te/ de ltar na re zhig gsang sngags gsar ma'i phyogs ni de tsam mo/
/gsang sngags rnying ma bka' gter du grags pa'i dang po bka' ma'i phyogs la/ na rag dong sprugs dam pa rigs brgya'i rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor chen por rim gyis lugs kyi
dbang rdzogs pa lung dang bcas pa/ rje bai ro tsa nas spang mi pham mgon po la snyan brgyud du gdams shing mi rabs bdun gyi bar 'ja' lus kyi ming can ye shes kyi sku mngon
du mdzad pa kho na byung ba'i zab chos rdo rje zam pa'i skor la/ yang dag grub pa lha bdun gyi rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor du sgom tshul bla ma'i byin rlabs rgyas 'bring
bsdus gsum tshe dbang dang bcas pa zhus nas rdo rje zam pa'i nyams khrid/ yi ge ma tshang ba med pa'i lung / bka' srung 'bar ba'i gdong can ma'i bka' gtad dang bcas pa/
phur pa man ngag drug pa'i dbang / lcam mchod gnas ma'i lugs kyi tshe dbang / gshin rje 'khor lo nag po'i skor la/ rig rgyal chen po lha zhe drug gi rdul tshon gyi dkyil
'khor chen por bam chen gsang pa'i dbang bzhi yongs su rdzogs pa/ dbang 'bring po/ bkra shis tshe dbang rnams zhus nas/ stod dkar po byang chub lam gyi sgron ma dang / smad
drag po las kyi 'khor lo nag por sgrub pa'i man ngag yongs su rdzogs pa/ 'jam dpal

gshin rje gshed dmar po phyi 'gyur gyi dbang bskur ba man ngag dang bcas pa ste/ grub chen dha na ta las gnubs yon tan rgya mtsho la gtad pa'i drag sngags gshin rje gshed dmar
nag yongs su rdzogs pa rnams thos/ gter ma la/ mnga' bdag khri srong lde btsan gyi skye ba bcu drug pa mnga' bdag myang ral pas srin mo sbar rjes nas spyan drangs pa'i
bla ma drag po dmar po'i dbang rgyas pa smin lam dbang gi rgyal po snang srid lha 'dre'i srog dbang / dbang rdo rje spyi lugs/ rtsa ba don dang yan lag gi dbang bzhi pa/
dbang bsdus pa cung mi 'dra ba gnyis/ byin rlabs lu gu rgyud kyi gtor dbang / dbang drag dpa' bo lha gsum gyi rjes gnang rnams zhus nas/ gzhung chen bde gshegs 'dus pa/
'bring po drag sngags me'i spu gri bsdus pa dpa' bo lha gsum rnams kyi man ngag ji snyed pa'i lung / lho brag kho mthing nas spyan drangs pa'i sgrub chen bka' brgyad bde
gshegs 'dus pa'i sgrub dbang rgyas pa dang / don dbang bsdus pa zhus nas/ bde bar gshegs pa thams cad 'dus pa'i rgyud la sogs pa rgyud lung nyi shu/ dbang gi mdo byang chen
po sogs man ngag bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i lung / bka' srung ye shes mgon po phyag bzhi pa lha bcu gcig gi bka' gtad/ sku gsung thugs khros pa'i rgyud dang / sgrub thabs
sogs man ngag du ma'i lung / yer pa ser ba gdong nas spyan drangs pa'i padma dbang chen yang gsang khros pa'i dbang / 'chi med tshe'i rdzong chung gi dbang / rgyud dang
man ngag du ma'i lung / bka' srung gying lnga gza' gdong gi srog dbang man ngag dang bcas pa/

rta mgrin bde gshegs 'dus pa lha lnga'i dbang / de'i tshe dbang man ngag gi yi ge mang po'i lung / rta mgrin dregs pa tshar gcod lha nyer lnga'i dbang / rgyud man ngag dang
bcas pa'i lung / rta mgrin rtsa ba lha bzhi'i dbang / de'i tshe dbang man ngag gi lung / rta mgrin lha lnga'i dbang / de'i rigs gtad yi ge'i lung / rta mgrin nA ga klu 'dul
gyi dbang / man ngag rab tu mang po'i lung / rta mgrin nag po lcags kyi ral pa can gnod sbyin nag po chen po'i rjes gnang man ngag zab mo dang bcas pa/ lha sa nas spyan
drangs pa'i thugs rje chen po rgyal po bka' 'bum du grags pa'i skor la/ thugs rje chen po 'gro 'dul lha stong dang nyer lnga'i dbang rgyas pa/ lha lnga'i dbang / tshe'i
dbang / rig pa rtsal lung 'bogs pa'i dbang / sems bskyed dang / bsnyen gnas kyi sdom rgyun lung rdzogs pa dang bcas pa rnams thob/ mnga' bdag gsung gi sprul pa gu ru rin
po che chos kyi dbang phyug gis gnam skas brag nas spyan drangs pa'i bla ma'i thugs sgrub gsang ba 'dus pa'i dbang / rnam pa nyi shus byang chub pa'i dbang / gtor dbang
gnad kyi shog gcig ma/ brgyad tshan brgyad sogs man ngag rdzogs pa'i lung / yang ti sangs rgyas mnyam sbyor gyi nyams khrid/ rig pa'i rtsal dbang / rgyud gsum/ stong thun
gsum/ khrid yig gsum yongs su rdzogs pa'i lung / thugs rje chen po yang snying 'dus pa'i dbang / rgyud dang man ngag ma tshang ba med pa'i lung / thugs rje chen po 'khor
ba dong sprugs kyi dbang / de'i gsang sgrub kyi dbang / kol ba dum bu'i rgyud man ngag dang

bcas pa'i lung / sgrub chen bka' brgyad gsang ba yongs rdzogs kyi dbang rgyas pa/ dregs pa'i srog dbang / rdo rje rgyal po bka' rab 'byams kyi dbang dang bcas pa/ rgyud dang
dbang 'bum sgrub 'bum gyi lung / rdo rje phur pa spu gri 'bar ba'i dbang / rgyud gzhung man ngag dang bcas pa ma tshang ba med pa/ rlung las byed 'khor lo'i rgyud 'grel
pa man ngag rjes gnang dang bcas pa/ rje btsun rig pa'i rgyal po'i dbang man ngag dang bcas pa/ lho brag gro bo lung nas spyan drangs pa'i chos drug sras mkhar ma'i khrid/
bdag 'jug rdo rje 'chang gi dbang / shog ril bco lnga'i lung / dzam bha la dmar po'i rjes gnang man ngag gi lung / bka' srung ma ning dregs pa'i srog dbang / spyi rgyud
las rgyud man ngag du ma dang bcas pa/ drang srong dri med kyi rjes gnang man ngag dang bcas pa/ bod skyong bstan ma'i srog dbang rnams nos/ gnubs chen sangs ye'i thugs
sras g.yas ban gyi skyes mtha' dum pa'i rgya zhang khrom gyi phung po ri bo che nas spyan drangs pa'i 'jam dpal tshe bdag nag po'i phyags rgya chen po zil gyis gnon pa lha
zhe drug gi rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor du bam chen gsang ba'i dbang thun mong dang thun mong ma yin pa/ bkra shis tshe'i dbang / sdig pa nag po snying la ru 'dzings pa'i
rgyud dang / sgrol ma drug pa sogs man ngag gi rigs du ma'i lung / rdza lhud mo nas spyan drangs pa'i 'jam dpal 'joms byed 'bar ba lha zhe gnyis kyi rdul tshon gyi dkyil
'khor du dbang bskur ba/ gshin rje dkar po lha bcu bdun pa'i tshe'i dbang 'char ka nag po'i zor gyi dbang / rgyud bdun la sogs pa'i man ngag ma

tshang ba med pa'i lung / bka' srung stag zhon nag po lha bcu gsum pa'i rjes gnang / man ngag ci rigs pa dang bcas pa rnams thob/ btsun pa ngan lam rgyal mchog gi skye ba sprul
sku tshe brtan rgyal mtshan chos kyi blo gros kyis mon chu phug nas spyan drangs pa'i bla ma rdo rje 'chang lha sum cu'i rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor du zab rgyas tshe
dbang du grags pa'i dbang rgyas pa/ rtsa ba gsum gyi gtor dbang zhus nas sgrub sde nyi shu rtsa bdun phal cher rdzogs pa'i lung / bla ma yakSha me sbal dbu dgu phyag bco
brgyad pa'i dbang zhus nas de'i man ngag yongs su rdzogs pa/ ayon tshe dbang rtsal lha bcu bdun gyi dbang / tshe sgrub bdud rtsi 'khyil ba yongs su rdzogs pa'i lung / sgrol
ma utpal phreng ba'i rjes gnang man ngag dang / sme brtsegs zhal gsum phyag drug pa'i khrus dbang man ngag dang bcas pa rnams thob/ sna nam rdo rje bdud 'joms kyi sprul
pa'i sku rig 'dzin chen po rgod kyi ldem phru can gyis zang zang lha brag nas spyan drangs pa'i skor la/ nyan thos kyi theg pa dang mthun pa'i bstan khrims dus khrims
kyi sdom pa/ rnam par snang mdzad lha so gsum gyi dkyil 'khor du byang chub sems dpa'i spyod dbang rin po che/ rgyud gsum man ngag dang bcas pa/ bla ma'i phyi sgrub thugs
rje chen po 'gro ba kun sgrol lha bcu gcig gi dbang / phyi ltar 'gro ba kun sgrol gyi rgyud la sogs pa rgyud gsum cha lag dang bcas pa/ yi ge med pa'i snyan rgyud kyi myong
khrid/ nang sgrub rje btsun chen po rdo rje drag po rtsal lha lnga bcu rtsa drug gi rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor chen po dbang bzhi yongs

su rdzogs pa'i dbang rgyas pa/ bum dbang rgyas pa smin grol rgya mtsho/ dbang 'bring po/ ka dag lhun grub rig pa'i rtsal dbang / byin rlabs thugs rje'i dbang lnga/ bla ma yum
can gyi gtor dbang / rgyal thabs spyi blugs kyi dbang / thems can dang thems med kyi man ngag ji snyed pa'i lung yang tig gces pa'i sgron me'i myong khrid/ gsang sgrub
bla ma zhi ba rig 'dzin gdung sgrub kyi rtsa dbang rnam pa nyi shus byang chub pa/ sgrub dbang rab 'byams bka'i dbang / gtor dbang thob chog blo bde/ thugs sgrub rin chen
'bar ba'i rgyud phyi nang gsang ba'i sgrub thabs sogs man ngag du ma/ sgrub chen bka' brgyad/ drag po rang byung rang shar chen po'i rtsa ba'i dbang / sgrub dbang rgyas
pa thun mong dang thun mong ma yin pa/ sgrub phran/ tshe lha/ nor lha/ khyung chen/ thod pa brtag pa/ bka' srung yongs rdzogs rnams kyi dbang rnams zhus/ rgyud bzhi/ bskyed
rdzogs kyi man ngag rab tu mang po'i lung / khrid gzhung ye shes zang thal dang / rim lnga'i myong khrid/ rang bzhin rdzogs pa chen po kun tu bzang po'i dgongs pa zang
thal du bstan pa'i skor la/ smin byed rgyal ba zhi khro'i rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor du bum pa'i dbang / rta phag yab yum gyi dkyil 'khor du dbang gong ma gsum/ ye shes
spyi blugs kyi dbang / nges don lta ba'i dbang / rtags grol gyi dbang rnams zhus nas/ dgongs pa zang thal gyi nyams khrid/ bla ma brgyud pa'i rnam thar rdzogs pa/ rgyud
nyi shu rtsa lnga man ngag mang pos brgyan pa dang / paN chen bi mA la'i lugs

kyi zhi khro'i dbang bzhi/ snying po thugs kyi dbang / rig pa rtsal dbang / ye shes spyi blugs/ rgyal thabs spyi blugs rnams nas/ khrid yig gzer bu gsum pa'i nyams khrid/ bi
mA la'i 'grel tig chen mo/ lo chen be ro tsa na'i snyan brgyud gsum thugs rgyud sogs slob dpon gsum gyi thugs bcud kyi man ngag thams cad rdzogs pa'i mthar gtad rgya dang
po rgyal tshab spyi blugs kyi dbang / gtad rgya bar pa bka' srung e ka dza ti'i bka' gtad/ rgyud sgrub thabs man ngag dang bcas pa/ gtad rgya gsum pa rig 'dzin nyi 'od
'bar gyi dbang sgrub thabs dang bcas pa rdzogs pa chen po rang byung rang shar gyi nyams khrid/ snying po spyod bsdus rig pa'i dbang / rgyud gnyis man ngag dang bcas pa'i
lung / yum rdo rje phag mo'i byin rlabs/ brtul zhugs gsang ba rmad byung gi nyams khrid man ngag dang bcas pa/ tshe dpag med kyi skor la/ phyi sgrub sman gyi bcud len tshe
dpag med rigs lnga rta mgrin dang bcas pa/ nang sgrub longs spyod rdzogs sku lha nyer gcig gsang ba rlung du sgrub pa lcags kyi sdong po/ yang gsang mi shigs pa thig
ler sgrub pa tshe dpag med dkar po lha bcu gsum pa rnams kyi dbang re re/ yang gsang tshe'i snyan brgyud 'chi med 'od kyi snang ba'i nyams khrid/ 'chi bdag zlog byed stobs
chen gyad kyi 'khor lo man ngag ma tshang ba med pa'i lung / dpal rdo rje gzhon nu che mchog dbu dgu phyag bco brgyad pa'i dbang / stod dkar po lam gyi sgron ma/ smad nag
po dug gi 'khor lo/ bar bka' nan lcags kyi ber ka'i man ngag

ji snyed pa'i lung / rdo rje phur pa yang gsang spu gri 'bar ba'i dbang / rgyud dang man ngag rdzogs pa'i lung / rdo rje gzhon nu dril sgrub kyi man ngag /bka' srung stag zhon
nag po'i rjes gnang / rgyud dang sgrub thabs man ngag dang bcas pa/ dug dbang shin tu zab pa/ lha chen stobs 'dul nag po dang / bsod nams dpal 'byor gyi rjes su gnang
ba/ phyi nang gi man ngag brgya rtsa brgyad/ dam can rdo rje legs pa rgyal blon lnga pa'i rjes gnang / gyin srog gi spu gri rgyud man ngag dang bcas pa/ gter srung so so'i
bka' gtad mchod 'phreng dang bcas pa ste mdor na gter kha 'di'i gdams pa phal cher rdzogs par thos shing khongs su chud la nyams su myong ba yin no/ /gnubs chen nam mkha'i
snying po'i sprul sku bya mang po ba dpal ldan rgyal mtshan gyis lha mtsho nas spyan drangs pa'i phyag rdor gsang sgrub lha bcu gcig gi rjes gnang man ngag dang bcas
pa dang / lo tsA ba chen po bai ro tsa na'i sprul sku rdo rje gling pas spa gro stag tshang nas spyan drangs pa'i gu ru drag dmar lha lnga'i dbang / thems byang lo rgyus
