ba med pa'i lung / gnam thang blang brag nas spyan drangs pa'i thugs rje chen po ngan song

kun skyob lha brgya rtsa brgyad kyi dbang bzhi/ ka dag rig pa'i rtsal dbang / thod rgal gyi dbang / gtor dbang / yi ge ma lus pa'i lung / gzhan ston bka' gtad kyi dbang dang
bcas pa/ rnam sras dmar po lha lnga'i rjes gnang man ngag dang bcas pa dang / de nyid kyi skye ba kun skyong gling pas spyan drangs pa'i bla ma drag po'i dbang man ngag
dang bcas pa thob la/ chos rgyal rin chen gling pas 'bri ldang ko ro brag nas spyan drangs pa'i gu ru drag dmar lha lnga'i dbang / rtsa ba/ sdong po/ yal ga'i man ngag rdzogs
pa'i lung / tshe sgrub bdud rtsi 'khyil ba'i dbang / nA ga raksha'i rjes gnang man ngag du ma dang bcas pa/ zhing skyong seng ge'i gdong can gyi rjes gnang man ngag
dang bcas pa dang / lha lcam padma gsal gyi skye ba sprul sku tshul khrims rdo rjes dang lung phra mo brag nas spyan drangs pa'i zab chos mkha' 'gro snying tig gi nyams
khrid/ smin byed rgyal ba rigs lnga'i dbang bzhi/ khyad par dbang lnga/ yi ge mtha' dag gi lung / dpal phyag na rdo rje dregs pa kun 'dul lha nyi shu'i dbang / rgyud dang
/ phyi nang gsang ba'i man ngag du ma'i lung / mkha' 'gro yid bzhin nor bu'i dbang man ngag dang bcas pa/ bka' srung gza' bdud chen po'i dbang man ngag dang bcas pa/ zhing
skyong ga ya dha ra'i srog dbang / rgyud dang man ngag ma tshang ba med pa'i lung / de nyid kyi skye ba mkhas pa chen po klong chen rab 'byams kyis mdzad pa'i mkha' 'gro'i
yang tig gi dbang drug shog ser/ shog 'dra shog skya'i skor shin tu tshang ba dang / bla ma yang tig yid bzhin nor bu'i myong khrid/ spros bcas/ spros med/ shin tu spros
med/ rab tu spros med kyi dbang / yi ge ma tshang ba med pa'i lung / bka' srung e ka

dza Ti'i rjes gnang rnams thob/ rgyal sras sad na legs kyi skye ba sprul sku sangs rgyas gling pas spu ri phug mo che nas spyan drangs pa'i bla ma dgongs pa 'dus pa'i skor
la/ padma badzra rtsal lha nyis brgya don bdun gyi dkyil 'khor du don dbang bsdus pa bdud rtsi'i thig pa/ gtor ma brda dbang / po ti lung dbang rnams zhus nas/ gter 'byung
lo rgyus/ spyi rgyud pad sdong brtsegs pa sogs skyed rim gyi skor phal cher rdzogs pa/ rdzogs rim rdzogs chen snying po gser gyi yang zhun yongs su rdzogs pa/ rta phag
mkha' 'gro rgya mtsho'i dbang / mkha' 'gro'i sgrub skor ma tshang ba med pa/ tshe sgrub bdud rtsi snying po'i yang zhun gyi dbang / blo 'phel shes rab ral gri'i rjes gnang
/ bka' srung rta nag dregs pa brgyad skor gyi srog dbang rtsa ba yan lag gi man ngag ma tshang ba med pa/ gshin rje sba dong nas spyan drangs pa'i 'jam dpal dkar po zhi
ba blo'i mun sel lha lnga'i rjes gnang / dmar po longs spyod tshe 'phel lha dgu'i tshe dbang / nag po bsrung bzlog thugs kyi tshal pa lha lnga'i dbang / rgyud dang man ngag
ma lus pa'i lung / tsa ri sgo srung rta mgrin mgul nas spyan drangs pa'i rta nag dregs pa lha gsum gyi rjes gnang dang man ngag gi lung / dgyer bye ma dkar po nas spyan
drangs pa'i tshe sgrub nyi zla kha sbyor gyi dbang man ngag dang bcas pa nos/ lcog ro klu'i rgyal mtshan gyi skye ba karma gling pas sgam po brdar gyi ri nas spyan drangs
pa'i zab chos zhi khro dgongs pa rang grol gyi dbang 'gro drug rang grol dang / dbang bzhi tshar tshad rang grol de'i nyams khrid/ bar do drug gi khrid yig sogs yi ge
ji

snyed pa'i lung / lang 'gro lo tsA ba chen po'i skye mtha' sprul sku ratna gling pas brag dmar ri mo can nas spyan drangs pa'i ghu ru'i thugs sgrub yang snying 'dus pa'i dbang
bzhi yongs su rdzogs pa/ gtor dbang yid bzhin nor bu/ gdams gtad kyi dbang / gsang khrid rim lnga'i nyams khrid/ sgrub pa sgrub chen/ kha skong dang bcas pa'i yi ge ma
tshang ba med pa'i lung / lho brag mkhar chu gsang phug nas spyan drangs pa'i ghu ru drag po dmar po'i dbang rgyas pa dregs pa'i srog thig dmar nag /dbang gong ma 'bring
po'i don dbang nor bu lugs/ bsdus pa gtor dbang byin rlabs sprin phung / thugs khrid kyi nyams khrid man ngag yongs su rdzogs pa'i lung / tshe sgrub rdo rje phreng ba'i
dbang rgyas pa dang / tshe dbang g.yang zhag 'khyil ba yi ge 'ga' zhig gi lung dang bcas pa/ klong gsal gyi tshe sgrub bka' rgya ma rnams thos la/ lha lcam padma gsal gyi
skye mtha' rig 'dzin chen po padma gling pas sman mdo nas spyan drangs pa'i bla ma nor bu rgya mtsho'i skor la sta gon dbang chog rdo rje'i go khrab/ rnam 'joms dkar po
lha bco lnga'i dbang / rtsa ba'i dbang rdzong chen dbang gi phreng ba/ bla ma gsang 'dus kyi dbang / gtor dbang rab 'byams bka' dbang / ghu ru sku lnga'i tshe dbang / dbang
nor bu sgron gsal/ gshin rje yang gsang bla med lha lnga/ phyag rdor yang gsang bla med lha gsum ste cig /phag mo yang gsang bla med lha so gsum/ drag po yang gsang bla
med lha lnga/ rta mgrin yang gsang bla med lha bcu gsum / rta nag dregs pa srog 'phrog lha

lnga rnams kyi dbang / thugs khrid/ yi ge rab tu mang po'i lung / tshe sgrub rdo rje phreng ba'i dbang / tshe'i nyams khrid/ rgyud dang man ngag ma tshang ba med pa/ ghu ru
drag po dmar chen zhal gsum phyag drug pa'i dbang / yi ge ma bu tshang ba'i lung / thugs rje chen po mun sel sgron ma'i dbang / de'i nyams khrid/ rgyud dang man ngag yongs
su rdzogs pa/ rdo rje phur pa spu gri 'bar ba'i dbang / rgyud dang man ngag yongs su rdzogs pa'i lung / rnam thos sras dmar po'i rjes gnang man ngag dang bcas pa/ mgon
po sde brgyad kyi rjes gnang / tshal brag phra rings nas spyan drangs pa'i phyag na rdo rje dregs pa kun 'dul lha nyer gcig gi dbang / rgyud dang man ngag ma tshang ba med
pa/ bsam yas mchod rten dkar po nas spyan drangs pa'i rang bzhin rdzogs pa chen po dgongs pa kun 'dus kyi dbang nor bu'i sgron ma/ zhi khro'i dbang rtags grol gyi dbang
/ de'i nyams khrid/ yi ge yongs su rdzogs pa'i lung / rig 'dzin rgod ldem pa'i sprul sku 'jam dbyangs bla mas sgrol byed nag po'i kha nas spyan drangs pa'i rtsa gsum gyi
dbang yi ge ma lus pa'i lung / rig 'dzin gsung sprul mnga' ris chos kyi rgyal pos bsam yas rnam snang thugs sgrom nas spyan drangs pa'i bka' brgyad yongs 'dus las/ ghu
ru zhi ba'i rtsa dbang rnam pa nyi shus byang chub pa/ sgrub dbang rgyas pa/ bla ma drag po dbu dgu phyag bco brgyad pa'i dbang bsdus pa/ rtsa ba'i dbang bzhi bde chen rol
pa/ sgrub dbang rgyas pa/ phan bde'i dbang / nus pa'i dbang / rab 'byams

bka'i dbang / rigs brgyud spel ba'i dbang / gong ma bzhi/ tshe sgrub ye shes 'od mchog gi dbang rgyas pa/ tshe sgrub phyi nang yongs rdzogs kyi dbang / 'jam dpal tshe bdag
zil gnon chen po 'od kyi thig le'i dbang / 'phags pa mi g.yo ba'i dbang / khyung chen gsang ba yang tig gi dbang / srin mo sbar rjes nas spyan drangs pa'i rnam pa bcu gnyis
kyis byang chub pa'i dbang / thugs gter nas byon pa'i ghu ru zhal gsum phyag drug pa lha bzhi bcu rtsa gcig gi dbang bzhi/ gtor dbang rnams zhus nas de dag gi yi ge shog
ser nas ji snyed 'gyur pa ma lus pa'i lung / kun bzang snying tig gi nyams khrid/ zhi khro dam pa rigs brgya'i dbang / padma snying tig dbang bzhi ye shes lnga rdzogs
sogs thor bu du ma'i lung / gzhan yang 'od gsal sgron ma drug pa'i dbang / nyams khrid/ zab mo rgyud lnga cha lag dang bcas pa'i lung / sprul sku grwa pa mngon shes kyi gdams
pa dzaM bha la dmar po dang / gnod sbyin zhang blon phyi grub ber nag can lha lnga'i rjes gnang / gter ston sta sde hUM 'bar gyi man ngag drag sngags mon pa ke ta'i
rjes gnang man ngag bcas pa/ rong zom chos kyi bzang po'i gter ma mkha' 'gro rig byed rtsal gyi rjes gnang man ngag gi lung / rgyud mgon legs ldan nag po'i rjes gnang / mdo
mgon ljang sngon drag po'i dbang bzhi yongs su rdzogs pa/ dur khrod mngon par rol pa mtshon cha 'khor lo'i rgyud/ dkyil 'khor bdun sogs man ngag mtha' yas pa'i lung rnams
thos te/ de ltar na/ 'bad pa chen pos bla ma dam pa rnams mnyes par

bgyis te/ kha sag dang stong zhus ma yin par gser gyi maNDal dang tshogs kyi 'khor lo sogs bla ma yi dam mkha' 'gro mnyes pa'i mchod gtor dang / yon gyis blus pa'i dbang lung
man ngag yongs su dril pas gsang sngags gsar ma'i phyogs la rgyud sde bzhi dang rjes su 'brel ba'i dpa' zung bka' brgya dang bcu drug /byin rlabs dgu bcu rtsa bzhi/ rjes
su gnang ba brgya dang bdun cu rtsa brgyad de/ spyi bka' rnams dang bsdoms pas dbang bskur ba sum brgya dang nyi shu rtsa gsum/ rjes gnang drug brgya lhag pa/ khrid bka'
brgya nyer gcig tsam dang bcas pa/ gsang sngags rnying ma'i phyogs la dbang brgya dang don gcig tsam dang / rjes su gnang ba sum cu so gcig khrid bka' sum cu rtsa brgyad
tsam zhig legs par thos shing / de dag thams cad la rang rang gi brgyud pa rim par byon pa rnams kyi phyag len phra rags/ tha na rdor dril 'dzin tshul dang rnga tshig
tshun ma 'dres par legs par sbyangs/ phal che ba zhig gi bris sku glegs bam/ dbang chas sogs ma tshang ba med par bzhengs/ rang don du thos bsam sgom gsum gang lcogs dang
/ gzhan don du 'chad dang rtsom pa gdul bya'i 'dod pa bzhin ngal ba med par bgyid bzhin pa 'di yin pas/ thob thob ces bya ba'i ming rkyang tsam du ma lus pa'i khungs yin
no/ /slad nas kyang / ji srid 'chi ba'i dus tha mar ma sleb kyi bar/ dge ba'i bshes gnyen bsten pa dang / da lta bka' ma nub par bzhugs pa'i mdo sngags gter gyi chos ji
snyed yod pa de dag ma lus shing lus pa med pa thob par 'gyur ba'i bsam sbyor skom pa chu 'tshol ba lta bu 'di nyid nam yang rgyun ma chad par brtson

pa 'di nyid yin te/ a ho sngon gyi dam pa de dag gi /dka' ba du mas bod 'dir bsgyur ba'i chos/ /snyan brgyud phal cher ston gyi chu 'dzin bzhin/ /mtshan yang lhag ma med pa'i
dbyings su yal/ /'ga' zhig grong khyer rnying pa'i khron pa bzhin/ /ding sang dus na mtshan tsam lhag mar lus/ /glegs bam phal cher dbul po'i gter bzhin du/ /sa rdul khrod
nas mun pa'i mal du gzims/ /dam pa'i rgyal po phal cher 'das gyur cing / /gdul bya'i 'bangs rnams bka' bzhin mi byed par/ /thos bsam sgom pa'i khrims la mthong chungs
pas/ /gsung rab slob dpon khros nas gsung mi 'byin/ /rgyu des dbang lung man ngag bshad pa'i bka'/ /cung zad lus pa'ang chu skam nya bzhin nam/ /nam gzhug chad pa'i me
tog ji bzhin du/ /lkog mar srog phyin gyur pa ma bzod nas/ /gzhan rkyen bstan la dad pa ches nyung zhing / /rang rkyen shes rab snying rjer mi ldan pas/ /bstan pa gsal ba'i
nus pa ma mchis kyang / /bstan pa'i sems khral tsam du ngas 'dir 'bad/ /ding sang dpyod ldan mkhas pa ches dkon zhing / /mkhas rlom phal cher phyogs re'i grub mthas khengs/
/ris med chos la dad pa'ang ma mthong na/ /mtha' yas dam chos 'tshol ba'i skal pa ci/ /'byor ldan phal cher blun po'i rkang pa 'dzin/ /'ga' zhig grags 'dod smig rgyu'i
rjes su 'brang / /phal cher lto gos sgrub pas rnam par g.yeng / /mkhas blun 'byed pa'i mig ldan nyin skar mtshungs/ /grogs dag dal 'byor 'di ni g.yo ba

dang / /slu med skye bo dam pa 'phrad par dka'/ /thub bstan nyin byed 'di'ang nub nye bas/ /myur du dam chos btsal na mi legs sam/ /de phyir nyin mtshan ngal ba yongs spangs
te/ /de bzhin gshegs pa'i bstan la rab gus pas/ /de ltar dka' bas dam pa'i chos btsal nas/ /de nyid rtogs pa'i thabs la 'bad 'tshal lo/ /zang zing bde skyid mching bus
mi mgu bar/ /dad brtson gtong phod gru rdzings cher bskyed de/ /ris med dam pa'i chos tshul rgya mtsho cher/ /thogs med 'jug par nus pa de su yin/ /de ltar thos pa tsam gyis
mi phan de'i don nyams su ma longs na mtsho gting gi rdo ba bzhin nam rgya mtsho'i 'gram du skom grir shi ba dang mtshungs pa gsungs 'dug pas rnam g.yeng thams cad spangs
nas mi med kyi lung stong zhig tu grogs med gcig pur sngo dang rde'u za zhing 'chi ba sgug sdod byed snyam pa lan gcig min par byung na'ang / byis pa'i dus su bsam med
rtsed mos g.yengs/ /dar la bab tshe gzhan ngo bsrung nas g.yengs/ /rgas tshe gzhan don ltar snang khur gyis g.yengs/ /blun po bdag la dal ba'i go skabs ci/ /shas cher
snyoms las le lo'i ngang du song / /kun rmongs gnyid kyi mun pas nye bar 'thibs/ /dgos med zing long mang pos mdun nas 'khyud/ /snying med bdag la gal chung chos su mchis/

yin pa/ nA ro mkha' spyod rnams thun re/ 'khor lo sdom pa lo nag dril gsum gang 'os re mos dang / gsang 'dus mi bskyod pa/ gshed dmar lha lnga/ bde chen ral gcig /phyag
rdor gtum chen/ yang phur gnyis rnams long skabs dang bstun pa'i dkyil 'khor rdzogs pa'am/ gtso rkyang gi mngon rtogs bzlas pa dang bcas pa/ phyag rdor u tsa/ sgrol dkar/
'od zer can/ tshe dpag med/ gzungs gra lnga rnams kyi mngon rtogs bzlas pa dang bcas pa/ mkha' 'gro chos skyong rnams la gtor bsngo thun bzhi/ gur gyi brag rdzong ma nang

bla med 'di rnams sku drin bsab phyir re re la'ang sgrub mchod brgya tshar re dang / bla chen thugs rje can de'i thugs dam gyi snying po 'jigs byed bcu gsum ma 'di stong
